语言的兴衰

The Rise and Fall of Languages

本书提出了一种研究语言变化的新方法，即间断平衡模型。该模型基于这样一个前提：在人类拥有语言的 10 万年或更长的时间里，大部分时间都处于平衡状态，语言特征在特定区域内传播，最终逐渐汇聚成一个共同的原型。有时，平衡状态会间断，民族和语言会扩张和分裂。最近，由于欧洲殖民和通信全球化，许多当前使用的语言面临灭绝。迪克森教授建议，每一位语言学家都应该承担起记录这些语言的责任，以免它们消失。

This book offers a new approach to language change, the punctuated equilibrium model. This is based on the premise that during most of the 100,000 or more years that humans have had language, states of equilibrium have existed during which linguistic features diffused across the languages in a given area so that they gradually converged on a common prototype. From time to time, the state of equilibrium would be punctuated, with expansion and split of peoples and of languages. Most recently, as a result of European colonisation and the globalisation of communication, many languages currently spoken face imminent extinction. Professor Dixon suggests that every linguist should assume a responsibility for documenting some of these languages before they disappear.

迪克森教授认为，常用的语言变化谱系模型适用于标点符号时期，但不适用于较长的平衡时期。他认为，语言学家、考古学家和遗传学家目前持有的许多观点都需要认真反思，并断然驳斥了最近关于人类原始语言可以重建的猜测。

Professor Dixon argues that the commonly used family tree model of language change is appropriate during a period of punctuation, but not during the longer periods of equilibrium. He suggests that many of the views currently held by linguists, archaeologists and geneticists need serious rethinking, and emphatically dismisses recent speculation that the original languages of humankind could be reconstructed.

1 简介

1 Introduction

目前，关于语言关系的研究往往采用“父子”联系的家族树模型，或采用相邻语言之间类别和形式传播的语言区域模型。家族树和语言区域通常被视为不同的现象；在本文中，我将尝试将它们整合到语言发展的全球视野中。

Current work on the relationship between languages tends to be in terms either of a family tree model of 'parent-and-child' linkage, or of a linguistic area model of the diffusion of categories and forms between adjacent languages. Family tree and linguistic area are most often treated as distinct phenomena; in this essay I will attempt to integrate them within a global view of linguistic development.

语言并非凭空而来，而是具有特定政治和经济制度的群体之间进行交流的手段。语言发展的综合理论必须关注使用已知语言或假定的语言早期阶段的群体的生活方式，以及他们与使用其他语言的邻近群体的政治、社会和语言关系。

A language does not exist in a vacuum but is the means for communication within a group of people, with a certain political and economic system. An integrated theory of language development must pay attention to the way of life of the group speaking a known language, or the postulated earlier stage of a language, and their political, social and linguistic relationships with neighbouring groups speaking other languages.

家谱模型是为印欧语系 (IE) 开发的，并且非常适合该语系。它已成为语言间关系的公认观点，因此语言学家试图在世界各地的每组语言中发现类似 IE 的家谱结构（无论其类型学概况如何）；同时还尝试进行详细的子分组。但在许多情况下，并没有认真尝试重建原始语言系统的一部分（这是必要的，作为家谱类型的遗传关系的证明）。对于某些语言组，例如闪米特语和波利尼西亚语，家谱模型完全适用。对于其他语言组，它可能不那么适用；被视为遗传关系证据的相似性可能实际上是由于区域扩散造成的。

The family tree model was developed for and is eminently appropriate to the Indo-European (IE) language family. It has become the received view of how languages are related, so that linguists attempt to discover an IE-like family tree structure in every group of languages, from anywhere in the world (whatever their typological profile); along with this goes an attempt at detailed subgrouping. But in many cases there is no serious attempt to reconstruct part of the system of a proto-language (which is needed, as proof of a family-tree-type genetic relationship). For some groups of languages for instance, Semitic and Polynesian the family tree model is entirely applicable. For others it may be less so; the similarities that have been taken as evidence for genetic relationship may really be due to areal diffusion.

原始语言的大致年代被确定为：原始印欧语距今约 6,000 年，原始乌拉尔语距今约 6,000 年，原始阿尔冈昆语距今约 3,000 年，等等。一般认为，没有哪个年代早于 10,000 年前。然而，考古学家和人类生物学家认为，人类至少在 100,000 年前就发展出了语言（许多人认为是更久远的过去）。在 100,000 年前或语言发展到现代家族的原始语言（6,000 年前或 10,000 年前）之间发生了什么？这个问题在文献中很少被提及，将成为下文讨论的核心内容。

Approximate dates have been assigned for proto-languages about 6,000 years before the present (BP) for proto-Indo-European, about 6,000 years for proto-Uralic, about 3,000 years for proto-Algonquian, and so on. No date earlier than around 10,000 BP is generally accepted. Yet archaeologists and human biologists believe that humankind developed language at least 100,000 years ago (many would put it considerably further in the past). What happened between 100,000 years ago or whenever language developed and the proto-languages of modern families, 6,000 or 10,000 years ago? This question, which is seldom addressed in the literature, will be a central item in the discussion below.

原始语言的重建部分往往呈现出整齐、同质的模式，几乎没有（如果有的话）不规则性。经证实的口语语言很少如此，通常有一个或多个底层（来自早期语言的特征，该语言已取代该语言）或上层（来自同一社会中一个主导群体以前使用的另一种语言的特征），以及许多杂乱的结构角落。我建议开发一种更现实的原始语言模型，关注可能产生原始语言的语言环境，以及从原始语言发展而来的内容；前者可能会为后者提供更多见解。

The parts of a proto-language that are reconstructed tend to show tidy and homogeneous patterns, with few (if any) irregularities. Attested spoken languages are seldom like this there are often one or more substrata (features from an earlier language which the given language has replaced) or superstrata (features from another language formerly spoken within the same society by a dominant group), and many untidy structural corners. I shall suggest that a more realistic model of a proto-language should be developed, paying attention to the sort of linguistic situation that may have given rise to the proto-language, as well as what developed from it; the former is likely to supply added insight to the latter.

语言本身是如何变化的？这是一个缓慢而渐进的过程（就像斜坡一样），还是变化发生得相对突然，中间有一段静止期（就像一系列台阶一样）？我认为，尽管某些变化可能是逐渐的词汇借用或音位变体的转变，但语言经历的大多数变化都是在相对较短的时间内完成的。这些变化包括从从属标记到头标记的转变（动词上粘性代词元素的发展，以及随之而来的格标记的删除）、从宾格系统到作格系统的转变（反之亦然），以及名词类别（或性别）的发展，以及其他变化。

How do languages change within themselves is it a slow and gradual process (like a slope), or do changes happen relatively suddenly, with periods of quiescence in between (like a series of steps)? I shall suggest that although some kinds of change may be gradual lexical borrowing, or shift of allophones the majority of changes that a language undergoes are completed in a relatively short time. These would include shift from a dependent-marking to a head-marking profile (the development of bound pronominal elements on the verb, and consequential dropping of case markers), shift from an accusative to an ergative system (or vice versa), and the development of noun classes (or genders), amongst other changes.

还有一个问题，即一种语言如何变成两种语言，相互理解的方言如何变成相互无法理解的语言。我再次指出，这种情况往往发生得相当快，只需几代人的时间，而不是拖延几个世纪（中间有一个很长的中间阶段，很难说我们拥有一种语言还是两种语言）。

There is also the question of how one language becomes two, how mutually intelligible dialects become mutually unintelligible languages. Again I suggest that this tends to happen rather rapidly, over the space of just a few generations, rather than being dragged out over centuries (with a long intermediate period when it is hard to tell whether we have one language or two).

在本书中，我提出了一个假设。受生物学中间断平衡模型（由 Eldredge 和 Gould 于 1972 年首次提出）的启发，有人提出了用于语言发展（和起源）的间断平衡模型。1在人类历史的大部分时间里，都存在着一种平衡局面。2 在特定的地理区域内，会存在若干规模和组织相似的政治团体，没有哪个团体比其他团体享有不应有的威望。每个团体都会说自己的语言或方言。它们会构成一个长期的语言区域，语言处于相对平衡的状态。没有什么是一成不变的，会有兴衰、变化和转变，但这些变化相对较小。然后平衡会被打断，发生剧烈的变化。这种间断可能是由于干旱或洪水等自然原因造成的；或者是新工具或武器的发明；或者是农业的发展；或船只进入新领土；或世俗或宗教帝国主义的发展。这些对平衡状态的中断可能会引发语言内部和语言之间的剧烈变化。它们导致民族和语言的扩张和分裂。与之前和之后的平衡时代相比，家谱模型适用的中断时期将很短暂。

In this book I put forward a hypothesis. Inspired by the punctuated equilibrium model in biology (first aired by Eldredge and Gould, 1972), a punctuated equilibrium model is suggested for the development (and origin) of language.1 Over most of human history there has been an equilibrium situation. In a given geographical area2 there would have been a number of political groups, of similar size and organisation, with no one group having undue prestige over the others. Each would have spoken its own language or dialect. They would have constituted a long-term linguistic area, with the languages existing in a state of relative equilibrium. Nothing is ever static there would be ebbs and flows, changes and shiftings around, but in a relatively minor way. Then the equilibrium would be punctuated, and drastic changes would occur. The punctuation may be due to natural causes such as drought or flooding; or to the invention of a new tool or weapon; or to the development of agriculture; or of boats, with movement into new territories; or to the development of secular or religious imperialism. These punctuations to the state of equilibrium are likely to trigger dramatic changes within languages and between languages. They give rise to expansion and split of peoples and of languages. It is during a period of punctuation which will be brief in comparison with the eras of equilibrium that precede and follow that the family tree model applies.

我认为，在平衡时期，语言特征往往会扩散到特定地区的各种语言中，因此在很长一段时间内，它们会汇聚成一个共同的原型。然后，在以扩展和分裂为特征的标点符号时期，一系列新的语言将发展起来，脱离共同的原始语言。

I suggest that, during a period of equilibrium, linguistic features tend to diffuse across the languages of a given area so that over a very long period they converge on a common prototype. Then, during a period of punctuation characterised by expansion and split a series of new languages will develop, diverging from a common proto-language.

这一假设自然延伸到语言起源的问题。存在着相互竞争的可能性。一种是语言发展到现代形式的过程非常缓慢，每隔几千年就会增加几百个单词和一些新的语法，从初级到原始，再到后原始，再到前现代，再到现代。我选择另一种情况。早期人类生活在相对平衡的状态中，认知和交流能力在发展，但没有语言。然后，通过某种标点符号过程，语言发展起来了。我认为它的发展速度会相当快，在几个世纪内（也许在几代人之内），就会出现某种可识别的东西，不是某种原始语言，而是一种相当成熟的语言，其复杂程度可与今天的语言相媲美。然后又会有一个平衡时期。

This hypothesis naturally extends to the question of the origin of language. There are competing possibilities. One is that language developed to its modern form very gradually adding a few hundred words and a few new bits of grammar every few millennia going from rudimentary to primitive to post-primitive to pre-modern to modern. I opt for the alternative scenario. Early humans lived in a state of relative equilibrium, with developing cognitive and communicative ability but no language. Then, by some process of punctuation, language developed. I suggest that it would have developed rather fast, and that within a few centuries (maybe within a few generations) there would have been something recognisable not as some kind of primitive speech but as a fairly fully developed language, comparable in degree of complexity with languages spoken today. There would then have ensued another period of equilibrium.

对语言发展间断平衡模型的可能回应如下。如果人类语言的历史（超过 10 万年或更长）一直以长期的平衡为特征，那么为什么我们今天在周围看不到这种平衡呢？答案很简单。过去 2000 年，特别是过去几百年，出现了壮观的间断（以前不太可能发生过）。世界宗教的兴起、帝国主义、枪支、写作和其他因素结合在一起，使得一些人和他们的语言变得更加强大，横扫了他们面前的一切。我们作为写作、阅读和研究语言学的民族，是这一现象不可或缺的一部分。当欧洲人闯入世界某个新地方时，他们提供了一个猛烈的间断。当科学观察员到达时（甚至他们到达时），社会和语言平衡就被破坏了。但只要仔细观察，它就可以被重建。促使我转向语言发展间断平衡假说的一个主要因素是试图（在 30 年的时间里）理解澳大利亚原住民的语言状况的经历，这个大陆的人民在数万年的时间里与世界其他地方只有最低限度的接触。回想起来，我们可以看到一个处于平衡状态的典型语言传播区。世界其他地方的语言状况可能也是如此；只有以适当的方式看待这些情况，才能认识到这一点。

A likely response to the idea of a punctuated equilibrium model of language development goes as follows. If the history of human languages, over 100,000 or more years, has been characterised by long periods of equilibrium, how is it that we see nothing of this around us today? The answer is straightforward. The last 2,000 years and especially the last few hundred have been the scene of a spectacular punctuation (such as is unlikely ever to have occurred before). The rise of world religions, imperialism, guns, writing, and other factors, have combined in such a way that some people and their languages have grown more powerful, and swept all else before them. We as a people who write and read and study linguistics are an integral part of this phenomenon. When Europeans intrude into some new part of the world they provide a violent punctuation. By the time scientific observers arrive (or even by the fact of their arrival), the social and linguistic equilibrium is destroyed. But it can, with careful attention, be reconstructed. A major factor in turning me towards a punctuated equilibrium hypothesis of language development has been the experience of trying (over a period of 30 years) to make sense of the linguistic situation in Aboriginal Australia, a continent whose people had only minimal contact with the rest of the world for tens of millennia. We can see here, in retrospect, a prototypical linguistic diffusion area that was in a state of equilibrium. The same may have been true of the linguistic situation in other parts of the world; these will only be recognisable if viewed in an appropriate way.

间断平衡语言发展模型的含义如下。家谱模型包含许多从共同的原始语言中分化出来的子语言，只适用于间断时期。在平衡的中间时期，语言区域通过特征的传播而建立，特定区域的语言将逐渐趋向于共同的原型。因此，在过去 10 万年或更长时间内人类语言的总体发展背景下，家谱模型的适用性有限。事实上，重建的极限是适中的。不幸的是，人们倾向于将家谱视为语言发展的唯一模型；该模型被过度应用，产生了不科学的“结果”。

The implications of a punctuated equilibrium model of language development are as follows. Family tree models, with a number of daughter languages diverging from a common proto-language, are only appropriate for periods of punctuation. In the intervening periods of equilibrium, linguistic areas are built up by the diffusion of features, and the languages in a given area will gradually converge towards a common prototype. Thus, the family tree model has a limited applicability in the context of the overall development of human languages over the past 100,000 or more years. The limits of reconstruction are, in fact, modest. Unfortunately, there has been a tendency to see family trees as the only model of language development; the model has been overapplied, producing 'results' that are not scientifically valid.

本文的最后一部分探讨了当今语言学的现状，即各大洲的语言都已消亡、濒临灭绝或濒临灭绝。它提出了一种语言如何才能生存下来的问题。答案是残酷的（但应该面对）。然后讨论了自称语言学家的人应该面对的主要优先事项。那就是走进这个领域，描述人类语言财富的某些部分，记录它消失之前的多样性。最后，我总结了如果我们要更好地理解语言的发展，无论是一般情况还是特殊情况，需要做哪些工作。

The final part of this essay looks at the linguistic picture today, where in every continent languages are dead, dying or endangered. It asks what it will take for a language to survive. The answer is grim (but it should be faced). There is then discussion of the major priority that should confront people who call themselves linguists. This is to get out into the field, and to provide description of some part of the wealth of human language, documenting the diversity before it is as it will be lost. Finally, I draw together conclusions about what work is needed if we are to achieve a better understanding of the development of language, in general and in particular instances.

此时需要提出警告。在当今世界的背景下，我说的很多话和得出的结论将被视为“政治上不可接受的”。此外，许多语言学家群体可能会因为别人对他们的专业领域所发表的言论而感到不快。不幸的是，这是试图从全球视角看待语言发展问题、试图诚实评估比较语言学和其他语言学分支的现状以及预测语言未来命运的必然结果。

A warning is in order at this point. Many of the things I say and the conclusions that are drawn will be regarded as 'politically unacceptable' in the context of today's world. In addition, many groups of linguists may be offended by what is said about their area of specialisation. This is, unfortunately, an inevitable consequence of trying to look at the question of language development in global perspective, of attempting an honest appraisal of the present state of comparative and other branches of linguistics, and of giving a projection of the future fates of languages.

 

 

2 准备工作

2 Preliminaries

“语言”一词至少有两种截然不同的含义。一种是政治意义上的，每个国家或部落都喜欢说自己说的语言与邻国不同。另一种是语言意义上的，两种可以相互理解的语言形式被视为一种语言的方言。通常，政治意义上的几种“语言”可能都是语言意义上的一种语言的方言。例如，在澳大利亚，大约有 700 个部落国家，但总共只有 260 种语言（语言意义上的）。它们通常是一些相邻的社区，讲一种语言的可以相互理解的方言。瑞典语和挪威语是不同的政治“语言”，但可以被视为一种语言的方言。相反的情况比较少见，因为中国是一个国家，人们有时把普通话、粤语、闽语、吴语等说成是政治意义上的单一“语言”的方言；事实上，按照语言学的定义，它们是不能互相理解的，是不同的语言。

The word 'language' is used in at least two rather different senses. There is the political sense where each nation or tribe likes to say that it speaks a different language from its neighbours. And there is the linguistic sense where two forms of speech which are mutually intelligible are regarded as dialects of a single language. Typically, several 'languages' in the political sense may each be a dialect of one language in the linguistic sense. For instance, in Australia there were about 700 tribal nations but only, in total, around 260 languages (in the linguistic sense). They were typically a number of adjacent communities speaking mutually intelligible dialects of a single language. Swedish and Norwegian are separate political 'languages' but could be regarded as dialects of one linguistic language. The opposite situation is found more rarely because China is one nation, people sometimes talk of Mandarin, Cantonese, Min, Wu, etc., as dialects of a single 'language', in the political sense; they are, in fact, not mutually intelligible and are separate languages, by the linguistic definition.

在本书的其余部分，“语言”一词均以其语言学意义使用；两种可以相互理解的言语形式被视为一种语言的方言。一旦坚决摒弃政治考虑，一般不难判断在特定情况下一个人是在与一种语言打交道还是与多种语言打交道。可以给一种语言的使用者一段用另一种语言写的口语或书面语，并通过一系列问题测试他们的理解能力。必须做出某些让步，特别是对于发音习惯。来自新奥尔良的英语使用者一开始可能会难以理解格拉斯哥的英语（反之亦然）；但经过几天的语音适应后，理解能力应该能达到 80-90% 的水平。

In the remainder of this book the term 'language' is used in its linguistic sense; two forms of speech which are mutually intelligible are regarded as dialects of one language. Once political considerations are firmly discarded, it is generally not a difficult matter to decide whether one is dealing with one language or with more than one in a given situation. A speaker of one variety can be given a spoken or written passage in another variety, and their comprehension tested by a series of questions. Certain allowances have to be made, especially for habits of pronunciation. A speaker of English from New Orleans might, at first, experience some difficulty in understanding the English spoken in Glasgow (and vice versa); but, after a few days of phonetic acclimatisation, comprehension should be at the 80-90% level.

当然，还可能存在其他复杂情况。一种情况涉及方言链，X 和 Y 的使用者可以相互理解，Y 和 Z 的使用者也可以相互理解，但 X 和 Z 方言几乎无法相互理解。而且，在极少数情况下，一个方向的可理解性可能更高。例如，葡萄牙语的使用者可以理解西班牙语，但反过来就不太适用了。（部分原因是西班牙语在某些方面具有更保守的结构；它有效地保留了底层形式，葡萄牙语已对其应用了各种历时变化。将西班牙语的 mano“手”和 color“颜色”与葡萄牙语的 mão 和 cor 进行比较。当必须将某些变化规则应用于西班牙语到葡萄牙语时，理解另一种变体要比必须解开葡萄牙语到西班牙语的变化更容易。）这些情况中的每一种方言链和单向可理解性都构成了边缘情况。必须做出决定（可能相当随意），并始终如一地应用，在这种情况下是谈论一种语言还是多种语言；我选择‘一种语言’。

There can be other complications, of course. One involves dialect chains, where speakers of X and Y can understand each other, and so do speakers of Y and Z, but dialects X and Z are scarcely mutually intelligible. And, rather rarely, intelligibility may be higher in one direction. For instance, speakers of Portuguese can understand Spanish but this applies less well the other way around. (Part of the reason is that Spanish has in certain respects a more conservative structure; it effectively retains the underlying forms, to which Portuguese has applied various diachronic changes. Compare Spanish mano 'hand' and color 'colour' with Portuguese mão and cor. It is easier to understand another variety when one has to apply certain rules of change Spanish to Portuguese than when one has to unravel changes Portuguese to Spanish.) Each of these situations dialect chains and one-way intelligibility constitutes a marginal situation. A decision (which may be fairly arbitrary) has to be taken, and consistently applied, about whether to talk of one language or more than one in such cases; I opt for the 'one language' decision.

我说过，撇开这些困难的情况（这些情况相当罕见），决定什么是语言通常没有什么困难。这是因为交流通常是一件相当简单的事情。读者可能经历过童年后学习语言的感觉。起初，人们几乎听不懂周围说的话或读到的内容；然后，突然间，人们听懂了大部分听到的内容（如果说得不是太快的话）或读到的内容。两种语言的使用者之间也是如此：他们要么听懂很少的内容（可能 10%），这里我们使用的是不同的语言，要么听懂几乎所有的内容（70% 或更多），这里我们使用的是同一种语言的方言。很少会遇到可理解性约为 50% 的情况。这与以下观点一致：当一种语言分裂成两种语言时，这种情况发生得相当快，只需几代人，而不是一个漫长的过程。

I said that, leaving aside these difficult cases (which are rather rare), there is generally little difficulty in deciding on what is a language. This is because communication is typically a fairly cut-and-dried matter. The reader may have experienced what it is like to learn a language after childhood. At first one understands almost nothing of what is said around one, or what one reads; then, quite suddenly, one understands a great deal of what one hears (if it is not spoken too fast) or reads. It is the same between users of two speech varieties: they either understand very little (maybe 10%) here we have different languages or almost everything (70% or more) we are here dealing with dialects of one language. Only rather seldom does one encounter a case of around 50% intelligibility. This is consistent with the suggestion that, when one language splits into two, this happens rather rapidly, over just a few generations, rather than being a long-drawn-out process.

我将做出以下基本假设，作为下文内容的基础。

I shall make the following basic assumptions, which underlie what follows.

假设 1

Assumption 1

每一种语言，以及语言中的每一种方言，都处于不断变化之中。每一代人的言语都与上一代人略有不同。

Every language, and every dialect within a language, is always in a state of change. The speech of each generation is slightly different from that of the preceding one.

假设 2

Assumption 2

一种语言的变化速度并不是恒定的，也是无法预测的。3相反，它取决于许多因素，尤其是该语言使用者所接触的其他语言。一般来说，没有近邻的语言变化可能相对较慢（例如冰岛语，其发达的文学传统的存在也在抑制变化方面发挥了重要作用）；如果有近邻，变化速度可能与其他语言在结构上的差异以及双语程度有关。4另一个因素是使用者对自己的语言和其他语言的态度；以及与此相关的政府的“语言政策”。非著名语言（或方言）可能会发生变化，变得更类似于大多数使用者都熟知的著名语言（或方言）。 （相反的情况不太可能发生，因为一种著名语言的使用者很少需要、也几乎从不关心学习附近使用的非著名语言（见第 6.2 节）。）

The rate at which a language changes is not constant and is not predictable.3 Rather, it depends on many factors, especially upon what other language(s) speakers of the given language are in contact with. Generally, a language with no immediate neighbours is likely to change relatively slowly (e.g. Icelandic, where the existence of a well-developed literary tradition has also played a major role in dampening change); and, if there are neighbours, the rate of change is likely to relate to how different in structure these other languages are, and to how much bilingualism there is.4 Another factor is the speakers' attitude towards their own language and towards other languages; and, as a related factor, the 'language policy' of the government. A non-prestige language (or dialect) is likely to change to become more similar to a prestige language (or dialect) which is known to most of its speakers. (The reverse situation is unlikely to occur simply because speakers of a prestige language seldom need to, and almost never care to, learn a non-prestige language that is spoken nearby see §6.2.)

一个不寻常的快速变化的例子是 Muyuw，一种在新几内亚海岸伍德拉克岛上使用的南岛语。Lithgow (1973) 报告说，在 50 年或更短的时间内，大约 13% 的词汇被替换了。语法也发生了重大变化，例如，说“我的膝盖”的旧方法是 gun-kitut（字面意思是“我的膝盖”），而新方法是 kitLtu-gw（字面意思是“膝盖我的”）。变化是如此之大，以至于一个离开 15 年后回到岛上的人最初无法完全理解他的话。Lithgow 评论说，“说话者喜欢借用邻近的语言和方言，无论是出于无聊、社会压力还是出于展示知识的愿望。我听到过村里的演说家在他们的演讲中夹杂着多布语和基利维拉语的词汇，就像一些说英语的人在他们的演讲中夹杂着法语和拉丁语的片段一样。”在这种情况下，社会态度导致词汇和语法变化的速度加快。

An unusual example of rapid change concerns Muyuw, an Austronesian language spoken on Woodlark Island, off the coast of New Guinea. Lithgow (1973) reports that about 13% of the vocabulary was replaced over a period of 50 years or less. There have also been significant grammatical changes for instance, the old way of saying 'my knee' was gun-kitut (lit. 'my-knee') whereas the new way is kitLtu-gw (lit. 'knee-my'). The changes were so great that a man who returned to the island after an absence of 15 years could not at first be fully understood. Lithgow comments that 'speakers love to borrow from adjacent languages and dialects, either from boredom, from social pressure, or from a desire to display their knowledge. I have heard village orators sprinkling their speeches with words from Dobu and Kilivila languages in the way that some English speakers sprinkle their discourse with snatches of French and Latin.' In this situation, social attitude engendered an accelerated rate of lexical and grammatical change.

假设 3

Assumption 3

核心词汇（最常出现的词素，见 §4.1 中的 (b)）比非核心词汇更不容易被借用，这并不是一个普遍的原则。这似乎适用于欧洲语言（见 Swadesh 1951）和世界许多其他地区的语言。但它并不适用于所有地方，也不能被视为公理，不能作为遗传相关性假设的部分基础。例如，在澳大利亚，通过比较相邻语言中的 100 个或 200 个或 400 个或 2,000 个词素，可以得到相似的共享词汇百分比。5

There is no universal principle that core vocabulary (the most frequently occurring lexemes see (b) in §4.1) is less likely to be borrowed than non-core items. This does appear to hold for the languages of Europe (see Swadesh 1951) and of many other parts of the world. But it does not apply everywhere, and cannot be taken as an axiom, a partial basis for the postulation of genetic relatedness. In Australia, for instance, similar percentages of shared vocabulary are obtained by comparing 100 or 200 or 400 or 2,000 lexemes, from adjacent languages.5

虽然目前几乎无需多言，但假设 2 和 3 意味着我们不应该关注任何据称由词汇统计计数证明的假定遗传联系，也不应该关注通过语言年代学方法推断出的语言过去阶段的年代（见 Hymes 1964：612ff.，以及 Bergslund 和 Vogt 1962）。正如 Birnbaum（1977：17）所说：“就词素和整个词汇的丢失（以及相反，保留）而言，语言变化率稳定（或至少可预测）且易于通过统计解释，这一基本假设必须被视为本质上错误的，因为它已被事实证据所推翻。”这将在 §4.1 的 (b) 中进一步讨论。

Although it scarcely needs to be said at this point in time, Assumptions 2 and 3 imply that we should pay little heed to any putative genetic links said to be justified by lexicostatistical counting, or to the putative dating of past stages of a language by the glottochronological method (see Hymes 1964: 612ff., and Bergslund and Vogt 1962). As Birnbaum (1977: 17) put it: 'the underlying supposition of a stable (or at any rate predictable) rate of linguistic change susceptible to statistical interpretation as far as the loss (and, conversely, retention) of morphemes and whole lexical items is concerned must be considered essentially false as it is controverted by factual evidence'. This is discussed further in (b) of §4.1.

我还将遵循历史语言学中普遍存在的一个假设，但这个假设最近受到了质疑。这对于本文其余部分提出的观点至关重要。

I shall also follow an assumption that has generally been made in historical linguistics, but one that has been questioned recently. It is crucial for the ideas put forward in the remainder of this essay.

假设 4

Assumption 4

在语言进化的正常过程中，每种语言都有一个母体。也就是说，当两个讲不同语言的群体合并形成一个拥有单一语言的社区时，这个群体将只是原始语言之一的遗传后代，而不是两种语言的遗传后代（不过，它可能具有来自第二种语言的相当大的底层或上层）。

In the normal course of linguistic evolution, each language has a single parent. That is, when two groups of people each speaking a distinct language merge to form one community, with a single language, this will be a genetic descendant of just one of the original languages, not of both of them equally (it is, however, likely to have a sizeable substratum or superstratum from the second language).

托马森和考夫曼 (1988) 在大多数语言出现的例子中都支持假设 4，但他们试图给出一些反例，即一种语言的语法和词汇似乎几乎平等地来自两种源语言。

Thomason and Kaufman (1988), while upholding Assumption 4 in most instances of language emergence, purport to give a number of counter-examples, where a language appears to have taken its grammar and lexicon almost equally from two source languages.

他们的一个反例是坦桑尼亚的 Ma'a。托马森和考夫曼将其描述为大量借用班图语的库希特语。他们认为，原始语言一定是库希特语，因为核心词汇的很大一部分是库希特语，但由于语法主要是班图语，所以我们这里的语言实际上有两个来源。曾在该地区进行过实地考察的 Mous (1994) 用不同的术语解释了这种情况。姆布古语有两种语域：一种是完全班图语的正常语域，另一种是“内部”语域（称为 Ma'a），它保留了班图语语法，但很大一部分词汇借用了邻近的库希特语。部落的每个成员都知道正常语域，这是一种未标记的语域，既可用于社区内部，也可用于与讲其他班图语的邻居交流。内姆布古语（Ma'a）为大多数（并非全部）姆布古人所知，并被用作内群体代码，以区分姆布古人和讲班图语的邻居。Mous 认为内姆布古语（Ma'a）是普通姆布古语使用者有意识地、有目的地创造的一种特殊词汇语域，以将自己与邻居区分开来。（请注意，Thomason 和 Kaufman 的结论部分源于论证错误。尽管他们在书中的其他地方提到了借用核心词汇的可能性，但在这种情况下，他们似乎假设，既然核心词汇基本上是库希特语，那么语言也必须是库希特语。6）

One of their counter-examples is Ma'a, from Tanzania. Thomason and Kaufman characterise this as a Cushitic language that underwent massive borrowing from a Bantu language. They argue that the original language must have been Cushitic since a substantial part of the core vocabulary is Cushitic, but since the grammar is predominantly Bantu we have here a language with, effectively, two parents. Mous (1994), who has done fieldwork in this area, explains the situation in different terms. There are two registers of the Mbugu language a normal variety which is fully Bantu, and an 'inner' variety (called Ma'a) which retains Bantu grammar but has a significant part of its lexicon borrowed from neighbouring Cushitic languages. Every member of the tribe knows the normal register, which is the unmarked variety both within the community and for communication with neighbours who speak other Bantu languages. Inner Mbugu (Ma'a) is known to most (not all) Mbugu and is used as an in-group code, to distinguish the Mbugu from their Bantu-speaking neighbours. Mous suggests that Inner Mbugu (Ma'a) is a special lexical register created by speakers of Normal Mbugu, consciously and on purpose, to set themselves apart from their neighbours. (Note that Thomason and Kaufman's conclusion resulted partly from an error of argumentation. Although elsewhere in their book they mention the possibility of borrowing core vocabulary, in this instance they appear to operate with the assumption that, since the core vocabulary is basically Cushitic, so must the language be.6)

托马森和考夫曼引用的另一个例子是白令海峡的铜岛阿留申语。这里的名词形态（以及语法的大多数其他部分）来自阿留申语，但有限动词形态来自俄语，词汇也来自两个来源。乍一看，这似乎是一种混合语言，有两个来源。然而，Golovko（1994）揭示了它的起源。他解释了 19 世纪阿留申群岛上存在着阿留申人和俄罗斯海豹猎人/毛皮商人，还有第三种群体，即“克里奥尔人”，他们是俄罗斯男人和阿留申女人的孩子。俄美公司（该地区的商业强国）承认克里奥尔人是一个特殊的社会群体，拥有自己的特权。 Golovko 讲述了克里奥尔人如何想要一种独特的民族身份，并认为正是出于这个原因，他们“发明”了自己的语言，这种语言可能始于一种代码转换游戏，然后逐渐制度化。我们之前指出，每个独立的政治团体都希望拥有自己独特的说话方式（并称之为语言，使用政治意义上的术语）。在极端情况下，他们可能会为此“发明”一种语言（这里将他们所知道的两种现有语言的部分拼凑在一起）。

Another example quoted by Thomason and Kaufman is Copper Island Aleut, from the Bering Strait. Here the noun morphology (and most other parts of the grammar) is from Aleut but the finite verb morphology is from Russian, with vocabulary also coming from both sources. This does at first sight appear to be a mixed language, with two parents. However, Golovko (1994) sheds light on its genesis. He explains how, on the Aleut Islands in the nineteenth century, there were Aleut people, and Russian seal hunters/fur traders, and also a third group, the 'creoles', who were children of Russian men and Aleut women. The Russian-American Company (the commercial power in the area) recognised the creoles as a special social group, with its own privileges. Golovko relates how the creoles wanted a distinctive ethnic identity, and suggests that for this reason they 'invented' their own language, which may have begun as a game of code-switching and then became institutionalised. We noted earlier that every separate political group wants to have its own distinctive way of speaking (and to call this a language, using the term in the political sense). In extreme cases they may 'invent' a language to this end (here cobbling together parts from two existing languages that they know).

假设 4，即每种语言都有一个单一的母语，包括“在正常的语言进化过程中”这一条件。这是指自发进化。我们确实发现了例外或准例外，如铜岛阿留申语和内姆布古语（Ma'a），在这些情况下，人们故意发明一种“混合语言”或一种特殊的语言语域，作为维护其政治身份的一种方式。7很可能所有“单一母语”原则的例外都是这种类型，这是由于有意识和深思熟虑的语言工程。8

Assumption 4, that each language has a single parent, includes the qualification 'in the normal course of linguistic evolution'. This is intended to refer to spontaneous evolution. We do find exceptions or quasi-exceptions like Copper Island Aleut and Inner Mbugu (Ma'a) in cases where people purposely invent a 'mixed language', or a special language register, as a way of asserting their political identity.7 It is likely that all the exceptions to the 'one parent' principle are of this type, being due to conscious and deliberate language engineering.8

需要先说明几个基本要点。首先，语言可能因为以下两个原因之一（或多个原因）而改变：

A couple more preliminary points need to be made. The first is that a language can change for one of two reasons (or for a mixture of these):

（一个） 接触引起的变化

如果某种语言的使用者中有些人也具有一定程度的第二语言能力，那么就可能导致词汇借用、音位变体的转变，以及语法类别和结构类型的变化，以及语法形式的借用。这将在下一章中讨论。

If some of the speakers of a given language also have some degree of competence in a second language, this may lead to lexical borrowing, allophonic shift, and also to change in grammatical categories and construction types, and some borrowing of grammatical forms. This will be discussed in the next chapter.

（二） 由于语言内部动态而产生的变化

正如 Baudouin de Courtenay 所说（Stankiewicz 1972: 63）：“语言（其结构和组成）的机制在任何特定时期都是其所有先前历史和发展的结果，而每个共时状态又决定了其未来的发展。”这在两种或两种以上在遗传上相关但在一段时间内未曾接触的语言以相同的方式发生变化时表现得非常明显（参见 Sapir 1921: 12791 中的经典讨论）。这种现象目前尚未完全理解，但似乎这些语言具有某种共同的内在动力，从而引发某种变化。例子包括：（i）格拉斯曼定律，将单词中两个送气辅音中的第一个去送气，在梵语和希腊语中独立应用；（ii）每个单词的第一个音节的去掉，这在澳大利亚不同的地理区域独立发生（Dixon 1980: 195ff.）； (iii) 德语和英语中独立出现了第二人称单数动词结尾 -st 的现象（Greenberg 1957: 46）；(iv) 一些藏缅语中也独立出现了相同类型的语法化，例如动词“send”或“give”成为使役标记，运动动词成为主要动词的方向标记，以及粘着代词的发展（LaPolla 1994 和 Matisoff 1991）。

As Baudouin de Courtenay said (Stankiewicz 1972: 63): 'the mechanism of language (its structure and composition) at any given time is the result of all its preceding history and development, and each synchronic state determines in turn its future development'. This is clearly seen when two or more languages that are genetically related but which have not been in contact for some time each changes in the same way (see the classic discussion in Sapir 1921: 12791). The phenomenon is not at present fully understood, but it seems that the languages share some common inner dynamic that engenders a certain sort of change. Examples include: (i) Grassmann's Law, deaspirating the first of two aspirated consonants in a word, applied independently in Sanskrit and Greek; (ii) the dropping of the first syllable from each word, which took place independently in separate geographical areas of Australia (Dixon 1980: 195ff.); (iii) the development of a second person singular verbal ending -st, independently in German and English (Greenberg 1957: 46); (iv) the same types of grammaticalisation having taken place, independently, in a number of Tibeto-Burman languages, e.g. a verb 'send' or 'give' becoming a causative marker, verbs of motion becoming directional markers on main verbs, and the development of bound pronouns (LaPolla 1994, and Matisoff 1991).

最后，提出一个反假设是恰当的，即质疑一个经常被提出的假设（即使只是隐含的）。即所有语言的发展，以及所有类型的遗传关系证明，都必须像印欧语系中发生的情况一样。正如 Benveniste (1966: 103) 所解释的那样：“印欧语系的构造模型不一定是遗传分类中不变的类型”。家谱模型非常清楚地解释了印欧语系语言的大部分发展和关系，它是一种重要的模型，在每种语言情况下都具有一定程度的适用性。但它并不是全部，正如本文的其余部分将试图展示的那样。

Finally, it is appropriate to make an anti-assumption, that is, to question an assumption that is frequently made (if only implicitly). This is that all language development, and all types of proof of genetic relationship, must be like what happened in the Indo-European family. As Benveniste (1966: 103) explained: 'il n'est pas certain que le modèle construit pour l'indo-européen soit le type constant de la classification génétique'. The family tree model, which so clearly explains most of the development of and the relationships between languages of the Indo-European family, is an important one, which has a measure of applicability in every language situation. But it is not the whole story, as the remainder of this essay will attempt to show.

 

 

3 语言区域及传播

3 Linguistic Areas and Diffusion

如果两种语言接触，而每种语言的使用者都对另一种语言有一定程度的熟练程度，那么他们可能会借用词素、语法类别和技巧以及一些语法形式（至少在一个方向上，通常是两个方向），并逐渐变得更加相似。

If two languages are in contact some of the speakers of each having a degree of competence in the other they are likely to borrow lexemes, grammatical categories and techniques, and some grammatical forms (in at least one direction, often in both directions) and gradually become more similar.

如果在一个地理连续的区域内使用多种语言，且该区域不存在跨文化交流的物理或社会障碍，则每个语言社区都会存在一定程度的多语言现象。多种语言特征会从一种语言传播到另一种语言，直到每种语言都适用于该地理区域内的相当大一部分地区，有时甚至整个地区。每种语言都可能与其他语言存在两种相似性：9遗传相似性，即从共同的原始语言中共同继承而来；以及地域相似性，即借用地理上的邻居。Emeneau (1956: 16) 将“语言区域”定义为“一个区域，该区域包括属于多个语系但具有共同特征的语言，这些特征不属于（至少）一个语系的其他成员”。这是一个很容易识别的区域。我们同样可以有一个区域，它包括几个语系的所有语言（任何语系的语言都不位于该区域之外）。如果每个语系的语言都分散在该地区，而不是聚集成一个整体，那么就有可能区分基因相似性和地域相似性。10 （亚马逊低地基本上就是这种类型的语言区。）

If a number of languages are spoken in a geographically continuous area which contains no physical or social impediments to cross-cultural communication there will in each language community be a degree of multilingualism. A number of linguistic traits will diffuse from language to language until each applies across a considerable region within the geographical area, sometimes across the whole area. Each language has two possible kinds of similarities to other languages9 genetic similarities, which are shared inheritances from a common proto-language; and areal similarities, which are due to borrowing from geographical neighbours. Emeneau (1956: 16) defined 'linguistic area' as 'an area which includes languages belonging to more than one family but showing traits in common which are found not to belong to other members of (at least) one of the families'. This is a readily recognisable area. We could equally well have an area which includes all the languages of each of several families (no language from any of the families being located outside the area). If the languages from each family were scattered over the area, rather than each being in a solid block, then it might be possible to distinguish genetic from areal similarities.10 (Lowland Amazonia is a linguistic area essentially of this type.)

值得注意的是，在一个语言区域，我们不会期望每个扩散的特征都传播到每种语言中。相反，每个特征都会有自己的分布，分布在特定区域内的大多数语言中；正是这些个别特征的叠加才建立了整个区域。

It is important to note that in a linguistic area we would not expect each diffused feature to have spread into every language. Rather, each feature would have its own distribution, over most of the languages within a certain region within the area; it is the super-imposition of these individual distinctions that establishes the area as a whole.

特征也可能有层次。桥本（1976b：50）展示了声调系统如何有助于将中国描述为一个政治和地理上界定的语言区域。但声调的数量各不相同，该地区北部的汉语有三种声调（紧随没有声调的阿尔泰语系语言之后），而南部的汉语有八种或九种声调（接近壮侗语系语言，这些语言本身也具有多种声调）。11

There can also be gradation of features. Hashimoto (1976b: 50) shows how a system of tones helps to characterise China as a politically and geographically defined linguistic area. But the number of tones varies, from three in Chinese languages in the north of the area (next to languages of the Altaic type, which have no tones) to eight or nine in the south (close to languages of the Tai-Kadai family, which themselves show a multiplicity of tones).11

每一个使用多种语言的地理区域都会或多或少地成为一个语言区域。我们也会得到区域内的地区，例如欧洲内的巴尔干半岛。文献中只讨论了这些区域中的一些。最著名的一个是北美西北海岸，从阿拉斯加一直到加利福尼亚北部（例如 Haas 1969，Sherzer 1976）。Campbell、Kaufman 和 Smith-Stark（1986）将中美洲描述为一个语言区域。

Every geographical area in which more than one language is spoken will become a linguistic area, to a greater or lesser extent. We also get areas within areas, e.g. the Balkans within Europe. Only some of these areas have been discussed in the literature. One of the best known is the north-west coast of North America, from Alaska down to northern California (e.g. Haas 1969, Sherzer 1976). Meso-America as a linguistic area is described by Campbell, Kaufman and Smith-Stark (1986).

Emeneau (1956, 1980) 和 Masica (1976) 将印度划定为一个语言区。这里的特征包括卷舌辅音、两种使役、与格主语和分类词（后者可能是从东南亚/东亚语言区流传过来的）。

Emeneau (1956, 1980) and Masica (1976) have delineated India as a linguistic area. The features here include retroflex consonants, two varieties of causative, dative subject and classifiers (the latter probably a flow-over from the south-east/east Asia linguistic area).

亚马逊河流域是一个资源丰富但研究较少的语言区。许多语言都具有这些特点（有时只在这一地区的一个区域，有时遍布整个地区）：闭中央元音，即单个流音；鼻音元音；以辅音元音 (CV) 为主的音节结构；倾向于使用塞擦音而不是擦音；多合成动词结构，带有许多后缀，表示情态类型以及位置、方向、持续时间、迭代等；从句通过名词化表示，并在动词上进行标记；单个核心论元与动词相互引用，对哪个论元进行复杂的条件设置，导致作格分裂；可让渡和不可让渡所有格之间的区别；名词上的所有者用代词词缀标记，代词词缀与标记动词核心论元的集合之一相同；复杂的分类器和/或性别系统；和证据性（参见第 9.1 节）。

The Amazon basin is a rich and little-studied linguistic area. Features which are found in many languages (sometimes in just a region within this area, sometimes across the whole area) include: close central vowel, i a single liquid; nasalised vowels; predominantly Consonant Vowel (CV) syllable structure; tendency to have affricates rather than fricatives; a polysynthetic verb structure with many suffixes, indicating types of modality plus location, direction, duration, iteration, etc.; subordinate clauses being shown through nominalisation, with marking on the verb; a single core argument being cross-referenced on the verb, with complex conditioning as to which argument this is, leading to ergativity splits; a distinction between alienable and inalienable possession; possessor marked on the noun by pronominal affixes identical to one of the sets marking a core argument on the verb; complex systems of classifiers and/or genders; and evidentiality (see §9.1).

在撒哈拉以南非洲，我们可以看到语言特征在大量相邻语言中传播的明显例子，例如声调、丰富的名词类系统、否定从句中有限的时态选择，以及（在一个地区）双发音塞音（例如，发音器官在 ag 处闭合，在 ab 处打开，就像伊博语的发音一样）。很少有人从传播的角度研究过非洲；乍一看，似乎有许多重叠的传播区。（这将在 §4.1 中进一步讨论。）而在最南部，还有一个额外的传播区，与其他一些以咔嗒声为特征的传播区重叠。

In Sub-Saharan Africa we get clear examples of the diffusion of a linguistic feature over a large number of contiguous languages, e.g. tones, rich systems of noun classes, restricted tenseaspect choices in negative clauses, and (in one region) doubly articulated stops (where, for instance, the vocal organs close on a g and open on a b, as in the pronunciation of the language name Igbo). Africa has scarcely been looked at from the point of view of diffusion; at first glance it appears that there are a number of overlapping diffusion areas. (This is further discussed in §4.1.) And in the far south there is an additional diffusion area overlapping with some of the others characterised by the occurrence of clicks.

新几内亚是世界上语言最集中的地方，在一个面积不到 90 万平方公里的群岛上（大约相当于德克萨斯州和俄克拉荷马州的面积）至少有 900 种不同的语言。其中约有 200 种语言属于南岛语系；其余语言分为约 60 个低级语系。有许多特征表明新几内亚是一个语言区，其他特征也适用于该语言区内的各个地区，例如，带头标记的从句结构；名词类；非人称动词；中间动词结构；束缚代词的双数（有时也包括三数或少数数）；代词非单数中第二人称和第三人称之间的对比中和。可能可以建立这些低级语系中的一些之间的遗传关系，但前提是可以解开地域和遗传相似性。首先需要对新几内亚境内的语言区域进行彻底的研究（例如 Foley 1986：2638），然后再找出看似由于扩散而产生的相似性，最后从非扩散的相似性中寻找共同的基因保留。

New Guinea shows the greatest concentration of languages in the world at least 900 separate languages within a group of islands of less than 900,000 square kilometres (about the same area as Texas plus Oklahoma). Around 200 of these languages belong to the Austronesian family; the remainder divide between about 60 low-level families. There are a number of features that characterise New Guinea as a linguistic area, and others that apply across regions within it, e.g. head-marking clause structure; noun classes; impersonal verbs; medial verb structures; dual (and sometimes also trial or paucal) number in bound pronouns; neutralisation of the contrast between second and third person in non-singular numbers for pronouns. It may be possible to establish genetic relations between some of these low-level families, but only if areal and genetic similarities can be disentangled. It is first necessary to make a thorough study of linguistic areas within New Guinea (e.g. Foley 1986: 2638), then to factor out similarities which appear to be due to diffusion, and finally to look for common genetic retentions from among non-diffused similarities.

澳大利亚也许是历史最悠久、融合程度最高的语言地区。它的特点是缺乏摩擦音；发音部位对比丰富（多达六个）；每个塞音对应一个鼻音；多达四个侧音；两个卷舌音；自由代词的三项数系统；不定代词也有疑问意义；代词使用主格绝对词形变化，名词使用绝对作格词形变化；在“禁忌”亲属面前使用特殊的“回避”语言风格。还有其他特征适用于该大陆较小区域：转换指称标记；名词类系统；一小部分进入许多复合词的词形变化动词；以及头标记系统，其中动词包括交叉引用核心论元的粘着代词。重要的是，几乎在每种情况下，特定特征都适用于连续的地理语言块。结构最独特的语言往往出现在沿海地区，一些传播模式尚未有机会到达那里。我们将在§6.3 的 (b) 中进一步讨论澳大利亚的语言情况。

Australia is perhaps the longest-established and most integrated linguistic area. It is characterised by a lack of fricatives; a rich set of contrasts by place of articulation (up to six); a nasal corresponding to every stop; up to four laterals; two rhotics; a three-term number system in free pronouns; indefinite pronouns also having interrogative sense; nominativeabsolutive inflection for pronouns but absolutiveergative for nouns; use of a special 'avoidance' language style in the presence of one of a class of 'taboo' relatives. There are other features which hold over smaller regions within the continent: switch-reference marking; systems of noun classes; a small set of inflecting verbs which enter into many compounds; and a head-marking system, with the verb including bound pronominals cross-referencing core arguments. The important point is that in almost every case a particular feature holds over a continuous geographical block of languages. The languages with the most individualistic structures tend to be on the coast, where some of the diffusional patterns have not yet had chance to reach. We shall discuss the Australian language situation further in (b) of §6.3.

 

 

3.1 什么可以扩散

3.1 What Can Diffuse

人类文化的任何方面都可以从一个社区借鉴到另一个社区，这种说法可能是正确的。萨丕尔（1921：205）说：“我们知道神话、宗教观念、社会组织类型、工业设备和其他文化特征可以从一个地方传播到另一个地方，逐渐在它们曾经陌生的文化中扎根。”在这个列表中，我们可以添加歌曲、仪式、政治制度、婚姻规则、动物驯养和农业。

It is probably true to say that any aspect of human culture can be borrowed from one community to another. Sapir (1921: 205) said 'we know that myths, religious ideas, types of social organization, industrial devices, and other features of culture may spread from point to point, gradually making themselves at home in cultures to which they were at one time alien'. To this list we can add songs, ceremonies, political systems, marriage rules, the domestication of animals, and agriculture.

语言作为一种文化特征，极易传播（见 Schmidt 1872）。哪些特征会传播往往因语言环境的不同而有很大差异。关于哪些特征会被借用以及在什么情况下会被借用，还需要进行大量研究。不过，可以提出一些初步的概括。

Language, as a cultural trait, is eminently open to diffusion (see Schmidt 1872). Which features diffuse tends to vary a good deal from one linguistic situation to another. A great deal more study is needed about which sorts of features are borrowed, and in what circumstances. It is, however, possible to put forward some tentative generalisations.

（一个） 语音学和音系学

人们自然倾向于让自己的发音习惯适应与之互动的人，这可能会导致产生新的音系对比（或消除旧的音系对比）。韵律对比和次要对比（如声调、喉音化、鼻音化）通常会消失。在大多数情况下，新的对比会出现，通过内部变化而不是借用形式来复制邻近语言中出现的内容。例如，印度-雅利安语通过一系列变化发展出回音（类似于达罗毗荼语），这些变化始于回音咝音，并通过同化等传播开来（Masica 1991：157ff）。

People naturally tend to accommodate their habits of pronunciation to those of people they interact with, and this can extend to the creation of new phonological contrasts (or the loss of old ones). Prosodic and secondary contrasts such as tone, glottalisation, nasalisation, will typically diffuse. In most cases a new contrast will arise to copy something that occurs in a neighbouring language by internal change, rather than through the borrowing of forms. For instance, Indo-Aryan languages developed retroflexion (to be like Dravidian) by a series of changes that began with a retroflex sibilant and spread by assimilations, etc. (Masica 1991: 157ff.).

（二） 词素

接触语言中新工具、新动物或新想法的名称可能会被新事物所取代。这是一种词汇借用。另一种词汇借用源于某些社会习俗，即忌讳使用死者的名字，也忌讳使用与该名字形式相似的词汇；这些词汇借用通常会被邻近语言的词汇所取代。

The name in a contact language for a new tool or animal or idea may be taken over with that new thing. This is one kind of lexical borrowing. Another kind stems from the custom in some societies of tabooing the name of a dead person, and also vocabulary items that have a similar form to this name; these are often replaced by a lexeme from a neighbouring language.

词汇借用的条件千差万别（将在 §3.2 中进一步讨论），但一般来说，任何词汇都可以借用（并且可能随着时间的推移传播到相当大的区域）。在世界某些地区，核心词汇（最常用的词，指身体部位、水、火、母亲、父亲等）的借用量少于非核心词汇；在其他地区则不受此限制。在许多情况下，名词的借用量比动词更自由；12那么，如果两种语言中动词的共同比例高于名词，则很可能表明它们之间存在密切的亲缘关系。然而，名词比动词更容易被借用这一特性并非无处不在，也不能被视为一般原则。13

The conditions for lexical borrowing vary greatly (and will be discussed further in §3.2) but, as a general rule, any lexeme may be borrowed (and may over time diffuse over a considerable area). In some parts of the world, core vocabulary (the most common words, referring to body parts, water, fire, mother, father, and the like) is borrowed less than non-core items; in other regions this restriction does not apply. In many situations nouns are borrowed more freely than verbs;12 then, if two languages have a higher proportion of verbs in common than of nouns, this is a likely indication of close genetic relationship. However, the trait of nouns being borrowed more readily than verbs does not apply everywhere, and cannot be taken to be a general principle.13

（三） 语法类别、构造类型和技巧14

语法的组织方式（而不是形式本身）总是倾向于适应其他语言的语法，而有些使用者对这些语言有积极的认识（并且这种情况会自发发生，而使用者对正在发生的事情没有任何意识）。15

The way in which a grammar is organised (but not the forms themselves) will always tend to be accommodated towards grammars of other languages of which some speakers have an active knowledge (and this will happen spontaneously, without any awareness of what is taking place).15

最常见的扩散特征可能是成分顺序（通常称为“词序”）。16文献中充斥着这样的例子，例如，在大多数闪族语言中，动词不在最后位置，但那些进入埃塞俄比亚的语言变成了动词最后位置，就像他们在那里接触到的库希特语一样（Leslau 1945）。成分顺序的相似性是遗传关系最糟糕的证据类型之一，也是试图重建原始语言的最无用的特征。

Perhaps the most common feature to diffuse is constituent order (often called just 'word order').16 The literature abounds with examples of this, e.g. in most Semitic languages the verb is not in final position but those languages that moved into Ethiopia became verb-final, like the Cushitic languages they came into contact with there (Leslau 1945). Similarity in constituent order is among the worst possible types of evidence for genetic relationship, and the least useful feature to try to reconstruct for a proto-language.

一种语言可以很容易地调整其功能特征，无论是中心标记还是从属标记（Nichols 1986），以适应与其接触的语言。分类器或名词类系统也很容易扩散具有这种系统的事实，而不是形式本身（通常来自语言的内部资源）。转换指称标记系统或连续动词构造通常也存在于连续区域的所有语言中。（例如，请参阅 Austin 1981 关于澳大利亚转换指称标记的区域分布。）

A language may readily adapt its functional profile whether head-marking or dependent-marking (Nichols 1986) to that of language(s) with which it is in contact. Classifiers or noun class systems also readily diffuse the fact of having such a system, not the forms themselves (which generally come from the language's internal resources). A system of switch-reference markers, or serial verb constructions, are also typically found in all the languages of a continuous region. (See, for instance, Austin 1981, on the areal distribution of switch-reference marking in Australia.)

其他类型的类别和技术（例如合并策略、名词化、关系从句）的扩散程度是一个需要在所有类型的借用情况下进行详细调查的课题。

The degree of diffusability of other types of categories and techniques (e.g. strategies for incorporation, nominalisation, relative clauses) is a topic which demands detailed investigation across all types of borrowing situations.

（四） 语法形式

世界各地之间也存在着巨大的差异，但总体而言，语法形式的借用不如词素或语法类别容易。不过，希思（1978）给出了澳大利亚阿纳姆地区的例子（例如，借用夺格后缀 -wala 和否定词缀 -?may?）。萨丕尔认为，语法形式对借用具有很强的抵抗力，因此，语法形式的相似性几乎总是表明了遗传关系。他提出（1921：203）“真正严重的形态影响也许并非不可能，但其作用非常缓慢，几乎没有机会融入到可供考察的相对较小的语言历史部分中”。确实，在家族树式扩张期间，相邻语言之间借用语法形式的机会很少。但是在语言平衡时期，时间充裕（也许是数万年），语法形式肯定会被借用。

There is again great variation between different parts of the world, but, by and large, grammatical forms are borrowed less readily than lexemes or grammatical categories. Still it does happen Heath (1978) gives examples from the Arnhem Land region of Australia (e.g. borrowing of ablative suffix -wala, and of negative affix -?may?). Sapir was of the opinion that grammatical forms are highly resistant to borrowing and, as a result, similarity of grammatical forms is almost always indicative of genetic relationship. He suggested (1921: 203) that 'a really serious morphological influence is not, perhaps, impossible, but that its operation is so slow that it has hardly ever had the chance to incorporate itself in the relatively small portion of linguistic history that lies open to inspection'. It is true that during a family-tree-type expansion there is little opportunity for grammatical forms to be borrowed between contiguous languages. But during periods of linguistic equilibrium there was time a-plenty (perhaps tens of millennia) and then grammatical forms certainly were borrowed.

然而，有些语法现象在任何情况下都不太可能被借用。这些是：

However, there are certain grammatical phenomena that are very unlikely to be borrowed, under any circumstances. These are:

（i）补充词，例如 good/better/best 和 go/went。

(i) suppletions, such as good/better/best and go/went.

(ii) 形态不规则，例如 sing/sang、bring/brought。

(ii) morphological irregularities, such as sing/sang, bring/brought.

(iii) 完整范例，例如代词范例、名词变格或动词变位。

(iii) complete paradigms, e.g. a pronoun paradigm, a noun declension or a verb conjugation.

由于这些特征最不容易被借用，因此它们成为了遗传关系最可靠的指标。

Since these features are least liable to be borrowed, they are as a consequence the surest indicators of genetic relationship.

 

 

3.2 接触语言

3.2 Languages in Contact

关于两种接触语言之间传播的可能性，有两个主要问题需要提出：（a）谁从谁那里借用了语言；（b）借用了什么。依次来看：

There are two major questions to be asked about the possibilities for diffusion between two languages that are in contact: (a) who borrows from who; and (b) what gets borrowed. Taking these in turn:

（一个） 谁向谁借钱？

这里有两个主要因素

There are two main factors here

（我） 声望

存在着两极分化的可能性。如果两种语言在一个社区中享有同等的声望，那么两个方向都可能存在双语现象（例如卢森堡的德语和法语）。但如果语言 X 作为统治阶级的语言或文化语言具有特殊的声望，那么 Y 语言的使用者将获得一些 X 语言的能力，但 X 语言的使用者不太可能理解或说 Y 语言。在这种情况下，Y 语言将变得更像 X 语言，而不是相反。

There are polar possibilities. If two languages are of equal prestige in a community there is likely to be bilingualism in both directions (e.g. German and French in Luxemburg). But if language X has particular prestige as the language of the ruling class, or the language of culture then speakers of Y will acquire some competence in X but speakers of X are unlikely to understand or speak Y. In this case, Y will change to become more like X, and not the reverse.

（二） 复杂

如果语言 X 比语言 Y 更复杂，那么 X 语言的使用者会发现学习和说 Y 作为第二语言比反过来更容易。（参见第 8 章 (c-iii) 中引用的例子。）在这种情况下，X 很可能会借用 Y，变得更像 Y，但 Y 不太可能向 X 的方向改变。

If language X is more complex than language Y, then speakers of X will find it easier to learn and speak Y, as a second language, than the other way round. (See the examples quoted at (c-iii) in Chapter 8.) In such a circumstance, X is likely to borrow from Y, and to get more like Y, but Y is less likely to change in the direction of X.

这种复杂性可能是音系上的，例如 X 可能有复杂的音节结构，比如 C(C)V(C)(C)，而 Y 只有简单的 CV。或者可能是语法上的，例如 X 可能主要通过动词中的粘性代词元素来标记句法功能，而 Y 采用对比成分顺序。

The complexity could be phonological, e.g. X may have complex syllable structure, say C(C)V(C)(C), while Y has simply CV. Or grammatical, e.g. X may mark syntactic function mainly by bound pronominal elements in the verb while Y employs contrastive constituent order.

有时，真正相对简单并不是激励因素，而是使用者对它的感知。兰迪·拉波拉（个人通信）报告说，在中国云南的某个地区，努苏语使用者和傈僳语使用者生活在一起，努苏人都学习傈僳语，但傈僳语使用者很少学习努苏语，因为他们认为努苏语太复杂，很难学（努苏语使用者同意并鼓励这种态度）。实际上，努苏语并不比傈僳语更复杂。

Sometimes it is not the actual relative simplicity that is the motivating factor, but rather speakers' perception of it. Randy LaPolla (personal communication) reports that, in a part of Yunnan China, where speakers of Nusu and Lisu live together, the Nusu people all learn Lisu but the Lisu seldom learn Nusu because they say it is too complicated and hard to learn (the Nusu speakers agree, and encourage this attitude). Actually, Nusu is no more complicated than Lisu.

即使每个方向都存在双语现象，我们也可能看到明显的方向性影响。正如魏因赖希在其经典研究（1953：41）中所说：“值得注意的是，在两种语法模式的干扰中，通常使用相对自由和不变的词素的模式，即更明确的模式，作为模仿的模型。这似乎不仅适用于创建新类别……也适用于开发一组新的共振峰来实现预先存在的语法功能的情况。”（他随后举了一些例子。）17

Even if there is bilingualism in each direction we may have a marked directionality of influence. As Weinreich stated, in his classic study (1953: 41): 'significantly, in the interference of two grammatical patterns it is ordinarily the one which uses relatively free and invariant morphemes in its paradigm one might say, the more explicit pattern which serves as the model for imitation. This seems to be true not only in the creation of new categories . . . but also in those cases where a new set of formants is developed to fulfil a pre-existing grammatical function.' (He follows this with illustrative examples.)17

另一个因素涉及可供借用的物品种类。如果 A 群体与 B 群体接触，并且 A 拥有 B 所没有的某些手工艺品、风俗和活动，那么 B 很可能会从 A 那里借用这些名称。通常，最有声望的群体拥有最多的新事物，非有声望的语言会从中借用，例如澳大利亚土著语言从英语中借用了“枪”、“酒吧”、“教堂”、“警察”、“汽车”、“衬衫”、“裤子”、“镜子”、“工作”、“购买”和“集合”等术语。但是，当一种有声望的语言是一种入侵者时，它可能会从土著语言中借用当地的植物群、动物群和手工艺品等术语；英语中从澳大利亚语言借用的词汇包括袋鼠、袋熊、虎皮鹦鹉和回旋镖。

Another factor concerns the kind of items that are available to be borrowed. If group A comes into contact with group B, and A has certain artefacts, customs and activities that B lacks, then B is likely to borrow the names of these from A. Generally, the group with the greatest prestige will be the one with the most new things and the non-prestige language will borrow from it, e.g. Australian Aboriginal languages have borrowed, from English, terms for 'gun', 'pub', 'church', 'policeman', 'car', 'shirt', 'trousers', 'mirror', 'work', 'buy' and 'muster'. But when a prestige language is an invader, it may borrow terms from the indigenous languages for local flora, fauna and artefacts; witness loan words in English from Australian languages such as kangaroo, wombat, budgerigar and boomerang.

（二） 借什么？

除了第 3.1 节中总结的关于哪些语言特征最适合借用的基本原则之外，社会和语言态度决定了在任何特定情况下发生的情况。

Over and above the general principles concerning what linguistic features are most open to borrowing, summarised in §3.1, social and linguistic attitudes determine what happens in any particular instance.

人们倾向于从语言的词典（名词、动词、形容词的开放类别）的角度来思考他们的语言。他们将其与词汇联系起来，并试图将其作为族群身份的指标。他们不太了解语法类别（或形式），也很少意识到这个领域可能发生的变化。

People tend to think of their language in terms of its dictionary (the open classes of noun, verb, adjective). They identify it with the lexicon and attempt to control this as an indicator of ethnic identity. They are not in the same way aware of grammatical categories (or forms) and are scarecely aware of changes that may take place in this area.

Aikhenvald (1996) 描述了哥伦比亚/巴西边境的沃佩斯河流域，那里的每个人都必须与来自不同语言群体的人结婚。正如一位发言者所说：“那些和我们讲同一种语言的人就像兄弟一样，我们不会和姐妹结婚。”这导致了多语言现象的猖獗。有趣的是，几乎没有词汇借用。人们特别注意不要混合语言，对他们来说，语言就是它的词典。然而，语法的传播非常广泛。塔利亚纳语（来自阿拉瓦克语系）是沃佩斯地区的一种非声望语言，它吸收了许多声望高的图卡诺安语的特征。这些特征包括转换指称标记和动词复合。塔利亚纳语已经重塑了它的情态、时态和证据系统，使其更类似于图卡诺安语。 （所有这些变化都涉及语法的组织；没有借用任何语法形式。）塔利亚纳语还开发了两个新的元音音素（高不圆唇中央 i 和中后 o），以形成更像图卡诺语的系统。甚至还有一种变化，即元音长度被音高重音取代，以更接近图卡诺语的声调系统。

Aikhenvald (1996) describes the Vaupés River basin, on the Colombia/Brazil border, where each person must marry someone from another language group. As one speaker put it: 'those who speak the same language as us are like brothers, and we do not marry our sisters'. This leads to rampant multilingualism. Interestingly, there have been almost no lexical borrowings. People take particular care not to mix languages, and for them a language is its dictionary. There has, however, been tremendous grammatical diffusion. Tariana (from the Arawak family) is a non-prestige language in the Vaupés region and has adopted many features from the prestige Tucanoan languages. These include switch-reference marking and verb compounding. Tariana has remodelled its modality, tenseaspect and evidentiality systems, to be more similar to those in Tucanoan. (All of these changes involve the organisation of the grammar; no grammatical forms have been borrowed.) Tariana has also developed two new vowel phonemes (high unrounded central i and mid back o) to produce a system more like Tucanoan. There is even a change in progress where vowel length is being replaced by pitch accent, to accord more nearly with the tone system in Tucanoan.

世界其他地方也有类似的例子。在 Gumperz 和 Wilson 对印度村庄 Kupwar 的经典研究 (1971) 中，他们发现当地的坎纳达语 (达罗毗荼语) 和马拉地语和乌尔都语 (印度-雅利安语) 已经融合在单一的句法结构和类似的形态系统上，但保留了不同的词汇和语法形式。18

There are similar examples from other parts of the world. In Gumperz and Wilson's classic study (1971) of the Indian village, Kupwar, they find that local varieties of Kannada (Dravidian) and of Marathi and Urdu (Indo-Aryan) have converged on a single syntactic structure and similar morphological systems, but maintain distinct lexical and grammatical forms.18

萨丕尔（1921：196）给出了另一个例子：“美洲阿萨巴斯卡语的使用者有着惊人的多元文化接触，但我们从未发现阿萨巴斯卡语方言自由地从邻近语言中借用任何词汇。这些语言总是发现通过组合现成的新元素来创造新词更为容易。因此，它们极力抗拒接受其使用者外部文化体验的语言印象。”

Sapir (1921: 196) gave another example: 'the Athabaskan languages of America are spoken by people that have had astonishingly varied cultural contacts, yet nowhere do we find that an Athabaskan dialect has borrowed at all freely from a neighbouring language. These languages have always found it easier to create new words by compounding afresh elements ready to hand. They have for this reason been highly resistant to receiving the linguistic impress of the external cultural experiences of their speakers.'

阿萨巴斯卡语缺乏借用可能部分有语言学方面的原因；这些语言结构复杂，大多为束缚形式，因此很难将外来形式分配给阿萨巴斯卡语词根。但毫无疑问，这在一定程度上是态度问题。似乎有些人只是不想借用词素，而是喜欢从语言内部资源中为新事物创造名称。

There may be a partial linguistic reason for the lack of borrowing by Athabaskan languages; the structures are complex, with mostly bound forms, so that it would be difficult to assign a foreign form to an Athabaskan root. But it is undoubtedly partly a matter of attitude. Some people, it seems, just do not want to borrow lexemes, but prefer to create names for new things from language-internal resources.

这类语言可能只占少数。在许多接触的情况下，我们确实发现词汇借用率稳定，而语法形式的借用率则要慢得多。这适用于澳大利亚大部分地区（但不是全部地区）。部分原因是需要替换因与已故亲属的名字相似而被禁忌的词语，19但部分原因是普遍愿意从邻近语言中借用词语。土著人确实认同他们的语言，但他们谈论的是某些关键词汇（或“这个”和“那个”之类的词）的差异，而不是整个词汇的差异。20

Such languages are probably in a minority. In many cases of contact we do find lexical borrowing at a steady rate, and borrowing of grammatical forms at a much slower rate. This applies in most (but not all) parts of Australia. It is partly motivated by the need to replace words tabooed due to similarity to the name of a dead relative,19 but partly by a general openness to take over words from neighbouring languages. Aborigines do identify with their languages, but they talk in terms of differences in certain critical lexemes (or words like 'this' and 'that'), not of the whole lexicon.20

因此，我们在澳大利亚看到了一个有趣的情况。如果两种语言接触，而共同的词汇很少，它们就会逐渐向两个方向借用，这个数字会上升，直到达到 50% 左右，然后稳定下来。如果一个部落分裂成两个，结果两种方言发展成（由于相互理解的丧失）不同的语言，X 和 Y，它们最初会有很高的共同词汇百分比（70% 左右）。随着词汇在每种语言中分别被替换，共享词汇的百分比就会降低。如果一个词在 X 中是禁忌词，那么 Y 不太可能采用新的形式，因为该语言可能具有与 X 相同的原始形式，而是来自其他邻近语言。共同词汇将逐渐减少，直到达到约 50% 的平衡水平。21因此，如果澳大利亚两种相邻语言共享约 50% 的词汇，则无法从这个数字判断它们是否具有密切的遗传关系。在这种情况下，我们可以查看 (a) 共同动词的百分比（如果超过 50%，则表明存在密切的遗传关系，如果低于 50%，则表明没有遗传关系）和 (b) 共同语法形式的百分比（密切的遗传联系将以高比例的共同语法形式（包括范式）为标志）。在澳大利亚语言区内，动词的替换速度往往比其他词素更慢，语法形式的替换速度则更慢。

We thus have in Australia an interesting situation. If two languages come into contact and there is little vocabulary in common, they will gradually borrow in both directions and this figure will rise until it reaches about 50%, where it will stabilise. And if one tribal group splits into two, with the result that what were two dialects develop (as mutual intelligibility is lost) into distinct languages, X and Y, they will at first have a high percentage of vocabulary in common (70% or so). As vocabulary is replaced, separately in each language, so the percentage of shared vocabulary will reduce. If a word is tabooed in X, a new form is unlikely to be taken from Y, since that language probably has the same original form as X, but rather from some other neighbouring language. The common vocabulary will gradually drop, until it reaches the equilibrium level of about 50%.21 Thus, if two contiguous languages in Australia share about 50% vocabulary it is impossible from this figure to decide whether or not they are closely genetically related. In this circumstance one can look at the percentage of (a) verbs in common (if more than 50% this suggests a close genetic relationship and if less than 50% the lack of one) and (b) grammatical forms in common (a close genetic connection will be marked by a high proportion of shared grammatical forms, including paradigms). Within the Australian linguistic area, verbs tend to be replaced more slowly than other lexemes, and grammatical forms still more slowly.

关于“上升到”或“下降到”50%词汇平衡水平的详细论证，可以在 Dixon (1972: 3317) 中找到。22

The detailed argumentation underlying the 'rising to' or 'falling to' a 50% lexical equilibrium level will be found in Dixon (1972: 3317).22

总之，语法类别和技巧总是有可能传播开来，但我们发现，由于各种原因，在某些接触情况下，词汇很少被借用，而在其他情况下，词汇则被自由借用。随着时间的推移，人们对借用的态度可能会发生变化。一种语言可能在几百年或几千年的时间内不愿意从其他语言借用词汇，但随后它可能会发生变化，开始大量借用词汇。日语就经历过这样的阶段（见 Loveday 1996）。这两个阶段在匈牙利语中以相反的顺序应用；有很多借用，但在后来的阶段，这些借用被语言内部的复合词或派生词所取代。

In summary, grammatical categories and techniques are always likely to diffuse, but in some contact situations we find for a variety of reasons that lexemes are scarcely borrowed, whereas in other situations they are freely borrowed. Over time, a people's attitude towards borrowing can change. A given language may be averse to borrowing from other languages for a period of some hundreds or thousands of years, but then it may change and begin borrowing in profusion. Japanese has been through stages like this (see Loveday 1996). The two stages have applied in reverse order in Hungarian; there were many borrowings but then, at a later stage, these were replaced by language-internal compounds or derivations.

 

 

4 家谱模型

4 The Family Tree Model

语言学中一直存在一种倾向，即采用一种观点（它永远只能是整体的一部分）并过度应用它。这在最近的大多数语法理论中都很明显。它当然也适用于语言分裂和关系的分支家族树模型。

There has been a persistent tendency in linguistics to take one idea (which could never be more than part of the whole picture) and to overapply it. This is evident in most recent grammatical theories. And it certainly applies to the branching family tree model for linguistic splitting and relationship.

在理想的家谱情况下，一种原始语言分裂成少数几个子语言（最好是两种），每种子语言又分裂成少数几个子语言，依此类推。该模型是为印欧语系开发的，广泛适用于该语系。然而，印欧语系家谱也存在一些不太理想的特点。首先，我们似乎需要将其主要分裂成十个分支，因为无法就这十个分支内的进一步表达达成共识。一种祖先语言同时分裂成十个子语言的可能性不大。（在第 7 节中，我们将研究另一种情况。）还有一个困难是，有些语言无法在树中被分配一个明确的位置；例如，僧伽罗语被认为属于印度-雅利安语分支，但它无法被分配到该分支内的任何特定节点。

In the ideal family tree situation we get one original language splitting into a small number of daughter languages (in the best instance, two), each of these in turn splitting into a small number of daughter languages, and so on. This model was developed for the Indo-European family and is broadly applicable to it. There are, however, a number of less than ideal features of the IE family tree. The first is that we appear to need a primary split into ten branches it has not been possible to reach any consensus on further articulation within this ten. That a single ancestor language should split simultaneously into ten daughters is unlikely. (In §7 we shall examine an alternative scenario.) There is also the difficulty that some languages cannot be assigned a clear place within the tree; for instance, Singhalese is acknowledged to belong to the Indo-Aryan branch, but it cannot be assigned to any specific node within this branch.

总体而言，印欧语的研究质量最高，并获得了应有的声誉。（此外，印欧语本身也包括当今世界上的主要声望语言。）因此，谱系树是语言关系的“公认模型”，其他领域的学者试图将其应用于自己的语言群体。有时，谱系树模型是适用的，可以用印欧语系的相同方式证明遗传关系，例如乌拉尔语、闪米特语、阿尔冈昆语。

Work on Indo-European is, by and large, of the highest quality and has acquired a justified prestige. (Add to this the fact that the I E languages themselves include the major prestige languages in the world today.) As a result the family tree is the 'received model' of linguistic relationship which scholars working in other areas attempt to apply to their own groups of languages. Sometimes the family tree model is applicable, and a genetic relationship can be proved in the same way that it has been for IE, e.g. Uralic, Semitic, Algonquian.

但在其他情况下，人们提出了一种家谱类型的图表，但没有正确的证据，或者没有任何可以提供这种证据的前景。

But in other instances a family-tree-type diagram has been posited without the right sort of proof, or any prospect that this could be provided.

本文的主要论点是，家谱模型虽然在许多情况下适用且有用，但并非适用于所有地方，也无法解释语言之间的所有关系。我们需要一个更具包容性的模型，将家谱和传播区域的理念融为一体。

A main thesis of this essay is that the family tree model, while appropriate and useful in many circumstances, is not applicable everywhere and cannot explain every type of relationship between languages. We need a more inclusive model, which integrates together the ideas of family tree and of diffusion area.

原始印欧语被认为是在大约 6,000 年前开始使用的；如今有超过 100 种印欧语。但人类语言被认为至少在 100,000 年前就已进化（许多专家会给出更早的数字）。假设有一种原始语言，即原始人类（这个问题将在 §5.3 中更详细地讨论）。在 100,000 年的时间跨度中，大约有 17 个 6,000 年的时期。如果印欧语类型的分裂是常态（一种语言在 6,000 年后有 100 个后代），那么原始人类现在应该已经产生了 102×17 = 1034，即 10 亿亿亿亿亿种语言；实际上我们有大约 5,000 种。 （以南岛语系为模型，可以得出更大的数字 1060，在南岛语系中，一种语言在预计不超过 5,000 年的时间跨度内产生了 1,000 多个子语言。）如果我们采用更适中的分裂率，假设一种语言每 6,000 年可能分裂成两种语言，那么我们预计原始人类将产生 217 种或约 130,000 种现代语言。如果我们允许在此过程中有许多语言灭绝，这个数字会更合理。但请注意，这个假设涉及一种语言每 6,000 年左右分裂成两种。这与我们所知的近几个世纪以来世界某些地区发生的情况完全不同，例如，印欧语系的罗曼语和印度-雅利安语支发展出了不同的语言，而我们确实有大量的书面记录。

Proto-Indo-European is considered to have been spoken about 6,000 years ago; there are today over 100 IE languages. But human language is thought to have evolved at least 100,000 years in the past (many specialists would give an earlier figure). Suppose there was one original language, proto-Human (this question will be more fully discussed in §5.3). There are about 17 periods of 6,000 years in a 100,000 year span. If IE-type splitting were the norm (one language having 100 descendants after 6,000 years), proto-Human should by now have spawned 102×17 = 1034, or 10 million billion billion billion, languages; in fact we have about 5,000. (An even larger figure, 1060, would be obtained by taking as a model the Austronesian family where one language has spawned over 1,000 daughters in a time span suggested to be no more than 5,000 years.) If we adopted a more modest rate of splitting, supposing that a language is likely to split into two languages every 6,000 years, we would expect proto-Human to have given rise to 217, or about 130,000, modern languages. If we allow for a number of languages becoming extinct along the way, this would be a more reasonable number. But note the assumption involved a language splits into two about every 6,000 years. This is something of a totally different magnitude from what we know has happened in some parts of the world during recent centuries for instance, the development of separate languages in the Romance and Indo-Aryan subgroups of IE, where we do have available a depth of written record.

从这些计算中可以得出的教训是，印欧语系和南岛语系所提出的语言分裂和扩张规模极不寻常。这种事情在人类语言史上很少发生。当然，不应将其视为语言发展的唯一模式。对于南岛语系来说，有一个简单的解释，可以解释这种大规模分裂扩张至少有一部分进入了太平洋岛屿，进入了以前未被占领的领土。对于印欧语系来说，我们只是一个侵略性和帝国主义的种族，正在传播和征服。（请注意，在过去几个世纪里，英语、西班牙语和葡萄牙语几乎完全取代了美洲和澳大利亚的本土语言；超过 1,000 种语言要么消亡，要么正在消亡。）

The lesson from these calculations is that language split and expansion on the scale that is put forward for the IE and Austronesian families is highly unusual. This sort of thing would have happened rather seldom in the history of human language. It should certainly not be taken as the only model for language development. For Austronesian there is a straightforward explanation for at least part of this mammoth split expansion into the Pacific Islands was into previously unoccupied territory. In the case of IE we simply have an aggressive and imperialistic race, spreading and conquering. (Note how, during the past few centuries, English, Spanish and Portuguese have almost entirely replaced the indigenous languages in the Americas and in Australia; well over 1,000 languages are either dead or dying.)

下面我要指出，家谱模型只适用于标点符号时期，而不适用于语言平衡时期。过去十多万年中的语言发展经历了长期的平衡时期，只有偶尔出现标点符号。

I shall suggest below that the family tree model is only applicable during a period of punctuation, and not during periods of linguistic equilibrium. Language development during the past 100,000 and more years has involved long periods of equilibrium, with only the occasional punctuation.

 

 

4.1 标准

4.1 Criteria

一张家族树图，顶部是 X，底部是 A、B、C……，表明 A、B、C……是由 X 通过多次语言分裂发展而来的。只有一种方法可以证明这种说法：(a) 重建假定的原始语言 X 的音系系统、至少几百个词素（涵盖词汇的所有领域）和部分语法系统（代词、指示词、疑问词和一些词缀）；然后 (b) 描述 X 发展成每个子语言 A、B、C……的系统变化过程。

A family tree diagram, with X at the top and A,B,C, . . . along the bottom, states that A,B,C, . . . developed from X, by a number of language splits. There is one and only one way to prove such a claim: (a) to reconstruct the phonological system, at least several hundred lexemes (covering all areas of vocabulary) and parts of the grammatical system (pronouns, demonstratives, interrogatives and some affixes) for the postulated proto-language, X; and then (b) to describe the systematic processes of change by which X developed into each of the daughter languages A,B,C, . . .

存在一种比较方法，这是一种准重建程序。如果以智能方式应用，在大多数情况下，这将提出一个合理的原型系统。23 （然而，比较方法绝不是万无一失的；它不是一种发现程序，一种可以机械地应用以提供重建的算法。附录讨论了将其作为发现程序应用会产生错误结果的情况。）

There exists the comparative method, a quasi-procedure for reconstruction. Applied in an intelligent way, this will in most cases suggest a plausible proto-system.23 (However the comparative method is by no means fool-proof; it is not a discovery procedure, an algorithm that can be applied mechanically to provide a reconstruction. The appendix discusses cases in which applied as a discovery procedure it would yield the wrong result.)

事实上，原始语言的语言学特征的得出方式本质上无关紧要。它可以通过相当严格的比较方法应用获得，也可以由语言学家凭直觉提出（或者甚至可以在梦中出现）。唯一的问题是，应该提供原始语言的很大一部分的描述，以便现代语言的系统可以通过一系列合理的系统变化从中衍生出来。

In fact, the way in which a linguistic characterisation of proto-language is arrived at is essentially irrelevant. It could have been obtained by fairly strict application of the comparative method, or it could have been suggested by a linguist intuitively (or it could even have come to them in a dream). The only point at issue is that a description of a good part of the proto-language should be provided, such that the systems of modern languages can be derived from it by a series of plausible, systematic changes.

当然，用家谱模型来说明印欧语系语言的亲缘关系，这一标准已经得到了充分证明。其他一些语系也已得到或正在得到证明。但对于许多被认为构成语系的语言群体，尚未有人认真尝试重建原始语言系统的一部分，而且似乎也不太可能做到这一点。

The genetic relationship of IE languages, in a family tree model, has of course been eminently proved by this criterion. Proof has also been provided or is being provided for some other language families. But for many groups of languages that have been posited to comprise a language family, no serious attempt has been made to reconstruct part of the system of a proto-language, nor does it seem likely that it will prove possible to do so.

我们经常发现，“遗传关系”和“语系”的概念与上述概念的理解方式截然不同。但这些术语的使用方式，就好像它们在意义上等同于 IE 或其他语系上下文中使用的相同术语，而这些语系的遗传关系证明标准已经得到满足。

Often we find that the ideas of 'genetic relationship' and 'language family' are conceived of in a quite different way from those described above. But then these terms are used as if they were equivalent in sense to the same terms used in the context of IE or other families for which the criterion of proof for genetic relationship has been met.

此类著作主要有三种类型学、词典学和“诺斯特拉学”。我们将依次讨论这些内容。

There are three main strands of such work typological, lexicostatistic and 'Nostratic'. We discuss these in turn.

（一个） 根据类型学特征

通常，人们会引用一些类型学特征，这些特征是一组语言共同存在的，并以此作为遗传联系的证据。例如，Shibatani (1990: 94118) 调查了日语和其他各种语言群体之间存在遗传关系的建议。其中包括 Fujioka (1908)，他提出了“乌拉尔-阿尔泰语系的十四个特征”，这些特征也适用于日语。这里只引用四个就足够了（第一个和之后的每个第四个）：“（a）词首位置没有辅音序列；……（e）没有语法性别区别；……（j）使用后置词而不是前置词；……（n）连词使用不广泛。”但所有这些特征都是扩散的特征。仔细检查表明，已建立的突厥语、蒙古语和通古斯语系形成了一个语言区域（称为阿尔泰语系），并且一些特征也与乌拉尔语系相同。这些与日语的类型学相似性可能是由于区域影响；或者它们可能是巧合。（来自世界其他地区的许多语言确实具有这些特征。）

Typically, a number of typological features are quoted, in which a group of languages concur, and this is taken as evidence of genetic connection. For example, Shibatani (1990: 94118) surveys the suggestions for a genetic relationship between Japanese and various other groups of languages. These include Fujioka (1908) who presented 'fourteen characteristic features of Ural-Altaic languages' that also apply to Japanese. It will suffice here to quote just four (the first and every fourth after that): '(a) no consonant sequences occur in word-initial position; . . . (e) there is no grammatical gender distinction; . . . (j) postpositions, instead of prepositions, are used; . . . (n) conjunctions are not used widely.' But all of these are characteristics which diffuse. Careful examination indicates that the established families, Turkic, Mongolian and Tungusic, form a linguistic area (called Altaic) and that some features are also shared with the Uralic family. These typological similarities with Japanese may possibly be due to areal influence; or they may be coincidental. (Many languages, from other parts of the world, do share these features.)

尚未成功重建“原始阿尔泰语”或“原始乌拉尔-阿尔泰语”或“原始乌拉尔-阿尔泰-日语（-韩语）”的语言系统，以及现代语言从这种原始系统发展而来的方式。没有给出足够的标准来证明在这里谈论遗传关系是合理的。我们只是有类型学上的相似性，这是完全不同的事情。

There has been no successful attempt to reconstruct a linguistic system for 'proto-Altaic' or 'proto-Uralic-Altaic' or 'proto-Uralic-Altaic-Japanese(-Korean)', and the ways in which the modern languages have developed from such a proto-system. Sufficient criteria have not been given that would justify talking of a genetic relationship here. We simply have typological similarities, which is a totally different matter.

非洲的语言学非常迷人，拥有 1,000 多种语言，其中许多语言的结构复杂得令人望而生畏。许多语言都得到了很好的描述，但对于许多语言，我们几乎没有发表过数据。大约 1,000 种语言被归类为一个假定的“尼日尔-刚果语系”，这是格林伯格 (1963) 提出的。人们会发现类似这样的陈述：“[格林伯格的] 主要结论现在已成为大多数学者的主流正统观念”（Williamson 1989: 8）。然而，人们徒劳地寻找这种“遗传关系”的证据。非洲学家倾向于回答局外人关于此事的询问，说只有非洲学家才能判断这类事情。也许吧。但在查阅了现有文献后，局外人不得不得出结论，非洲学家和研究世界其他地区语言的学者对遗传关系概念和“语系”一词的使用方式截然不同。

Africa is linguistically fascinating, with well over 1,000 languages, many of them showing dauntingly complex structures. A number have been well described but for many languages we have very little published data. About 1,000 languages have been grouped together in a putative 'Niger-Congo family', suggested by Greenberg (1963). One finds statements like '[Greenberg's] major conclusions have by now become the prevailing orthodoxy for most scholars' (Williamson 1989: 8). However, one searches in vain for proof of this 'genetic relationship'. Africanists tend to respond to queries about this matter from outsiders by saying that only Africanists can judge such matters. Maybe. But after reviewing the available literature an outsider is forced to conclude that the idea of genetic relationship and the term 'language family' are used in quite different ways by Africanists and by scholars working on languages from other parts of the world.

为支持“尼日尔-刚果”而引用的共同特征是声调系统和名词类（或性别）。但请注意，并非每种尼日尔-刚果语言都具有这两个特征。格林伯格（1963：10）指出：“虽然这些 [名词类] 词缀的存在是与尼日尔-刚果语系有联系的重要证据，但没有这些词缀并不证明缺乏联系”。 （例如，假定的曼德语支群中没有名词类。）格林伯格建立“尼日尔-刚果”是基于他所谓的“大量比较”，检查一组语言中的词素形式是否存在明显的相似性。没有任何地方只给出八种语言中的七个单词的全套数据（格林伯格 1963：4）。标记名词类的词缀之间确实存在一些形式上的相似性，但这些词缀在某些语言中是前缀，而在其他语言中是后缀。格林伯格有理由认为，它们可能是从指示词发展而来的。

Common features quoted in support of 'Niger-Congo' are systems of tones, and of noun classes (or genders). Note, though, that not every Niger-Congo language has even these two characteristics. Greenberg (1963: 10) states: 'while the presence of these [noun class] affixes is important evidence for affiliation with the Niger-Congo family, absence of the affixes does not prove lack of connection'. (Noun classes are absent from the putative Mande subgroup, for instance.) Greenberg's establishment of 'Niger-Congo' was based on what he calls 'mass comparison', inspecting the forms of lexemes in a sample of languages for apparent similarities. Nowhere is the full set of data given just a sample of seven words in eight languages (Greenberg 1963: 4). It is true that there are some formal similarities between the affixes that mark noun classes but these are prefixes in some languages and suffixes in others. Greenberg suggests, plausibly, that they may have developed from demonstratives.

提到的“尼日尔-刚果”的其他特征包括：CVCV 词根结构；后缀的 -CV 形状；元音和谐；鼻音加塞音序列或前鼻音塞音；动词序列化；主语-宾语-动词或主语-动词-宾语的构成顺序 (Williamson 1989: 20ff.)。与声调和名词类一样，这些都是在世界其他地方反复出现的特征，它们都极易传播。名词类词缀本身不太可能被借用，但它们据说来自指示词，而这些指示词更容易传播。

Other features mentioned as characteristics for 'Niger-Congo' include: CVCV root structure; -CV shape for suffixes; vowel harmony; nasal-plus-stop sequences or else prenasalised stops; verb serialisation; and either subject-object-verb or subject-verb-object constituent order (Williamson 1989: 20ff.). Like tones and noun classes these are all features which recur in other parts of the world and they are all eminently open to diffusion. Noun class affixes themselves are not too likely to be borrowed, but they are said to come from demonstratives and these are more likely to diffuse.

“尼日尔-刚果语系”假说最早是在近五十年前提出的。在此期间，没有人试图用印地语、乌拉尔语、阿尔冈昆语等标准来证明这一假说。事实上，正如第 3 节所述，撒哈拉以南非洲似乎以一系列重叠的扩散区为特征（这些特征通常被视为遗传关系的标志）。

The hypothesis of a 'Niger-Congo family' was first put forward almost fifty years ago. During the intervening period no attempt has been made to prove this hypothesis by the criteria used for IE, Uralic, Algonquian, etc. In fact, as mentioned in §3, it appears that Sub-Saharan Africa is characterised by an overlapping series of diffusion areas (for those features that are generally taken as indicative of genetic relationship).

这并不是否认在这个语言区域内可以建立一些遗传分组。有些已经建立（例如班图语），其他无疑将会建立。但是，任何关系假设都必须通过重建大量原始语言的语言系统，并详细描述现代语言从中发展而来的系统变化来证明。显然，首要任务是尝试重建“尼日尔-刚果族谱”上一些较低节点的原始语言，然后看看是否有可能从这些节点进一步研究。并且应该始终牢记，语言之间的任何相似性都可能有几个原因，包括遗传保留、区域传播或偶然的类型相似性。

This is not to deny that some genetic groupings may be establishable within this linguistic area. Some have been (e.g. the Bantu languages) and others undoubtedly will be. But any hypothesis of relationship must be proved by reconstructing a good deal of the linguistic system of a proto-language, and by detailing the systematic changes by which modern languages developed from this.
