Plainly, the first task is to try to reconstruct proto-languages for some of the lower nodes on the 'Niger-Congo family tree', and then see if it is possible to work further from these. And it should always be borne in mind that there are several possible reasons for any similarities between languages genetic retention, areal diffusion, or just chance typological similarity.

尼日尔-刚果的情况是一个典型的例子，将IE型家谱作为语言关系的唯一模型，并随意使用，没有适当的谨慎和标准。

The Niger-Congo situation is a classic example of taking the IE-type family tree as the only model of linguistic relationship, and employing it willy-nilly, without proper care and criteria.

更近一些，格林伯格（1987）将同样的“大规模比较”方法应用于美洲，并声称已经“证明”了几十个不同家族和许多语言孤立体之间的遗传关系。这一次，他发表了部分数据库，他的原始笔记本也存档了。有人指出，（i）格林伯格在开始收集数据之前已经确定了他的关系方案；（ii）许多数据是不正确的，24要么取自与所指语言不同的语言，要么取自语音不可靠的旧资料（忽略了更可靠的现代资料）。（参见 Chafe 1987、Campbell 1988、Adelaar 1989、Goddard 1990、Rankin 1992、Kimball 1992 和 Berman 1992 等批评）。25

More recently, Greenberg (1987) has applied the same method of 'mass comparison' to the Americas, and purports to have 'proved' the genetic relationships between several dozen distinct families and many language isolates. This time he has published a part of the data base, and his original notebooks are on file. It has been pointed out that (i) Greenberg had finalised his scheme of relationships before he began assembling the data; and (ii) much of the data is incorrect,24 being taken either from a different language to that indicated or else from old sources that are not phonetically reliable (passing over more modern sources that are reliable). (See, among other critiques, Chafe 1987, Campbell 1988, Adelaar 1989, Goddard 1990, Rankin 1992, Kimball 1992, and Berman 1992).25

在美洲（尤其是北美），人们确实拥有大量可用的数据，其中大部分都是高质量的，并且有使用与 IE 领域相同的标准建立遗传关系的传统。格林伯格关于美洲语言的研究没有采用建立遗传关系的既定标准，而且显然是不充分的。26它也有点像钟敲十三下一样，不仅本身难以置信，而且使人们对之前的一切产生了怀疑。也就是说，它让一些人（包括我）回头看看应用于非洲语言的“大规模比较”方法，并意识到它的局限性。但至少“尼日尔-刚果”确实具有语言区域的一些特征，而美洲则不能这么说。而且，假定的“尼日尔-刚果谱系”的某些部分很可能被证明具有遗传统一性，而格林伯格提出的美洲既定语言家族和孤立语言之间的联系很少或根本没有可能被证实。

In the Americas (particularly in North America) one does have extensive data available, much of it of high quality, and a tradition of establishing genetic relationships using the same criteria as those employed in the IE field. Greenberg's work on the languages of the Americas does not employ established criteria for establishing genetic relationships and is transparently inadequate.26 It is also rather like the clock that strikes thirteen not only is it implausible in itself but it casts doubt on all that has gone before. That is, it has made some people (including me) go back and look at the 'mass comparison' method as applied to African languages, and perceive its limitations. But at least 'Niger-Congo' does have some of the characteristics of a linguistic area, which is more than can be said of the Americas. And it is likely that some parts of the putative 'Niger-Congo family tree' will be proved to have genetic unity, whereas few or none of the links Greenberg suggests between the established language families and isolates in the Americas are ever likely to be proved.

（二） 词汇统计学和语言年代学

Swadesh (1951) 提出了一个建立“遗传”关系的神奇公式。从此以后，就无需花费数十年时间编纂语法和词典，然后寻找系统对应关系并进行重建。只需收集多种语言中指定的 100 个（或 200 个）核心词汇列表，然后进行比较，通过检查注意这些核心词汇之间有多少项似乎是同源的。然后，公式会告诉你这些语言之间的关系（词汇统计）以及它们共同的原始语言的时间深度（语言年代学）。这种方法带来了一系列新术语。“语言家族”一词被赋予了全新的含义，因为这些语言共享 3681% 的核心词汇。我们还有“stock”、“microphylum”、“mesophylum”和“macrophylum”（这里同源百分比不到 1%！）（Gudschinsky 1956）。

Swadesh (1951) put forward a magical formula for establishing 'genetic' relationships. There would no longer be any need to spend decades compiling grammars and dictionaries, then looking for systematic correspondences and working on reconstruction. One simply gathered a specified 100- (or perhaps 200-) word list of core vocabulary in each of a number of languages and compared them, noting by inspection how many items appeared to be cognate between these core vocabularies. Then a formula told you how the languages were related (Lexicostatistics) and also the time-depth of their common proto-language (Glottochronology). Together with this method came an array of new terminology. The term 'language family' was used with a quite new sense, for languages sharing 3681% of core vocabulary. We also had 'stock', 'microphylum', 'mesophylum' and 'macrophylum' (here the cognate percentage is less than 1%!) (Gudschinsky 1956).

像所有捷径一样，这种方法行不通。它基于不正当的假设，即人们可以仅从词汇中推断出遗传关系；所有语言的词汇总是以恒定的速度更新；核心词汇的表现方式总是不同于非核心词汇。在词汇统计学被彻底否定之前，（对某些人来说）有几年疯狂而快乐的 100 词列表比较（参见 Bergslund 和 Vogt 1962；以及 Hoijer 1956、Arndt 1959、Teeter 1963、Campbell 1977：63-5、Embleton 1992）。27

Like all short cuts, this didn't work. It was based on illicit assumptions that one can infer genetic relationships from lexicon alone; that the lexicon of all languages is always replaced at a constant rate; and that core vocabulary always behaves in a different way from non-core. There were (for some people) a few mad, happy years of 100-word list comparison before lexicostatistics was decisively discredited (see Bergslund and Vogt 1962; and also Hoijer 1956, Arndt 1959, Teeter 1963, Campbell 1977: 63-5, Embleton 1992).27

当然，比较核心词汇并不是无用的练习。在处理新语言时，这是一个非常有用的第一步，可能会提出有关可能关系的假设，这有助于规划详细的描述和比较工作。但它绝不应该被当作遗传关系的证据。（有时词汇统计结果与仔细比较和重建所证明的结果有很好的相关性，但在其他情况下则 不然。）

Comparison of core vocabularies is not, of course, a useless exercise. It is a very helpful first step when dealing with new languages and may suggest hypotheses about possible relationships which can be an aid in planning detailed descriptive and comparative work. But it should never be taken as proof of genetic relationships. (Sometimes lexicostatistics results do correlate well with what is proved by careful comparison and reconstruction, but in other circumstances they do not.)

许多遗传群和亚群都是根据词汇统计比较得出的。尽管词汇统计早已失去信誉，但仍有人根据这些遗传群进行研究，认为这些分类应该根据适当的标准予以证明，否则就应该被抛弃（例如澳大利亚的“帕马-尼永甘亚群”）。

A number of genetic groups and subgroups were put forward on the basis of lexicostatistical comparison. Although lexicostatistics has been long discredited, some people still work in terms of these genetic groups they should be proved, according to proper criteria, or else discarded (e.g. the 'Pama-Nyungan subgroup' in Australia).

（三） “诺斯特拉蒂克”

如果一个人只有家谱模型，那么他就会忍不住反复应用它。为什么要停下来呢？许多语言家族已经牢固地确立了（或正在确立中）；为什么不尝试将它们关联起来，形成一个更高级别的家谱呢？

If the family tree model is all one has, there is a temptation to apply it, apply it again, and yet again. Why stop? A number of language families have been firmly established (or are in the process of being established); why not attempt to relate them together, into a higher-level family tree?

Pedersen (1931: 3349) 调查了一些观点，认为印欧语系可能与闪米特语系有关（因此，可能与其他非亚细亚语系有关）；和/或与乌拉尔语系有关；可能与突厥语系、蒙古语系和通古斯语系有关；可能与爱斯基摩语系有关；可能与某些高加索语系有关；可能与巴斯克语系有关。他建议：“作为与印欧语系有关的语系的统称，我们可以使用诺斯特拉特语（来自拉丁语 nostras *“我们的同胞”）这一表达。”

Pedersen (1931: 3349) surveyed opinions that IE might be related to Semitic (and thus, presumably, to the rest of Afroasiatic); and/or to Uralic; perhaps to Turkic, Mongolian and Tungusic; perhaps to Eskimo; perhaps to some of the Caucasian families; perhaps to Basque. He suggested: 'as a comprehensive designation for the families of languages which are related to Indo-European, we may employ the expression Nostratian Languages (from Latin nostras * "our countryman")'.

近年来，一群主要由俄罗斯学者重新使用这个术语（并将其修改为“诺斯特拉语”），以涵盖 IE、乌拉尔语、突厥语、蒙古语、通古斯语、28达罗毗荼语、南高加索语（Kartvelian）和可能还有亚非语系（对此的看法不一）之间的假定联系29。这些“诺斯特拉语学者”声称通过组合同源集，采用比较法进行工作。然而，他们只是通过允许过多的音系和语义余地来实现他们的结果。在“重构”中，几乎没有指定任何元音（仅给出 V），N 经常用于表示未指定的鼻音，等等。

During recent years this term has been revived by a group of mainly Russian scholars (and modified to 'Nostratic') to cover a putative linkage of language families IE, Uralic, Turkic, Mongolian, Tungusic,28 Dravidian, South Caucasian (Kartvelian) and perhaps Afroasiatic (opinions vary on this29). These 'Nostraticists' purport to work in terms of the comparative method, by assembling cognate sets. However, they achieve their results only by allowing excessive phonological and semantic leeway. In the 'reconstructions', scarcely any vowels are specified (given just as V), N is often employed for an unspecified nasal, and so on.

当然，寻找已建立的语言家族之间的可能联系是完全合理的。 Collinder (1965: 304) 对乌拉尔语和印欧语系之间可能存在联系发表了一些有用的观察。但我们应该一步一步来。突然把七个（或八个）家族联系在一起是相当难以置信的，尤其是当其中一些家族（达罗毗荼语、非罗亚细亚语）的原始语言仍需要大量工作时。30 “诺斯特拉语学家”并没有止步于此。也有人提出基因单位有爱斯基摩-诺斯特拉语（“同源”集包括原始爱斯基摩语 *mac(j)a 和原始诺斯特拉语 **mV[z *]V 'sun'）、汉藏语加上东北和西北高加索语（汉高加索语）、纳-德内​​语加上东北和西北高加索语；然后是诺斯特拉语加上汉高加索语。 （例如，参见 Shevoroshkin 和 Manaster Ramer 1991。）等等。为什么要停止？31

It is of course perfectly reasonable to look for possible links between established language families Collinder (1965: 304) has some useful observations about the possibility of a connection between Uralic and IE. But one should always proceed a step at a time. To suddenly link together seven (or eight) families is more than a little implausible, especially when, for some of them (Dravidian, Afroasiatic), the proto-language of that family still needs considerable work.30 The 'Nostraticists' do not stop here. There have also been suggestions of genetic units Eskimo-Nostratic ('cognate' sets include proto-Eskimo *mac(j)a and proto-Nostratic **mV[z *]V 'sun'), Sino-Tibetan plus North-east and North-west Caucasian (Sino-Caucasian), Na-Dene plus North-east and North-west Caucasian; and then Nostratic plus Sino-Caucasian. (See, for instance, Shevoroshkin and Manaster Ramer 1991.) And so on. Why stop?31

有必要探究一下，在俄罗斯这样一个在其他科学领域（例如物理和数学）都拥有高标准的国家，诺斯特拉的思想是如何被接受为正统思想的。诺斯特拉的思想扎根于俄罗斯知识分子与世界其他地区断绝密切联系的时代，当时俄罗斯处于一种“蝇王”式的境地；没有同行群体能够采用适当的科学评估标准，并证明这种思想的基础不合理。

It is relevant to enquire how this Nostratic idea came to be accepted as an orthodoxy in a country like Russia which has such high standards in other scientific fields (physics and mathematics, for example). The Nostratic idea took root at a time when Russian intellectuals were cut off from close contact with the rest of the world, in a sort of Lord-of-the-Flies situation; there was no peer group available that would have employed proper standards of scientific assessment and demonstrated the unsound basis of the idea.

俄罗斯诺斯特拉主义者公开吹嘘（并且仍在吹嘘）他们比前人更聪明，这就是为什么他们能够同时将许多家族联系起来，这是以前从未实现过的。“然而，事实上，头脑清醒的学者们之所以回避大型比较，并不是因为大型比较太难，而是因为它们太容易了。当考虑的语言数量如此之多，当它们之间的关系（如果有的话）很遥远，并且声音对应的标准很宽松时，找到在声音和意义上或多或少相似的“音位语义相似”形式并不难”（Matisoff 1990：10910）。

The Russian Nostraticists openly boasted (and still boast) that they are cleverer than anyone who has come before, which was why they were able to relate many families together, all at once, something that had not previously been achieved. 'In fact, however, sober-minded scholars have shrunk from megalocomparisons not because they are so difficult, but because they are so easy. When the number of languages being considered is so large, when their relationship (if any) is remote, and the criteria for sound correspondences are lax, it is not very hard to find "phono-semantic lookalikes" forms which more or less resemble each other both in sound and in meaning' (Matisoff 1990: 10910).

比较语言学的方法是这样，如果将应该严格遵守的标准放宽一点，就有可能从字面上证明任何事物都与一切事物相关。Swadesh (1960) 声称通过允许大量的音位和语义对应，建立了中美洲许多不同语言家族之间的遗传联系，类似于诺斯特拉主义者。Longacre (1961) 和 Olmsted (1961) 对该方法和结果提出了令人钦佩的批评。然后 Callaghan 和 Miller (1962) 证明，使用与 Swadesh 使用的一样有效的常规“同源集”，可以证明英语是一种“大米斯特卡”语言。例如，他们将原始大米斯特卡语中的 *yute“梳子”形式与英语中的 head 联系起来，将 *yeti-ni 或 *yeyet-ni“皮肤”与英语的 hide 联系起来，“证明”了 y:h 和 t:d 的对应关系。他们的观点是，凭借 Swadesh 所允许的那种语义和音韵自由，可以“证明”任何语言都与 Macro-Mixtecan（或任何其他语系）相关。

The methods of comparative linguistics are such that, if criteria which should be strictly maintained are relaxed, just a little, it is possible to prove literally that anything is related to everything. Swadesh (1960) purported to establish genetic connections between a number of distinct language families in Central America by permitting generous phonological and semantic correspondences, similar to the Nostraticists. Longacre (1961) and Olmsted (1961) provided admirable critiques of the method and results. And then Callaghan and Miller (1962) demonstrated that, with regular 'cognate sets' just as valid as those used by Swadesh, English can be shown to be a 'Macro-Mixtecan' language. For example they connected the form *yute 'comb' in proto-Macro-Mixtecan with head in English, and *yeti-ni or *yeyet-ni 'skin' with English hide, 'demonstrating' correspondences y:h and t:d. Their point was that, with the sort of semantic and phonological latitude which Swadesh allowed himself, it can be 'shown' that any language is related to Macro-Mixtecan (or to any other family).

所有这些工作的错误不仅在于未能以适当的科学态度比较语言，还在于依赖家谱作为语言关系的唯一模型。在语言关系的综合模型（结合家谱和传播模型）中，如果对“原始语言”概念所涉及的困难有了更清晰的认识，就不会有犯下“诺斯特拉式”之类的行为的诱惑。

The error in all this work is not just in failing to take proper scientific care in comparing languages, but in relying on family trees as the only model of linguistic relationship. Within an integrated model of linguistic relationships (combining the family tree and diffusion models) and with a clearer idea of the difficulties involved in the idea of 'proto-language', there could be no temptation to perpetrate anything such as 'Nostratic'.

综上所述，在很多情况下，家谱模型是适用的，并且可以通过重建原始语言的语言系统的重要部分以及产生现代语言的系统变化来证明。但这种情况必须与我们仅有类型学相似性的情况仔细区分。

In summary, there are many situations where the family tree model isappropriate, and can be proved through reconstruction of a significant part of the linguistic system of a proto-language, together with the systematic changes that have given rise to the modern languages. But such cases must be carefully distinguished from situations in which we just have typological similarities.

语言之间的遗传联系是否可证明取决于许多因素，包括相关语言的形态类型和形式的平均长度。多音节形式之间的同源集比涉及单音节或单音节形式的同源集提供的证据要好得多。如果动词“go”在两种语言中都是 -gimlar-，那么这比它是 -a- 更有力地证明了它们之间的关系。对于许多词根由单个辅音组成的语言组（例如西北高加索语言），重建比大多数词根是多音节的语言组（例如乌拉尔语）更困难。

Whether a genetic connection between languages is provable depends on a number of factors, including the morphological type of the languages concerned and the average length of forms. A cognate set between polysyllabic forms provides much better evidence than one involving monosyllables, or single-segment forms. If the verb 'go' is -gimlar- in two languages, this is a stronger evidence of relationship than if it were -a-. For a group of languages where many roots consist of a single consonant (such as North-west Caucasian) reconstruction is more problematic than where most roots are polysyllabic (e.g. Uralic).

语言大致可分为三类：孤立语，每个意义元素组成一个独特的词（例如越南语和汉语）；黏着语，一个词可能包含多个意义元素，但这些意义元素显然是可分离的（例如土耳其语和斯瓦希里语）；融合语，一个词包含多个意义元素，其中一些意义元素融合在一起，因此一个元音可以同时标记时态、语态、人称和主语数（例如拉丁语和梵语）。

Languages can be roughly classed into three types: isolating, where each meaning element makes up a distinct word (e.g. Vietnamese and Chinese); agglutinative, where a word is likely to contain several meaning elements but these are clearly separable (e.g. Turkish and Swahili); and fusional, where a word will contain several meaning elements some of them being fused together, so that a single vowel may simultaneously mark, say, tense, voice, and person and number of subject (e.g. Latin and Sanskrit).

遗传关系的证明主要依赖于语法元素，包括词缀。理想的情况是原始语言是黏着语1 32，现代语言从黏着语变为融合语。如果一组现代语言基本上都是孤立的，语法词缀很少，那么可能永远不可能像黏着语组那样有信心地证明遗传联系。

Proof of genetic relationship rests heavily on grammatical elements, including affixes. The ideal situation is to have a proto-language that is agglutinative132 and modern languages that vary from agglutinative to fusional. If a group of modern languages are all basically isolating, with few grammatical affixes, it may never be possible to prove genetic connection with the same degree of confidence as for an agglutinative group.

随着语言的演变，它们会大致沿着一个类型学循环移动：从孤立语到黏着语，再到融合语，再回到孤立语，等等。如果我们将孤立语类型放在钟面的四点钟位置，黏着语类型放在八点钟位置，融合语类型放在十二点钟位置，那么我们就可以描述不同语系的近期变化。原始印欧语大约在十二点钟位置，但现代语系的分支以不同的速度向更孤立的位置移动（一些移到一点或两点钟位置，另一些移到三点钟位置）。早期汉语被认为大约在三点钟位置，古典汉语是一种相当纯粹的孤立语类型，位于四点钟位置，而现代汉语正在获得一种温和的黏着结构，位于五点钟位置。原始达罗毗荼语处于黏着语的孤立侧，大约在七点钟方向，而现代达罗毗荼语则沿着这个循环向九点钟方向移动。原始芬兰-乌戈尔语可能在九点钟方向，而现代语言则向十点或十一点钟方向移动（Dixon 1994: 1835）。对于有着悠久历史的埃及语，Hodge (1970) 描述了它在大约 3,000 年的时间里如何沿着这个循环移动，从融合语又回到融合语。33

As languages change over time, they tend very roughly to move around a typological circle: isolating to agglutinating, to fusional, back to isolating, and so on. If we place the isolating type at the four o'clock position, agglutinative at eight o'clock and fusional at twelve o'clock, around a clock-face, it is possible to describe recent movements in various language families. Proto-Indo-European was at about twelve o'clock but modern branches of the family have moved, at different rates, towards a more isolating position (some to one or two o'clock, others towards three o'clock). Early Chinese is thought to have been at about three o'clock, Classical Chinese was a fairly pure isolating type at four o'clock, while Modern Chinese languages are acquiring a mildly agglutinative structure, towards five o'clock. Proto-Dravidian was on the isolating side of agglutinative, at about seven o'clock, and modern Dravidian languages have moved around the cycle towards nine o'clock. Proto-Finno-Ugric may have been at around nine o'clock, with modern languages moving to ten or eleven o'clock (Dixon 1994: 1835). For Egyptian, which has a long recorded history, Hodge (1970) describes how it moved right around the cycle, from fusional back again to fusional, over a period of about 3,000 years.33

现代孤立语言可能有一个融合性祖先，其混合词素因音系和形态变化而消失；34可能永远无法重建原始语言的轮廓。现代黏着性语言可能有一个更具孤立性的祖先，其中原本不同的词发展成为语法词缀（例如，后置词变成格）。达罗毗荼语系大致属于这种类型，在这里人们可以成功恢复大量原始语言。如果原始语言是黏着性的，那么它的许多或大多数现代后代很可能已经将语法词素合并为更具融合性的结构；重建原始词素可能不是一件容易的事，但根据各个语言中的融合类型以及某些现代语言中黏着性仍然明显的程度，可能会取得一定程度的成功。

Modern-day isolating languages may have had a fusional ancestor, whose portmanteau morphemes have been lost through phonological and morphological change;34 it may never be possible to reconstruct even an outline of what the shape of the proto-language was like. Present-day agglutinative languages may have had an ancestor of more isolating profile, with what were distinct words having developed into grammatical affixes (e.g. postpositions into cases). The Dravidian family is roughly of this type and here one can successfully recover a good deal of the proto-language. If the proto-language was agglutinative then many or most of its modern descendants are likely to have merged grammatical morphemes into a more fusional structure; reconstructing the original morphemes is not likely to be an easy task, but depending on the types of fusion in individual languages and on how much agglutination is still evident in some modern languages a measure of success may be achieved.

需要注意的是，在所有这些情况下，我们都无法确定我们是否获得了正确的结果。如果一组现代语言都是孤立的，那么原始语言也可能是孤立的；或者它可能是融合的。如果我们对试图重建的语言类型没有绝对的把握，那么假定的重建的每个细节都会受到质疑。

The caveat is that in none of these cases can we be certain that we have achieved the correct result. If a group of modern languages are all isolating, the proto-language could also have been isolating; or it could have been fusional. And if there is no absolute certainty about the type of language we are attempting to reconstruct, this throws an element of doubt over every detail of the putative reconstruction.

相关学科的专家对语言学家提出的家谱图非常感兴趣。考古学家、遗传学家和人类学家喜欢得到一个明确的语言学假设，关于原始语言在何时何地使用，以及它是如何分裂和传播的。他们乐于接受任何制作的家谱，而不必停下来问它是否有充分的基础，是否被大多数语言学家接受。因此，格林伯格和“诺斯特拉主义者”的过激言论在语言学之外得到了认可。在报纸上也是如此，“原始世界”是一条新闻，而“世界上有 200 多个语言家族，几乎没有可能在它们之间提供更高级的遗传联系”则直接被扔进了垃圾箱。

Specialists in related disciplines take great interest in the family treediagrams put forward by linguists. Archaeologists, geneticists and anthropologists like to be given a clear-cut linguistic hypothesis, about where and when a proto-language was spoken and exactly how it split and spread. They happily accept any family tree that is produced, without stopping to ask whether it is soundly based, and whether it is accepted by the majority of linguists. The excesses of Greenberg and the 'Nostraticists' have thus received acceptance outside linguistics itself. And also in newspapers, where 'proto-World' is a news item while 'there are more than 200 language families in the world, with little prospect of providing higher-level genetic links between them' goes straight into the trash bin.

轻信的媒体，尤其是科普杂志和电视上的科学节目，已经接受了关于语言关系的最荒诞的想法，甚至鼓励其支持者用“原始世界”说一两句话！结果，公众对真正的语言学家所做的事情以及语言学作为一门科学能够证明什么产生了扭曲的认识。世界上没有一位著名的历史语言学家35接受格林伯格和诺斯特拉提克主义者的主张。然而，几乎没有人从他们的学术追求中抽出时间来引起公众对哪些语言关系可以得到科学证明的事实的关注。历史语言学的结果可能并不引人注目，但这并不是忽视它们而青睐引人注目但空洞的推测的理由。

A credulous media especially the popular science magazines and science programs on TV have embraced the most crackpot ideas about language relationships, even encouraging their proponents to speak a sentence or two in 'proto-World'! As a result, the public gains a distorted idea of what real linguists do, and of what linguistics, as a science, is capable of proving. There is no reputable historical linguist,35 anywhere in the world, who accepts the claims of Greenberg and the Nostraticists. Yet, scarcely any have taken time away from their academic pursuits to draw to the public's attention the facts about what language relationships can be scientifically proved. The results of historical linguistics may not be spectacular, but this is no reason for ignoring them in favour of spectacular but vacuous speculations.

当语言学家告诉考古学家和遗传学家，某某假定的家谱没有科学依据时，他们得到的回答是“给我们另一个家谱来代替它吧。”如果语言学家回答说，家谱模型可能不适用于所讨论的语言群体，这是一个类型学相似性和语言区域的问题，那么非语言学家可能会耸耸肩转过身去（并且可能会继续使用没有根据的家谱，只是因为他们认为他们需要这样的东西来将他们的考古学和遗传学理论与之联系起来）。36

When linguists tell archaeologists and geneticists that such and such a putative family tree is without scientific basis, the response is 'give us another family tree to replace it then.' If the linguists answer that the family tree model may not be applicable for the groups of languages in question that it is a matter of typological similarity and linguistic area the non-linguists may turn away with a shrug (and will probably continue using the unjustified family tree, just because they consider they need something like this, to tie their archaeological and genetic theories to).36

这是语言学家必须抵制的外部压力。我们必须着手证明任何可以证明的遗传关系，但我们必须小心，不要提出没有尝试重建或不可能重建的家谱。我们必须教育我们专业以外的人，让他们了解语言之间存在的各种关系，以及家谱只是一种模型，只适用于某些情况。

This is an outside pressure that linguists have to resist. We must set out to prove whatever genetic relationships can be proved, but we must take care not to suggest family trees where no reconstruction has been attempted or is likely to be possible. And we must educate people outside our profession both about the different kinds of relationships that are found between languages, and that the family tree is just one model, which is only applicable in certain situations.

 

 

4.2 原始语言

4.2 Proto-Languages

自然语言就像一件被修补过的旧衣服。整体轮廓或多或少是可以辨认出来的，但有些部分已经磨损并被替换，一个部分可能完全丢失，而另一个地方可能从其他地方补上了一点。相比之下，通常重建的原始语言就像一件刚从工厂里出来的衣服，每个纽扣都完好无损，每个拉链都完好无损，每条缝线都缝得整齐均匀。

A natural language is rather like an old garment that has been patched and mended. The overall outline is perceivable, to a greater or lesser extent, but some parts have worn away and been replaced, one section may have been lost altogether, and in another place a bit from another source may have been tacked on. In contrast, a proto-language as it is generally reconstructed resembles a garment straight from the factory, every button in place, every zip working, every seam sewn neatly and evenly.

也就是说，自然语言的语法中可能存在补充和不规则的词形变化，词汇中可能存在一个或多个底层/顶层，语法和音系中也可能存在一个或多个底层/顶层。然而，许多原始语言在重建时都是规则和同质的。人们常说，这是比较方法的本质，否则就无法做到。大多数（但不是全部）历史语言学家都同意，重建的原始语言充其量只能近似于给定语言家族的假定唯一祖先。

That is to say, a natural language is likely to have suppletions and irregularities of inflection in its grammar, and one or more substrata/superstrata in lexicon and perhaps also in grammar and phonology. Yet many proto-languages, as they are reconstructed, are regular and homogeneous. It is often said that this is the nature of the comparative method that one cannot do otherwise. It is agreed by most (but not by all) historical linguists that a reconstructed proto-language can be, at best, an approximation to what the putative unique ancestor of a given language family may have been like.

由此可见，比较已建立的语言家族的重建原始语言，以查看它们之间是否存在任何更高层次的遗传联系，是一项高度推测性的冒险。一种是比较可能在某种程度上与实际祖先语言的某些部分相对应的系统。

It follows from this that comparing the reconstructed proto-languages of established linguistic families, to see whether there is any higher-level genetic connection between them, is a highly speculative venture. One is comparing systems that may correspond, to some extent, to just some part of what the actual ancestor language was like.

考虑一下现在的英语。假设在未来的某个时候，语言学家试图根据一些后期的后裔语言重建英语（没有关于现在英语的直接信息或其他历史记录，也没有关于其他印欧语系语言的信息）。这些语言学家会不会重建一种第二人称的单一形式，不指定数字，而第一人称和第三人称代词具有不同的单数和复数形式？动词和名词词形变化的不规则性目前正在逐步消除（dreamed 代替 dreamt，oxes 代替 oxen）；这些不规则性中的任何一个都可以恢复吗？那么法语起源的词汇上层（在词典计数中超过一半，但在文本计数中不到一半）又如何呢？它的音位结构与本土日耳曼词汇不同。随着语言的变化和词形的简化，这些音系差异可能会变得不那么明显，从而消除许多首辅音和尾辅音组等（类似于拉丁语到西班牙语的发展）。那么，词汇的两个层次可以区分吗？据我所知，在任何原始语言的重建中，很少区分出不同的层次（印欧语除外）。

Consider present-day English. Suppose that at some time in the future linguists try to reconstruct English, on the basis of a number of latter-day descendant languages (with no direct information on present-day English, or other historical records, and no information on other IE languages). Would these linguists reconstruct a single form, unspecified for number, for second person, while first and third person pronouns have distinct singular and plural forms? Irregularities in verbal and nominal inflection are at the present time steadily being eliminated (dreamed in place of dreamt, oxes rather than oxen); would any of these irregularities be retrievable? And what about the vocabulary superstratum of French origin (more than half on a dictionary count, but much less than half on a text count), which has different phonotactic structure from native Germanic vocabulary. These phonological differences might well become less evident as the language changes and the forms of words are simplified, eliminating many initial and final consonant clusters, etc. (something like what happened in the development from Latin to Spanish). Could the two strata of vocabulary then be distinguished? Different strata seldom have been distinguished, to my knowledge, in any reconstruction of a proto-language (except for Indo-European).

研究可以在现代罗曼语基础上重建的原始语言，然后将这一结果与拉丁语（Hall 1950、1976、1983）进行比较，并将现代印度-雅利安语和梵语（Southworth 1958）进行比较，这些研究都是有益的（尽管必须记住，Hall 和 Southworth 分别已经熟悉拉丁语和梵语）。他们表明，可以重建原始罗曼语和原始印度-雅利安语的内容确实出现在拉丁语和梵语中，但只能恢复原始语言系统的一部分。也就是说，重建是一种部分近似。

Studies of the proto-language that can be reconstructed on the basis of modern Romance languages, and then comparing this result with Latin (Hall 1950, 1976, 1983), and similarly for modern Indo-Aryan languages and Sanskrit (Southworth 1958), are instructive (although one must bear in mind that Hall and Southworth were already familiar with Latin and Sanskrit respectively). They show that what can be reconstructed for proto-Romance and proto-Indo-Aryan did occur in Latin and in Sanskrit but that only a part of the original linguistic system could be retrieved. That is, the reconstruction is a partial approximation.

我们将在第七节中结合第六节中描述的间断平衡模型进一步讨论原始语言的问题。

We will discuss the question of proto-language further in §7, in the light of the punctuated equilibrium model that will be described in §6.

 

 

4.3 约会

4.3 Dating

如前所述，语言的变化速度各不相同，这取决于许多因素。这些因素包括语言的内部动态（语言系统内部变化的可能性）、与其他语言的接触程度（以及这些语言的结构类型）以及使用者的态度。我们只有少数几种情况，其中涉及希腊语、印度-雅利安语、希伯来语和埃及语的漫长历史记录，这些历史记录长达 3,000 年或最多 4,000 年，这仅仅是该语言被认为存在的 100,000 年左右的一小部分。

As noted earlier, languages change at a variable rate, depending on a number of factors. These include the internal dynamics of the language (the potential for change within the linguistic system), the degree of contact with other languages (and the types of structure in those languages), and the attitude of speakers. We have just a few scenarios with lengthy historical records involving Greek, Indo-Aryan, Hebrew and Egyptian and these extend to 3,000 or at most 4,000 years, a small fraction of the 100,000 or so years that language is thought to have been around.

令我始终感到惊奇的是，许多历史语言学家都十分自信地为他们重建的原始语言指定一个日期。（这些人大体上都坚决拒绝语言年代学的花言巧语。）我们被告知，原始印欧语是在大约 6,000 年前使用的。可以相当肯定的是，原始印度-雅利安语和现代印度-雅利安语之间的时间间隔约为 3,000 年。但是，谁能说从原始印欧语到原始印度-雅利安语的发展又花了 3,000 年呢？

What has always filled me with wonder is the assurance with which many historical linguists assign a date to their reconstructed proto-language. (And these are, by and large, people who firmly reject the glib formulas of glottochronology.) We are told that proto-Indo-European was spoken about 6,000 years ago. What is known with a fair degree of certainty is the time between proto-Indo-Aryan and the modern Indo-Aryan languages something of the order of 3,000 years. But how can anyone tell that the development from proto-Indo-European to proto-Indo-Aryan took another 3,000 years?

Mallory (1989) 给出了关于印欧语起源和年代的最清晰的讨论之一。他认为“原始印欧人是新石器时代晚期或大石器时代社会，大约在公元前 4,500 年至 2,500 年开始分化”（第 127 页）。这一年代测定基于与陶器、家养动物（绵羊、牛和马）和农业有关的重构词汇，以及这些特征的古老性。传统上，人们将原始语言与考古学家认为是物质文化中的独特创新联系起来。例如，Kargan 文化（因其在古墓的深井中埋葬的习俗而得名）与原始印欧语有关。但为什么某种原始语言应该与某种物质文化相关，而不是与其他物质文化相关呢？考古学家表达的不同观点表明，这通常带有随意性。

One of the clearest discussions of Indo-European origins and dating is given by Mallory (1989). He suggests that 'the proto-Indo-Europeans were a Late Neolithic or Encolithic society which began to diverge about 4,500 to 2,500 BC' (p. 127). This dating is based on reconstructed words to do with pottery, domesticated animals (sheep, cow and horse), and agriculture, and what is thought to be the antiquity of these traits. There is a tradition of relating proto-languages to what archaeologists recognise as distinctive innovations in material culture. For instance, the Kargan culture (named for its practice of burial in deep shafts within a barrow) has been linked with proto-Indo-European. But why should a particular proto-language be related to a particular material culture, and not to some other? The varying opinions expressed by archaeologists suggest that there is generally an element of arbitrariness involved.

实际上，语言年代测定应该基于语言证据。但众所周知，语言的变化速度各不相同。无法知道从假定的原始印欧语系同质性到原始印度伊朗语系、原始凯尔特语系、原始日耳曼语系等语言多样性需要多长时间。这些变化可能很快（如伍德拉克岛）也可能很慢。我们根本不知道。

Really, linguistic dating should be based on linguistic evidence. But languages are known to change at different rates. There is no way of knowing how long it took to go from the presumed homogeneity of proto-Indo-European to the linguistic diversity of proto-Indo-Iranian, proto-Celtic, proto-Germanic, etc. The changes could have been rapid (as on Woodlark Island) or slow. We simply don't know.

在印欧语系学者们发表完他们的意见后，研究其他语系的学者们给出了他们的年代。如果语言差异被认为与印欧语系大致相同，那么时间深度也大致相同；如果差异较小，那么时间深度也稍小；等等。对于原始阿尔冈昆语，大约 3,2002,900 年前的年代被定为暂定年代（Siebert 1967）。对于原始乌拉尔语，6,0007,000 年前是公认的年代（Campbell，即将出版-b）。

After the Indo-Europeanists have had their say, scholars working on other families present their dates. Linguistic divergences thought to be of about the same order of magnitude as IE are accorded about the same time depth; or a little less, for a little less divergence; and so on. For proto-Algonquian about 3,2002,900 BP has been given as a tentative date (Siebert 1967). For proto-Uralic, 6,0007,000 BP is a generally accepted date (Campbell, forthcoming-b).

我们之前提到，印欧语系的分裂和分化不可能是常态；这是一种不寻常的现象。我们有一些书面记录，而最近 3,000 年的扩张后期可能比早期快得多，甚至慢得多。为什么原始印欧语不能在 10,500 年前使用？37这与一个重大的社会经济发展，即农业的引入有关，考古学家将这一地区的农业引入确定为大约 10,500 年前（参见 Harris 1996）。为什么原始阿尔冈昆语不能在 6,000 或 7,000 年前使用（这与人们进入美洲的公认日期 12,000 年前完全一致）？当然，对于关于原始语言的年代问题，唯一真正诚实的答案是“我们不知道”。或者，有人可能会猜测‘可能是在距今 5,000 到 12,000 年前之间’。

We noted earlier that the split and divergence involved in the Indo-European family cannot be the norm; this is an unusual occurrence. The later part of this expansion the last 3,000 years, for which we have some written records may have been very much quicker, or even very much slower, than the earlier part. Why couldn't proto-Indo-European have been spoken about 10,500 years ago?37 This would correlate with a major socio-economic development, the introduction of agriculture, which archaeologists date at about 10,500 BP for this part of the world (see Harris 1996). Why couldn't proto-Algonquian have been spoken about 6,000 or 7,000 years ago (this would be fully compatible with the accepted date of 12,000 BP for the entry of people into the Americas)? Surely, the only really honest answer to questions about dating a proto-language is 'We don't know.' Or, one might venture something like 'probably some time between 5,000 and perhaps 12,000 BP'.

在过去 30 年里，在研究澳大利亚语言的过程中，我有时会尝试假设这些语言属于同一个语系，然后寻找一个语系树模型（下文将讨论另一种情况）。然后出现的问题是：原始语言的日期可能是什么时候？经过仔细考虑，似乎唯一诚实的答案是：可能是任何日期，4,000 年前或 40,000 年前都是完全可能的（两者之间的任何日期也是可能的）。

While working on the languages of Australia, over the past 30 years, I have at times experimented with the hypothesis that the languages are related as one family and then looked for a family tree model (an alternative scenario is discussed below). The question that then presented itself was: what could have been the date of the proto-language? After careful consideration, it seemed that the only honest answer is: it could be anything 4,000 years BP or 40,000 years BP are both perfectly possible (as is any date in between).

普遍接受的观点是，原始印欧语的年代应为 6000 年前左右，其他原始语言的年代应以此为基准。我发现这个问题很难让专家讨论。然而，它确实似乎是一座纸牌屋（一度被语言年代学的幻想所强化）。这是一个需要仔细重新审视的问题，需要讨论和比较各种可能性。38

The received opinion of a date of around 6000 BP for proto-Indo-European with dates for other proto-languages being calibrated on this scale is an ingrained one. I have found this a difficult matter to get specialists to even discuss. Yet it does seem to be a house of cards (reinforced, at one time, by the chimera of glottochronology). This is a question that demands careful re-examination, with a full range of possibilities being discussed and compared.38

 

 

4.4 子群

4.4 Subgrouping

在族谱中重建子群，并确定分裂发生的方式，可能比首先确定这组语言在遗传上是否有关联要困难得多。它依赖于并非总是可用的证据：一个族中的一组语言中，每一种语言都有许多独特的共同创新，这表明它们构成了一个子群，并且在整个族的原始语言和这些现代语言之间有一个共同的祖先。39

Reconstructing the subgrouping within a family tree the ways in which the splits occurred can be a much more difficult matter than deciding, in the first place, that this group of languages is genetically related. It relies on evidence that is not always available: a number of distinctive shared innovations in each of a set of languages within a family points to their constituting a subgroup, with a common ancestor part-way between the proto-language for the entire family and these modern languages.39

例如，丹麦语、瑞典语、挪威语、冰岛语、英语、荷兰语和德语由于都经历了某些变化而被确立为印欧语系中的日耳曼语支（据说这些变化发生在原始印欧语和原始日耳曼语之间）。其中最著名的一组声音变化就是被称为格林定律的声音变化。送气浊塞音，如 bh，变成了相应的平塞音 b（比较梵语 bhara:mi“我忍受”与英语动词 bear）；不送气浊塞音，如 b，变成了相应的清塞音 p（比较希腊语 kannabis 与英语 hemp）；清塞音，如 p，变成了相应的擦音 f（比较拉丁语 pater 与英语 father）。

For instance, Danish, Swedish, Norwegian, Icelandic, English, Dutch and German are established as the Germanic subgroup within the Indo-European family by virtue of certain changes that they have all undergone (these are then said to have taken place between proto-Indo-European and proto-Germanic). One of the best-known is the set of sound changes known as Grimm's Law. An aspirated voiced stop, such as bh, became the corresponding plain stop, b (compare Sanskrit bhara:mi 'I bear' with the English verb bear); an unaspirated voiced stop, such as b, became the corresponding voiceless stop, p (compare Greek kannabis with English hemp); and a voiceless stop, such as p, became the corresponding fricative, f (compare Latin pater with English father).

任何亚群划分的尝试都必须充分考虑地域特征。特别是，如果假定亚群的所有成员彼此相邻，那么他们共同的创新可能最近在一种语言中发展起来，并传播到其他语言中；那么它们就不是亚群划分的证据。但很难判断这种情况是否发生过。

Any attempt at subgrouping must take full account of areal features. In particular, if all the members of a putative subgroup are in contiguity with one another, their shared innovations may have developed recently, in one language, and diffused into the others; they would not then be evidence for subgrouping. But it can be difficult to tell whether this has happened or not.

判断的一个方法是查看邻近语言（来自另一个语系），看看它们是否也表现出这些特征。如果是，它们可能是一种地域特征；如果不是，它们很可能是亚群的迹象。

One way of deciding can be to look at neighbouring languages, from another family, and see if they also show the features. If so, they are probably an areal trait; if not, they may well be an indication of subgrouping.

南美洲提供了一个理想的实验室，因为每个主要语系都分散在地理上不同的区域，周围都是其他语系的语言。例如，有人建议将阿拉瓦克语系划分为亚群，但几乎在每种情况下，亚群的所有语言都位于一个地理区块中（见 Aikhenvald，即将出版）。需要做的是研究每个假定亚群的特征，看看其中哪些特征也出现在邻近的非阿拉瓦克语中，这也是尚未完成的工作。一旦排除这些因素，任何剩余的共同创新（如果有的话）都可以作为划分亚群的证据进行评估。40

South America provides an ideal laboratory since each major language family is scattered in geographically separate pockets, surrounded by languages from other families. A subgrouping has been suggested for the Arawak family, for instance, but in almost every case all the languages of a subgroup are in a single geographical block (see Aikhenvald, forthcoming). What is needed and this is work which has still to be done is to examine the features that characterise each putative subgroup and see which of them is also found in neighbouring non-Arawak languages. Once these are discounted, any remaining shared innovations (if there are any) can be assessed as evidence for subgrouping.40

可以通过两个例子来说明与子类划分相关的困难。第一个是示意图。假设语言 X 分为 A、B 和 C。现代语言 B 和 C 位于某个区域，与 A 相距较远，并且具有某些共同的特征（例如名词类别和声调），这些特征在 A 中没有，但在其所在区域的其他语言中却有。至少有两种可能性。

The difficulties associated with subgrouping can be demonstrated through two examples. The first is schematic. Suppose that language X splits into A, B and C. Modern languages B and C are in a certain area, distant from A, and share certain features (say, noun classes and tones) that are not found in A but do occur in other languages of their area. There are at least two possibilities.

（a）X 语言分裂为 A 语言和原始 BC 语言。原始 BC 语言迁入另一个地区并接受了该地区的传播特征。后来，它分裂为 B 语言和 C 语言，新特征被这两种现代语言继承。

(a) X split into A and proto-BC. Proto-BC moved into another area and accepted the diffusional features of that area. Later, it split into B and C, with the new features being inherited by both modern languages.

(b) X 分裂为 A、B 和 C，中间没有子群。然后 B 和 C 迁入其现在的地区，并通过采用其特征来适应这种语言环境。作为密切相关的语言，它们可能会以类似的方式从其自身的内部资源中发展出声调和名词类别（因为这些内部资源是相似的）。

(b) X split into A, B and C with no intermediate subgrouping. Then B and C moved into their present-day area and both adapted to this linguistic milieu by adopting the features that characterise it. Being closely related languages they would be likely to develop tones and noun classes, from their own internal resources, in similar ways (since these internal resources would be similar).

这两种替代方案可以概括如下：

The two alternatives can be schematised:

图 4.1

Figure 4.1

重点是，仅从现代语言学的情况来看（有 A、B 和 C），很难区分这两种可能性。我们没有理由根据邻近语言中也出现的共同特征来假设一个由 B 和 C 组成的子群。

The point is that, given just the modern linguistic situation (with A, B and C), it would be difficult to distinguish between these two possibilities. We would not be justified in positing a subgroup consisting of B and C on the basis of shared features that also occur in neighbouring languages.

可以看出，由于可用数据的限制，只有语言家族发展过程中发生的部分子群是可以检索的。

It will be seen that only a part of the subgrouping that has taken place in the development of a language family may be retrievable, just because of the limitations on the data that is available.

第二个例子更加具体。以当今的德语、英语和法语为例。对现代语言的考察表明，德语和英语在遗传上密切相关（有许多共同的语法形式和大量最常用的词汇，包括那些具有不规则屈折的词汇），但英语在词汇方面以及某种程度上在语法和音系方面都具有相当大的法语上层。如图 4.2 所示。

The second example is more concrete. Consider present-day German, English and French. Inspection of the modern languages shows that German and English are closely genetically related (sharing many grammatical forms and a high proportion of the most frequently used lexemes, including those with irregular inflections), but that English has a sizeable French superstratum in lexicon and to some extent in grammar and phonology. This is shown in figure 4.2.

图 4.2

Figure 4.2

现在假设在未来的某个时候，语言学家只有德语、英语和法语衍生语言的数据（没有历史信息）。英语的语法和词汇将在其衍生语言中发生相当大的变化。语法不规则性可能已经消失。一些德语词缀可能已经消失，法语词缀可能变得更加多产（例如，re-enter 中的 re- 和 glorify 中的 -ify，以及已经建立的 -able 之类的词缀）。此外，英语词汇中罗曼语词源的单词可能会越来越多地使用，而德语词素则会减少（这在印度英语中已经发生，参见 Subrahmanian 1978；Kachru 1965、1983；和 Dixon 1991a）。

Now suppose that at some time in the future linguists only have data on languages descended from German, English and French (with no historical information). The grammar and lexicon of English will have undergone considerable changes in its descendants. Grammatical irregularities are likely to have been lost. Some Germanic affixes may have been lost and affixes of French origin may have become more productive (e.g. re-, as in re-enter, and -ify, as in glorify, in addition to things like the already established -able). In addition, words of Romance origin in English vocabulary could be used more and more, at the expense of Germanic lexemes (this already happens in Indian English see Subrahmanian 1978; Kachru 1965, 1983; and Dixon 1991a).

如果所有这些完全合理的变化都发生了，我们假设的未来语言学家可能无法察觉到重建英语和重建德语之间的密切遗传联系。他们只能假设图 4.3 中的图表。

If all these perfectly plausible changes were to take place, our linguists of the hypothetical future might not be able to perceive a close genetic link between reconstructed English and reconstructed German. They could only posit the diagram in figure 4.3.

图 4.3

Figure 4.3

总之，通常只能恢复语言家族中的某些子群。当然，词汇统计学提供了完美表达的谱系树（通常采用二元或三元划分）；但这是基于词汇相似性，而词汇相似性并不是充分标准。印欧语的情况说明了这一点。如果将原始印欧语视为一种语言，我们需要首先将其划分为不少于十个主要子群。将 IE 型谱系树模型应用于其他语言群体的人中，很少有人如此宽容，通常（但并非总是）假设将其划分为两个、三个或四个分支。

In summary, it is generally only possible to recover some of the subgrouping within a language family. Lexicostatistics, of course, provided a perfectly articulated family tree (with, as a rule, binary or ternary splits); but this is based on vocabulary similarities, which are not a sufficient criterion. The Indo-European situation makes the point. Taking proto-Indo-European to be a single language, we need a first split into no less than ten primary subgroups. Few of the people applying an IE-type family tree model to other groups of languages have been so forbearing splits into two, three or four branches are normally (though not invariably) posited.

 

 

五种变革模式

5 Modes of Change

语言内部的变化和语言变化（语言分裂）都有两种基本可能性：突然或渐进。我将依次讨论这些可能性，然后在第 5.3 节中考虑语言的起源方式。

There are two basic possibilities sudden or gradual both for changes within languages and for changes to languages (language splitting). I discuss these in turn and then, in §5.3, consider the way in which language may have originated.

 

 

5.1 语言内部的变化

5.1 Changes within Languages

我认为，语言中的许多变化都不是渐进的，而是相当突然发生的，通常在一代或两代人的时间内发生。也就是说，变化更像是一系列的步骤，而不是稳步上升。

I suggest that many types of change within a language are not gradual but rather happen fairly suddenly, often within the space of a generation or two. That is, change is more like a series of steps than it is like a steady incline.

如果一种新的语法机制被创新，这很可能是一次性发生的，而不是一点一点发生的。班图语有大约 16 个前缀，它们结合了名词类和数（单数或复数）的标记。祖先语言不太可能一开始只有一个前缀，然后稍后添加第二个前缀，然后再添加另一个，依此类推，直到最终有 16 个前缀。我并不是说这一定是一次性发生的（尽管它可能是这样），而是说这不会涉及超过两三个阶段。例如，可能首先有“人类”与“非人类”的标记，然后在“非人类”中有更多的区别。

If a new grammatical mechanism is innovated this is likely to happen all at once, rather than bit by bit. Bantu languages have about sixteen prefixes which combine marking of noun class and of number (singular or plural). It is unlikely that the ancestor language began with just one prefix, then added a second one a bit later, then another a bit later still, and so on, until eventually there were sixteen. I am not suggesting that this necessarily happened all at once (although it could have), but that there would not have been more than two or three stages involved. There might first have been a marking of 'human' versus 'non-human', for instance, and then more distinctions within 'non-human'.

当后置介词发展成为格系统时，整个系统可能会或多或少同时发展，而不是一个后置介词变成一个格（名词的词缀，而不是与其在句法构造中的自由形式），然后一百年后第二个后置介词发展成为第二个格，依此类推，这样就形成了一个在七个独立阶段中发展出的七个格的系统。

When postpositions develop into a case system, the whole system is likely to evolve more or less at the same time, rather than one postposition becoming one case (an affix to a noun rather than a free form in syntactic construction with it), then a hundred years later a second postposition developing into a second case, and so on, so that a system of seven cases developed in seven separate stages.

合并也类似。当一种语言开始将名词置于动词结构中（两侧是语法词缀）时，这可能从几个惯用组合开始，但很快就会推广到相当多的名词（例如，所有主要身体部位，加上“火”、“水”和其他几个名词），而不是逐渐扩展，一次添加几个名词。

Similarly with incorporation. When a language begins to place nouns within the structure of a verb (flanked on each side by grammatical affixes), this may begin with a couple of idiomatic combinations but will then, very quickly, be generalised to a fair-sized set of nouns (say, all major body parts, plus 'fire', 'water' and a few more nouns) rather than being gradually extended, adding more nouns a few at a time.

我并不是说不能在既定的语法类别中添加新词。一旦一种语言拥有了五种格的系统，就很可能会添加其他格；或者添加新的名词类别；或者添加更多名词。我的观点是，当一种新类别出现时，它会以决定性的方式出现。可能根本没有格，然后也许在几代之内就会出现一个由六个左右的格组成的系统，而不是一个、两个、三个……但随后，作为进一步的增量，在稍后的某个阶段可能会出现第七种格。

I am not suggesting that an established grammatical category cannot be added to. Once a language has a system of, say, five cases, others may well be added; or a new noun class; or further nouns may become open to incorporation. My point is that, when a new category develops, it will do so in a decisive manner. There will be no cases at all and then within perhaps a couple of generations a system of half-a-dozen or so cases, rather than one, then two, then three, . . . But then, as a further increment, a seventh case could well develop at some later stage.

类似的说法也适用于束缚代词的发展。在语言发展的某个阶段，主语和宾语由动词外的自由代词表示。然后，这些自由代词发展成为每个动词都必须包含的强制性附着代词（无论是主语和宾语的核心成分，还是只有一个核心成分）。第一人称单数代词不太可能首先成为强制性的束缚附着词，而其他代词则保持自由形式。在大多数情况下（有已知的例外，但这种情况相当罕见），一套相当完整的束缚代词会或多或少同时发展。（然后，它们当然可能会逐渐融入动词词中，主语和宾语束缚形式可能会减少并合并为一个混合词素。）

Similar remarks apply to the development of bound pronouns. At one stage of a language's development subject and object are shown by free pronouns outside the verb. Then these develop into obligatory clitic pronouns that every verb must include (either for both core constituents, subject and object, or just for one). It is unlikely that the first person singular pronoun would first become an obligatory bound clitic, while other pronouns remained as free forms. In most cases (there are known exceptions, but these are rather rare), a fairly full set of bound pronouns would develop more or less simultaneously. (And then of course they may gradually become more integrated into the verbal word, with perhaps subject and object bound forms reducing and merging into a single portmanteau morpheme.)

当一种语言改变其语法特征的某个部分时，比如从作格变为宾格或反之亦然，这也可能发生得相当突然。在澳大利亚西北部，有七种语言组成的地区性群体，即恩加雅尔达语群。41其中三种语言的名词词形变化采用作格系统，与大多数澳大利亚语言一样，作格（元音后为 -nku * 或 -lu，辅音后为 -tu）标记 A（及物主语）功能，而绝对格（零实现）标记 S（不及物主语）和 O（及物宾语）。还有一个格后缀 -ku，标记外围关系与格。其它四种语言已经发展出宾格系统，A 和 S 没有标记，原来的与格后缀 -ku 用于 O（也保留用于与格）。 Dench (1982) 和 Dixon (1994: 198ff.) 讨论了变化机制。需要注意的是，Ngayarda 语系中的每种语言的主句要么有明显的作格词形变化系统，要么有明显的宾格系统。没有中间状态。当从作格变为宾格时，变化迅速而干净。

When a language changes some part of its grammatical profile say, from ergative to accusative or vice versa this is also likely to take place fairly suddenly. In the north-west of Australia there is an areal group of seven languages, the Ngayarda group.41 Three of these languages have an ergative system of inflection on nouns, like most Australian languages ergative case (-nku * or -lu after a vowel and -tu after a consonant) marks A (transitive subject) function while absolutive (with zero realisation) marks S (intransitive subject) and O (transitive object). There is also a case suffix -ku which marks the peripheral relation dative. The other four languages have developed an accusative system A and S have zero marking with the original dative suffix, -ku, being used for O (and also being retained for dative). The mechanism of change is discussed by Dench (1982) and Dixon (1994: 198ff.). The point to note is that each language from the Ngayarda group has either a clearly ergative system of inflection in its main clauses, or a clearly accusative system. There is nothing in between. When the change from ergative to accusative happened, it took place swiftly and cleanly.

除了名词类、并入、格系统、束缚代词的演变，以及语法中某些部分从作格到宾格的转变，还可以添加其他突然变化的例子。我认为，任何语法类别或构造类型的发展都可能是通过一系列阶梯式变化来实现的，而不是逐渐实现的。

Other examples of sudden changes could be added to those given the evolution of noun classes, of incorporation, of case systems, of bound pronouns, and a shift from an ergative to an accusative profile in some part of the grammar. I suggest that the development of any grammatical category, or construction type, is likely to be implemented by a series of step-like changes, rather than gradually.

但当然，有些类型的变化本质上是渐进的。人们认为，英语元音大转变始于高元音的双元音化（i > ai 和 u > au），然后其他元音占据更高的发音位置来填补空缺。整个过程可能至少持续了几个世纪。

But, of course, some types of change are essentially gradual. The great English vowel shift is thought to have begun by the diphthongisation of high vowels (i > ai and u > au), with other vowels then assuming higher places of articulation to fill in the gaps, as it were. The whole process may have taken at least a couple of centuries.

虽然范畴的演变相当迅速，但它们的消失却可能相当缓慢。范畴的消失可能是由于音系的损耗，而音系损耗本质上是一个渐进的过程。例如，在英语中，词尾鼻音消失了，然后是词尾非重读元音；因此，格尾消失了（属格 -s 除外）。例如，有与格单数后缀 -e（在强变格中）或 -an（在弱变格中），还有与格复数后缀 -um（在两种变格中）；所有这些形式都消失了，而与格后缀所标记的句法功能现在必须由介词 to 或 for 来表示。

And while the evolution of categories happens rather quickly, their loss may be quite gradual. The loss of a category can be due to phonological attrition, which is by its nature a gradual process. In English, for instance, final nasals were lost and then final unstressed vowels; as a result of this, case endings disappeared (except for genitive -s). For example, there was a dative singular suffix -e (in the strong declension) or -an (in the weak declension) and also dative plural suffix -um (in both declensions); all these forms were lost, and the syntactic function that had been marked by the dative case suffix has now to be shown by a preposition, to or for.

我们说过，当语法中建立一个新的范畴时，可能会增加新的术语，这是一种渐变。总的来说，渐变涉及细节问题，而突变涉及语法概况的转变。

We have said that when a new category is established in the grammar it may be augmented by new terms, which is a kind of gradual change. Overall, gradual change concerns matters of detail, while sudden changes relate to shift in grammatical profile.

其他渐进变化包括：音素内的音位变体转换（例如，见Jakobson 1962: 20220）；词素或结构类型意义的扩展；用规则的屈折结尾替代不规则的屈折结尾；新复合词的形成（尽管引入一种新的复合词类型很可能是一种突然的变化）；以及接受来自邻近语言的借词。

Other gradual changes include: allophonic shifting within a phoneme (see, for example, Jakobson 1962: 20220); the extension of meaning of a lexeme or of a construction type; analogising regular inflectional endings to replace irregular ones; the formation of new compounds (although the introduction of a new type of compounding is likely to be a sudden change); and the acceptance of loan words from neighbouring languages.

语法特征中的一些变化是语言内部动态自发引发的。澳大利亚就是一个例子。最初，名词以作格形式变格，代词以宾格形式变格。然后，束缚代词以宾格形式发展起来。自由代词现在很少使用，主要用于强调。内部动机的变化是将自由代词像名词一样以作格形式变格。（可以说，它们现在被视为一种特殊的专有名称。）这种情况适用于瓦尔皮里语和其他语言（见 Dixon 1994：967）。

Some changes in grammatical profile are self-triggered, by the internal dynamics of the language. An example can be given from Australia. Originally, nouns inflected on an ergative, and pronouns on an accusative, pattern. Then bound pronouns developed, on an accusative pattern. Free pronouns were now used sparingly, mainly for emphasis. The internally motivated change was to inflect free pronouns on an ergative pattern, like nouns. (It could be said that they are now treated like a special kind of proper name.) This scenario has applied in Warlpiri, among other languages (see Dixon 1994: 967).

然而，大多数变化都是由于邻近语言或语言群体的类别传播所致。如果 X 语言使用者接触的语言都有名词类别（或性别）系统，那么 X 语言很可能发展出自己的系统，不是通过借用邻居的形式，而是通过从内部资源（通常来自通用名词）中演变名词类别词缀。而且，正如前面提到的，这个过程很可能在短短几代内完成。42

However, the majority of changes are due to the diffusion of a category from a nearby language or group of languages. If the languages with which speakers of X are in contact all have a system of noun classes (or genders), then language X is likely to develop its own system generally, not by borrowing forms from its neighbours but by evolving noun class affixes from its internal resources (often, from generic nouns). And, as already mentioned, the process is likely to be completed within just a few generations.42

 

 

5.2 语言分裂

5.2 Language Splitting

每种语言以及语言中的每种方言总是处于变化过程中。两种相邻的方言或两种相邻的语言之间的关系从来都不是静止的，它们可能在某些方面越来越接近，而在其他方面却越来越疏远。相邻的方言或语言可能会在一段时间内逐渐趋同，然后改变方向并开始分化。这在很大程度上取决于其使用者之间的接触类型（友好还是敌对），无论他们彼此之间是贸易往来、与另一群体通婚、参加体育或音乐嘉年华、在另一群体的军队中服役等等。

Every language and every dialect within a language is always in a process of change. The relationship between two adjoining dialects, or two contiguous languages, is never static they may be moving closer together in some features and further apart in other ways. Neighbouring dialects or languages may gradually converge for a period, and then change direction and begin to diverge. This will be motivated largely by the type of contact between their speakers friendly or hostile, whether they trade with each other, marry into the other group, take part in sporting or musical carnivals, serve in the army of the other group, and so on.

一旦一个国家或部落分裂成两个，每个都有自己的政治组织，这两个群体就会抓住语言特征作为自我认同的标志。少数几个词素和/或代词就足够了。两个新国家或部落的方言可能完全可以理解，重要的政治问题是小心使用某些词语并避免使用其他词语。

Once a nation or tribe splits into two, each with its own political organisation, the two groups will seize on linguistic features as tokens of self-identification. A handful of lexemes and/or pronouns can be sufficient. The dialects of two new nations or tribes may well be fully intelligible, the important political thing being to take care to use certain words and to avoid others.

最终，两种方言可能会分化到无法理解的程度，必须被视为不同的语言。

Eventually, two dialects may diverge to such an extent that they cease to be intelligible and must be considered distinct languages.

这可能以两种方式发生，取决于方言是否失去或保留地理联系。我们将逐一讨论这些可能性。

This can happen in two ways, according to whether the dialects lose geographical connection, or retain it. We shall discuss these possibilities one at a time.

（一个） 地理隔离下的语言分裂

假设某种语言的部分使用者前往新的地方（越过大海或山脉）并在那里生活，而其余使用者则留在原地。进一步假设两组之间没有（或几乎没有）接触。两组方言都会发生变化，方言总是会发生变化，而且会以不同的方式发生变化，方言会逐渐变得越来越不同。如果在 X 年后重新建立联系，方言可能仍然可以相互理解。如果在更长的时间（Z 年）后重新建立联系，那么就不会相互理解，我们将拥有两种截然不同的语言。

Suppose that some of the speakers of a language travel to a new place (across the sea, or over the mountains) and live there, leaving the remainder of the speakers in the original location. Suppose further that there is no (or almost no) contact between the two groups. The dialects of each of the two groups will change, as dialects always do, and they will change in different ways the dialects will gradually become more and more different. If contact were re-established after a period of X years, the dialects might still be mutually comprehensible. If contact were re-established after a much longer period, Z years, there would be no mutual intelligibility and we would have two distinct languages.

在这种地理隔离的情况下，从一种语言发展为两种语言将是一个渐进的过程。这是因为各群体之间没有接触；他们没有试图相互交流。因此：43

In this situation, of geographical separation, the development from one language into two would be a gradual process. This is because there is no contact between the groups; they are not trying to communicate with each other. Thus:43

图 5.1

Figure 5.1

假设在中间的某个时间重新建立了联系。第一组的一些成员原本留在自己的祖国，现在可能也移民到同一片新土地。这可能发生在某个阶段（图表上的时间 Y），此时的可理解性如此之高，以至于很难分辨我们拥有的是同一种语言的两种高度不同的方言，还是两种截然不同（但非常相似）的语言。如果发生这种情况，情况很快就会自行解决。两个群体的使用者要么建立密切的关系，要么各自将自己的语言向另一群体的语言靠拢，从而将它们确立为一种语言的明确方言。45或者，在另一种可能的情况下，每个群体都可能对另一个群体采取冷漠的态度，团结起来，进一步改变自己的说话方式，使其与另一个群体的说话方式更加不同。在很短的时间内，我们就会清楚地看到两种截然不同的语言的情况。

Suppose that contact were re-established at an intermediate time. Some of the members of the first group, who had originally remained in their homeland, might now also emigrate to the same new land. This could happen at a stage (time Y on the diagram) when intelligibility is such that it is hard to tell whether we have two highly divergent dialects of a single language, or two distinct (but very similar) languages. If this happened the situation would quickly resolve itself. Either speakers of the two groups would establish close relations and each would accommodate44 its speech towards that of the other group, establishing them as clear dialects of one language.45 Or, in the other possible outcome, each group might adopt a standoffish attitude towards the other, closing ranks and engineering further changes in their way of speech so that it became more different from that of the other group. Within a short time we would then have the clear situation of two distinct languages.

地理分离下的分裂的一个例子来自日本南部的冲绳。公元 700 年之前的某个时候，冲绳由说古日语方言的人定居。在接下来的 800 年左右，冲绳和日本之间的接触很少，到 15 世纪末第一次有书面记录的时候，冲绳语和日语（一种独特的（虽然密切相关的）语言）是互不相通的。冲绳在 19 世纪末成为日本的一部分，并稍微接近日语（通过借词等），但仍然是一种独立的语言。第二次世界大战及其后果带来了巨大的变化。从 1945 年到 1972 年，冲绳由美国管理，并与标准日语使用者进行了大量的接触；冲绳人的语言向日语靠拢。自 1972 年冲绳回归日本以来，这种现象愈演愈烈。这里的统一发生的时间比图 5.1 中的时间 Y 稍晚。冲绳语和日语已经发展成为两种语言；冲绳语发生了一定程度的克里奥尔化，再次成为日语的一种方言。年轻一代可以听懂 1940 年以前的冲绳语，但不会再说这种语言，而老年人仍然保留着这种语言。46

An example of splitting under geographical separation comes from Okinawa, just to the south of Japan. Sometime before 700 AD, Okinawa was settled by speakers of a dialect of Old Japanese. For the next 800 years or so there was minimal contact between Okinawa and Japan and, by the time of the first written records, at the end of the fifteenth century, Okinawan was mutually unintelligible with Japanese a distinct (although closely related) language. Okinawa became part of Japan at the end of the nineteenth century and moved a little closer to Japanese (through loan words, etc.) while still remaining a separate language. The Second World War and its aftermath then produced a drastic change. From 1945 until 1972 Okinawa was administered by the USA and came into a great deal of contact with speakers of Standard Japanese; Okinawans accommodated their speech towards Japanese. This has intensified since Okinawa was restored to Japan in 1972. Here the reunification happened slightly later than time Y in figure 5.1. Okinawan and Japanese had developed to be two languages; there has been a degree of creolisation involved in Okinawan changing to again become a dialect of Japanese. The younger generation can understand, but no longer speak, pre-1940 Okinawan, the form which is maintained by older people.46

许多语言分裂都与地理隔离有关，如大部分太平洋岛屿上的居民被说南岛语的人们迁移到别处；说阿萨巴斯坎语的人们从加拿大迁移到新墨西哥州和亚利桑那州；而且，很有可能，说僧伽罗语的人们迁移到斯里兰卡。

Many language splits have involved geographical separation much of the peopling of the Pacific Islands by speakers of Austronesian languages; the movement of speakers of Athapaskan languages down from Canada into New Mexico and Arizona; and, in all probability, the movement of speakers of what became Singhalese into Sri Lanka.

（二） 保持地理连续性的同时实现语言分裂

当两种方言发展成为不同的语言并保持连续性时，我们会看到完全不同的场景，两个群体的成员仍然保持一定程度的联系和交流。在这种情况下，分裂相当突然，因此：

We get a totally different scenario when two dialects develop into distinct languages and remain in contiguity, with members of the two groups still maintaining some degree of contact and communication. In this situation the split is rather sudden, thus:

图 5.2

Figure 5.2

我在第 2 节中提到，当“语言”以相互理解性来定义时，判断两组语言是同一种语言的方言还是两种不同的语言并不困难。可理解性可以是 10% 左右（两种密切相关的语言）或 70% 或更高（一种语言的方言）；几乎从不会在 50% 左右。也就是说，一旦两种方言达到足以失去相互理解性并成为独立语言的阶段，这种情况就会迅速发生，只需几代人的时间。每种方言都会经历相当彻底的语法变化，并以比平常更快的速度替换词素；发音也可能发生变化。

I mentioned, in §2, that there is seldom much difficulty in deciding whether the speech of two groups constitutes dialects of one language or two distinct languages, when 'language' is defined in terms of mutual intelligibility. The intelligibility can be about 10% (two closely related languages) or 70% or more (dialects of one language); it is almost never around 50%. That is, once two dialects reach the stage of being different enough to lose mutual intelligibility and become separate languages, this happens rapidly, within a couple of generations. Each undergoes fairly radical changes in grammar and replaces lexemes at a faster rate than usual; there are also likely to be changes in pronunciation.

分裂总是有政治动机的。说 A1 方言的人与北方说完全不同的语言 B 的邻居建立了更密切的社会和贸易联系，而与南方说 A2（同一种语言的方言）的人则没有。同样，说 A2 方言的人更愿意与他们南方说第三种语言 C 的人交往和认同，而不是与说 A1 方言的人交往和认同。A1 会变得更像 B，A2 会变得更像 C，直到 A1 和 A2 成为两种截然不同（但密切相关）的语言。

There is invariably political motivation for a split. Speakers of dialect A1 develop closer social and trade contacts with their neighbours to the north, who speak a quite different language, B, than with speakers of A2, a dialect of the same language, to the south. Similarly, speakers of A2 will prefer to associate with and identify with speakers of a third language, C, to the south of them, rather than with speakers of A1. A1 will become more like B and A2 will become more like C until A1 and A2 are two distinct (but closely related) languages.

在“地理上分离”的情况下，如图 5.1 所示，一种方言的使用者不知道另一种方言的存在，也不知道他们说话的方式。每种方言都以正常的、渐进的速度发生变化。在“地理上相邻”的情况下（图 5.2），每个群体都充分了解对方，不同的方言突然升级为不同的语言主要是出于政治目的，目的是制度化政治自我认同并表达对另一个群体的反感。47

In the 'geographically separate' situation, shown in figure 5.1, speakers of one dialect did not know of the existence of the other group, and how they spoke. Each dialect changed at a normal, gradual rate. In the 'geographically contiguous' situation (figure 5.2), each group is fully aware of the other, and the sudden escalation of diverging dialects into distinct languages is primarily a political move, to institutionalise political self-identity and demonstrate antipathy towards the other group.47

正如上文所提到的，如果将“地理上分离”的情况转变为“连续”的情况，在可理解性处于中间阶段时，根据各群体之间的政治和社会态度，这种情况将很快转变为“一种语言”或“两种语言”。

As was mentioned, if the 'geographically separate' situation were transformed into a 'contiguous' situation, at a time when intelligibility was at an intermediate stage, the situation would speedily resolve itself into 'one language' or 'two languages', according to the political and social attitudes between the groups.

 

 

5.3 语言的起源

5.3 The Origin of Language

如果语言的分裂通常是突然的（除非两个群体在地理上分开并且不知道彼此的存在），那么语言的最初出现又如何呢？

If language split is typically sudden (save in the situation where two groups are geographically separate and unaware of the existence of each other), what then about the initial emergence of language?

有两种截然不同的情况。

There are two, polar, scenarios.

（一个） 逐步发展

早期人类发展出了一种非常初级的语言，只有几个单词，可能只有一个并列两个单词的语法设备，一个不及物谓语及其论元（例如，当一个小孩的句子都是妈妈油漆或婴儿重的形式时）。每隔几百年或几千年就会增加几个单词和稍微复杂的语法，直到最终形成一种具有现代语言典型复杂性的语言。根据这种观点，我们首先会得到一种初级语言（几十个单词），然后是一种原始语言（几百个单词），然后是后原始阶段，接着是前现代语言，最后是现代语言（数千个单词和一个语法，其结构和规则需要几百页才能以相当完整的方式描述）。如果语言发展是渐进的，那么从最初的语言觉醒到斯瓦希里语、日语或芬兰语的复杂性可能需要数万年的时间。

An early group of people developed a very rudimentary type of language, with just a few words and maybe only one grammatical device juxtaposing two words, an intransitive predicate and its argument (as when a young child's sentences are all of the form mammy paint, or baby heavy). A few more words and a little more grammatical complexity would be added every few hundred or few thousand years until a language with the complexity typical of modern language was eventually achieved. Under this view we would first get a rudimentary language (a few dozen words), then a primitive language (a few hundred words), then the post-primitive stage, followed by pre-modern and finally modern (many thousands of words and a grammar whose structures and rules need several hundred pages to describe in a reasonably full manner). If language development were gradual it could take tens of thousands of years to progress from the first linguistic awakening to the complexity of Swahili or Japanese or Finnish.

（二） 突然发展

在进化的某个阶段，人们能够相当清晰地思考，尽管他们还没有发展出语言。他们有一套完善的心理概念，能够将事物分为不同类别等。然后语言发展起来。有些词可能是拟声词，比如鸟的名字可能基于它的叫声，“劈开”这个动词可能基于木头劈开的声音。48会有一些声音符号基础，49 oo 倾向于与大而圆的东西相关，ee 倾向于与小而薄的东西相关。1 50

At a certain stage of evolution people were able to think fairly clearly, although they had not yet developed a language. They had a well-developed set of mental concepts and could categorise things into classes, etc. Then language developed. Some words would have been onomatopoeic the name for a bird could be based on its call, the verb for 'split' could be based on the sound of wood being split.48 There would have been some sound-symbolic basis,49 oo tending to relate to things that are large and round and ee to those that are small and thin.150

语言会迸发出来。一旦某些物体有了名字，人们需要指称的每种事物、动作、状态和品质都会产生名字；151再加上一整套将这些词语结合在一起的语法结构；再加上代词（“我”和“你”）、指示词（“这”、“这里”）和时间词（“明天”、“今天”）等转换词。语言一旦发展起来，它当然会协助思考和概念形成的过程，语言和思想两者相互滋养，齐头并进。

Language would have burst forth. Once there were names for some objects, names evolved for every type of thing and action and state and quality to which people needed to refer;151 plus a full set of grammatical constructions to bind these words together; plus shifters such as pronouns ('I' and 'you'), deictics ('this', 'here') and time words ('tomorrow', 'today'). Once language developed, it would of course assist the process of thinking and concept formation, the two language and thought feeding each other and developing in tandem.

我更倾向于第二种选择，即突然发展，因为这更符合我们所知道的语言变化和分裂的方式（一旦有了语言）。当然，这是一个永远无法无可辩驳地证明的假设（就像任何关于宇宙起源的假设都无法无可辩驳地证明一样）。但它确实解释了许多事情。例如，事实上，目前世界上使用的所有语言的复杂程度大致相同。没有任何东西可以被称为“原始语言”（只有几百个单词和很少的语法）。当一种皮钦语（两个语言群体共享的初级第二语言）在短短几代内发展成为一种克里奥尔语（一个群体的第一语言）时，它就变成了一种语言系统，其复杂程度在词汇量和语法资源丰富性方面可与任何成熟的语言相媲美。

I prefer the second alternative, of sudden development, as being more in keeping with the way we know languages change and split (once there is a language in the first place). This is, of course, a hypothesis that can never be incontrovertibly proved (any more than any of the hypotheses about the origin of the universe can be incontrovertibly proved). But it does explain a number of things. For instance, it is a fact that all the languages presently spoken in the world are about equal in complexity. There is nothing that could be called a 'primitive language' (with just a few hundred words and only a little grammar). When a pidgin (the rudimentary second language shared by two linguistic groups) develops into a creole (the first language of a group) within just a couple of generations it becomes a linguistic system comparable in complexity to any well-established language in terms of size of vocabulary and richness of grammatical resources.

当今世界（或有记载的历史）没有“原始语言”的原因可能是，实际上从未有过任何语言。语言最初发展时，就像一场爆炸。当然，一代人不可能掌握 5,000 个单词，但我认为每一代人都会从父母那里学到相当多的词汇。人类的大脑在心理上已经为语言做好了准备，然后它就会发明语言，几乎是一个完整的系统。

It may be that the reason there are no 'primitive languages' in the world today (or in recorded history) is that there never really were any. When language first developed, it was like an explosion. One would not of course have got to 5,000 words in one generation but I am suggesting that each generation would have added appreciably to the vocabulary they learnt from their parents. The human mind would have been mentally ready for language, and then it would have invented it, almost as a complete system.

还有其他证据支持这一观点。首先，我们应该指出，现代人类社会之间，即使经济基础不同，社会交往也没有什么本质区别。纽约、撒哈拉沙漠或澳大利亚沙漠、非洲、新几内亚或亚马逊丛林中的相邻族群，都倾向于与邻居进行类似的交往，通婚有限，等等。所有这些情况都涉及复杂的语言，每种语言都包含数千个单词和微妙的语法结构，并且语言的限制对于成人学习者来说很难完全掌握。假设存在原始语言，每种语言只有几百个单词和最低限度的语法。这些语言很容易学习。每个人都能说其他人的语言。除非对语言使用有特殊的社会限制，否则语言会趋于融合，族群也会随之融合。这里要指出的是，我们熟悉的那种社会交往需要非原始语言。这与从未存在过原始语言的想法一致，除非它是一种局部和短暂的现象。

There are further lines of support for this idea. We should first point out that there is no essential difference in social interaction between modern human societies that have varying economic bases. Contiguous ethnic groups in New York, or in the Saharan or Australian desert, or in the African or New Guinean or Amazonian jungle, all tend to have similar kinds of interaction with their neighbours, limited intermarriage, and so on. All of these situations involve complex languages each consisting of thousands of words and subtle grammatical structures and constraints languages which are difficult for an adult learner to achieve a full mastery of. Suppose there were primitive languages, each with just a couple of hundred words and minimal grammar. These would be easy to learn. Everyone would be able to speak everyone else's language. Unless there were exceptional social constraints on language use, the languages would tend to merge together, and with them the ethnic groups. The point being made is that the kind of social interaction we are familiar with demands non-primitive languages. This is consistent with the idea that there never have been such things as primitive languages, except as a local and transitory phenomenon.

我不发表意见的问题是语言是只发展了一次（单源论）还是分别在两个或多个地方发展（多源论）。这两种情况似乎都是完全有可能的。可能有两个或多个早期人类群体，处于大约相同的智力发展阶段，他们生活在不同的地方，并开始彼此独立地使用语言。或者它可能只发生过一次。

The question about which I offer no opinion is whether language developed just once (monogenesis) or separately in two or more places (polygenesis). Either of these seems to be perfectly possible. There could have been two or more groups of early humans, at about the same stage of mental development, who were living in different places and began to use language independently of each other. Or it could have happened just once.

 

 

6 间断平衡模型

6 The Punctuated Equilibrium Model

这里提出的假设是为了描述和解释语言自诞生以来十多万年的发展，即存在着长期的平衡时期，在此期间，许多语言在特定区域内或多或少和谐地共存，没有发生任何重大变化。有时，平衡状态会被一些灾难性事件打断；这将导致语言状况发生彻底变化，并可能引发多次“分裂和扩张”（这可以用家谱图适当地模拟）。中断可能是由于某些自然事件（洪水、干旱、火山爆发），或是由于激进的政治或宗教团体的出现，或是由于某些惊人的技术创新，或者仅仅是由于进入新的原始领域。在导致中断的事件结束后，将出现新的平衡状态。

The hypothesis put forward here to describe and explain the development of language during the 100,000 or more years since its first emergence is that there have been long periods of equilibrium during which a number of languages have coexisted in a more or less harmonious way within a given region without any major changes taking place. From time to time the state of equilibrium is punctuated by some cataclysmic event; this will engender sweeping changes in the linguistic situation and may trigger a multiple 'split and expansion' (which would be appropriately modelled by a family tree diagram). The punctuation may be due to some natural event (floods, drought, volcanic eruption), or to the emergence of an aggressive political or religious group, or to some striking technical innovation, or simply to entry into new and pristine territory. After the events which caused the punctuation have run their course, a new state of equilibrium will come into being.

我认为，在人类语言的历史上，与平衡期相比，标点符号的出现时间相对较短。上一次大规模的标点符号出现始于 15 世纪，当时欧洲殖民了世界上几乎所有其他地方，现在仍处于中期；这已经导致或正在导致绝大多数语言的灭绝。

I suggest that, over the history of human language, periods of punctuation have been relatively short in duration, by comparison with periods of equilibrium. The last major punctuation began in the fifteenth century, with European colonisation of almost all the rest of the world, and is still in mid-stream; this has led, or is leading, to the extinction of the great majority of languages.

欧洲科学家之所以能够观察到标点符号的时间，是因为无论欧洲人（带着他们的武器、宗教和文字）走到哪里，他们都会给现有的平衡状态带来标点符号。从事件的本质来看，语言学家不可能观察到平衡状态，因为这种观察必然会打断平衡状态。但是，持续平衡期的假设对于解释语言的发展方式以及解释当今世界许多地方的语言状况是必要的。澳大利亚很可能拥有最长的平衡期，没有任何严重的标点符号。在这种情况下，平衡状态可以很容易地重建；事实上，正如我将在下文中展示的那样（参见 Dixon，即将出版），它是唯一能够解释澳大利亚语言之间关系的模型。

European scientists have only ever been able to observe a time of punctuation since, wherever Europeans go (with their weapons and religions and writing), they effect a punctuation in the existing state of equilibrium. It is, in the nature of events, impossible for a linguist to observe a state of equilibrium since that very observation is bound to interrupt it. But the hypothesis of sustained periods of equilibrium is necessary to explain how language has developed, and to explain the present-day linguistic situations in many parts of the world. It is likely that Australia has had the longest period of equilibrium, without any serious punctuation. In this instance, the equilibrium state can be readily reconstructed; indeed as I shall demonstrate below (and see Dixon, forthcoming) it is the only model able to explain the relationships between languages in Australia.

第 6.1 节讨论了均衡情况，第 6.2 节讨论了标点符号的类型。第 6.3 节考虑了许多特定的地理情况。

§6.1 discusses the equilibrium situation and §6.2 deals with types of punctuation. Then, in §6.3, a number of particular geographical situations are considered.

 

 

6.1 语言平衡

6.1 Linguistic Equilibrium

随着标点符号时代的结束，特定地区的语言将逐渐稳定下来，形成一种平衡模式。使用这些语言的社会可能具有以下特点：52

As a period of punctuation draws to a close, the languages in a given area will gradually settle down into an equilibrium pattern. The societies that speak them are likely to be characterised by the following features:52

(a) 将会存在若干个政治团体，每个团体通过以下方式表明自己的身份（对自己和其他团体而言）：（i）自己独特的方言或语言；（ii）团体和/或方言/语言的名称；53（iii）自己的一套传统、信仰和法律；（iv）自己的亲属关系制度、婚姻法等等。

(a) There will be a number of political groups, identifying as such (to themselves, and to other groups) through each having: (i) its own distinctive dialect or language; (ii) a group and/or dialect/language name;53 (iii) its own set of traditions, beliefs and laws; (iv) its own kinship system, marriage laws, and so on.

（b）每个政治团体的人口都应与该地区其他团体的人口相当。也就是说，一个团体的人口可能是另一个团体的四倍，但不会是另一个团体的一百倍。（整个地区的总人口在整个均衡时期将保持大致不变。）

(b) Each political group would have a population comparable to those of other groups in the area. That is, one group could be, say, four times as big as another, but not a hundred times as big. (The overall population of the complete area will remain approximately constant during the whole period of equilibrium.)

(c) 所有群体在生活方式和信仰方面大致相似。也就是说，他们拥有的工具和武器、他们建造的庇护所类型以及他们可用的食物资源的复杂程度都相当。他们拥有类似类型的（非攻击性）宗教信仰。

(c) All groups would be roughly similar in terms of life-style and beliefs. That is, they would have a comparable level of sophistication in the tools and weapons they possess, the sorts of shelters they build, and the food resources they have available. They would have comparable types of (non-aggressive) religious beliefs.

(d) 在任何相当大的区域，没有哪个群体的威望会比其他群体高得多。一个群体可能在短时间内享有较小的威望（也许是因为他们创新了一些歌曲或仪式），但这种威望可能很快就会转移到另一个群体身上。一个群体享有的威望不会维持足够长的时间，不足以广泛传播，也不足以让该群体建立起对邻国的统治力量。

(d) No group would have substantially greater prestige than others, over any significantly large portion of the area. There could be minor prestige associated with one group for a short period (perhaps due to some song or ceremony they had innovated) but this might soon shift to another group. The prestige accorded one group would not be maintained long enough for it to spread widely, or for that group to establish a power of dominance over its neighbours.

(e) 与此相关，没有一种语言（或一种语言的方言）能够拥有长时间的盛誉。

(e) Associated with this, no one language (or dialect of a language) would have any extended period of prestige.

我并不是说，在平衡时期，特定地区的政治和语言状况将保持完全静止。总是会发生变化，永远有起有落。在平衡时期的开始，特定地区可能有五十种语言。几千年或几万年后，那里可能仍有大约五十种语言。但它们不会被识别为相同的语言。如前所述，语言总是在变化，尽管变化的速度可能有所不同。有些语言会停止使用（它们可能作为另一种语言的底层而存在），而语言分裂的情况也不少。我要指出的是，平衡时期的变化相对较小，与标点时期的变化顺序完全不同，标点时期可能会有大量语言在短时间内停止使用，其他语言可能会多次分裂和扩展。

I am not suggesting that, during a period of equilibrium, the political and linguistic situation in a given area would remain entirely static. There would always be changes taking place a perpetual ebb and flow. At the beginning of an equilibrium period there might be, say, fifty languages spoken in a given area. Some thousands or some tens of thousands of years later there might still be about fifty languages there. But they would not be recognisable as the same languages. As noted before, a language is always changing, although the rate at which it changes can vary. And there will have been some languages that ceased to be spoken (they might survive as a substratum within another language), while there would have been some modest instances of language split. The point being made is that changes during a period of equilibrium would be relatively minor, and of a quite different order from the changes during a period of punctuation, when large numbers of languages may cease to be spoken within a short time-span, and there can be multiple split and expansion of other languages.

在平衡时期，各种文化特征都会在给定区域内传播。特别是，语言特性会传播（如第 3 节所述；参见 Schmidt 1872）。这样，一个地区使用的语言在很长一段时间内会变得越来越相似。语法类别会传播，这些类别通常会分布在相当大的区域。词素会被借用，给定的形式可能会在更有限的区域内的许多语言中找到。在 §3.1 中，我们注意到萨丕尔的估计，语法形式的借用非常缓慢，在可以考察的相对较短的语言历史时期内几乎不会被注意到。然而，我们在这里假设的时间跨度足够长，足以让语法词缀、代词等被大量借用。54

During a period of equilibrium all sorts of cultural traits will diffuse within a given area. In particular, there will be diffusion of linguistic properties (as described in §3; and see Schmidt 1872). In this way the languages spoken in an area will, over a very long period, become more and more similar. Grammatical categories will diffuse and these typically spread over a considerable region. Lexemes will be borrowed and a given form may be found in a number of languages over a more restricted region. In §3.1 we noted Sapir's estimation that the borrowing of grammatical forms is so slow as to be hardly noticeable in the relatively small period of linguistic history that is open to inspection. However, we are here positing long time-spans long enough for there to have been significant borrowing of grammatical affixes, pronouns, and the like.54

在标点符号时期，一种特定的语言（其使用者具有特定的物质或意识形态优势，以及因此带来的声望）可能会经历多次分裂，建立一个语言家族，对于该家族来说，树形图可以适当地表示一组从共同的原始语言中分离出来的现代语言。

During a period of punctuation a given language (whose speakers have a particular material or ideological ascendancy, and the prestige that this brings) may undergo multiple splits, establishing a language family for which a tree diagram is an appropriate representation a group of modern languages that have diverged from a common proto-language.

在平衡时期，接触的语言会相互扩散特征，变得越来越相似。这些相似之处会逐渐汇聚，趋向于一个共同的原型。因此，我们可以说，语言家族是在标点符号时期（可能是几百年或几千年）迅速形成的，并在随后的漫长平衡时期（可能延续数万年）慢慢模糊。

During a period of equilibrium, languages in contact will diffuse features between each other, becoming more and more similar. These similarities will gradually converge, towards a common prototype. We can thus say that language families are rapidly made during a period of punctuation (which may be a few hundred or a few thousand years), and slowly blurred during the long period of equilibrium (which may extend for tens of millennia) that follows.

探究两种语言在很长一段时间内接触的可能性是有益的。它们有可能融合吗？我相信这个问题的答案是“不”（很快就会加上限定词）。我们对正常语言发展的所有观察都表明，一种语言永远不会有多个母体（尽管它可能有来自所谓“继母”的大量底层或上层）。没有理由相信这不适用于所有情况。

It is instructive to enquire what the possibilities are for two languages in contact over a very long period of time. Could they conceivably merge? I believe that the answer to this question is 'no' (with a qualification to be added soon). All our observation of normal linguistic development suggests that a language never has more than one parent (although it may have considerable substratum or superstratum from what could be called 'step-parents'). There is no reason to believe that this would not apply in all circumstances.

假设在平衡状态下，两种语言在潮起潮落中接触，它们共同的词汇和语法形式相当少，而语法组织却存在差异。它们的语法概况类别和结构类型将逐渐变得更加相似。共享词汇量将稳步上升，直到达到约 50% 的平衡水平（见 §3.2）。55共享语法词素的数量也将增加，但速度要慢得多。假设这两个群体现在进行政治合并（其中一个群体或两个群体的人数可能已经下降到无法生存的水平，可能是由于疾病或大屠杀）。新兴群体自然会只采用一种语言。在其语法形式和大部分词汇中，它将只与原始语言之一相符，尽管相当一部分词汇和更少的语法形式可能来自第二种语言（构成底层或上层）。可以说，新语言来自同一个祖先，它的大部分语法和词汇都来自这个祖先。

Suppose that in the ebb and flow of movement in an equilibrium situation two languages come into contact and they have rather few lexemes and grammatical forms in common, together with differences in grammatical organisation. Their grammatical profiles categories and construction types will gradually become more similar. The shared vocabulary will steadily rise until it reaches the equilibrium level of about 50% (see §3.2).55 The stock of shared grammatical morphemes will also rise, but at a much slower rate. Suppose that the two groups now effect a political merger (the numbers in one, or both, groups may have dropped to a non-viable level, perhaps through disease or a massacre). The emerging group will naturally adopt just one language. In its grammatical forms and in most of its lexicon it will be identified with just one of the original languages, although a significant minority of words and a smaller number of grammatical forms may have come from the second language (constituting a substratum or superstratum). The new language can be said to have come from a single parent, that from which it received most of its grammar and lexicon.

现在考虑一个略有不同的场景。我们有两种语言在遗传上密切相关，具有相似的语法和词素。它们分开了，并在相当长的一段时间内与不同的邻居群体接触。最终，它们又重新开始接触。假设在它们分离的几个世纪或几千年里，同源词汇的百分比显着下降到 30%。双方都会借用，这个数字会上升，直到达到约 50% 的平衡水平。然而，在分离的几年里，两种语言共享的语法形式的百分比不会下降到与假设两种语言之间大约 80% 的语法形式仍然相同的程度。
