Now consider a slightly different scenario. We have two languages that are closely genetically related, with similar grammars and lexemes. They move apart and for a considerable time have contact with different sets of neighbours. Eventually, they move back into contact. Suppose that the percentage of cognate vocabulary has dropped markedly during their centuries or millennia of separation to, say, 30%. There will be borrowing in both directions and the figure will rise, until it reaches the equilibrium level of about 50%. However, during the years of separation the percentage of grammatical forms shared by the two languages will not have dropped to anything like the same extent suppose that about 80% of grammatical forms are still the same between the languages.

如果现在讲这两种语言的政治团体合并，那么新团体的单一语言将会是什么样的？在语法层面，很难将其与真正的合并语言区分开来。两种原始语言之间 80% 或更多的语法形式是共同的，这些语法形式将融入新语言。其余的语法形式可能主要来自其中一种原始语言，但一些语法形式可能来自另一种语言。我们应该能够根据词汇来确定来源。大约 50% 的词汇来自共同的词汇，但剩余的 50% 可能主要来自一种原始语言（提供 20% 语法形式大部分的语言）。

If there were now a merger of the political groups speaking the two languages, what would the single language of the new group be like? At the grammatical level it would be hard to distinguish it from a genuine merged language 80% or more of the grammatical forms were held in common between the two original languages and these will go into the new language. The balance would be likely to come mostly from one of the original languages, but a few grammatical forms may come from the other language. It is in terms of lexicon that we should be able to assign parentage. About 50% of the lexicon comes from the common stock but the remaining 50% is likely to be taken mostly from just one original language (the language that supplied most of the balance of 20% of the grammatical forms).

澳大利亚的一些语言情况表明，这种情况可能会有另一种结局。瓦尔皮里语（西部沙漠语言）和位于澳大利亚中部的其他语言都为许多概念提供了一套同义词。在西部沙漠语言中，社区中的所有使用者都知道 waru、warlu、karla和 kunjinkarrpa 表示“火”；karli、yirrkili 和 walanu 表示“回旋镖”等（信息来自 Hansen 1984）。虽然说这种语言的每个人都熟悉这些同义词，但一个地方群体倾向于使用其中一种，而另一个群体则更喜欢另一种（部分是作为群体内身份的标志）。当某人去世并且与其名字相似的名词被禁忌时，它将被其中一个同义词取代；但原始词汇很可能会在一段相当长的时间间隔后重新使用。

There are some language situations in Australia which suggest an alternative ending to this scenario. Warlpiri, the Western Desert language, and other languages in a block right in the middle of the continent have a set of synonyms for many concepts. In the Western Desert language, all the speakers in a community will know waru, warlu,56 karla and kunjinkarrpa as words for 'fire'; and karli, yirrkili and walanu for 'boomerang', etc. (information from Hansen 1984). Although everyone speaking the language is familiar with these synonyms, one local group will tend to use one of them more than the rest, while another group will prefer another (partly as a mark of in-group identity). When someone dies and a noun similar to their name is tabooed, it will be replaced by one of the synonyms; but the original lexeme is likely to return to use after a decent interval.

这种具有多个同义词的词汇是如何演变的？一种可能性是刚刚描述的接触情况。如果两种语言有一组非常相似的语法词素和大约 50% 的共同词汇，它们很可能会合并。新语言将接管两种原始语言的所有词素，并将它们保留为同义词。在这种相当特殊的情况下，我们确实可以得到一种混合语言，有两个父母（必然是密切相关的）。它只是结合了父母双方的几乎所有形式。

How could such a lexicon, with multiple synonymy, evolve? One possibility is in the contact situation just described. If two languages have a very similar set of grammatical morphemes and about 50% vocabulary in common, they may well merge. The new language will take over all the lexemes of both original languages, retaining them as synonyms. In this rather special circumstance we could indeed get a mixed language, with two parents (necessarily closely related). It has simply combined almost all the forms from both parents.

 

 

6.2 标点符号

6.2 Punctuation

现在我们来考虑平衡期的结束。这通常与人口扩张有关，导致一个政治集团分裂成几个新的政治集团，语言也随之分裂，因此每个政治集团都会有一种语言。在结束期间，新语言将以稳定的速度发展。随着结束期的结束，可以用家谱图来建模。随着新的平衡期的到来，由于语言特征在整个平衡期内的扩散，家谱图的原始遗传关系将逐渐变得模糊。

We now consider the punctuation of an equilibrium period. This is often associated with population expansion, leading to the fragmentation of one political group into several new ones and a corresponding splitting of languages, so that there will be one for each political group. During a period of punctuation new languages will develop at a steady rate. As the period of punctuation comes to an end, it can be modelled by a family tree diagram. As a new period of equilibrium sets in, the original genetic relationships of the family tree diagram will become progressively blurred, due to the diffusion of linguistic features throughout the equilibrium period.

与语言相关的第一个转折点就是语言本身的出现。我假设，一群早期人类曾生活在平衡状态中一段时间​​。不用去推测他们如何或为何会进化出语言，很明显，这种进化会对他们生活的平衡产生巨大的影响。我在 §5.3 中提出，语言可能从无到有发展得相当迅速，发展成一个在丰富性和复杂性上可与现代语言相媲美的系统。（当然没有那么复杂，但可能只有现代语言的一半；肯定没有现代语言的百分之一复杂。）

The first punctuation associated with language would have been the emergence of language itself. I hypothesise that a group of early humans had been living for some time in a state of equilibrium. Without trying to speculate on how or why they came to evolve language, it is clear that this evolution would have produced a drastic punctuation to the equilibrium in which they lived. I suggested in §5.3 that language probably developed rather rapidly from nothing to a system comparable in richness and complexity to modern-day languages. (Not quite as complex, certainly, but perhaps half as complex; certainly not one-hundredth as complex.)

语言的进化将为早期人类的生活增添新的维度。他们将更有能力在生活的各个方面进行合作，并规划联合活动。标点符号很可能不仅仅涉及语言的进化。标点符号可能是更复杂的生活方式、更好的食物采集和准备的触发因素，从而导致人口增加和向新领土的扩张。随着社会群体在习惯和栖息地上的分歧，第一批讲语言的人可能会迅速分裂成两个。然后他们可能会再次分裂。语言的进化很可能只是标点符号时期的开始，而标点符号时期导致了人群的扩张和语言的分裂，从而产生了第一个语系。

The evolution of language would have added new dimensions to the life of these early humans. They would have been more equipped to cooperate together in all aspects of life, and to plan joint activities. It is likely that the punctuation would not have just involved the evolution of language. This could have been the trigger for the development of a more sophisticated life-style, better food gathering and preparation, leading to population increase and expansion into new territories. The first language-speaking people could have rapidly split into two, as social groups diverged in habits and habitat. And then these might have split again. It is likely that the evolution of language was just the beginning of a period of punctuation that led to the expansion of peoples and split of languages, creating the first language family.

一旦某个地理区域有了使用语言的人，就会进入一段巩固期，进入平衡期。有时还会有进一步的中断，尽管在长期平衡期之间，这种情况相当罕见。57

Once a certain geographical area was populated, with language-using people, a period of consolidation would have set in an equilibrium period. From time to time there would be further punctuations, although these would be rather rare events between long periods of equilibrium.57

语言平衡状态的出现可能是出于语言或非语言原因。首先，从语言触发因素的可能性来看，一种语言可能已经（从其内部，就像一种突变）进化出一些新型的语法类别或从句结构，使其在某些交流目的上更有效。这些可能赋予了它特殊的威望或主导地位。或者一种语言可能与另一种结构截然不同的语言接触，并借用了某些语法特征，这些特征加上其先前的语法库，再次赋予了它交流优势，58导致特殊的威望和/或主导地位。在这两种情况下，装备更好的语言可能会分裂和扩张，使其他语言走向灭绝。这些是应该考虑和研究的话题；但就我们目前的知识水平而言，它们只是推测。

The punctuation of a state of linguistic equilibrium could come about for non-linguistic or linguistic reasons. Looking first at the possibility of a linguistic trigger, one language could have evolved (from within itself, like a sort of mutation) some novel types of grammatical category or clausal construction that made it more effective for certain communicative purposes. These might have endowed it with special prestige or dominance. Or one language could have come into contact with another which had a markedly different structure, and borrowed certain grammatical features which added to its previous grammatical inventory again gave it a communicative advantage,58 leading to special prestige and/or dominance. In either of these cases the better-equipped language could split and expand, pushing other languages into extinction. These are topics that should be considered and investigated; but in our present state of knowledge they are simply speculations.

大多数标点符号的例子可能都源于非语言因素。59这里有两个主要参数需要考虑：（1）是否由于（a）自然原因，或（b）物质创新，或（c）民族侵略倾向的发展（在这种情形下，写作的发展起着重要的伴随作用）；（2）地理参数，要么是（a）扩展到无人居住的领土，要么是（b）标点符号局限于一个地理区域，要么是（c）扩展到以前占领的领土。现在将逐一讨论这些问题。

It is likely that most examples of punctuation stem from non-linguistic factors.59 There are here two major parameters to consider: (1) whether due to (a) natural causes, or (b) material innovations, or (c) development of aggressive tendencies in a people (the development of writing plays a major concomitant role in this type of scenario); and (2) geographical parameters, either (a) expansion into uninhabited territory, or (b) punctuation confined within a geographical area, or (c) expansion into previously occupied territory. These will now be discussed, one at a time.

（1 ） 原因

(1) Causes

人类生活和语言的平衡状态的中断有三类主要非语言原因。

There are three major types of non-linguistic cause for the punctuation of an equilibrium state of human living and language.

（1a） 自然原因

(1a) Natural Causes

第一类自然原因与环境有关：干旱、洪水、海平面变化和火山爆发。火山、干旱或洪水可能会彻底改变一个居住区，使其不再适合居住。人口规模可能会减少，一些政治团体会消失，而另一些会合并。生活条件可能会急剧恶化，以至于某个地区的部分（或全部）人可能会决定搬迁（越过水域、山脉或沙漠）以寻找更好的居住地。

The first type of natural cause concerns the environment drought, floods, changing sea-levels, and volcanic eruptions. Volcanoes, drought or floods may radically change a living area, making it less habitable. Population size may reduce, with some political groups disappearing and others merging. Living conditions could deteriorate so radically that some (or all) of the people in a certain area may decide to move (across water or over mountains or desert) to seek a better place to live.

重大变化可能是海平面下降或上升，从而形成通向以前无法到达的地方的陆桥，或者大大减少生存空间，甚至可能将一个连续的区域切割成两个或多个独立的区域。60

A major change would have been a fall or rise in sea-levels establishing land bridges to previously inaccessible places, or else drastically reducing living space and perhaps cutting what was one continuous area into two or more separate regions.60

另一种自然原因可能是疾病。如果某种新病毒进入一个地区，而人们对这种病毒几乎没有免疫力，那么它可能会导致人口急剧下降。（如果这种情况同时发生，可能是由于入侵，那么耗尽的残余人口将无法进行抵抗，而他们本来可以做到的抵抗力将大大减弱。）

A different type of natural cause would be disease. If some new virus were introduced into an area, something to which the people had little immunity, it could cause a drastic drop in population. (And if this happened at the same time as perhaps by reason of an invasion, the depleted remnant would be able to put up much less of a fight than they might otherwise have done.)

基因突变也有可能。各种突变都有可能发生；其中一种突变可能会在食物获取或其他生活方面带来额外优势。因此，这种突变所培育的种群可能会开始走上统治和扩张的道路。

There is also the possibility of genetic mutation. All sorts of mutations are possible; there could be one that would add some extra advantage in food-getting, or in some other aspect of living. The population in which it developed could, as a result, start on a course of dominance and expansion.

（1b） 材料创新

(1b) Material Innovations

新的工具和武器将使拥有它们的人在人生游戏中获得显著优势。新的工具可能遍布各地：用于研磨的杵和臼、筛子、磨碎器、用于烹饪和储存的各种陶器、吹管、弓箭、斧头、回旋镖。另一种情况是，一群人获得了强大的武器，将用它来进一步实现他们的帝国主义野心。枪支就是最好的例子。在有枪的人群和没有枪的人群之间的每一场冲突中，前者最终都会获胜。在每种情况下，持枪者的语言都会蓬勃发展，而无枪者的语言则会逐渐但不可避免地走向灭绝。

New tools and weapons will give the people who possess them a significant advantage in the game of life. The new implements may just spread across an area pestle and mortar for grinding, sieves, graters, all sorts of pottery for cooking and storage, blow guns, bows and arrows, axes, boomerangs. An alternative scenario is that a group who get a powerful weapon will use it to further their imperialistic ambitions. Guns provide the prime example. In every conflict between a group of people with guns and one without, the first group has eventually won. And in every case the language of the gun-toters flourishes while those of the gunless people sink away gradually but inevitably towards extinction.

交通工具是另一项重要创新。陆路交通工具如马车和驮畜。但比这更重要的是水路交通工具。这包括用于在内陆河流上旅行的独木舟和木筏，以及远洋船只。这些首先为捕鱼提供了巨大的帮助，可以大大增加食物供应。它们还可以促进探索和移民到新的土地。

Means of transportation is another important innovation. Land transport such as carts and beasts of burden. But, more important than this, water transport. This includes canoes and rafts for travel on inland rivers, and also sea-going craft. These first of all provide great assistance for fishing, and can significantly increase the food supply. And they can also facilitate exploration and immigration into new lands.

也许最重要的物质创新是农业的发明。有人猜测，为什么一群人在经过数万年的觅食之后，会想到清理花园、种植庄稼和除草。这可能发生在土壤、气候条件和可用植物特别有利的时间和地点。据说农业在几个不同的地方独立发展（近东、华南、中美洲、南美洲高地和新几内亚高地）。贝尔伍德（1996）认为，这种创新可能在几个例子中引发了大规模的中断，导致农业民族及其语言的分裂和扩张。动物的驯化（狗除外）经常发生在农业发展之后，并起到强化作用（帮助种植和运输，并增加肉类供应）。

Perhaps the most important material innovation was the invention of agriculture. There is speculation about the reasons why a group of people would after tens of millennia of just foraging get the idea of clearing gardens, planting crops and weeding them. It would have happened at times and places where the soil, climatic conditions and available plants were especially favourable. Agriculture is said to have developed independently in several different places (the Near East, South China, Central America, highland South America and highland New Guinea). Bellwood (1996) has suggested that this innovation may in several instances have been the trigger for a large-scale punctuation, with split and expansion of the agricultural people and their languages. The domestication of animals (with the exception of the dog), where it occurred, often followed the development of agriculture and served as a reinforcement (assisting in planting and cartage, and adding to the meat supply).

（1c） 攻击性倾向的发展

(1c) Development of Aggressive Tendencies

平衡时期的必要条件是，一些群体相对和谐地生活在一起，各自或多或少地尊重邻居及其思想和宗教，不试图把自己或自己的宗教强加于他人。61政治团体的规模应该相当小（从几百人到几千人不等），组织也相当混乱。我们可以想象它们很像 1788 年白人入侵之前的澳大利亚部落；或者像今天在亚马逊丛林中幸存的一些部落。没有酋长，只有一些长老。村庄团体或亲属团体应该做什么的决定将通过协商一致的方式达成，由团体中的一些资深成员指导讨论。

The necessary scenario for a period of equilibrium is a number of groups living in relative harmony with one another, each more or less respecting their neighbours and their neighbours' ideas and religion, and not trying to foist either themselves or their religion on others.61 The political groups would have been fairly small in size (ranging from a few hundred to a few thousand) and fairly anarchic in organisation. We can imagine them as being rather like Australian tribes before the white invasion in 1788; or being like some tribes that survive today in the Amazon jungle. There would be no chief, just a number of elders. Decisions on what a village group or a kinship group should do would be reached by consensus, with some senior members of the group guiding the discussion.

如果出现等级制度，这种平衡很可能会遭到破坏。一个具有足够魅力和口才的地方首领可能会渴望获得更具包容性的权力。越来越多的地区和越来越多的人逐渐落入他的指挥之下。然后组建军队，发动远征征服其他民族。其目的是增加原有部落或国家的权力和财富，特别是其领导人的权力和财富。（我想到的是成吉思汗、匈奴王阿提拉、亚历山大大帝，当然还有希特勒和斯大林。）

This equilibrium is likely to be broken if a hierarchy emerges. A local chief endowed with sufficient charisma and rhetoric may aspire to more inclusive power. A greater and greater area, and a greater number of people, steadily fall under his command. Then an army is raised, expeditions made to conquer other peoples. The purpose is to add to the power and wealth of the original tribe or nation, and particularly of its leader. (I have in mind people like Genghis Khan, Attila the Hun, Alexander the Great and, of course, Hitler and Stalin.)

或者一种新的宗教可能出现。“神”将向他的大祭司传达一个信息，大祭司也将具有超凡的魅力和雄辩的口才，即必须向所有人民传达这个令人喜悦的信息（即使他们不想要）。它可能通过剑来传播（就像在穆斯林扩张的最初几个世纪中发生的那样），或者更微妙地传播，就像过去几个世纪中许多基督教派别的传教士渗透到各大洲的部落社会时发生的那样。当然，并非所有宗教都是侵略性的（澳大利亚、大洋洲、非洲的土著人民和大多数美洲人的宗教都不侵略性），但那些具有侵略性的宗教不容任何挑战。“我们有我们希望与所有人分享的信息，不，我们坚持要分享它。” 62

Or a new religion may evolve. The 'deity' will convey a message to his high priest who will also be endowed with charisma and rhetoric that all peoples must be given the joyous message (even if they don't want it). It may be spread by the sword (as happened during the first centuries of the Moslem expansion) or more subtlely, as has happened when over the past few centuries a swath of missionaries from many Christian sects has infiltrated the tribal societies of every continent. Of course not all religions are aggressive (those that were practised by the indigenous people of Australia, Oceania, Africa, and most of those in the Americas were not) but those that are brook no challenge. 'We have the message which we wish to share with all peoples nay, we insist on sharing it.'62

如果一个群体通过新武器、新工具或新农业等创新，或通过成为一个国家的统治精英或一个宗教的祭司阶层，或仅仅通过数量优势而获得特殊的重要性，那么他们的语言就会成为该地区的威望语言。

If one group gains particular importance through innovations such as new weapons or tools or agriculture, or through being the ruling elite of a nation or the priestly class of a religion, or just through weight of numbers then its language will become the prestige language of that area.

当一个地区同时存在一种声望极高的语言和多种非声望极低的语言时，通常就会出现单向的双语现象。许多非声望极高的语言使用者会掌握一些声望极高的语言（他们需要这样做，比如贸易和教育），但声望极高的语言使用者不太可能学习很多非声望极高的语言。63 仅举一个例子，在今天的津巴布韦，声望极高的语言是绍纳语（超过四分之三的人口使用这种语言）；其次是恩德贝莱语。几乎所有恩德贝莱语使用者都懂一些绍纳语，但很少有绍纳语使用者学习过恩德贝莱语。这种选择性的双语现象进一步向下延伸。在恩德贝莱地区，有一片卡兰加语飞地，这种语言使用者较少，声望也较低。大多数卡兰加语使用者都能说恩德贝莱语（当然，也包括绍纳语），但相对较少的恩德贝莱语使用者能听懂或使用卡兰加语。这种情况在世界其他地方都有。印度尼西亚的少数民族语言使用者会懂一些印尼语（他们在学校学习，在收音机里听到），但母语为印尼语的人中很少有人学过当地语言。北美、南美、非洲、印度和澳大利亚的情况也类似。

When one has the situation of a prestige language and a number of non-prestige languages in a given area, there is typically one-way bilingualism. Many speakers of the non-prestige languages will acquire some competence in the prestige language (they will need to do this, for things like trade and education) but speakers of the prestige language are unlikely to learn much of the non-prestige languages.63 To take just one example, in Zimbabwe today the prestige language is Shona (spoken by more than three-quarters of the population); next in importance is Ndebele. Almost all speakers of Ndebele know some Shona but few Shona have learnt Ndebele. And this selective bilingualism extends further down. Within Ndebele territory there is an enclave of Kalanga, a language with fewer speakers and lesser prestige. Most speakers of Kalanga have competence in Ndebele (and also, of course, in Shona), but relatively few Ndebele speakers can understand or use Kalanga. Such situations are found in every other part of the world. Speakers of minority languages in Indonesia will know some Bahasa Indonesian (they are taught it in schools, hear it on the radio) but very few people whose first language is Bahasa Indonesian will have learnt a local language. And similarly in North America, South America, Africa, India and Australia.

有时我们发现，非主流语言的使用者（他们也必然了解一些主流语言）会故意只用主流语言和他们的孩子说话，以帮助他们脱离非主流社会群体并获得更好的生活方式。这是非主流语言失去使用者并消亡的方式之一。

Sometimes we find that speakers of a non-prestige language (who also, necessarily, know something of the prestige language) will purposely speak to their children only in the prestige language, in order to assist them to move out of their non-prestige social group and get a better life-style. This is one of the ways in which a non-prestige language loses its speakers and dies.

还有另外一个特点，虽然它不是标点符号的确切原因，但却是一个强有力的伴随因素。

There is another feature which while not precisely a cause of punctuation is a strong concomitant factor.

（1d） 写作和其他形式的交流

(1d) Writing and Other Forms of Communication

毫无疑问，书写是人类最重要的创新之一，它以两种完全不同的方式发挥着重要作用。第一种方式通常有益于使任何类型的信息或任何文学作品都可以被大量用户获取，并帮助人们进行远距离通信，规划复杂的行动，例如会议、商业活动和战争。第二种方式有选择性地有益于绝大多数书面文件都是用一个国家的权威语言编写的。64

Writing is without doubt one of the most important innovations of humankind important in two entirely different ways. The first is generally beneficial enabling any type of information, or any literary work, to be available to a huge range of users, and assisting people in communicating over a distance, planning complex manoeuvres such as conferences, commercial enterprises and wars. The second is selectively beneficial the great majority of written documents are produced in the prestige language of a nation.64

非顶级语言的使用者被顶级语言的教科书、报刊和小说所淹没，这是这些语言被其使用者抛弃的一个积极因素。

Speakers of non-prestige languages are swamped by school texts, newspapers and novels in the prestige language; this is an active factor in these languages being discarded by their speakers.

我曾提出，在人类历史的大部分时间里，人们生活在自给自足的政治团体中，没有任何领导层级，每个小社区都与邻居保持着一定程度的和谐。这些群体没有文字。文字之所以没有在平衡时期发展，仅仅是因为当时并不需要它。

I have suggested that during most of the history of mankind people lived in self-contained political groups, without any hierarchy of leadership small communities each maintaining a degree of harmony with its neighbours. These groups did not have writing. Writing was not developed during periods of equilibrium simply because it was not needed.

只有当大国兴起，有了国王、领主、军队和有组织的军事行动；当有组织的宗教发展起来，有了神圣的经文、固定的祈祷词等；当广泛的贸易渠道发展起来时，文字才变得有用和受欢迎。赫梯语、苏美尔语和埃及语中最早的书面记录往往是产品、商品、职业等的清单。不久之后，就有了国王功绩的记录（Nissen、Damerow 和 Englund 1993）。

It was only when larger states evolved, with kings and lords and armies and organised martial campaigns; and when organised religion developed with sacred texts, set prayers and the like; and when extensive trade channels were developed it was only then that writing became useful and desirable. The earliest written records in Hittite and Sumerian and Egyptian tend to be lists of produce, commodities, occupations, etc. Soon after came a record of the exploits of the king (Nissen, Damerow and Englund 1993).

请注意，文学和写作之间没有必然联系。所有社会都有（或曾经有过）丰富的口头叙事、诗歌和歌曲。社会的每个成员都熟悉这些作品，它们通过口口相传代代相传。荷马史诗、古印度吠陀经和旧约全书都是通过口头保存了几个世纪，直到写作出现，它们才被记录在纸上。没有书写的人记忆力发达，头脑中储存着大量的技能和文学知识。一旦他们掌握了读写能力，记忆就不再被重视或完全保持。新的态度是：“一切都在书中，我们随时可以查阅”。正如柏拉图警告的那样：“这种（文字的）创新将使那些学习使用它的人的头脑变得健忘，因为他们不会锻炼记忆力”（《斐德罗篇》1275，借苏格拉底之口说的）。65

Note that there is no necessary connection between literature and writing. All societies have (or had) rich repertoires of oral narrative, poetry and song. Each member of the community would be familiar with such work, which was handed down by word of mouth through the generations. Homer's epic poems, the Vedas of Ancient India and the books of the Old Testament were all preserved orally for several centuries before, with the advent of writing, they were committed to paper. People without writing have a well-developed memory and store in their mind enormous knowledge of skills and literature. Once they acquire literacy, memory is no longer valued or fully maintained. The new attitude is: 'it's all in a book, we can always look it up'. As Plato warned: 'this innovation [of letters] will produce forgetfulness in the mind of those who learn to use it, because they will not exercise their memory' (Phaedrus 1275, put into the mouth of Socrates).65

文字与大型、组织良好的政治和宗教团体有关；它是管理和维护这些团体的重要组成部分。也就是说，它是与平衡状态中各种侵略类型相关的一个不可或缺的因素。近几个世纪以来，随着一个主导文明席卷一个新地区，当地居民接触到了英语、西班牙语、葡萄牙语等书面材料。66他们可能会被教导阅读和书写自己的语言，但所有这样做的人也将能够阅读和书写入侵者的语言。而且，以这种威望语言提供的书面材料将比以当地语言提供的多很多倍。

Writing is associated with large, well-organised political and religious groups; it is a vital component in regulating and maintaining these groups. That is, it is an integral factor associated with the types of aggression that punctuate a state of equilibrium. During recent centuries, as a dominant civilisation has swept across a new area, the indigenous inhabitants have been exposed to written materials in English, Spanish, Portuguese, etc.66 They may be taught to read and write their own languages but all who do so will also be able to read and write the language of the invader. And there will be many times more written material available in the prestige language than in their local tongues.

随后是其他形式的交流。广播，主要使用当地语言。然后是电视。有人尝试每周用当地语言播放几个小时的广播节目。但在有电视的地方，人们更喜欢电视而不是广播。而且，用只有几万（或更少）使用者的语言制作电视节目成本太高。

Other forms of communication follow. Radio, largely in the prestige language. And then television. Some attempt may be made to put out a few hours a week of radio programs in local languages. But where TV is available people prefer this over radio. And it is too expensive to make TV programs in a language that has only a few tens of thousands (or less) of speakers.

小型地方语言被民族语言或地区语言淹没并最终消亡，而这些语言是学校教学的媒介，也是报纸、杂志、广播和电视使用的媒介，这种情况在世界各地都适用。在西伯利亚，楚科奇语在俄语的重压下正在消失；坦桑尼亚的许多地方语言在斯瓦希里语的侵蚀下逐渐衰落；等等，这些例子可以成百上千倍地增加。

The swamping and eventual extinction of small local languages by national or regional languages which are the medium for instruction in schools, and are used in papers and magazines, radio and TV applies in every part of the world. In Siberia, Chukchee is disappearing under the weight of Russian; many local languages in Tanzania are failing before the encroachment of Swahili; and so onthese examples could be multiplied a hundred-fold.

（2 ） 地理参数

(2) Geographical Parameters

我们可以再次逐一回顾这些可能性。

We can again review the possibilities, one at a time.

（2a） 向无人居住的地区扩张

(2a) Expansion into Uninhabited Territory

生活在平衡区域的一群人迁入某个全新区域的原因可能有很多。可能是由于海平面变化，陆桥刚刚开通。可能是由于多种原因之一，原来的领土变得不再适合居住。可能是他们最近获得了航海船，可以进行必要的旅行。在这些情况下，迁移行为提供了间断。或者，平衡状态可能因农业的出现而中断。既定的零人口增长原则被抛弃，人口增长，人们寻找新的领土来扩展和开展农业。

There can be a number of reasons why a group of people, living in an equilibrium area, move into some quite new area. It could be that, with changing sea-levels, a land bridge has just opened up. It could be that, for one of a number of reasons, the original territory is becoming a less attractive place in which to live. It could be that they have recently acquired sea-going craft and can make the required journey. In these instances, the act of moving provides the punctuation. Alternatively, the state of equilibrium could have been punctuated by something like the advent of agriculture. The established principle of zero population growth is abandoned, the population grows and the people seek new territory in which to expand and practise their agriculture.

在平衡状态下，人口必须保持大致稳定。但一旦开辟新领土，人口数量就会迅速增加。伯德塞尔（1957）对相关文献进行了深入研究，并提出，如果有无限的食物和土地，人口每代将大致翻一番。他计算出，人类首次抵达澳大利亚后，可能仅用了大约 2000 年的时间，整个大陆就被填满。澳大利亚的人口数量将在两千年内从一两艘船的人口增长到大约一百万；然后在数万年的平衡期内稳定在这个数字上。

In an equilibrium situation the population must remain roughly stable. But once new territory is opened up numbers will rapidly increase. Birdsell (1957) carried out a thorough study of the relevant literature and suggested that a population will roughly double each generation if unlimited food and land are available. He calculated that it might only have taken about 2,000 years after the first arrival of humans in Australia for the whole continent to be populated. The number of people in Australia would have grown from one or two boat-loads to perhaps I million within two millennia; it then stabilised at that figure during an equilibrium period of some tens of thousands of years.

随着人口的增长，政治集团也随之分裂，语言也随之分裂。在第一次占领新领土后，新语言以稳定的速度发展。等到领土被完全占领时，清晰的家谱将成为语言间关系的准确模型。随着随后的平衡期推进，这种关系将变得模糊。

With population expansion comes the split of political groups and thus of languages. Following the first occupation of a new territory we get new languages developing at a steady rate. By the time the territory is fully occupied, a well-articulated family tree will be an accurate model of the relationships between languages. This will then become blurred as the ensuing period of equilibrium advances.

§6.3 将考虑扩展到新领土的三个例子：大洋洲；澳大利亚和新几内亚；以及美洲。

§6.3 will consider three examples of expansion into new territory Oceania; Australia and New Guinea; and the Americas.

（2b） 标点符号局限于某个地理区域

(2b) Punctuation Confined within a Geographical Area

一个地理区域的平衡状态可能会被该地区内起源的某种事物所打断，而这种事物的影响也仅限于该地区。

It is possible for the state of equilibrium in a geographical area to be punctuated by something that originated within the area, and whose effects are confined to the area.

一个假定的例子是农业被引入南美洲低地。在此之前，亚马逊森林很可能完全被狩猎采集者部落所占据，他们使用属于各种语系的多种语言。农业可能由一个部落在一个地方发展起来，然后可能扩散到一些邻近的部落。这种转变引发了一系列人口扩张和语言分裂。农业人口使用属于少数语系（主要是阿拉瓦克语、加勒比语和图皮语）的语言，分布在亚马逊大部分地区（在一些地方甚至更远），取代或同化了狩猎采集者部落。如今，在农业人口之间生活着一些狩猎采集者群体的聚居地（尤其是马库人、穆拉皮拉罕人、南比克瓦拉人和瓜希博人）；他们可能是原始狩猎采集者人口的残余。

A putative example here is the introduction of agriculture into lowland South America. Before this happened it is likely that the Amazonian forests were fully inhabited by tribes of hunters and gatherers speaking a range of languages belonging to a variety of language families. Agriculture was probably developed in one place by one tribe and may then have diffused into some neighbouring tribes. This punctuation set off a series of population expansions and language splits. Agricultural people, speaking languages belonging to a small number of language families (principally Arawak, Carib and Tupí), spread over a large part of Amazonia (and, in some places, beyond), displacing or assimilating tribes of hunters and gatherers. There are today a few enclaves of huntergatherer groups living between the agriculturists (notably the Makú, Mura-Pirahã, Nambikwara and Guahibo people); they are probably remnants of the original huntergatherer population.

（2c） 向先前占领的领土扩张

(2c) Expansion into Previously Occupied Territory

某个地区的平衡状态可能会因入侵而中断。入侵者可能拥有一些物质优势（例如农业、枪支）和/或受到某种政治理想（或至高无上感）或宗教狂热的驱使。他们对原住民施加统治，他们的语言成为威望语言。如果被入侵的领土由许多小群体组成，每个群体都有自己的语言（如美洲和澳大利亚），或者入侵者的数量大大超过原住民（如新西兰），那么所有原始语言都将衰落，并最终被威望语言取代。

The state of equilibrium in a certain area may be punctuated by invasion. The invaders are likely to have some material advantage (e.g. agriculture, guns) and/or to be spurred on by some political ideal (or sense of supremacy) or religious fanaticism. They exercise dominance over the original population and their language becomes the prestige language. Where the invaded territory consists of many small groups, each with its own language (as in the Americas and Australia), or where the numbers of the invader greatly exceed those of the original inhabitants (as in New Zealand), all the original languages will decline and will in time be replaced by the prestige language.

如果被入侵的领土确实有发达的政治团体、拥有数百万使用者的语言，或许还有一种或多种高度发达的宗教（如南亚和非洲），那么本土语言的使用就不会减少。但入侵者的语言仍会成为主流语言，在入侵者被驱逐后仍将保持这一地位（尤其是在拥有多种本土语言的国家）。事实上，在印度和尼日利亚，印度英语和尼日利亚英语是通用语，用于不同语言群体之间的交流。如果这些多语言大国继续保持目前的形式（而不是分裂成较小的国家，每个主要语言群体都有一个国家），那么昔日入侵者语言的影响力和使用可能会继续逐渐增加。尤其是当英语成为世界的主要主流语言时。

Where the invaded territory does have well-developed political groups, languages with millions of speakers and perhaps also one or more highly developed religions (as in South Asia and Africa), then the indigenous languages will not decline in use. But the language of the invader still becomes the prestige language, and after the invader has been expelled will still maintain this status (especially in countries with a number of indigenous languages). Indeed, in India and Nigeria, Indian English and Nigerian English are the lingua francas, used for communication between people from different linguistic groups. If these large multi-language nations continue in their present form (rather than breaking up into smaller nations, one for each major language group), then the influence and use of the erstwhile invaders' languages is likely to continue gradually to increase. Especially when, as is the case with English, it is the major prestige language of the world.

偶尔，入侵者的语言可能会被废弃，就像诺曼法语在英格兰的情况一样；但即使在这里，它也为现代英语提供了非常重要的上层。请注意，诺曼人的数量相对较少，他们来自相似的文化，与英国人没有重大的物质或宗教差异。当时，英国只有一种主要语言，而印度有 15 种国家语言，尼日利亚有 8 种或更多的主要语言。

Very occasionally, the invaders' language may fall into disuse, as happened with Norman French in England; even here, though, it has provided a very significant superstratum within Modern English. Note that the number of Normans was relatively small, and they came from a similar culture with no major material or religious differences from the English. And there was just one major language in England at that time, as against fifteen national languages in India and eight or more major languages in Nigeria.

 

 

6.3 一些例子

6.3 Some Examples

欧洲、亚洲和非洲是相连的大陆，人类已在此生活了数十万年甚至数百万年。据推测，语言最初可能是在这些大陆之一发展起来的。

Europe, Asia and Africa are connected land masses in which humans have been living for hundreds of thousands, perhaps millions, of years. It is presumed that language would originally have developed in one of these continents.

考古学家已经能够确定人类到达世界其他地区的时间。人类向太平洋岛屿扩张的时间略少于 4,000 年前；澳大利亚/新几内亚（当时是一块陆地）的扩张时间约为 5060,000 年前；美洲的扩张时间至少为 12,000 年前（也许 20,000 年前）（普遍认为这涉及到从西伯利亚穿越白令海峡）。现在我们将依次讨论这三次扩张。

Archaeologists have been able to date the arrival of mankind in other parts of the world. A bit less than 4,000 years ago for expansion into the islands of the Pacific; about 5060,000 years for Australia/New Guinea (which was then one land mass); and at least 12,000 years (maybe 20,000 years) ago for the Americas (there is general agreement that this involved crossing from Siberia at the Bering Strait). We will now discuss these three expansions, in turn.

（一个） 南岛语族

南岛语系无疑是世界上最大的（完全合理的）语系，拥有超过 1,000 种不同的语言。学者们确认了四个一级亚群，其中三个位于台湾（每个亚群由几种语言组成），第四个亚群涉及从马达加斯加语到复活节岛的 1,000 多种语言。原始家园合理地位于台湾。人们认为，南岛人扩张的触发因素是农业的获得（Bellwood 1991, 1996）。凭借这项新技能，南岛人向西南扩散到菲律宾、婆罗洲和印度尼西亚，向东南扩散到新几内亚的沿海地区。所有这些地区都曾有人居住。

The Austronesian language family is easily the biggest (fully justified) family in the world, with over 1,000 distinct languages. Scholars recognise four first-order subgroups, three situated in Taiwan (each consisting of a handful of languages) with the fourth involving more than 1,000 languages spread from Malagasy across to Easter Island. The proto-homeland is, reasonably, placed at Taiwan. The trigger for the expansion of Austronesian people is thought to have been the acquisition of agriculture (Bellwood 1991, 1996). With this new skill the Austronesians spread south-west to the Philippines, Borneo and Indonesia, and south-east to the coastal regions of New Guinea. All of these areas are known to have been previously inhabited.

距今 3,500 年前不久，南岛人从俾斯麦群岛（新几内亚东北部）出发，占领了整个太平洋，并带走了农作物和猪。据信，在南岛人到达之前，所罗门群岛以外的每个岛屿都无人居住。考古学家能够相当准确地确定斐济和汤加的这一进程的日期，距今 3,200 年前，最后是新西兰，距今 800-1,000 年前。

Soon after 3,500 BP the Austronesians set out from the Bismarck Archipelago (north-east of New Guinea) and colonised the whole Pacific, taking with them crops and pigs. Every island, beyond the Solomons, is believed to have been uninhabited before the Austronesians arrived there. Archaeologists are able to give fairly firm dates for this progress in Fiji and Tonga by 3,200 BP and, last of all, in New Zealand by 8001,000 BP.

南岛语系的大洋洲分支包括大约 500 种语言，据信它们都起源于一个祖先，即不到 4,000 年前使用的原始大洋洲语。这是扩张和分裂的典型例子，家谱模型非常适合于此。由于分裂速度太快，并非所有分支都能被发现，例如，当前的家谱在原始大洋洲语系下有大约十几个主要分支。但在家谱的下层，可以重建许多细节，特别是在波利尼西亚亚群中，分裂之间有足够的间隔，可以进行重大创新，这些创新贯穿到每个子语言中。（参见 Pawley 和 Ross 1995、Pawley 1981。）

The Oceanic branch of Austronesian includes about 500 languages, all believed to be descended from a single ancestor, proto-Oceanic, spoken less than 4,000 years ago. This is a classic example of expansion and split for which the family tree model is eminently appropriate. Because of the rapidity of splits not all can be uncovered for instance, the current family tree has about a dozen primary branches under proto-Oceanic. But lower down the family tree a lot of detail can be reconstructed, especially within the Polynesian subgroup, where there was sufficient gap between splits for significant innovations to have taken place, which came through into each daughter language. (See Pawley and Ross 1995, Pawley 1981.)

南岛人进入大洋洲就是一个拥有农业和良好航海技术（以及非凡航海技能）的民族开始探索新大陆的例子。一旦他们到达一个特定的群岛，并在那里完全定居，长途航行就更少使用了。例如，新西兰完全被殖民后，没有记录显示毛利人曾返回他们来自的波利尼西亚中部岛屿。一段平衡时期才刚刚开始。（几百年后，欧洲人的到来才打破了平衡。）

The Austronesian spread into Oceania is an example of a people with agriculture and good sailing craft (together with exceptional sailing skills) simply setting out to explore new lands. Once they arrived in a particular group of islands, and had fully populated it, long sea voyages were used more sparingly. For instance, once New Zealand was fully colonised there is no record of the Maoris there making trips back to the central Polynesian islands, from where they had come. A period of equilibrium was just beginning. (Only to be punctuated by the arrival of Europeans a few hundred years later.)

（二） 澳大利亚

在距今约 12 万年至距今约 1 万年间海平面上升期间，澳大利亚和新几内亚形成了一个连续的区域。考古学家认为人类最早在距今约 5 万年前定居澳大利亚/新几内亚。事实上，在距今约 5 万年前，海平面曾多次处于低位（Chappell、Omura、Esat 等人，1996 年）。当时，从东南亚大陆（当时延伸到巴厘岛）前往澳大利亚/新几内亚需要进行多次短途海上航行。Birdsell（1977 年）研究了许多替代的“跳岛”路线。例如，从加里曼丹经苏拉威西到新几内亚的路线涉及 10 个水峡，最大的一个长达 93 公里，而从巴厘岛到西澳大利亚金伯利海岸的路线涉及 8 个水峡，其中一个长达 87 公里，一个长达 29 公里，一个长达 19 公里，其余每个水峡都不足 10 公里（可能这两条路线都有不同的群体走）。（Butlin 1989 讨论了类似的情况。）从东南亚到澳大利亚/新几内亚的旅程特别令人感兴趣，因为它涉及最早的海上航行（实际上是最早的人类合作活动）。所使用的船只可能比欧洲人接触时澳大利亚人和巴布亚人使用的任何船只都更坚固（不包括新几内亚的南岛人，他们到达的时间不到 4,000 年前）。67

Australia and New Guinea formed one continuous area between about 120,000 BP and the rise of sea level at about 10,000 BP. The earliest agreed archaeological dates for human occupation of Australia/New Guinea are roughly 50,000 BP. In fact the sea level was low on a number of occasions around 50,000 BP (Chappell, Omura, Esat et al. 1996). At that time there would have been a number of short sea voyages required to travel from the south-east Asian land mass (which then extended to Bali) to Australia/New Guinea. Birdsell (1977) investigated a number of alternative 'island hopping' routes. For instance, a route from Kalimantan via Sulawesi to New Guinea involved 10 water gaps, the largest of 93 km, while a route from Bali to the Kimberley coast of Western Australia involved 8 water gaps, one of 87 km, one of 29 km, one of 19 km, with the remainder each being less than 10 km (it could be that both routes were followed, by different groups). (Butlin 1989 discusses a similar scenario.) The journey from south-east Asia to Australia/New Guinea is of particular interest since it would involve the earliest dated sea voyaging (indeed, the earliest attested cooperative activity of humans). The boats used were likely to have been more substantial than any in use among Australians and Papuans at the time of European contact (excluding those of the Austronesian population of New Guinea, who arrived less than 4,000 years ago).67

澳大利亚和新几内亚大约在 10,000 年前才分裂成两个大陆块。因此，人们可能认为这两个现代岛屿上的语言之间存在遗传联系。事实上，没有发现任何联系。68

Australia and New Guinea only became separated into two land masses about 10,000 years ago. One might thus expect there to be genetic connections between the languages spoken in these two modern islands. In fact none have been found.68

澳大利亚约有 260 种语言（1788 年白人入侵时）表现出许多反复出现的相似性，据说它们构成了一个语系。新几内亚有约 200 种南岛语系语言，分布在部分海岸和近海岛屿，这些语言被认为是最近才到达的。除了这些语言之外，新几内亚和附近岛屿还有约 700 种“巴布亚语”（该术语的意思是“非南岛语系”）语言，它们分为约 60 个小语系（见 Foley 1986）。如第 3 节所述，新几内亚在整个岛屿和特定地理区域都存在许多地域特征。只有对这些特征进行更彻底的研究，才有可能尝试区分地域相似性和遗传相似性，以研究高水平的遗传联系。尽管新几内亚的语言多样性令人惊叹（对于这样一个面积如此之小的国家而言，其语言多样性堪称世界之最），但可用的优秀语法却屈指可数，而大多数已尝试进行的比较研究质量参差不齐，毫无帮助（其中大部分基于词汇统计计数）。就目前的文献记录而言，关于新几内亚的语言状况，我们能说的不多。

The c. 260 languages of Australia (at the time of the white invasion, in 1788) show many recurrent similarities, and have been said to comprise a single language family. In New Guinea there are c. 200 languages of the Austronesian family, along parts of the coast and offshore islands, which are acknowledged to have arrived recently. Leaving these aside there are c. 700 'Papuan' (the term simply means 'non-Austronesian') languages of New Guinea and nearby islands, which divide into c. 60 small families (see Foley 1986). As mentioned in § 3, there are in New Guinea a number of areal features both across the whole island and in particular geographical areas. Not until these have been more thoroughly studied will it be possible to try to distinguish between areal and genetic similarities with a view to investigating high-level genetic links. Despite the amazing linguistic diversity in New Guinea (the greatest in the world, for such a land area), only a handful of good grammars are available while most of the comparative work that has been attempted is of mixed quality and unhelpful (much of it is based on lexicostatistical counting). Little more can be said about the linguistic situation in New Guinea in the present state of documentation.

我们经常发现，一个语系或一组语系与某种地形有关。例如，在南美洲，图皮语系、加勒比语系和阿拉瓦克语系主要局限于丛林，而杰语系则局限于草原。这些族群之间还存在其他差异：图皮语系、加勒比语系和阿拉瓦克语系使用吊床、制作陶器并实行刀耕火种农业，而杰语系则缺乏所有这些。图皮语系、阿拉瓦克语和加勒比语之间还存在类型学关系，这使他们与杰语系有所区别（见 Dixon 和 Aikhenvald，即将出版）。

We often find that a language family, or a group of families, is associated with a certain type of terrain. In South America, for instance, the Tupí, Carib and Arawak families were largely confined to the jungles and the Jê family to the grassy plains. There are additional differences between these groups Tupí, Carib and Arawak use hammocks, make pottery and practise slash-and-burn agriculture, while the Jê tribes lacked all of these things. There are also typological relationships between Tupí, Arawak and Carib, which set them apart from Jê (see Dixon and Aikhenvald, forthcoming).

澳大利亚/新几内亚分为两个地理区域。新几内亚大部分地区为山区，覆盖着雨林，其中一条小岛延伸至澳大利亚东北海岸。澳大利亚的其余地区是相当平坦的土地，有稀疏的森林、草原或沙漠。我们预计这两个地区会存在不同类型的语言。按照南美模式，我们可能预计森林地区的语言多样性会比平原地区更多。正如刚才所述，这就是我们所发现的。

Australia/New Guinea divides into two geographical areas. There is mountainous territory, covered with rain forest, over a good deal of New Guinea, with a finger extending down the north-east coast of Australia. The remainder of Australia is fairly flat country, with sparse forest, grasslands or desert. We would expect different kinds of languages to be found in the two areas. On the South American model, we might expect more linguistic diversity in the forested regions than on the plains. As just described, this is what is found.

我们还可能期待在澳大利亚东北海岸的山区雨林地带找到新几内亚类型的语言（或许还有遗传上的联系）。大约 10,000 年前，海平面上升将澳大利亚与新几内亚分开时，很可能就是这种情况。有证据表明，凯恩斯周围的雨林中存在着另一种人种，即尼格利陀人种（Tindale 和 Birdsell 1941）。但在这几千年间，这片地区已经被说正常澳大利亚类型语言的人所渗透（Dixon 1977：1516 对此进行了讨论）。

What might also be expected is to find languages of the New Guinea type (and perhaps genetic affiliation) in the strip of mountainous rainforest down the north-east coast of Australia. It is likely that this was the case at the time sea level rose to separate Australia from New Guinea, about 10,000 years ago. There is evidence for a different kind of people, the Negrito type, in the rainforest around Cairns (Tindale and Birdsell 1941). But during the intervening millennia this area has been infiltrated by people speaking languages of the normal Australian type (there is discussion of this in Dixon 1977: 1516).

现在我们可以把重点放在澳大利亚了。澳大利亚大陆各地都有早期的考古年代。澳大利亚很可能在第一次殖民后的几千年内就有人居住了，大约在 50,000 年前。许多学者认为，所有澳大利亚语言都属于一个语系。根据这一假设，有两种替代方案：

We can now focus on Australia. There are early archaeological dates from all parts of the continent. It is likely that the whole of Australia was populated within a few thousand years of the first colonisation, about 50,000 BP. Many scholars believe that all Australian languages belong to one linguistic family. Assuming this hypothesis there are two alternative scenarios:

（我） 原始澳大利亚语是所有现代语言的假定祖先，约 50,000 年前，澳大利亚的一些首批居民使用该语言。 (ii) 现代澳大利亚语言源自更近的原始语言，例如 10,000 或 5,000 年前。
（二） 根据假设 (ii)，现代澳大利亚语系的语言会遍布整个大陆，取代已经存在的语言。这个想法有两个难点。首先，我们可能期望找到早期语言的遗迹（可能在山上或沙漠中）；但事实并非如此。或者我们可能期望在某些语言中找到非澳大利亚的底层；但显然没有。其次，很难想象一个语系（由约 260 种语言组成）如何在整个大陆取代另一个语系。在世界其他地方，语言更替是由于帝国主义和征服；但少数狩猎采集者不太可能在有限的局部地区以外进行征服。这可能是通过一些物质创新实现的，但没有证据表明有任何足够重大的技术进步。 （尽管新几内亚高地的农业很发达，但澳大利亚却没有。）也就是说，这种扩张需要剧烈的间断，而且很难想象什么样的触发条件才是合适的。
（三） 我们只剩下情景 (i)，这是目前最有可能的。原始澳大利亚语，即假定的祖先，可能由一个最多几千人的小政治团体使用。有了之前大陆的食物资源，人口就会增加，群体会迁往新的领土，语言也会分裂。等到整个大陆都有人居住时，这可能只用了几千年的时间，语言之间的关系就可以通过家谱来记录，这是在扩张和分裂情景之后合适的模型。
（四） 然后，一旦这片大陆完全被人类占据，就会形成一种平衡状态，并持续 50,000 年，直到被英国入侵突然打破。如 § 6.1 所述，在平衡时期，没有什么是静止的，有不断的起伏。语言特征也在不断传播。而在标点符号时期，许多新语言从原始语言中分离出来，而在平衡时期，语言相互借用，因此它们倾向于向共同的原型靠拢。

澳大利亚（1788 年）是长期传播区域的典型例子。几乎所有可以映射到音系、形态和句法的特征都适用于连续区域（即其传播范围）中的所有语言69。有一个显著的特征有时被用来将语言分为两组。在中北部地区，语言已经发展出复杂的动词结构，其前缀包括指称核心论元的粘着代词。但这个前缀区域与其他传播区域并不重合。例如，一些语言只有少量的屈折动词词根；其他动词概念涉及非屈折形式与其中一种屈折词根的组合。发现这种情况的区域与前缀区域部分重叠，但并不与之重合。一些前缀语言缺乏这种特征，而一些非前缀语言则具有这种特征。

Australia (as at 1788) provides a prototypical example of a long-term diffusion area. Almost every feature that can be mapped phonological, morphological, syntactic applies over all the languages69 in a continuous area, its range of diffusion. There is one striking feature that is sometimes taken to divide the languages into two groups in an area in the central north, languages have developed complex verb structures with prefixes that include bound pronouns referring to core arguments. But this prefixing area does not coincide with other diffusional areas. For instance, some languages have only a small number of inflecting verbal roots; other verbal concepts involve combination of a non-inflecting form with one of these inflecting roots. The area in which this is found partly overlaps the prefixing area but does not coincide with it some prefixing languages lack this feature while some non-prefixing languages have it.

在词汇统计时代，有人认为澳大利亚有 29 个“系科”，除了两三个之外，其余的都在前缀领域。一个名为帕马-尼永根语的大非前缀“系科”覆盖了该大陆约 85% 的地区。事实上（与有时的说法相反）帕马-尼永根语和其他语言之间没有明确的语言界限。可以为许多类型的语言特征绘制等语线，但它们很少重合。每个特征都有自己的应用领域（其中大多数领域包括一些前缀语言和一些非前缀语言、一些非帕马-尼永根语和一些帕马-尼永根语）。

In the days of lexicostatistics it was suggested that there were 29 'phylic families' in Australia, all but two or three in the prefixing area. One large non-prefixing 'phylic family', called Pama-Nyungan, covers about 85% of the continent. In fact (contrary to what has sometimes been said) there is no clear linguistic boundary between Pama-Nyungan languages and the rest. Isoglosses can be drawn for many types of linguistic features but they seldom coincide. Each feature has its own area of application (and most of these areas include some prefixing and some non-prefixing languages, some non-Pama-Nyungan and some Pama-Nyungan languages).

在澳大利亚，有可能建立由 2 到 12 种语言组成的低级亚群，这些语言似乎具有密切的遗传关系。除了两种例外，所有这些语言在地理上都是相邻的。没有高级别的家谱可以证明将低级亚群联系起来。（缺乏清晰的家谱是反对上述情景 (ii) 的另一个证据。如果原始澳大利亚语仅在几千年前被使用，那么分裂和扩张就会在最近发生，家谱模型应该适用。）

It is possible to establish low-level subgroups in Australia groups of from two to a dozen or so languages that appear to have a close genetic relationship. With two exceptions, all of these are geographically contiguous. No higher-level family tree can be justified, linking the low-level subgroups. (This lack of an articulated family tree is another piece of evidence against scenario (ii) above. If proto-Australian had been spoken only a few thousand years ago, the split and expansion would have happened rather recently, and a family tree model should be applicable.)

低级亚群表明了以下情景：（i）大陆所有地方都有人居住；（ii）水资源减少，大片内陆地区变得无法居住，人口向沿海地区和主要河流迁移；（iii）内陆地区再次变得适合居住，人们迁移到离内陆最近的地区。70步骤(iii) 会引发许多小的标点，每个标点都代表一个低级亚群。

The low-level subgroups suggest the following scenario: (i) all parts of the continent were inhabited; (ii) water resources declined so that large inland tracts became uninhabitable, with the population contracting to the coast and major rivers; (iii) the inland areas again became inhabitable, and people moved into those parts nearest them.70 Step (iii) would have triggered many minor punctuations, each of which accounts for one of the low-level subgroups.

我们知道，在第一批土著人抵达和白人入侵之间，澳大利亚没有大规模移民。所有条件都有利于该地区长期保持语言平衡。现代语言学的图景是重叠的扩散区，语言在整个大陆上具有相似的类型学特征（存在区域差异）。我们处于一种趋同的情况。这可能最初始于从单一原始语言发展而来的语言，尽管这无法得到确切证明。来自几个不同语系的语言进入澳大利亚地区，并通过数万年的平衡接触和扩散融合其特征，这并非不可能。

We know of no significant immigrations into Australia between the time the first Aborigines arrived and the white invasion. All the conditions were right for a long state of linguistic equilibrium in this area. The modern linguistic picture is of overlapping diffusion zones, and languages having a similar typological profile over the whole continent (with areal variations). We have a situation of convergence. This may originally have begun with languages that had developed from a single proto-language, although this cannot be proved with certainty. It is not impossible that languages from several different families came into the Australian area and have merged their character through tens of millennia of equilibrium contact and diffusion.

澳大利亚的语言具有许多共同的反复出现的特征（见第 3 章）。此外，还有许多类型学参数使这些语言有所不同。在某些情况下，可以观察到参数内的变化周期性运动。例如：（i）在一个地区，粘性代词前缀由自由代词发展而来，然后主语和宾语形式融合，然后一些形式经历了语音截断，以至于不再有完整的语义区别（主语和宾语的人称和数字）；为了解决这个问题，又从自由形式发展出了额外的粘性代词；（ii）许多语言从以作格为主转变为以宾格为主，其中两种语言完成了循环，再次成为作格；（iii）名词类前缀在北部地区的所有语言中都已发展，然后由于来自缺乏名词类的邻近语言的扩散压力，这些前缀从其中一些语言（该地区的边缘）中消失了。

The languages of Australia share many recurrent features (see Chapter 3). There are also a number of typological parameters in terms of which the languages differ. In some cases one can observe a cyclical movement of change within a parameter. For example: (i) in one area, bound pronominal prefixes developed from free pronouns, then subject and object forms fused, and then some forms underwent phonological truncation such that the full set of semantic distinctions (person and number of subject and of object) were no longer made; to remedy this, additional bound pronouns developed again from free forms; (ii) many languages have shifted from a predominantly ergative to a predominantly accusative profile, and two of them have completed the circle, becoming ergative again; (iii) noun class prefixes have evolved in all the languages over a region in the north, and then they have been lost from some of these languages (on the edge of the region), because of diffusional pressure from neighbouring languages that lack noun classes.

迪克森（即将出版）对这些周期性运动进行了详细的说明，并全面讨论了澳大利亚的扩散情况，并提出了关于扩散特征的起源和扩散方向的建议。71

Dixon (forthcoming) provides detailed illustration of these cyclic movements, and also a full discussion of the diffusional situation in Australia together with suggestions about the origin and direction of spread of diffused features.71

（三） 美洲

北美洲、中美洲和南美洲与澳大利亚形成了鲜明的对比，它们包括几十个语系（没有一个语系的成员超过 50 个）和相当数量的孤立语系。直到最近，考古学界普遍认为美洲最早在 12,000 年前开始有人居住。有人认为美洲最早在 16,000 年前甚至 20,000 年前开始有人居住，但这些数字并没有得到普遍认可。72人们普遍认为美洲的人口来自亚洲，当时他们通过白令海峡的陆桥进入美洲。美洲语系的多样性强烈表明，有相当多的独立群体（可能有十几个）使用不同的语言踏上了这段旅程。

North, Central and South America present a striking contrast to Australia they include several dozen language families (none with more than 50 members) and a fair number of isolates. Until recently, the accepted archaeological opinion was that the Americas were first populated about 12,000 years ago. There have been some suggestions of an earlier date (16,000 or even 20,000 years) but these figures are by no means generally agreed on.72 It is generally accepted that the populating of the Americas involved movement from Asia, over what would then have been a land bridge at the Bering Strait. The diversity of families in the Americas strongly suggests that quite a number of separate groups (maybe a dozen or so) speaking different languages made the journey.

如此多的语系至今仍能被辨认出来，这与 12,000 至 20,000 年的时间深度相符（相比之下，澳大利亚的语系约为 50,000 年）。尤其是在南美洲，同一语系的语言往往分散成许多地理上不同的群体，彼此之间被其他语系的语言隔开。上文（§ 4.4）提到，在阿拉瓦克语系中，每个地理群体都通过传播而与该地区的其他语言具有共同的特征。在许多语言区域，不同语系的语言都趋向于共同的结构和音系。

The fact that so many language families can still be recognised is compatible with a time depth of 12,00020,000 years (as compared to about 50,000 years for Australia). In South America, especially, languages from one family tend to be scattered into many geographically distinct groups, separated from each other by languages from other families. It was mentioned above (§ 4.4) that in the Arawak family each geographical group has features in common with other languages from its region, through diffusion. There are a number of linguistic areas where languages from distinct families are all converging on a common structure and phonology.

Nichols (1990) 认为，12,000 年甚至 20,000 年的时间不足以解释美洲的语言多样性；她认为必要的时间深度约为 35,000 年。我的观点截然相反。如此多的语系可识别这一事实表明一系列语言分裂相对较近，与 12,000 至 20,000 年的时间相当吻合。再给美洲的语言 20,000 年，现在出现的传播模式将变得更加普遍。

Nichols (1990) has argued that 12,000 years, or even 20,000 years, is insufficient time to explain the linguistic diversity in the Americas; she suggests a necessary time depth of about 35,000 years. I take a viewpoint that is diametrically opposed. The fact that so many language families are recognisable indicates a relatively recent series of language splits, quite compatible with a 12,00020,000-year period. Give the languages in the Americas another 20,000 years and the diffusional patterns that are now emerging would become far more pervasive.

由于这里的地理多样性比澳大利亚更为显著，我们不会期望整个北美洲或整个南美洲会像澳大利亚一样成为一个单一的传播区，但我们会预期语言特征会大量传播到一些较小的区域。73我认为，再过 20,000 年，一个地区的语言将会趋同，形成一个共同的原型，以至于目前显而易见的遗传关系（阿拉瓦克语、加勒比语、图皮语等）将变得模糊，不再可辨别。

Since there is more geographical diversity than in Australia, we would not expect the whole of North America or the whole of South America to become a single diffusion area in the same way as Australia, but we would expect a great deal of diffusion of linguistic features over a number of smaller areas.73 I suggest that in 20,000 more years there would be such convergence of the languages in an area, to a common prototype, that the genetic relationships which are clearly evident at present (Arawak, Carib, Tupí, etc.) would become blurred, and no longer discernible.

对于刚刚讨论过的三个地区，大洋洲、澳大利亚和美洲的考古研究为人类首次占领提供了时间深度。非洲则呈现出不同的景象，人类和前人类已经在非洲生活了数百万年，这里很可能是语言最早进化的地方，距今已有 10 万年或更久。

For the three areas just discussed Oceania, Australia and theAmericas archaeological research provides a time-depth for their first human occupation. Africa presents a different picture humans and pre-humans have been in Africa for millions of years and it is a likely place for language to have first evolved, 100,000 years or more in the past.

如第 3 节所述，撒哈拉以南非洲目前的语言状况似乎具有多个重叠扩散区的特征。毫无疑问，存在一些遗传群体，但其中许多群体仍有待证实。最紧迫的任务是区分区域特征（这些特征被错误地视为遗传关系的标志）和遗传归属的真实指标。

As mentioned in § 3, the current linguistic situation in Sub-Saharan Africa appears to be characterised by a number of overlapping diffusion areas. There undoubtedly are some genetic groups but many of them still have to be proved. The most urgent task is to distinguish between areal features (which have, illicitly, been taken as marks of genetic relationships) and real indicators of genetic affiliation.

从现有信息来看，非洲大部分地区目前的语言状况似乎介于美洲和澳大利亚之间。非洲可识别出的遗传群体可能比澳大利亚多，但比美洲少；非洲的地域特征似乎比美洲更广泛，但比澳大利亚少。如前所述，语言确实以不同的速度变化，这取决于所涉及的政治和社会制度类型、语言的内部动态、与其他语言的接触程度和这些语言的结构以及使用者的态度。有了这个警告，人们得到的总体印象是，非洲大部分地区目前的语言状况表明，该语言区域的时间深度介于美洲和澳大利亚之间。

It does seem, from the information available, as if the current linguistic situation over most of Africa is part-way between that in the Americas and that in Australia. There are probably more genetic groups recognisable than in Australia, but less than in the Americas; and there appear to be more widespread areal features than in the Americas, but less than in Australia. As stressed earlier, languages do change at different rates, depending on the types of political and social systems involved, the internal dynamics of the languages, the degree of contact with other languages and the structures of those languages, and speakers' attitudes. With this caveat, the general impression one gets is that the current language situation over most of Africa indicates a time-depth for the linguistic area somewhere between those of the Americas and of Australia.

概括起来，间断平衡语言发展模型的两个要点是：

In summary, two of the main points of the punctuated equilibriummodel of language development are:

(a) 在标点符号时期，人们通常会看到民族及其语言的扩张和分裂场景。在这种情况下，家谱模型是合适的，因为许多不同的语言与共同的原始语言不同。

(a) During a period of punctuation one typically gets an expansion-and-split scenario, of peoples and of their languages. This is where a family tree model is appropriate a number of separate languages diverge from a common proto-language.

(b) 在标点符号之间的长期语言平衡期间，特定地区的人们生活得相对和谐。许多文化特征，包括许多语言特征，都扩散开来。该地区的语言将变得更加相似，它们将趋向于一个共同的原型。随着时间的推移，这种趋同将掩盖原始的遗传关系（最后一个标点符号时期家谱的终点）。

(b) During the long periods of linguistic equilibrium that intervene between punctuations, the people in a given area live in relative harmony. Many cultural traits, including many linguistic traits, diffuse. The languages in the area will become more similar they will converge towards a common prototype. In time, the convergence will obscure the original genetic relationships (the end points of the family trees during the last period of punctuation).

关键点在于，语言分裂几乎总是伴随着向新领土的扩张。对此有一个明显的反例。东北高加索（纳赫-达吉斯坦）语系有 2530 名成员，人们认为他们一直居住在现在的领土上。但我们这里是崎岖的山地地形。一个政治团体很可能分裂成几个，而且这种情况发生过多次，每个团体与邻居的接触都很有限。这可能只会发生在山区。（将新几内亚约 60 个非南岛语系与澳大利亚假定的单一语系进行比较，时间深度大致相同，可以作为山区和平原地区可能发生的不同事情的例子，山区难以进入，平原地区容易交流。）

A key point is that language split is almost always accompanied by expansion into new territory. There is an apparent counter-example to this. The North-east Caucasian (Nakh-Daghestanian) family, with 2530 members, is thought always to have been located in its present territory. But what we have here is rugged mountain terrain. It is likely that one political group split into several, and that this happened a number of times, with each group having only limited contact with its neighbours. This could probably only happen in mountainous country. (Compare the c. 60 non-Austronesian language families in New Guinea with the putative single family in Australia with about the same time-depth as an example of the different kinds of things that can happen in mountainous country, which is difficult of access, and flat country, with easy communication.)

7 有关原始语言的更多信息

7 More on Proto-Languages

比较语言学家以家族树模型为特征，从扩张和分裂的角度来思考，通常认为原始语言是标点符号时期快速分裂的结果。但事实可能并非如此。标点符号时期通常会打断一段较长的平衡期，而语言家族的开端很可能位于语言区域内趋同所产生的语言环境类型中。事实上，语言家族的基础可能不只在一种语言中。

Thinking in terms of expansion and split, characterised by the family tree model, comparative linguists typically regard a proto-language as if it were the result of rapid splitting during a period of punctuation. But it is probably not. A period of punctuation typically interrupts a long interval of equilibrium and the beginning of a language family is likely to lie in the type of linguistic situation that is produced by convergence within a linguistic area. Indeed, a language family may not have its basis in just one language.

§ 4.2 初步讨论了某个语言家族的假定祖先语言应如何被视为与我们当今世界上的语言相似，具有补充、不规则、底层等。现在已经介绍了间断平衡模型，我们可以将这个讨论更进一步。

§ 4.2 had preliminary discussion of how the putative ancestor language of a family should be seen as similar to the languages that are around us in the world today with suppletions, irregularities, substrata, etc. Having now introduced the punctuated equilibrium model, we can take this discussion one stage further.

在平衡时期，相邻语言会传播音系结构和系统（及其语音实现）、语法类别、词素和（速度较慢的）语法形式等特征。在特定地区，我们可能会发现两三种语言在结构上趋于一致，在形式上也趋于一致。它们将属于许多截然不同但关系密切的政治团体。根据严格的可理解性标准，它们将是不同的语言，尽管语言社区的许多成员可能都会说两种或三种语言。

During a period of equilibrium contiguous languages diffuse features phonological structures and systems (together with their phonetic realisations), grammatical categories, lexemes and (at a slower rate) grammatical forms. In a given area we may have two or three languages that have converged together in structure and, to an appreciable extent, in forms. They will belong to a number of distinct although closely allied political groups. They will be separate languages in terms of the strict criterion of intelligibility, although many members of the language community are likely to be bilingual or trilingual.

假设这样一个地区的政治和语言平衡被一位魅力非凡的军事或宗教领袖的出现、农业的发展或其他原因所打破。这种打破可能导致扩张和分裂，从而形成一个语系。需要指出的是，这个语系可能不是源自单一语言，而是源自一小群具有相似结构和形式的不同语言。

Suppose that the political and linguistic equilibrium in such an area is punctuated by the arising of a charismatic military or religious leader, or by the development of agriculture, or for some other reason. This punctuation may give rise to expansion and split, the establishment of a language family. The point to be made is that the language family may have emanated not from a single language, but from a small areal group of distinct languages, with similar structures and forms.

这种关于语言家族起源的假说（一种自然地从间断平衡假说中得出的想法）值得研究。对印欧语、乌拉尔语、南岛语、阿尔冈昆语、阿萨巴斯卡语、玛雅语、阿拉瓦克语和达罗毗荼语等公认家族的这一想法进行彻底和不带偏见的研究可能会决定，在某些情况下，单一原始语言的想法是最合适的，但在其他情况下，一个家族从一个小的语言区域发展而来的想法最能解释事实。74

Such a hypothesis concerning the origin of a language family an idea that follows naturally from the hypothesis of punctuated equilibrium bears investigation. A thorough and unprejudiced study of the idea for acknowledged families such as Indo-European, Uralic, Austronesian, Algonquian, Athapaskan, Mayan, Arawak and Dravidian may decide that in some cases the idea of a single proto-language is most appropriate, but that in other cases the idea of a family developing from a small linguistic area explains the facts best.74

很常见的是，在为特定语系重建假定的原始语言时，人们会想出比任何一种语言可能具有的更多的形式，这些形式被赋予了特定的含义或功能。例如，代词中的某个人/数字组合、某个指示词或疑问词或某些身体部位有两种形式。75这很可能表明实际上存在一个“原始语言区域”（涉及多种语言），而不是一种原始语言。76

Not uncommonly, when reconstructing the putative proto-language for a given language family, one comes up with more forms to which a particular meaning or function is assigned than any one language is likely to have. For instance, two forms for a certain person/number combination in pronouns, or for a certain demonstrative, or interrogative, or for certain body parts.75 This might well be an indication that there was in fact a 'proto-linguistic-area' (involving more than one language) rather than a single proto-language.76

回到原始语言的年代问题，从 §4.3 可以看出，一个小的语言区域，即一个语言家族的起源点，可能已经存在了数千年。分裂可能始于这个区域，方言开始分离，然后标点符号的爆发释放了一个扩展和分裂阶段。由此可见，为原始语言（或原始语言区域）指定一个确切日期的想法可能既荒诞又具有误导性。

Returning to the question of dating a proto-language, from §4.3, it will now be seen that a small linguistic area, which was the point of origin for a language family, may have existed for some thousands of years. Splits would have begun within this area, with dialects starting to move apart, before the burst of punctuation released a phase of expansion and split. It follows from this that the idea of assigning an exact date to a proto-language (or proto-linguistic-area) could be both chimeral and misleading.

一个语言家族所处的语言区域的所有语言可能都属于同一个原始家族，也可能来自多个遗传源。或者，如果平衡区域已经存在了很长一段时间，那么原始遗传特征可能已经受到扩散的影响，以至于家族成员不再是一个有用的概念。

The languages in a linguistic area from which a language family developed may all have belonged to a single original family or they may have been from several genetic sources. Or, if the equilibrium area has been in existence for a long period, the original genetic features could have been so affected by diffusion that family membership ceases to be a useful concept.

在讨论平衡时期时，我们在 §6.1 中提出，尽管政治团体和他们的语言之间会存在普遍的和谐，但情况总是会时好时坏。政治团体之间会出现一定程度的分裂（尽管不像标点符号时期那样严重）和一些合并。根据每种语言都有一个母体的原则，新政治团体的语言将与其中一个组成团体的语言相一致，尽管其他团体的语言可能会有相当大的底层或顶层。

When discussing equilibrium periods, in §6.1, we suggested that, although there would have been general harmony between the political groups and their languages, the situation would always be shifting a degree of ebb and flow. There would be a certain amount of splitting (although nothing like so much as during a period of punctuation) and some merging of political groups. On the principle that each language has a single parent, the language of a new political group would be identifiable with the language of one of the constituent groups, although there would be likely to be a considerable substratum or superstratum from the language(s) of the other group(s).

这些考虑可以解释现代语系假定的原始语言之间的一些相似之处。例如，考虑印欧语和乌拉尔语。77假设它们都来自一种原始语言。印欧语可能是 A 语系的 A1 语言，其底层来自 B 语系的 B2 语言，而原始乌拉尔语可能是 B1 语言，其底层来自 A 语系的另一种语言 A2。或者这些语系可能起源于不同的语言区域，但其中一个区域的语言与另一个区域的语言非常相似。印欧语和乌拉尔语之间存在相似之处（例如，参见 Campbell 1990），但除了假设进一步的、更高级别的语系树之外，还有许多方法可以解释这些相似之处。78

These sorts of considerations could explain some of the points of resemblance between postulated proto-languages of modern families. Consider, for example, Indo-European and Uralic.77 Suppose that each did come from a single proto-language. It could be that Indo-European was language A1, from family A, with a substratum from language B2 of family B, while proto-Uralic was language B1 with a substratum from A2, another language of family A. Or these families could have originated in distinct linguistic areas, but with a language in one of the areas showing close similarities to one from the other area. There are similarities between Indo-European and Uralic languages (see, for instance, Campbell 1990) but they are explainable in a number of ways other than by positing a further, higher-level, family tree.78

另一种可能，也是最有可能的一种，是印欧语和乌拉尔语起源于同一语言区域（可能是一个较大的区域，包含几十种语言）不同地区的语言，这些语言是在长期的语言平衡期结束时形成的。建立两个语系的两种语言（或语言群）具有许多类型学上的相似性，并且有许多共同的词素和一些语法形式。但原始印欧语和原始乌拉尔语之间可能无法证明存在密切的家族树型关系（就像许多现代澳大利亚语言一样，尽管它们在结构和形式上具有相当大的相似性）。在长期的平衡期结束时，语言区域中的语言确实表现出相似性，但这些是向共同原型趋同的迹象，而不是遗传关系的证据。也就是说，我们可以得到如图 7.1 所示（高度示意性的方式）的情况。

A further alternative and perhaps the most likely of all is that Indo-European and Uralic had their origins in languages from different parts of the same linguistic area (perhaps a largish area, containing a few dozen languages) at the end of a long period of linguistic equilibrium. The two languages (or groups of languages) which founded the two language families, would have many typological similarities, and also a number of lexemes and a few grammatical forms in common. But it is likely that a close family-tree-type relationship between proto-Indo-European and proto-Uralic would not be demonstrable (as it is not for many modern Australian languages, despite their considerable structural and formal similarity). Languages in a linguistic area, at the end of a long equilibrium period, do show similarities, but these are an indication of convergence towards a common prototype, rather than being evidence of genetic affiliation. That is, we could get a situation like that shown (in a highly schematic fashion) in Figure 7.1.

图 7.1

Figure 7.1

在第 1 节中，我首先指出，如果家谱是语言关系的唯一可用模型，人们就会尝试将其应用于所有情况。如果原始印欧语和原始乌拉尔语之间存在显著的共同特征，那么它们必须以家谱式的方式相互关联（诺斯特拉谬误）。我试图提出一种看待事物的替代方式，这一想法的部分动机是需要描述和解释澳大利亚的现代语言状况，部分动机是提出一个假设，以解释 10 万年或更长时间的语言发展和互动。

I began, in §1, by remarking that if the family tree is the only available model of linguistic relationship, people will try to apply it in all circumstances. If there are significant features in common between proto-Indo-European and proto-Uralic ergo, they must be related in a family-tree-type way (the Nostratic fallacy). I have tried to put forward an alternative way of looking at things, an idea that was motivated partly by the need to describe and explain the modern linguistic situation in Australia, and partly to provide a hypothesis that will account for 100,000 years or more of linguistic development and interaction.

藏缅语和汉语之间的关系非常有趣，但尚未得到充分解释。这两组语言中都出现了许多关键的词素，并有规律的声音对应。但事实证明，要取得更大的进展很难。（例如，参见 Norman 1988：1216。）如果为汉藏语考虑一些超越简单家谱分裂的更广泛的关系模型，其中之一可能会提供更合适的场景，并提出进一步的研究方向。79

The relationship between Tibeto-Burman and Sinitic (Chinese) languages is a fascinating one that has not yet been fully explained. There are a number of critical lexemes that appear in both groups of languages, with regular sound correspondences. But it has proved difficult to progress much beyond this. (See, for instance, Norman 1988: 1216.) If a number of wider models for relationship going beyond simple family-tree splitting were considered for Sino-Tibetan, one of them might provide a more appropriate scenario, and suggest further directions for investigation.79

 

 

8 最近的历史

8 Recent History

概括欧洲的统治如何强加于世界大部分地区并随后逐渐撤回，以及 (b) 概述通信领域的最新发展，然后 (c) 描述语言和方言如何已经和正在消失以及其原因，这些都是很有用的。

It will be useful (a) to summarise the way in which European dominance was imposed on most of the rest of the world, and then withdrawn; and (b) to outline the recent developments in communication; before (c) describing the ways in which languages and dialects have been and are being lost, and the reasons for this.

（一个） 入侵

白种人最初只生活在欧洲和非洲与亚洲的紧邻地区。然后，从 15 世纪开始，他们开始殖民世界其他地区，建立政治统治地位，并将他们的语言（英语、西班牙语、葡萄牙语、阿拉伯语、荷兰语、法语、德语和意大利语）强加给他们统治的人民。

The white race originally lived just in Europe and the immediately adjacent parts of Africa and Asia. Then, from the fifteenth century, they began to colonise the rest of the world, establishing political dominance and imposing their languages English, Spanish, Portuguese, Arabic, Dutch, French, German and Italian on the peoples they governed.

从十六世纪开始，美洲是第一批被系统性接管的大陆。随后是南部非洲、南亚、印度尼西亚、澳大利亚和新西兰、太平洋岛屿、新几内亚、东南亚大部分地区，最后是非洲几乎所有其他地区。到 1910 年，唯一没有被白人统治的主要国家是利比里亚、埃塞俄比亚、泰国、中国、西藏、日本和韩国。然后，从 1947 年开始，钟摆又摆了回来。土著人民要么自己夺取政权，要么被他们昔日的主人匆匆授予权力（只有法国和美国坚决保留了部分殖民地）。

The first continents to be systematically taken over were the Americas from the sixteenth century. These were followed by Southern Africa, South Asia, Indonesia, Australia and New Zealand, the islands of the Pacific, New Guinea, most of South-east Asia and, finally, almost all the rest of Africa. By 1910 the only major countries that were not governed by white people were Liberia, Ethiopia, Thailand, China, Tibet, Japan and Korea. Then, from 1947, the pendulum swung back. The indigenous peoples either seized power for themselves or were hurriedly granted it by their erstwhile masters (only France and the USA have resolutely held onto some of their colonial territories).

第二次世界大战后，白人的统治地位在世界各地都被打破，非洲、亚洲、新几内亚和太平洋岛屿上的所有国家中，土著人仍占人口的大多数。然而，在北美、南美、澳大利亚和新西兰，白种人已确立了文化和人口的主导地位，土著人口已缩减到以前的几分之一（由于疾病和谋杀的双重原因），并且在新兴的欧洲式国家中仍然是弱势的少数民族。他们的许多语言已经消亡，其他语言正在消亡，几乎所有其他语言都濒临灭绝。

After the Second World War, white dominance was broken in every part of the world where the indigenous people still comprised the majority of the population every nation in Africa, Asia, New Guinea and the Pacific Islands. However, in North America, South America, Australia and New Zealand, the white race had established a dominance of culture and of numbers the indigenous populations have shrunk to a fraction of their former size (through a combination of disease and murder) and remain an under-privileged minority in the new European-style nations. Many of their languages are dead, others are dying, and almost all the rest are endangered.

这些源自欧洲的入侵打破了世界许多地方存在的语言平衡状态。

The invasions, emanating from Europe, punctuated the states of linguistic equilibrium that were in existence in many parts of the world.

（二） 通讯发展

自 1830 年左右以来，通讯领域出现了重大创新。交通工具火车、轮船、公共汽车、汽车和飞机以及媒体都提高了识字率、教育、报纸、广播和电视。这导致了更大的集中化，来自农村地区的人们可以更容易地前往城市，而且往往更喜欢住在城市里；报纸、广播和电视节目都来自大城市。所有这些都有助于缩小一种语言的方言传播范围，并减少少数民族语言的使用。

The period since about 1830 has seen major innovations in communication. Both transport trains, steamships, buses, cars and planes and media increased literacy, schooling, newspapers, radio and TV. This has led to greater centralisation people from rural areas can more easily visit cities and often prefer to live in them; newspapers, radio and TV programs come from the major cities. All of this contributes to narrowing the dialectal spread of a language, and to reduction in use of the languages of minority groups.

学校教育开始实行后，教学通常采用国家最有名望的语言，而且总是采用该语言最有名望的方言。父母讲爱尔兰语、威尔士语或约克郡英语方言的孩子，则接受伦敦英语方言的教育，任何偏离这一规范的行为都会受到惩罚。80

Once schooling was introduced, instruction was generally through the prestige language of the nation, and invariably in the prestige dialect of that language. Children whose parents spoke Irish or Welsh or the Yorkshire dialect of English were schooled in the London dialect of English and punished for any deviation from this norm.80

这几乎适用于世界各地。例如，1985 年，我在斐济的 Boumaa 地区住了几个月，那里有自己的方言，与标准方言 Bau 可以互相理解。当地学校的所有教学都使用 Bau 方言。曾经有一段时间，孩子们因为在学校使用自己的方言而受到惩罚；不过，现在这种行为已经可以容忍了。所有教堂礼拜都使用 Bau 方言（圣经被翻译成 Bau 语）。有一天，我被邀请做祷告，我用 Boumaa 方言做了祷告。为此，我受到了谴责，基督教牧师说，上帝只喜欢用 Bau 语称呼他。毫不奇怪，Boumaa 方言正逐渐向 Bau 方言靠拢；几代人之前，他们共享大约 80% 的词汇，但现在这个数字已经达到 90% 左右。

This applies just about everywhere in the world. For instance, in 1985 I lived for some months in the Boumaa region of Fiji which has its own dialect, mutually intelligible with the standard dialect, Bau. All instruction at the local school is through the Bau dialect. At one time children were punished for using their own dialect on the school premises; this is, however, now tolerated. All church services are conducted in the Bau dialect (the Bible is translated into Bau). One day I was invited to say a prayer and did so in the Boumaa dialect. For this I received a reprimand God, the Christian priests had said, only likes to be addressed in Bau. Unsurprisingly, the Boumaa dialect is gradually moving closer to Bau; a couple of generations ago they shared about 80% vocabulary but the figure is now around 90%.

昆士兰东北部迪尔巴尔语部落的土著儿童从 1950 年左右才被允许进入当地学校就读。从那时起直到 20 世纪 60 年代，他们被禁止在校园里说自己的母语（如果听到有人说母语，会受到鞭刑）。如今，学校氛围更加自由，但教育仍然完全以英语进行。当然，迪尔巴尔人接触的媒体也完全是英语。1963 年，当我开始实地考察时，35 岁以上的每个人都以迪尔巴尔语为母语；除了几个非常年长的人外，每个人都能说一些英语。当时大约有 100 名迪尔巴尔语使用者。30 年后，只有 65 岁以上的人会说这种语言，只有六七个人。一些年轻人为能够听懂老年人说的迪尔巴尔语而感到自豪；但几年后，将没有人能听懂。

Aboriginal children of the tribes speaking Dyirbal, in north-east Queensland, were only allowed to attend the local school from about 1950. From then until well into the 1960s they were forbidden to speak in their own native language in the school grounds (and would be caned if heard doing so). Today the atmosphere is more liberal but education is still entirely in English. And, of course, the media that Dyirbal people are exposed to is entirely English. In 1963, when I began fieldwork, everyone over about thirty-five had Dyirbal as their first language; everybody except for a couple of very old people also had some competence in English. There were then perhaps a hundred speakers of Dyirbal. Thirty years later only those over about sixty-five can speak the language there are just half-a-dozen of them. Some of the younger people are proud of being able to understand the Dyirbal language, as spoken by the older people; but in a few years there will be no one left to understand.

世界各地交流的改善正在导致语言的消失，方言的分化也大大减少。在英国、斐济和其他国家，地方方言正逐渐向标准或主流语言转变。新语言的发展源于方言的分化。不仅语言在现代世界中消失，而且创造新语言的机会（通过克里奥尔化除外）也在不断减少。

Improved communication, all over the world, is leading to the loss of language and also a great diminution in dialect differentiation. In England, in Fiji, and in every other country, regional dialects are gradually moving towards the standard or prestige language variety. The development of new languages comes from diverging dialects. Not only are languages being lost in the modern world, but the chances of new languages being created (except through creolisation) are reducing all the time.

如果情况一直保持 1800 年的状态，美式英语和澳大利亚英语就会逐渐与英式英语分化；随着时间的推移，它们将失去可理解性，并被视为不同的语言。但轮船的发明，以及随后的电影、广播和电视的发明，带来了完全不同的局面。目前，这三种方言正在融合。当这些国家的人们观看彼此的电影和电视节目时，他们从彼此的单词、习语和语法结构中学习到了说话习惯，甚至一些发音习惯。81

If things had remained as they were in 1800, American English and Australian English would be steadily diverging from British English; in time, intelligibility would be lost and they would be considered separate languages. But the innovation of the steamship and then of the cinema, radio and TV has produced a quite different situation. At the present time the three dialects are converging. As people in these nations watch each other's movies and TV programs, they pick up speech habits from each other words and idioms and grammatical constructions, and even some habits of pronunciation.81

如第 6.1 节所述，均衡情况涉及多个政治集团，每个集团都有自己的语言或方言，存在于平等的氛围中。没有一个集团在其邻国中建立统治地位，也没有一种语言或方言获得威望地位（除非是短暂的，并且只在一个相当小的地区）。在当今世界，我们拥有庞大的政治集团（国家），每个集团都有一个占主导地位的种族和/或社会群体。占主导地位的群体的语言或方言享有威望，并在大多数类型的交流中使用。（也有例外，即拥有多种官方语言82的国家，如瑞士和巴拉圭，但这种情况很少见。）

The equilibrium situation, as described in §6.1, involved a number of political groups, each with its own language or dialect, existing in an egalitarian atmosphere. No one group established dominance over its neighbours and no one language or dialect acquired a prestige status (except in a transitory manner, and over a rather small region). In the present-day world we have large political groups (nations), each with a dominant racial and/or social group. The language or dialect of the dominant group is accorded prestige and is used the majority of types of communication. (There are exceptions in the form of nations with more than one official language82 such as Switzerland and Paraguay but they are rare.)

总之，交流的发展加强了白人入侵的影响，打破了直到最近世界上还存在的语言平衡区。即使在入侵者已被驱逐（或自愿离开）的地方，欧洲人造成的骚乱仍在继续，而且越来越严重。非洲被分成许多国家，不是根据种族、语言或宗教划分的，而只是欧洲殖民的产物。几乎每个现代非洲国家都是种族和语言多元化的，这带来了政治紧张，有时甚至导致屠杀。这些国家的交流不断发展。少数语言（有时只有一种）是写作、学校教育、报纸、广播、电影和电视的基础。结果，少数人使用的语言正在逐渐减少，直至被废弃。

In summary, developments in communication have reinforced the effects of white invasions, in providing punctuation of the linguistic equilibrium areas which existed in the world until recently. Even in places where the invader has now been expelled (or left voluntarily), the disturbance engendered by Europeans continues and increases. Africa was divided into a number of states, not on ethnic or linguistic or religious lines, but simply as an artefact of European colonisation. Almost every modern African state is ethnically and linguistically diverse, which brings with it political tension and sometimes massacres. There is continual development of communication in these nations. A small number of languages (sometimes just one) are the basis for writing, schooling, newspapers, radio, films and TV. As a result, the minority languages those with a small number of speakers are shrinking towards disuse.

（三） 语言丧失

我们可以发现，在过去几个世纪的标点符号使用过程中，有许多语言已经消失。

We can distinguish a number of situations in which languages have been lost, during the punctuation of the past few centuries.

（我） 人口减少

这可能是通过谋杀或疾病。有整个群体被入侵者消灭的例子。1857 年，澳大利亚昆士兰州东南部塔鲁姆附近的整个 Yeeman 部落在白人定居者的大屠杀中被消灭。（没有记录下他们的语言，我们所知道的只是部落的名字。）这种种族灭绝在澳大利亚、南美洲和北美洲反复发生。

This can be by murder or by disease. There are instances of whole groups being exterminated by the invader. The entire Yeeman tribe, from around Taroom in south-east Queensland, Australia, was wiped out in a massacre by white settlers in 1857. (Not a word of its language was recorded, all we know is the name of the tribe.) This kind of genocide was repeated throughout Australia, South America and North America.

另一种选择是俘虏一个民族，奴役他们，然后让他们累死。1492 年，克里斯托弗·哥伦布踏上巴哈马群岛，在新大陆遇到的第一批人是泰诺人（阿拉瓦克族）。在二十五年内，西班牙人将整个人口带到附近的伊斯帕尼奥拉岛当奴隶，他们在几代人的时间里就灭绝了。海明（1978 年）讲述了亚马逊河口的欧洲定居者如何逆流而上，俘虏一个部落，把他们带到恶劣的种植园里工作，然后等他们灭绝后（通常在十年左右），他们又逆流而上，俘虏并奴役另一个部落。

An alternative was to capture a people, enslave them, and literally work them to death. The first people Christopher Columbus encountered in the New World, when he set foot in the Bahamas in 1492, were the Taino (an Arawak group). Within twenty-five years the Spanish had carried off the entire population to slavery on the nearby island of Hispaniola, where they died out within a couple of generations. Hemming (1978) tells how the European settlers at the mouth of the Amazon would travel upriver, capture a tribe, bring them down to work on their plantations under harsh conditions, then when they died out (often, within about ten years), go upriver again to capture and enslave another tribe.

白人入侵者带来了麻疹、天花和普通感冒等疾病，而其他大陆的人们对此没有免疫力。1789 年（欧洲人抵达后两年内），在澳大利亚悉尼的第一个英国定居点附近，大约有一半的土著人死于天花。这种流行病很可能蔓延到了大部分或整个大陆；随后又发生了更多的流行病。当白人入侵者到达某个地方时，当地人口已经大大减少，白人的疾病使他们士气低落，他们没有像以前那样奋起反抗。

The white invaders brought with them diseases measles and smallpox and the common cold to which people in other continents had no immunity. About half the Aborigines in the vicinity of the first British settlement in Australia, at Sydney, died of smallpox in 1789 (within two years of the Europeans' arrival). It is likely that the epidemic spread across most or all of the continent; and it was followed by further epidemics. By the time the white invaders reached a particular locality the population was greatly reduced and demoralised by the white man's diseases, and put up less of a fight than they might have otherwise.

南美洲也发生了同样的情况。巴西从 1500 年起就被殖民，但欧洲人直到 19 世纪末才进入亚马逊最茂密的丛林。疾病在他们之前就已经存在；印第安人的人口已降至 1500 年的四分之一甚至更少。人口减少、部落合并和语言消失的过程一直在持续。民族学家 Franz Caspar (1956:221) 曾在 Tupari 部落生活过一段时间，部落告诉他“在他们的祖父和曾祖父时代，几个小部落合并了。托普托可以毫不犹豫地说出每个男人和每个女人的血统。” Vaikorotá、Aumeh 和 Mensiató 三个部落各剩下一个人。五个人是真正的“Tupari”。其余的人……都是“Vakarau”……他说，甚至部落现在的语言也不是古老的 Tupari，因为少数民族已经采用了 Vakarau 的语言。但人们仍然可以回忆起各个部落的语言，Topto 还告诉我一些真正的 Tupari 语言。也就是说，许多部落群体合并，并为新的联合群体采用了一种语言（可能带有其他原始群体语言的底层）。

The same happened in South America. Brazil was colonised from 1500 but Europeans only penetrated the densest jungles of Amazonia in the late nineteenth century. Their diseases preceded them; the Indian population had fallen to a quarter or less of what it had been in 1500. The process of population reduction, merging of tribes, and loss of languages has been continuous. The ethnologist Franz Caspar (1956:221) lived for a while among the Tupari tribe and was told by them that 'in the days of their grandfathers and great-grandfathers several small tribes had merged. Of every man and every woman Topto was able to say without hesitation of what extraction they were. There was only one man left out of each of the ''Vaikorotá", "Aumeh" and "Mensiató" tribes. Five were real "Tupari". All the rest . . . were "Vakarau" . . . Even the present language of the tribe, he said, was not the old Tupari, for the minorities had adopted the language of the Vakarau.
