But people could still recall how the various tribes had spoken and Topto told me a few words of the real Tupari language.' That is, a number of tribal groups had merged and adopted a single language for the new combined group (probably with substrata from languages of the other original groups).

同样的故事在南美洲和世界其他地方上演。人们会意识到，调查亚马逊地区今天的语言状况是一项艰巨的任务。由于政治团体的合并，许多语言已经不再被使用，而那些仍然存在的语言则有来自不同来源的大量基础。

The same story is repeated all over South America and in other parts of the world. It will be appreciated that investigating the language situation in Amazonia today is a difficult task. Many languages have ceased to be spoken, through the merger of political groups, and those languages that remain have considerable substrata from varying sources.

（二） 被迫丧失语言能力

有时，一种语言的消亡是因为统治群体直接禁止使用这种语言，或者通过某种手段使这种语言无法使用。在澳大利亚，一个部落的幸存者（在疾病和/或屠杀之后幸存下来的人）会被当局分开，其中一些被送到这个政府定居点或传教区，另一些被送到另一个政府定居点或传教区。由于几乎没有人可以用自己的语言交谈，他们自然会转向英语。许多传教区的一种常见做法是将七八岁的孩子从父母身边带走，关进上锁的宿舍，如果听到他们说父母的语言，就会受到惩罚。这种做法在南美洲、澳大利亚和新几内亚（可能还有其他地方）一直持续到本世纪中叶，是导致语言消亡的主要因素。

Sometimes a language has died because the dominant group simply forbade it to be spoken, or engineered things so that it could not be spoken. In Australia the survivors of a tribe (those remaining after disease and/or massacres) would be split up by the authorities, with a few being sent to this government settlement or mission and a few to that one. With scarcely anyone to speak to in their own language, they would naturally turn to English. A common practice at many missions was to take children from their parents at the age of seven or eight and place them in locked dormitories where they would be punished if heard to speak in the parents' language. This practice continued in South America, Australia and New Guinea (and probably elsewhere) until the middle of this century and was a major factor contributing to language death.

（三） 自愿转换语言

在许多情况下，一种语言的放弃是因为使用者的选择，无论是父母的选择，还是孩子的选择。

In many situations a language is abandoned by choice of its speakers either choice of parents, or choice of children.

如前所述，非主流语言的使用者可能总是会说主流语言。我的第一位 Dyirbal 语言老师 Chloe Grant 精通母语和英语。但 Chloe 和她的丈夫只用英语和他们的孩子说话，因为他们觉得这样可以让他们在世界上有更好的机会。这无疑对孩子们有帮助，但副作用是他们现在不能用父母的语言说话（并且后悔他们不能）。

As mentioned earlier, the speakers of a non-prestige language are likely always to know the prestige language. My first teacher of Dyirbal, Chloe Grant, was fluent in her own language and in English. But Chloe and her husband spoke only in English to their children, since they felt it would give them a better chance in the world. This undoubtedly did help the children, but the side effect was that they cannot now speak in their parents' language (and regret that they can't).

如今，爱尔兰语是爱尔兰岛西北部仅有的几千人的第一语言，他们属于社会经济地位最低的群体。都柏林的中产阶级正在积极努力复兴这种语言，但在西北部的许多家庭中，父母故意只用英语和孩子说话。正如他们所说，在其他人都说英语时，他们却说爱尔兰语，这使他们成为最弱势的群体，他们认为没有理由继续这种状况。

Irish is spoken today, as first language, by only a few thousand people in the far north-west of the island; they belong to the lowest socio-economic group. The middle class in Dublin is actively working to try to revive the language, but in many of the families in the north-west, parents are purposely speaking only in English to their children. As they remark, talking Irish while everyone else spoke English has left them as the most disadvantaged group and they see no reason to perpetuate this situation.

在其他情况下，做出选择的则是儿童。他们听到周围有人说两种语言，出于一个或多个原因，他们选择通用语而不是他们的传统语言。他们自己可能认为通用语更有用，在更多地方有更多人使用。或者他们可能更喜欢通用语，只是因为它结构更简单，更容易学习。这是巴布亚新几内亚塞皮克地区的 Yimas 儿童说托克皮辛语（国家克里奥尔语）而不是面对 Yimas 的语法复杂性的主要原因。这也是巴西普鲁斯河畔 Paumarí 社区的年轻成员说当地葡萄牙语而不是 Paumarí 语（其结构确实更复杂）的原因。

In other contexts it is the children who make the choice. They hear two languages spoken around them and opt for the lingua franca rather than their traditional language, for one or more reasons. They may themselves perceive that the lingua franca is more useful, that it is used by more people in more places. Or they may prefer the lingua franca simply because it is simpler in structure and easier to learn. This is a major reason given by Yimas children in the Sepik region of Papua New Guinea for speaking Tok Pisin, the national creole, rather than confronting the grammatical complexities of Yimas. It is also the reason given by younger members of the Paumarí community, on the Purús River in Brazil, for speaking the local variety of Portuguese rather than Paumarí (which does have a more intricate structure).

（四） 非自愿的语言转换

在平衡情况下，双语现象通常是一个双向的过程：许多 X 语言的使用者也会精通 Y 语言，而许多 Y 语言的使用者也会了解很多 X 语言。现代社会并不是平等的，当一种语言具有声望地位（通过被最多人使用或被主导群体使用）时，双语现象很可能是单向的。

In an equilibrium situation, bilingualism would generally have been a two-way process many speakers of language X would also have competence in Y, and many speakers of Y would know a good deal of X. Modern societies are not egalitarian, and when one language has a prestige status (through being spoken by the largest number of people, or being used by the dominant group), bilingualism is likely to be one-way.

如果一个人懂两种语言，他们往往会在不同的情况下使用它们。当地语言将用于传统活动仪式、狩猎旅行等，而威望语言或接触语言则用于工作场所、教堂等更广泛的场合。威望语言也将在大多数或所有时间在学校、杂志和电视上使用。可能发生的情况是，使用当地语言的环境会逐渐缩小并消失。语言会随着它作为交流媒介的文化环境而逐渐消失。

If someone knows two languages they tend to use them in different circumstances. The local language will be employed in traditional activities ceremonies, hunting trips and the like and the prestige or contact language in wider circumstances in the workplace, in church, etc. The prestige language will also be employed, most or all of the time, in school, in magazines and on TV. What can happen is that the contexts in which the local language is used simply contract and disappear. The language slips from use with the cultural milieu in which it was the medium of communication.

这种语言的消亡在每个国家的少数群体（使用者少于 10,000 人）的语言中都发生过或正在发生。

This type of language loss has happened or is happening with the languages of small minority groups (those with less than 10,000 speakers) in every country.

从 20 世纪 60 年代末开始，美国的纳瓦霍人、澳大利亚的土著人、新西兰的毛利人等民族的自豪感又开始复苏。人们重新树立了对自己身份和语言的自豪感。但他们也意识到，这种语言正在逐渐被人们遗忘，大多数孩子都没有学会它。人们做出了巨大的努力来试图扭转这一趋势。例如，在新西兰，现在有毛利语授课的幼儿园、小学和中学。然而，这一计划收效甚微；许多毛利儿童讲的是一种混合了毛利语和英语的克里奥尔语。

From about the late 1960s there has been a resurgence of pride in ethnic identity among Navajos in the USA, among Aborigines in Australia, among Maoris in New Zealand, and so on. People have reasserted a pride in their identity and in their language. But they have also become aware that the language is gradually slipping from use, that it is not being learnt by most children. Strenuous efforts have been displayed to try to reverse this trend. In New Zealand, for instance, there are now Maori-medium kindergartens, primary schools and high schools. However, this program is having only limited success; many Maori children are talking in a developing creole that mixes Maori with English.

除了幼儿时期，语言学习是一件很难的事情，需要认真运用和集中注意力。学习语言必须有功利性的理由，而不是出于民族自豪感（从最近的经验来看）。

A language is a difficult thing to learn, other than as a young child, and requires application and concentration. There has to be a utilitarian reason for learning it, something more (to judge from recent experience) than ethnic pride.

同样，任何一种语言一旦在日常生活中停止使用，就永远不会再复兴。有时人们会提到希伯来语作为这一说法的假定反例。但希伯来语一直在使用，既作为书面媒介（在书籍、期刊和信件中），也用于宗教仪式。83它逐渐发展成为一个群体的第一语言，这个群体确实付出了不同寻常的努力和奉献，但这个群体具有政治统一性。希伯来语并不是作为少数民族的小语种而出现的，而是作为一个国家的官方和权威语言而出现的。只有在这些情况下，这种复兴才有可能发生。

It is also the case that no language once it has ceased to be used in everyday life has ever been revived. Mention is sometimes made of Hebrew as a putative counterexample to this statement. But Hebrew was always in use, both as a written medium (in books, journals and correspondence) and in religious services.83 It was augmented into the first language of a group which did take unusual application and dedication but this group had a political unity. Hebrew did not burst out as the minor language of a minority group, but as the official and prestige language of a nation. Only in these circumstances would such a resurgence be likely to happen.

在世界偏远地区，有许多小民族，他们的语言目前似乎没有受到威胁。这仅仅是因为他们与外界的交流很少。过去五年来，我一直在亚马逊南部的贾拉瓦拉人中工作。贾拉瓦拉人大约有 150 人，居住在 7 个偏远的丛林村庄，所有村庄都以贾拉瓦拉语为第一语言，但几乎所有人都只懂一点葡萄牙语（用于与附近的白人交易衣服、弹药、电池、盐、糖等）。贾拉瓦拉人有正当的愿望，希望获得与巴西其他公民相同的社会福利，如学校、医疗站、电视等。当这种情况发生时，语言必然会受到影响。人口很少；如果一些贾拉瓦拉人愿意搬家，住在最近的城镇，这将扰乱社区并威胁到语言。如果世界继续按照目前的方式发展，贾拉瓦拉人失去传统文化和语言只是时间问题，巴西其他地区和世界其他地区也已经发生过这种情况。对于亚马逊、新几内亚或非洲的这么小的群体来说，保留自己的语言的唯一方法就是与世界其他地方保持隔绝。

There are many small ethnic groups in the more remote parts of the world whose languages appear, at the present time, not to be threatened. This is simply because they have as yet little communication with the outside world. During the past five years I have worked among the Jarawara people, in Southern Amazonia. There are about 150 of them, in 7 remote jungle villages, all with Jarawara as first language, but almost all with a rudimentary knowledge of Portuguese (for trading with nearby whites for clothing, ammunition, batteries, salt, sugar and the like). The Jarawara have justifiable aspirations to be accorded the same social benefits as other citizens of Brazil a school, a medical post, access to TV. When this happens it is bound to impinge upon the language. The population is small; if some Jarawara should prefer to move, and live in the nearest town, it will disrupt the community and threaten the language. If the world continues on its present course, it is just a matter of time before the Jarawara lose their traditional culture and language, as has happened in other parts of Brazil and other parts of the world. The only way for such a small group in the Amazon, in New Guinea or in Africa to maintain its own language is to remain in isolation from the rest of the world.

我们可以做点什么。书写可以很好地用于编写供当地学校使用的入门书（尽管如果孩子们不在家里使用当地语言，他们永远不会仅仅因为在学校学习当地语言而说当地语言）。书写也可以用来记录传统故事和歌曲。在语言消失之前，可以将其记录下来。语言的消失可以稍微减缓一点；但它无法停止或逆转。

Something can be done. Writing can be put to good use in producing primers for use in local schools (although children will never speak a local language from just having it taught to them in school, if it is not also used in the home). And writing can also be used to record traditional stories and songs. The language can be documented, before it vanishes. The loss of a language can be slowed a little; but it cannot be halted or reversed.

应该关注基督教传教士的影响，因为在过去的四五个世纪里，他们在记录语言方面发挥了重要作用，往往加速了语言的消亡，而最近他们又试图帮助语言生存下来。

It is appropriate to pay some attention to the effect of Christianmissionaries since they have for the past four or five centuries played a major role in recording languages, often in hastening their demise, and more recently in attempting to assist their survival.

早期在美洲的天主教传教士经常使用武力（加上永恒诅咒的威胁）迫使当地群体放弃其文化、宗教和语言。最近，福音派和其他（包括一些天主教）团体采取了不同的立场。他们希望将《新约》翻译成当地语言，以便人们可以用自己的语言接受基督教。令人悲伤的是，这些语言中的每一种都在减少使用或消亡。翻译完成后，完全没有使用这种语言的人，这是意料之中的事。引用两个澳大利亚的例子，瑟尔克尔德（1857 年，1892 年出版：126）在介绍他的圣经译本时哀叹，在他研究阿瓦巴卡尔的 20 年里，这种语言已经不再使用：“在这种情况下，圣路加福音的翻译现在只能成为一件令人好奇的作品，记录一个曾经存在过的部落的语言。” 140 年后，在大陆的另一端，吉恩·柯顿 (Jean Kirton) 经过 30 年的研究，研究了 Yanyula 的语法并翻译了部分圣经，他“深感悲痛”地发现，孩子们不再学习这种语言了（Kirton 和 Charlie 1996：x）。

The early Catholic missionaries in the Americas often applied force (plus threats of eternal damnation) to get an indigenous group to abandon its culture, religion and language. More recently, evangelical and other (including some Catholic) groups have adopted a different stance. They wish to translate the New Testament into the local language so that the people may adopt Christianity in their own language. The sad part of it is that every one of these languages is diminishing in use or dying. It is not unknown for there to be no speakers left at all, by the time the translation is completed. To quote two Australian examples, Threlkeld (1857, published 1892: 126) introduced the publication of his Bible translation by lamenting that, during the 20 years he was working on Awabakal, the language had ceased to be used: 'under such circumstances, the translation of the Gospel by St Luke can only be now a work of curiosity a record of the language of a tribe that once existed'. And, 140 years later at the other end of the continent, Jean Kirton after 30 years of studying the grammar of Yanyula and translating parts of the Bible noted 'with deep personal sorrow' that the language was no longer being learnt by children (Kirton and Charlie 1996: x).

据我所知，几乎在所有情况下，当《新约》被翻译成当地语言时，那些能读懂的人也能用通用语（英语、西班牙语、葡萄牙语等，或克里奥尔语）阅读。尽管传教士经常试图用当地语言而不是通用语来教授读写能力，但情况却并非如此。因此，将《圣经》翻译成小语种（使用人数不到 10,000 人左右）并不能让那些本来就读不懂的人获得这些材料。当然，它确实让这些材料以当地语言的形式出现，一些使用当地语言的人可能会在一两代人中重视这一点。但随之而来的是试图用一种普遍的世界宗教取代与民族认同密切相关的传统宗教。这往往会加速融入世界文化，从而迅速导致人们远离当地语言。

In almost every case I know of, by the time the New Testament had been translated into an indigenous language, those people who could read it were also able to read it in the lingua franca (English, Spanish, Portuguese, etc., or a creole). And this despite the fact that the missionaries had often tried to teach literacy in the local language but not in the lingua franca. Thus, Bible translation into small languages (with less than 10,000 or so speakers) does not make this material available to anyone who would not be able to read it anyway. Of course it does make it available in the local language, and some speakers may for one or two generations value this. But a concomitant effect is the attempt to replace the traditional religion which is intimately connected with ethnic identity by a general world religion. This tends to hasten assimilation into the world culture, which rapidly leads to movement away from the local language.

传教士有时会不自觉地引入来自自己社会的思想，而这些思想会对当地情况产生有害影响。84其中一个是声望语言或方言的观念。斐济有数百种当地方言，但早期的传教士决定将《圣经》翻译成一种方言，即巴乌语。巴乌语在当地确实声望有限，但传教士赋予了它更多的声望；这是逐渐削弱其他方言的个性并使其趋向巴乌语的主要因素（如本节前面 (b) 中所述）。在巴西的沃佩斯河地区，天主教传教士发现人们使用多种语言。他们选择了在当地声望有限的图卡诺语作为他们工作的唯一载体。结果是，随着人们将他们的语言忠诚度转向图卡诺语，该地区的其他语言已经消亡或濒临消亡。（当然，随着时间的推移，在葡萄牙语的压力下，图卡诺语也会逐渐消失。）

Missionaries tend sometimes unwittingly to introduce ideas from their own society which have a deleterious effect on the local situation.84 One is the idea of a prestige language or dialect. There are hundreds of local dialects in Fiji but the early missionaries decided to translate the Bible into just one dialect, Bau. It is true that Bau had a limited local prestige but the missionaries endowed it with more; this has been a major factor in gradually eroding the individual characteristics of other dialects, and causing them to converge towards Bau (as discussed under (b), earlier in this section). In the Vaupés River region of Brazil, Catholic missionaries found a multitude of languages spoken. They chose Tucano, which had a limited local prestige, as the sole vehicle for their work. The result is that other languages of the region have died, or are close to death, as people switch their linguistic allegiance to Tucano. (In time, of course, Tucano will also fade, under pressure from Portuguese.)

传教士还会产生其他影响，既有好的也有坏的。他们的存在带来了外部世界，带来了一套不同的文化价值观。在许多情况下，这种联系已经建立；在其余情况下，这种联系无论如何都会建立起来。具有适当态度的传教士可以帮助部落群体适应正在闯入他们生活的外部世界；他们可以保护他们免受剥削和剥夺，并通过提供药品和适当的教育形式来提供帮助。如果传教士学习当地语言，将有助于人们树立对自己身份的自豪感。这可能有助于减缓语言的消失85（尽管如前所述，它永远无法阻止或逆转它）。

Missionaries can have other effects, both good and bad. Their presence brings in the outside world, with a different set of cultural values. In many cases this contact had already been established; in the remainder it would have happened anyway. Missionaries with the appropriate sort of attitude can assist a tribal group to come to terms with the outside world that is stealing into their lives; they can protect them from exploitation and dispossession, and help by providing medicines and an appropriate form of schooling. If the missionary learns the local language it will assist the people to assert pride in their own identity. This may help slow the loss of language85 (although, as stressed before, it can never halt or reverse it).

近年来，我有机会近距离观察了巴西的一些福音传教士。他们中有些人对传统文化（包括宗教86）抱有基本的尊重，发挥了有益的作用。但也有其他人属于不同的类型，他们对土著社区的文化造成了巨大的破坏。这种人对“不信教者”不宽容，强行压制传统宗教，支持基督教，本质上是通过恐吓阴谋来传播“基督教”信息。他们的目的基本上是将印第安人转变为传教士理想中的中产阶级美国郊区社区。我在澳大利亚也目睹了这种运动的后期阶段，那里的人们失去了原有的身份，但没有获得任何可以取代它的东西。他们失去了自己的文化和语言，以及所有精神。

During recent years I have had the opportunity to observe, at close quarters, a number of evangelical missionaries in Brazil. There are some with a basic respect for traditional culture (including religion86) who fill a useful role. But there are others of a different ilk, who do great cultural damage to indigenous communities. This type is intolerant of 'unbelievers' and forcibly suppresses the traditional religion in favour of Christianity, getting their 'Christian' message over essentially by a conspiracy of fear. Their aim is, basically, to convert the Indians into something like the missionaries' ideal of a middle-class suburban American community. I have also witnessed, in Australia, the later stages of such a campaign, where a people have lost their original identity but not acquired anything to take its place. They have lost their own culture and language, and all spirit.

有些传教士从事有用的语言工作，提供语法和词典。事实上，有关濒临消亡和濒危语言的出版材料中，超过一半来自传教组织；质量有好有坏。（最不宽容的传教士往往也从事最差的语言工作，这也许并不奇怪。）

Some missionaries do useful linguistic work, providing grammars and dictionaries. Indeed, well over half the material being published on dying and endangered languages is from missionary organisations; the quality of it varies from good to poor. (It is perhaps unsurprising that the most intolerant missionaries tend also to do the poorest linguistic work.)

 

 

9 当今优先事项

9 Today's Priorities

现代世界的多样性丧失已达到临界点。现存的森林中含有具有药用价值的植物，这些植物为森林居民所知。在许多情况下，现代医学尚未研究它们的性质和价值。如果这些植物因砍伐森林而被毁坏，或者如果了解这些植物的人被同化到国家主流，从而失去传统知识，那么现代医学又怎么可能研究它们呢？

The loss of diversity in the modern world is reaching critical proportions. The remaining forests contain plants with medicinal uses that are known to the people who live in the forests. In many cases their nature and value have not yet been investigated by modern medicine. How could they ever be, if the plants are destroyed as a consequence of forest-clearing, or if the people who know them are assimilated into the mainstream of their nation, thereby losing traditional knowledge?

语言是人类最宝贵的资源。每种语言都有不同的音系、形态、句法和语义组织。只有通过研究所有语言的不同可能性，我们才能大致了解人类大脑与语言活动相关的本质。通过研究一些鲜为人知的语言中意义的组织方式，语言学家可能会揭示语义结构的某些普遍特征，或发展出一些有助于解决现代世界问题的新思维方式。

Language is the most precious human resource. Each language has a different phonological, morphological, syntactic and semantic organisation from every other. Only by studying the varied possibilities across all languages can we gain a general picture of the nature of the human brain as it relates to language activity. By examining the ways meanings are organised in some little-known language, the linguist may shed light on some universal feature of semantic structure, or evolve some new mode of thinking that could help to deal with problems in the modern world.

下一节将提供语言参数、其相互关系及其连续变化的例子，说明记录每种已知语言的重要性。第 9.2 节揭露了现代语言学的一个神话，这种神话正在削弱该学科。第 9.3 节详细说明了自称语言学家的人的工作重点应该是什么。

The next section will provide examples of linguistic parameters, their interrelations and their sequential changes, illustrating why it is important to document every known language. §9.2 exposes a myth of modern linguistics that is crippling the discipline. And §9.3 details what the work priorities should be for people who call themselves linguists.

 

 

9.1 为什么要费心？

9.1 Why Bother?

据估计，在当今世界使用的 5,000 多种语言中，到 2100 年，至少有四分之三（有人说 90% 或更多）将不再使用，而这首先是由于欧洲殖民者使用标点符号。在这些语言消失之前，记录这些语言是一项紧迫的任务。

It is estimated that of the 5,000 or so languages spoken in the world today at least three-quarters (some people say 90% or more) will have ceased to be spoken by the year 2100, as a consequence of the punctuations engendered in the first place by European colonisation. It is an urgent task to document these languages before they disappear.

对这种请求，典型的顽固回应是：何必呢？这些语言都是无足轻重的语言，由无足轻重的民族、奇怪的部落和少数群体使用，它们会因为世界上伟大的文明国家不断向全球社会迈进而消失。一群狩猎者和采集者整天跋涉在炎热的沙漠中寻找蜥蜴和草籽，一群刀耕火种的农民每隔几年就搬一次村子，因为他们已经耗尽了那片森林的食物资源，他们的语言有什么意义呢？这些语言怎么能告诉我们任何我们不知道的东西呢？我们已经研究了法语、德语、西班牙语、英语和俄语的丰富资源，也许还加入了芬兰语、土耳其语、希伯来语、阿拉伯语、印地语、日语、中文和斯瓦希里语。适者生存。让这些原始民族的贫乏语言畅通无阻地消失吧。也许可以记录其中的一些，作为样本，但尝试更多则浪费时间和资源。

A typical hard-nosed response to this plea is: Why bother? These are insignificant languages spoken by insignificant peoples, odd tribes and minority groups that will disappear simply because of the relentless advancement of the great civilised nations of the world towards a global community. What interest can there be in the language of a group of hunters and gatherers who spend their days trudging over hot desert sand looking for lizards and grass seed, or of a group of slash-and-burn agriculturalists who move their village every few years because they've exhausted the food resources of that patch of forest? How can these languages tell us anything that we don't know already from studying the rich resources of French, German, Spanish, English and Russian, perhaps throwing in for good measure Finnish, Turkish, Hebrew, Arabic, Hindi, Japanese, Chinese and Swahili? It is the fittest who will survive. Let these meagre languages of primitive peoples pass into oblivion unimpeded. Maybe record a bit of a few of them, as a sample, but it is a waste of time and resources to attempt more.

这种回应形式反映了几种错觉。首先，物质文化有限的人必须拥有相对简陋的语言。事实往往恰恰相反。小型政治团体通常具有复杂的社会结构，具有清晰的分类关系和共同义务体系。（相比之下，城市居民的社交网络还处于初级阶段，可以恰当地描述为原始的。）与这种社会结构相关的往往是复杂的代词系统，具有多种数字区别（可能有单独的代词表示“你（单数）”、“你们两个”和“你们所有人”，有时还有“你们几个”）。非单数第一人称通常有一个包容/排他的区别，这涉及两个不同的代词表示“我们两个”，一个指“我和你”，另一个指“我和你以外的其他人”。

This form of response reflects several illusions. The first is that people with a limited material culture must have a proportionately threadbare language. The reverse tends to be the case. Small political groups generally have an intricate social structure with an articulated system of classificatory relationships and communal obligations. (In contrast, the social networks of city dwellers are rudimentary, and could appropriately be described as primitive.) Associated with this social structure tend to go complex systems of pronouns, with several number distinctions (there may be separate pronouns for 'you (singular)', 'you two' and 'you all' and sometimes also 'you few'). There is often an inclusive/exclusive distinction for non-singular first person this involves two different pronouns for 'we two', one referring to 'me and you' and the other to 'me and someone else, other than you'.

现代语言学发现，所有语言在整体复杂性方面大致相同。不同语言的复杂性各不相同，一种语言的动词结构简单，名词复杂，另一种语言则相反。我们只有分别研究每种语言，并根据一个共同的理论框架比较它们的特征，才能了解人类语言的可能性范围。假设几百年前一颗巨大的陨石落在南部非洲，消灭了所有居民。谁会想到喀哒声可以用作语音？如果有人告诉我们喀哒声可以用于词语，谁会相信一种语言会有 55 种对比喀哒声，就像布什曼的 !Xu * 方言中发现的那样（Snyman 1970: 4950）？

It is a finding of modern linguistics that all languages are roughly equal in terms of overall complexity. The areas of complexity vary between languages one may have a simple verbal structure but complex nouns while another reverses this. We can only get an idea of the range of possibilities available to human languages by looking at every language individually and comparing their features in terms of a common theoretical framework. Suppose that a large meteor had fallen on southern Africa a few hundred years ago, wiping out all the inhabitants. Who would have imagined that clicks could be used as speech sounds? And if we were told that clicks could be used in words, who would have believed that one language could have fifty-five contrastive clicks, as are found in the !Xu * dialect of Bushman (Snyman 1970: 4950)?

所有语言中都有某些语法类别，但它们的实现方式不同。以否定为例。在欧洲语言中，从句否定用一个助词（如英语中的 not）表示，该助词通常位于动词之前。事实上，这是世界上所有语言中最常见的否定标记类型。但它并不是唯一的类型。在相当多的语言中，否定是用动词的词缀、前缀或后缀表示的。在西北高加索语系的卡巴尔达语中，否定在限定从句中用动词后缀 -q'em* 表示，但在非限定从句中用动词前缀 me-* 表示（Kumakhov and Vamling 1995: 96）。在少数语言中，否定只能通过主动词来表示，其字面意思是“事实并非如此 [那...]”。在斐济语中，否定动词是 sega，要表达“我没看见你”必须使用：

Certain grammatical categories are found in all languages, but they are realised in different ways. Take negation for instance. In European languages clausal negation is shown by a particle (like English not) which typically comes immediately before the verb. This is in fact the most common type of negative marking across the languages of the world. But it is not the only type. In quite a few languages negation is shown by an affix to the verb a prefix or a suffix. In Kabardian, from the North-West Caucasian family, negation is shown by a suffix -q'em* to the verb in a finite clause but by a verbal prefix me-* in a non-finite clause (Kumakhov and Vamling 1995: 96). In a few languages negation can only be shown through a main verb which literally means 'it is not the case [that . . .]'. In Fijian the negative verb is sega and to express 'I didn't see you' one must use:

（1）esega[ni-urai-cii'o]

(1)esega[ni-urai-cii'o]

事实并非如此，我看见了你

itbe not the caseTHAT-Isee-TRANSITIVISERyou

字面意思是“我看见你不是事实”或“我看见你不是事实”。 （更详细的内容见 Dixon 1988：40，27984。）

This is, literally, 'that I saw you is not the case' or 'it is not the case that I saw you'. (Fuller details are in Dixon 1988: 40, 27984.)

人们普遍认为所有语言都有三种时态：过去时、现在时和将来时。但事实并非如此。例如，圣经希伯来语没有时态，而是使用语法标记来表示完成体（具有时间结束的动作，例如“约翰唱了一首赞美诗”）或未完成体（没有指定时间结束的动作，例如“约翰唱了”）。斐济语有过去时和将来时态标记，但这些是可选的；例如，句子 (1) 中没有时态说明。Snyman (1970) 报告称，布什曼语 !Xu * 没有时态或体态的语法标记，尽管它有时间副词，例如“现在”、“很久以前”、“昨天”、“最后”、“然后”和“将”。

It is a common belief that all languages have three tenses past, present and future. This is far from being so. Biblical Hebrew, for instance, had no tenses, using instead grammatical marking for aspect perfective (an action with a temporal end, e.g. 'John sang a hymn') or imperfective (an action with no temporal end specified, e.g. 'John sang'). In Fijian there are past and future tense markers but these are optional; there is no tense specification in sentence (1), for instance. Snyman (1970) reports that the Bushman language !Xu * has no grammatical marking for tense or aspect, although it does have temporal adverbs such as 'now', 'long ago', 'yesterday', 'finally', 'then' and 'will'.

在确实具有时态语法系统的语言中，过去/现在/将来的区别相当罕见；这种区别在古典希腊语中很常见，但在其他一些语言中很少见。最常见的时态系统只有两种选择，过去和非过去；例如，在僧伽罗语和东非尼罗河语言图尔卡纳语中就可以看到这种区别。而且，还有比我们熟悉的欧洲语言中更复杂的系统。例如，在澳大利亚和新几内亚之间的托雷斯海峡西部岛屿上使用的语言有不少于四种过去时（“昨晚”、“昨天”、“不久前”和“很久以前”）和三种将来时（“马上”、“不久前”和“很久将来”）。

In languages that do have a grammatical system of tenses, a past/present/future distinction is rather rare; it is found in Classical Greek but in few other languages. The most common tense system has just two choices, past and non-past; this is found in Singhalese and in Turkana, a Nilotic language from East Africa, for instance. And there can be much more complex systems than are found in the familiar languages of Europe. For instance, the language spoken on the western islands of the Torres Strait, between Australia and New Guinea, has no less than four past tenses ('last night', 'yesterday', 'near past' and 'remote past') and three futures ('immediate', 'near' and 'remote future').

否定和时态是常见的类别。我们一直在讨论它们的不同实现方式以及系统的大小。但是，有些语法规范在最广泛使用的语言中根本找不到。其中之一就是证据性。它涉及对陈述所基于的证据类型的强制性说明，例如，说话者是否亲自观察到了它，或者有人告诉他们，或者他们推断了它，或者假设了它（或者只是有一种“直觉”，认为它一定是发生的事情）。证据性存在于世界各地的语言中，如巴尔干半岛、藏缅语、古典日语（但它几乎在现代日语中消失了）、一些北美语言和许多南美语言，包括安第斯山脉和亚马逊河流域（参见 Chafe 和 Nichols，1986 年的论文）。

Negation and tense are familiar categories. We have been talking about the different ways they can be realised, and the size of the system. But there are some grammatical specifications that are not found at all in the most widely spoken languages. One of these is Evidentiality. It involves an obligatory specification of the type of evidence on which a statement is based, e.g. whether the speaker observed it themself, or someone told them, or they inferred it, or assumed it (or just had a 'gut feeling' that it must be what happened). Evidentiality is found in languages from various parts of the world the Balkans, Tibeto-Burman languages, Classical Japanese (but it has almost been lost from Modern Japanese), some languages from North America and many from South America, both on the Andes and in the Amazon basin (see the papers in Chafe and Nichols, 1986).

有些语言只有两个词的证据对比（最常见的是：目击者/非目击者），但其他语言则有其他区别。最发达的系统出现在图卡诺安语系的多种语言和阿拉瓦克语系的一种语言中，这些语言共同使用于沃佩斯河流域一个紧密联系的小语言区，与哥伦比亚和巴西重叠（见§3.2）。这里有一个五种证据选择的系统（例如，见 Barnes 1984）。假设我想说“狗吃了鱼”。我必须包括以下证据标记之一：

Some languages have just a two-term evidentiality contrast (most commonly: eyewitness/non-eyewitness) but others make additional distinctions. The most developed system is found in a number of languages of the Tucanoan family and one language of the Arawak family, spoken together in a small, tightly knit linguistic area in the Vaupés River basin, overlapping Colombia and Brazil see §3.2. Here there is a system of five evidentiality choices (see, for instance, Barnes 1984). Suppose that I want to say 'The dog ate the fish.' I must include one of the following evidentiality markers:

(a) 如果我看到狗吃鱼就会用视觉来表达。

(a) Visual would be used if I saw the dog eat the fish.

(b) 如果我听到厨房里的狗叫声（但没有看到它）或者，比如说，我闻到狗呼吸中带有鱼腥味，则使用非视觉方法。

(b) Non-visual would be used if I heard the dog in the kitchen (but did not see it) or if, say, I smelled fish on the dog's breath.

(c) 假设狗周围的地板上铺着鱼骨，它看起来很满足，就像刚吃过一顿好饭一样，那么就可以使用“明显”这个词。

(c) Apparent could be used if there are fish bones spread on the floor around the dog, which looks satisfied, as if after a good meal.

(d) 报告有人告诉我狗吃了鱼。

(d) Reported someone told me that the dog ate the fish.

(e) 假设鱼是生的，而人们不吃生鱼，所以一定是狗叼走了它。

(e) Assumed the fish was raw and people do not eat raw fish so it must have been the dog that took it.

如果用英语强制说明证据，那不是很棒吗？想想警察的工作会变得多么轻松。这会如何让政客们对国家预算状况更加诚实。然而，详细的证据系统往往只存在于非工业化人群中。为什么？这是一个目前很少被理解的话题，但它肯定与人们对谈话的具体性、对信息交流的慷慨程度以及对说真话的态度有关。

Wouldn't it be wonderful if there was obligatory specification of evidence in English? Think how much easier the job of a policeman would be. And how it would make politicians be more honest about the state of the national budget. However, detailed systems of evidentials tend to be found only among non-industrialised people. Why? This is a topic at present little understood, but it must surely relate to the people's attitude towards specificity in talking, towards how generous one should be in the communication of information, and towards telling the truth.

最近对亚马逊地区证据性的研究有两个主要发现。（a）证据性语法类别必须至少在六个不同的地方和时间独立发展。亚马逊盆地人民的文化倾向似乎使他们倾向于将“证据性质”发展为一种强制性语法系统。（b）一旦一种语言发展出证据性系统，它就会扩散到邻近的语言中。邻近的语言接管了证据性的概念，但从其内部资源中发展了证据性选择的实际语法标记。（见 Aikhenvald 和 Dixon，即将出版。）

A recent study of evidentiality in Amazonia has two main findings. (a) That a grammatical category of evidentiality must have developed, independently, in at least six different places and times. It appears that the cultural orientation of people in the Amazon basin is such that they tend to evolve 'nature of evidence' as an obligatory grammatical system. (b) That once a language develops an evidentiality system, this tends to diffuse into neighbouring languages. The next-door languages take over the category the idea of evidentiality but develop the actual grammatical marking of evidentiality choices from their internal resources. (See Aikhenvald and Dixon, forthcoming.)

这件事给我们一个教训。如果语言学家没有在接种黄热病、伤寒、破伤风和各种肝炎疫苗、携带抗疟药等后前往亚马逊丛林研究这些语言，我们就无法充分认识到人类语言的一个重要维度，即复杂的证据系统。

There is a lesson to be learnt from this. If linguists hadn't gone out into the Amazonian jungle after having inoculations against yellow fever, typhoid, tetanus and all the varieties of hepatitis; loading up with malaria pills; and so on to study these languages, we wouldn't have full awareness of an important dimension of human language, complex systems of evidentials.

为了最后说明人类语言的多样性、类别之间的相关性以及相关变化，我们将简要介绍两个参数：（1）标记主语和宾语功能的不同方式；（2）不同种类的形容词类别。

As a final illustration of the variety across human language, correlations between categories, and linked changes, we will briefly look at two parameters: (1) different ways of marking subject and object functions; and (2) different kinds of adjective classes.

1 标记句法功能

1 Marking Syntactic Function

每种语言的主要子句类型都以动词为中心，动词是子句的头部。动词需要一些核心参数（主语和宾语），这些参数取决于动词。任何语法都要求区分主语和宾语，这样人们才能知道谁在对谁做某事。简单来说，有三种基本方法可以实现这一点。

The major clause type in every language centres on a verb, as head of the clause. The verb requires a number of core arguments (subject and object) which depend on the verb. A requirement on any grammar is to distinguish between subject and object, so that one can tell who is doing something to whom. Simplifying a little, there are three basic ways of achieving this.

（一个） 按元素顺序

因此，在英语中，主语在动词之前，宾语在动词之后；这样，Fred hit Bill 与 Bill hit Fred 就区分开来。

Thus in English the subject precedes the verb and the object follows; by this means, Fred hit Bill is distinguished from Bill hit Fred.

（二） 通过标记家属87

在许多语言中，动词的每个论元都会添加后缀，以表明其句法功能。例如，在拉丁语中，单数主语用 -us 标记，单数宾语用 -um 标记，名词的变格从一而终。因此，Domin-us serv-um audit（“主人-主语奴隶-宾语听到”）是“主人听到奴隶的声音”，而 Serv-us domin-um audit 是“奴隶听到主人的声音”。这些句子中的单词可以按任何顺序出现，而不会改变含义，因为主语和宾语由名词的结尾表示。88

In many languages a suffix is added to each argument of the verb, indicating its syntactic function. In Latin, for instance, a singular subject is marked by -us and a singular object by -um with nouns from one declension. Thus Domin-us serv-um audit ('master-SUBJECT slave-OBJECT hears') is 'The master hears the slave' and Serv-us domin-um audit is 'The slave hears the master.' The words in these sentences can occur in any order, without change of meaning, since what is subject and what is object are shown by endings on the nouns.88

（三） 头上的记号

标记句法功能的第三种方式出现在动词具有强制性前缀和/或后缀的语言中，这些前缀和/或后缀提供有关主语和宾语的人称和数字（通常还有性别）的信息。在这里，动词及其代词词缀可以组成一个完整的句子。例如，在卡巴尔达语中，人们可以说 0122-01.gif“他们看见了我”，其中前缀 s- 表示“我”是宾语，后面的 -a- 表示“他们”是主语（Kumakhov 和 Vamling 1995：96）。89

The third way of marking syntactic function is found in languages where the verb has obligatory prefixes and/or suffixes providing information about the person and number (and often gender as well) of subject and object. Here the verb, with its pronominal affixes, can make up a complete sentence. For example, in Kabardian one can say 0122-01.gif 'they saw me', where the prefix s- indicates 'me' as object and the following -a- is 'they' as subject (Kumakhov and Vamling 1995: 96).89

现在让我们看看语言如何从一种标记类型转换为另一种标记类型；这里我们将重点关注类型 (b) 和 (c)。几乎所有语言变化都是循环的，语言可以很容易地从中心标记转换为从属标记，然后再转换回来。

Let us now look at how a language can switch from one type ofmarking to another; here we will focus on types (b) and (c). Almost all linguistic change is cyclic, and a language can readily switch from head marking to dependent marking, and then back again.

（我） 从头部标记到依赖性标记

原始阿拉瓦克语是南美洲最大语系的祖先语言，据重建，该语言只有词头标记。及物动词的主语（A）用动词前缀标记，宾语（O）用后缀标记。90所有现代阿拉瓦克语都保留了主语前缀。大约一半保留了 O 后缀，但其余的已经丢失了。塔利亚纳语是这一组语言之一，它获得了一些从属标记，即后缀 -nuku，可以添加到任何非主语功能的名词中。毫无疑问，塔利亚纳语是通过来自同一语言区内所有具有从属标记的图卡诺安语的扩散压力而发展出从属标记的。重要的是，一半的词头标记（宾语部分）已经丢失，而一些从属标记（对宾语和其他非主语成分）已经获得，这实际上是补偿（Aikhenvald 1996）。

Proto-Arawak, the ancestor language of the most extensive family in South America, is reconstructed to have had just head marking. With a transitive verb, the subject (A) was marked by a prefix to the verb and the object (O) by a suffix.90 All modern Arawak languages retain the subject prefix. About half keep the O suffix but the remainder have lost it. Tariana is one of this group and it has gained some dependent marking, a suffix -nuku which can be added to a noun in any non-subject function. Tariana has undoubtedly developed dependent marking through diffusional pressure from the Tucanoan languages spoken in the same linguistic area, which all have dependent marking. The important point is that half the head marking (the object part) has been lost, and some dependent marking (on objects and other non-subject constituents) has been gained, effectively in compensation (Aikhenvald 1996).

（二） 从依赖性标记到头部标记

显然，在早期阶段，澳大利亚语言完全是依赖标记，使用格后缀来指示句法功能。在一个地理区域，语言已经发展出包括前缀在内的复杂动词结构；动词有强制性代词词缀，表示主语和宾语的人称和数。在其中一些语言中，性别也由动词词缀标记，至少对于第三人称是如此。正是头部标记的一般特征已经传播到该地区的所有语言中，每种语言都独立地从其自己的自由代词发展出绑定代词词缀。在所有语言中，（a）“我看见他”和（b）“他看见我”都可以表达为一个单词的句子，但动词成分的排序规则不同。使用 A 表示主语前缀，O 表示宾语前缀或后缀，主要有以下几种可能性：

It is clear that at an earlier stage Australian languages were entirely dependent marking, using case suffixes to indicate syntactic function. In one geographical area the languages have developed complex verb structures including prefixes; there are obligatory pronominal affixes to the verb, indicating the person and number of subject and object. In some of these languages, gender is also marked by verbal affixes, at least for third person. It is just the general feature of head marking that has diffused across all the languages of the region each language has developed bound pronominal affixes independently, from its own free pronouns. In all the languages (a) 'I saw him' and (b) 'He saw me' can be expressed as a one-word sentence, but there are different rules for ordering the components of the verb. Using A for subject prefix and O for object prefix or suffix, there are the following main possibilities:

AO-动词，即 (a)‘I-him-saw’，(b)‘he-me-saw’，例如在 Djamindjung 中；

A-O-verb, i.e. (a) 'I-him-saw', (b) 'he-me-saw', e.g. in Djamindjung;

OA-动词，即 (a) 'him-I-saw', (b) 'me-he-saw'，例如 Ungarinjin 中；

O-A-verb, i.e. (a) 'him-I-saw', (b) 'me-he-saw', e.g. in Ungarinjin;

动词-O，即（a）“我看见了他”，（b）“他看见了我”，例如在恩吉纳语中；

A-verb-O, i.e. (a) 'I-saw-him', (b) 'he-saw-me', e.g. in Njigina;

A 和 O 都是动词词根的前缀，但顺序不取决于句法功能，而是取决于人称：第一人称标记位于第二人称或第三人称形式之前，第二人称位于第三人称之前（无论句法功能如何

both A and O are prefixes to the verb root but the ordering depends not on syntactic function but on person: a first person marker precedes a second or third person form and second person precedes third person (whatever the syntactic functions

nvolved），即（a）‘我-他-看见’，（b）‘我-他-看见’，例如在 Mangarrayi 中。91

nvolved), i.e. (a) 'I-him-saw', (b) 'me-he-saw', e.g. in Mangarrayi.91

在带有头标记的语言中（包括第三人称的性别指定），动词的代词词缀足以表明论元的句法功能，因此不再需要依赖标记。澳大利亚大部分地区都存在作格后缀（标记 A 功能中的名词短语），其原始形式为 *-dju。一些带有头标记的语言保留了这种后缀（同化和弱化产生 -dji 或 -yi），但现在它只是可选使用。其他带有头标记的语言已经失去了它，现在已完成向完全带有头标记系统的转变。

In languages with head marking (where this includes gender specification for third person), the pronominal affixes to the verb adequately indicate the syntactic function of arguments, so that dependent marking is no longer needed. An ergative suffix (marking a noun phrase in A function) occurs over most of Australia with the original form *-dju. Some of the head-marking languages retain this (with assimilation and lenition giving -dji or -yi) but it is now used only optionally. Other head-marking languages have lost it, the shift to a fully head-marking system now being complete.

2 形容词类

2 Adjective Classes

世界上的语言中有两种形容词类。一种是开放类，有数百个形容词；可以通过借用其他语言或通过创造新词来增加新的形容词。另一种是小型的封闭类。有些语言只有五个形容词，其他语言可能有一百个，但在每种情况下都不能向类中添加任何新词。除欧洲外，各大洲都有小型形容词类的语言（见 Dixon 1982），它们具有相似的语义组成，通常包括指大小、颜色、年龄和价值的词。西非的伊博语只有八个形容词：“大”和“小”；“黑、暗”和“白、亮”；“新”和“旧”；以及“好”和“坏”（Welmers and Welmers 1969）。有必要问一问，在英语等语言中，其他被编码为形容词的概念会发生什么。同样，可以注意到一个普遍的趋势：指物理属性的词（“热”、“湿”、“重”）往往被放在动词类中（字面意思是“石头很重”），而指人类倾向的词（“悲伤”、“粗鲁”、“聪明”）往往是名词（字面意思是“她很聪明”）。

There are two kinds of adjective classes across the languages of the world. One is an open class with hundreds of members; new members can be added to the class, through borrowing from other languages or through coinages. The other is a small closed class. Some languages have only five adjectives, others may have a hundred, but in each case no new item can be added to the class. Languages with small adjective classes are found in every continent except Europe (see Dixon 1982), and they have similar semantic composition, typically including words referring to size, colour, age and value. Igbo, from West Africa, has just eight adjectives: 'large' and 'small'; 'black, dark' and 'white, light'; 'new' and 'old'; and 'good' and 'bad' (Welmers and Welmers 1969). It is relevant to ask what happens to other concepts that are coded as adjectives in languages such as English. Again, a general tendency can be noted words referring to physical properties ('hot', 'wet', 'heavy') tend to be placed in the verb class (one says, literally, 'the stone heavies') while words referring to human propensities ('sad', 'rude', 'clever') tend to be nouns (literally, 'she has cleverness').

大型开放形容词类分为四类：（a）形容词在语法属性上与名词非常相似，它们显示性别、数和格，就像名词一样（例如拉丁语和西班牙语）；（b）形容词在语法上与动词非常相似，例如，它们会根据时态或体而变化（如马来语）；（c）形容词兼具名词和动词的语法属性（例如北非的柏柏尔语）；（d）形容词的语法属性不同于名词和动词（例如英语）。类型 (c) 和 (d) 相当罕见，大多数具有大型形容词类的语言都属于类型 (a) 和 (b)。

Large open adjective classes fall into four types: (a) adjectives are very similar in their grammatical properties to nouns they show gender and number and case, like nouns (e.g. Latin and Spanish); (b) adjectives are grammatically very similar to verbs, e.g. they inflect for tense or aspect (as in Malay); (c) adjectives combine grammatical properties of nouns and of verbs (e.g. Berber languages from North Africa); (d) adjectives have grammatical properties which are distinct from those of nouns and of verbs (e.g. English). Types (c) and (d) are rather rare, most languages with large adjective classes being of types (a) and (b).

3 中心词/从属标记与形容词类型的相关性

3 Correlation between Head/Dependent Marking and Adjective Type

我们刚刚概述的两个参数之间存在很强的统计相关性。

There is a strong statistical correlation between the two parameters we have just outlined.

相关性

Correlations

（I） 以头为标记的语言往往具有 (b) 类型的形容词类，其中形容词在语法上与动词相似。

(I) Head-marking languages tend to have an adjective class of type (b), where adjectives are grammatically similar to verbs.

（II）依存标记语言往往具有（a）类型的形容词类，其中形容词在语法上与名词相似。

(II) Dependent-marking languages tend to have an adjective class of type (a), where adjectives are grammatically similar to nouns.

理由很明显。形容词往往处于事物的中心。名词和动词中任何一个带有句法功能标记，那很可能就是形容词类在语法上最相似的类。

The rationale is evident. Adjectives tend to be in the centre of things. Whichever of noun and verb bears the marking for syntactic function, that is likely to be the class to which the adjective class is grammatically most similar.

4 后续变化

4 Consequential Changes

我们已经说明了具有中心标记的语言如何向依赖标记转变，反之亦然。这些变化往往发生得相当快；它们很容易被重建。毫无疑问，一种语言可以从具有 (a) 类型的形容词类转变为具有 (b) 类型的形容词类，反之亦然，但所有迹象都表明，这种变化比中心标记和依赖标记之间的变化要慢得多。

We have illustrated how a language with head marking may shift towards dependent marking, and vice versa. These changes tend to take place quite rapidly; they can readily be reconstructed. There is no doubt that a language can change from having an adjective class of type (a) to having one of type (b), and vice versa, but all the indications are that such a change would be much slower than one between head and dependent marking.

我们可以回顾阿拉瓦克人和澳大利亚人在标记句法功能的技术转变方面的例子。

We can return to the Arawak and Australian examples of shift in the technique for marking syntactic function.

（我） 从头部标记到依赖性标记

原始阿拉瓦克语完全是头标记。我描述了塔利亚纳语如何失去了一些头标记并获得了一些从属标记。原始阿拉瓦克语似乎有一个开放的形容词类 (b)，像动词一样带有时态和体后缀。这在保留完整头标记的现代语言中仍然延续。然而，塔利亚纳语中的形容词虽然仍然带有时态和体后缀，但已经发展出一些与名词一致的属性。形容词和名词都可以（在塔利亚纳语中，但在其他阿拉瓦克语中则不行）与分类词一起出现，例如“圆形物体”分类词 -da，例如：

Proto-Arawak was entirely head marking. I described how Tariana has lost some head marking and gained some dependent marking. Proto-Arawak appears to have had an open adjective class of type (b), taking tense and aspect suffixes just like verbs. This is continued in the modern languages that retain full head marking. However, adjectives in Tariana while still taking tense and aspect suffixes have developed some properties that align them with nouns. Both adjectives and nouns can (in Tariana but not in other Arawak languages) occur with a classifier, e.g. the 'round thing' classifier -da, as in:

heku-da'圆树（树干）'

heku-da'round tree (trunk)'

树（名词）-分类器

tree (noun)-CLASSIFIER

matfia-da'美丽的圆形物体'

matfia-da'beautiful round thing'

美丽（形容词）-分类器

beautiful (adjective)-CLASSIFIER

总之，塔里安娜语已从头标记转变为混合头标记和从属标记的配置，与此相关的是，形容词正在从纯类型 (b) 系统（如动词）转变为具有某些类型 (a) 特征（某些属性如名词）的系统。

In summary, Tariana has shifted from a head-marking to a mixed-head-and-dependent-marking profile and, in correlation with this, adjectives are moving from a pure type (b) system (like verbs) to a system with some features of type (a) (some properties like nouns).

（二） 从依赖性标记到头部标记

我曾说过，在早期阶段，所有澳大利亚语言都是从属标记；许多语言现在仍然是从属标记，但北部的一个地区群体已经转变为主要或完全以头语标记为主。澳大利亚语言有大量形容词类，总是属于 (a) 类，在语法上与名词相似。92这与我们的相关性一致。

I have said that at an earlier stage all Australian languages were dependent marking; many still are but an areal group in the north have shifted to be predominantly or entirely head marking. Australian languages have large adjective classes, invariably of type (a), being grammatically similar to nouns.92 This is in keeping with our correlation.

北部地区的头标记发展得相当晚。我曾提出，形容词类类型的转变可能比从从属标记转变为头标记（或反之亦然）要慢得多。事实上，在一些头标记语言中，形容词类型才刚刚出现变化的迹象。例如，在埃米语中，形容词仍然采用与名词相同的格词缀，但它们在否定方面表现得像动词。名词用否定系词 piya 来否定，但动词和形容词用助词 way 来否定（Ford，即将出版）。

Head marking has developed rather recently in the northern area. I have suggested that a shift in type of adjective class is likely to be a slower matter than a shift from dependent to head marking (or vice versa). In fact, there are just the first signs of a change in adjective type, in some of the head-marking languages. In Emmi, for instance, adjectives still take the same case affixes as nouns, but they behave like verbs with respect to negation. A noun is negated by the negative copula piya, but verb and adjective are negated by the particle way (Ford, forthcoming).

根据相关性（I）和相关性（II），我们可以得出以下结论：

We can draw the following conclusions, following on from correlations (I) and (II):

（三）语言从中心标记转变为从属标记相当容易，反之亦然。

(III) Languages change fairly easily from head marking to dependent marking, and vice versa.

(IV) 如果一种中心标记语言具有从属标记的特征，它的形容词类将会发生变化，但在语法上变得与名词类更相似的速度会慢得多。

(IV) If a head-marking language takes on features of dependent marking, its adjective class will tend to change but much more slowly to become grammatically more similar to the noun class.

(V) 同样地，如果一种从属标记语言采用中心标记，它的形容词类就会慢慢发生变化，在语法上变得更类似于动词类。

(V) Similarly, if a dependent-marking language takes on head marking, its adjective class will slowly change to become grammatically more similar to the verb class.

还有其他伴随变化的例子，但第 (I)(V) 点暂时应被视为暂定的，随着从这个角度研究越来越多的语言，可能会进行修改。

There are other examples of these concomitant changes, but points (I)(V) should for the time being be regarded as tentative, subject to revision as more languages are studied from this point of view.

这些例子应该足以回答“为什么要费心？”这个问题。如果人们只研究几十种语言，这些语言都被大群体使用，那么人类语言的多样性和复杂性的十分之九仍未被发现。

These illustrations ought to suffice to answer the question 'why bother?' If one simply examines a few dozen languages, all spoken by large communities, nine-tenths of the diversity and complexity of human language will remain undiscovered.

每种语言都有自己的特点、自己的兴趣点，以及比其他语言更能清晰表达的某些事物。只有通过描述每种可能的语言，研究其类别之间的关联以及这些关联的变化方式，我们才有可能合理地理解人类语言是什么、它如何构造以及它如何演变。

Every language has it own genius, its own points of interest, certain things that can be said in it more clearly than in other languages. And only by describing every possible language investigating the correlations between their categories, and the ways in which these change can we hope to achieve a reasonable understanding of what human language is, how it can be structured, and the ways in which it evolves.

 

 

9.2 一些现代神话

9.2 Some Modern Myths

语言学有两个相互交织的方面：理论和描述。我们必须在理论框架下工作，使用音素、单词、形容词、主语、宾语、关系从句、否定、时态和证据性等理论概念来描述一种语言。如上一节所述，描述性工作反馈到理论中，有助于完善和扩展我们对语言如何变化和变化以及人类语言的描述。

There are two interwoven aspects to linguistics: theory and description. One must work in terms of a theoretical framework to describe a language using theoretical notions such as phoneme, word, adjective, subject, object, relative clause, negation, tense and evidentiality. As described in the last section, descriptive work feeds back into theory, helping to refine and extend our characterisation of how languages vary and change, of what human language is like.

现代语言理论起源于公元前几世纪希腊第一批语法学家的工作（他们的工作建立在柏拉图和亚里士多德的哲学思想之上）。几百年前，最伟大的语法学家帕尼尼* 撰写了一本梵语语法书。他的作品直到十九世纪才在西方为人所知，随后被融入希腊传统。在过去的几百年里，世界各地的语言都得到了研究，语言理论的许多方面也因此得到了重新思考、重新表述和完善。

Modern linguistic theory originated from the work of the first grammarians of Greek, at about the time of Christ (and their work was founded in the philosophical ideas of Plato and Aristotle). Some hundreds of years earlier, the greatest grammarian of all, Panini *, wrote a grammar of Sanskrit. His work only became known in the West in the nineteenth century and was then assimilated into the Greek-based tradition. Over the past few hundred years work has been done on languages from every part of the world, with many aspects of linguistic theory being rethought, reformulated and refined as a result.

“基础语言学理论”这个术语最近开始用于指代所有语言描述和变化工作以及人类语言一般属性的假设所依据的基本理论概念。

The term Basic Linguistic Theory has recently come into use for the fundamental theoretical concepts that underlie all work in language description and change, and the postulation of general properties of human languages.

如果语言学家受过适当的训练，他们必须对《基础理论》中使用的标准以及描述技巧有扎实的基础。在制定语言语法时，必须提出备选分析，权衡其优缺点，并决定哪种分析最合适。考虑“什么是单词？”这个问题。有两种标准：音系标准（例如，每个单词都有一个重读音节）和形态标准（例如，每个单词有一个屈折词缀）。有时它们一致，但有时它们不一致，因此语言学家必须识别两个单位，音系词和语法词，其中语法词可能由一个或多个音系词组成​​（反之亦然）。（Dixon 1988：2131 中对斐济语进行了说明。）

If a linguist is properly trained, they must have a solid grounding in the criteria employed in Basic Theory, and also in descriptive techniques. In working out the grammar of a language, alternative analyses have to be posited, their advantages and disadvantages weighed, and a decision reached on which is the most appropriate. Consider the question 'What is a word?' There are two kinds of criteria phonological (e.g. each word has one stressed syllable) and morphological (e.g. there is one inflectional affix per word). Sometimes these coincide but other times they do not, and the linguist then has to recognise two units, Phonological Word and Grammatical Word, where a grammatical word may consist of one or more than one phonological words (or vice versa). (There is an illustration of this, for Fijian, in Dixon 1988: 2131.)

我们可以简短地说明如何评估相互竞争的分析，同样来自斐济语（Dixon 1988: 26）。这种语言有两个音系限制：（1）单音节词必须包含长元音或双元音，而不仅仅是短元音；（2）如果一个词的最后一个元音是短元音，倒数第二个元音也必须是短的，也就是说，它不能太长。现在考虑这两个词：93

We can offer a short illustration of how competing analyses may be assessed, also from Fijian (Dixon 1988: 26). This language has two phonological constraints: (1) a monosyllabic word must include a long vowel or diphthong, not just a short vowel; (2) if a word has a final short vowel, the penultimate vowel must also be short, i.e. it cannot be long. Now consider the two words:93

caa '坏'ca-ta '认为坏，讨厌'

caa 'bad'ca-ta 'consider bad, hate'

也就是说，我们有一个词根 caa/ca。不带后缀时，它是一个形容词“坏”；带及物后缀 -ta 时，它是一个及物动词“认为不好，讨厌”。问题是：底层词根的形式是什么，caa 还是 ca？两种选择都是合理的：

That is, we have a root caa/ca. Used without a suffix it is an adjective 'bad'; used with the transitive suffix -ta it is a transitive verb 'consider bad, hate'. The question is: what is the form of the underlying root, caa or ca? Either choice is plausible:

（a） 可以将底层形式取为 caa，并指定元音缩短，当添加后缀 ta 时，给出 ca，以满足规则（2），即当最后一个元音很短时，我们不能在单词的倒数第二个音节中得到长元音。

(a) One could take the underlying form to be caa, and specify that the vowel is shortened, giving ca, when the suffix- ta is added, to satisfy rule (2), that we cannot get a long vowel in the penultimate syllable of a word when the final vowel is short.

(b) 或者可以将基础形式取为 ca，并说当后面没有后缀时，短元音会被拉长，以满足规则 (1)，即单音节词不能只包含短元音。

(b) Or one could take the underlying form to be ca, and say that the short vowel is lengthened when no suffix follows, to satisfy rule (1), that a monosyllabic word cannot contain just a short vowel.

我们如何在这些选项之间做出选择？选择的基础来自语法的另一部分。部分重复的过程仅适用于少数具有复数含义的形容词。考虑一下：

How do we choose between these alternatives? The basis for choice comes from another part of the grammar. There is a process of partial reduplication which applies to just a handful of adjectives, with plural meaning. Consider:

levu'big'le-levu'很多大事'

levu'big'le-levu'lots of big things'

vou'new'vo-vou'很多新事物'

vou'new'vo-vou'lots of new things'

caa'bad'ca-caa'很多坏事'

caa'bad'ca-caa'lots of bad things'

该过程在词根之前重复了首辅音，随后又重复了短元音。请注意，对于 vou 来说，重复中只包括 o，而不是整个 ou。

The process repeats, before the root, the initial consonant and following short vowel. Note that for vou it is just the o, not the whole ou, that is included in the reduplication.

现在考虑替代分析（a）和（b）：

Now consider alternative analyses (a) and (b):

（a）如果基础形式是 caa，则重复会产生 ca-caa。

(a) if the underlying form were caa, reduplication would yield ca-caa.

(b) 如果基础形式是 ca，则重复会产生 ca-ca，这在该语言中是一个完全可以接受的词。

(b) if the underlying form were ca, reduplication would yield ca-ca, which would be a perfectly acceptable word in the language.

事实上重复形式是 ca-caa，表明 (a) 是最合适的分析，其底层词根被视为 caa。

In fact the reduplicated form is ca-caa, indicating that (a) is the most appropriate analysis, with the underlying root being taken to be caa.

要想成为任何领域的专业人士，必须接受适当的培训，然后当学徒。外科医生在医学院学习，然后进行常规手术，然后从事创新工作，例如心脏移植或整形手术（或撰写有关外科手术原理或外科手术新方向的书籍）。语言学家必须学习基础语言理论的原理，并接受如何描述语言的指导（通过现场方法课程）。理想的计划是从事一种以前从未描述过（或很少描述过）的语言的原创现场工作，并撰写一份全面的语法作为博士论文。每种语言都提出了某种理论挑战，解决这一问题可能会导致理论反馈，有助于扩大和完善理论。

To become a professional in any field one has to undertake the appropriate training, and then serve an apprenticeship. A surgeon attends medical school and then does routine operations before going on to do innovative work in, say, heart transplantation or plastic surgery (or to write a book on the principles of surgery, or on new directions in surgery). A linguist must be taught the principles of Basic Linguistic Theory, and also receive instruction in how to describe language (through Field Methods courses). The ideal plan is then to undertake original field work on a previously undescribed (or scarcely described) language, and write a comprehensive grammar of it as a Ph.D. dissertation. Every language poses some kind of theoretical challenge, and solving this is likely to lead to feedback into theory, helping to enlarge and refine it.

在后期阶段，对某一特定语系和/或语言领域有深入了解，并且精通其中一种或最好多种语言的语言学家可以着手进行比较研究。他们可能会尝试重建原始语言，或研究子群，或调查传播类型（或将所有这些结合起来）。

At a later stage a linguist who has a thorough grounding in a particular language family and/or linguistic area with good knowledge of one, or preferably more than one, of its languages can embark on a comparative study. They may attempt to reconstruct a proto-language, or study subgrouping, or investigate types of diffusion (or combine all of these).

这是应该发生的事情。这也是过去发生的事情。但如今世界上大多数地方的情况并非如此。94在过去的四十年左右，语言学学科已经失去平衡。我将尝试解释这是如何发生的。

This is what should happen. This is what used to happen. But it is not what happens today over most of the world.94 Over the last forty years or so the discipline of linguistics has been knocked off balance. I will try to explain how this came about.

最主要的发展是发明了许多有限的形式主义集，这些形式主义集被称为“理论”。每种理论都基于基础语言学理论的某些部分。每种理论都可用于描述某些类型的语言关系，但提出时却好像是一套完整的语言理论。“理论”一词的使用方式新颖。

The major development has been the invention of a number of restricted sets of formalisms, that have been called 'theories'. Each is based on some part of Basic Linguistic Theory. Each is useful for describing certain kinds of linguistic relationships, but it is put forward as if it were a complete theory of language. The word 'theory' is being used in a novel way.

这些形式主义（非基础理论）往往只持续很短的时间；典型的半衰期为六到十年。但是，当某种形式主义像时尚潮流一样流行时，它的追随者宣称它是语言运作的唯一可行模型。据说不应该混合理论（就像不应该混合宗教一样），但事实上，每种理论都建立在基础理论的不同部分之上，使用不同形式主义的思想来描述语言的不同部分是有益的。当然，从事各种形式主义工作的人们提出了一些很好的想法，这些想法反馈到了基础理论中。

These formalisms (non-basic theories) tend to last for only a short time; the typical half-life is six to ten years. But while a particular formalism is in vogue rather like a fad in fashion its adherents proclaim it to be the only viable model of how language works. It is said that one shouldn't mix theories (just like one shouldn't mix religions) but in fact each is founded on a different part of Basic Theory, and it can be profitable to use ideas from different formalisms in describing different parts of a language. Of course, some excellent ideas have been put forward by people working within the various formalisms, and these feed back into Basic Theory.

少数语言学家继续按照以前的做法，以基础理论的形式撰写语言语法，并自然而然地扩展和完善该理论。然而，他们没有为所使用的理论命名；对他们来说，这只是撰写语法，就像人们几千年来所做的那样。

A minority of linguists have continued as before, writing grammars of languages in terms of Basic Theory, and naturally expanding and refining the theory. However, they didn't have a name for the theory they were using; for them, it was just writing grammars, as people have been doing for millennia.

形式主义者确实为他们的“理论”起了名字。95他们经常说，那些编写语言语法的人（除了极少数例外，他们自己不会这样做）是在没有理论的情况下工作的。就好像人们可以在没有理论基础的情况下进行任何语言分析一样。

The formalists do have names for their 'theories'.95 And they often say that the people writing grammars of languages (something that, with rare exceptions, they do not do themselves) are working without a theory. As if one could possibly undertake any linguistic analysis without a theoretical basis.

直到最近几年，“基础语言学理论”这个术语才开始使用，用来描述所有描述语言和制定人类语言本质普遍性的工作的根本理​​论手段。

It is only within the last few years that the term Basic Linguistic Theory has come into use, to describe the fundamental theoretical apparatus that underlies all work in describing languages and formulating universals about the nature of human language.

每种形式主义（非基础理论）都提供了一套关于语言结构的假设，即一种可以相信每种语言都适合的框架。当用基础语言理论来写语法时，我们不能想当然。每个分析决策都必须作为一个开放的问题来处理。识别一个或两个单位“词”（一个“音系词”和一个“语法词”）是否合适？是否存在一种结构类型，它具有通常被视为定义“关系从句”的属性？对于这种语言，识别“动词短语”类别是否有效？相反，每种非基础理论都假定某些类别与所有语言相关，只需找到它们即可。例如，治理和约束形式主义规定所有语言都有“动词短语”，因此人们所要做的就是发现给定语言中的动词短语是什么（人们不必提供任何理由来识别动词短语类别）。

Each of the formalisms (the non-basic theories) provides a set of postulates about the structure of language, a framework into which every language can it is believed be fitted. When writing a grammar in terms of Basic Linguistic Theory one takes nothing for granted. Each analytic decision has to be approached as an open question. Is it appropriate to recognise one unit 'word' or two (a 'phonological word' and also a 'grammatical word')? Is there a construction type that has the properties normally taken as defining a 'relative clause'? Is it valid, for this language, to recognise a category of 'verb phrase'? In contrast, each of the non-basic theories posits that certain categories are relevant for all languages one has only to find them. For instance, the Government and Binding formalism specifies that all languages have 'verb phrases', so that all one has to do is discover what the verb phrase is in a given language (one doesn't have to provide any justification for recognising a category of verb phrase).

在基础语言理论中，每一项分析都必须给出依据，并进行一系列论证。在非基础理论中，几乎没有论证的余地96，这只是将语言的某些部分放入预先设定的分类中（如果某些部分似乎没有合适的位置，那么它就没有什么意义，因为它超出了该特定理论的范围）。不用说，这种方法往往会使所有语言看起来都很相似，并忽略了不符合任何期望的真正有趣的特征。

When working in terms of Basic Linguistic Theory, justification must be given for every piece of analysis, with a full train of argumentation. Working within a non-basic theory there is little scope for argumentation96 it is just a matter of slipping bits of the language into pre-ordained pigeon holes (and if there is some bit for which no slot seems appropriate, then that is of little interest since it falls outside the scope of that particular theory). Needless to say, such an approach tends to make all languages seem rather similar, and ignores the really interesting features which do not conform to any expectations.

语言学家对“分析”一词有两种截然不同的使用方式。对于直接从事基础语言理论研究的人来说，语言分析意味着识别意义的操作要素、其基本形式以及它们的组合和编码以产生语音流。非基础理论的拥护者以完全不同的方式使用“分析”一词，以描述将语言纳入他们的公理框架。

The term 'analysis' is used in two quite different ways by linguists. For people working directly in terms of Basic Linguistic Theory, the analysis of a language implies recognising the operative elements of meaning, their underlying forms, and their combination and coding to produce a stream of speech. Adherents of non-basic theories use the term 'analysis' in a totally different way, to describe fitting a language into their axiomatic framework.

事实上，很少有形式主义者会尝试编写全面的语言语法（这也很好，因为没有一种形式主义能够完全胜任这项任务）。他们有时只研究语言的一小部分；这通常不是一件明智的事情，因为每个部分都与整体相关，只有在整体的背景下才能正确理解。他们通常只局限于研究自己的母语。但他们中的一些人确实会不时地参考真正的语言学家编写的描述性语法（就基础语言理论而言），并尝试在他们的形式主义中重新表述其中的部分内容。

In fact few formalists do attempt to write comprehensive grammars of languages (which is just as well, since no formalism is fully adequate for the task). They sometimes work on just a bit of a language; this is generally not a sensible thing to attempt since each part relates to the whole and can only be properly understood in the context of the whole. Most often they confine themselves to working on their native language. But some of them do, from time to time, consult the descriptive grammars written by real linguists (in terms of Basic Linguistic Theory) and attempt to reformulate parts of them within their formalism.

现代语言学中有一个主要的神话，它比其他任何事情都更能导致该学科与其研究主题——语言研究——脱节。神话如下。语言学家基本上有两种类型。描述学家，他们从事实地工作并撰写语法。“理论家”（即形式主义者，研究非基础理论的人）自己不收集数据，而是从他们所选择的形式主义的角度来解释数据。神话是“理论家”所做的工作比描述学家所做的基础工作更困难、更重要、更智力化，总之处于更高的层次。

There is one major myth in modern linguistics which is responsible more than anything else for the discipline losing contact with its subject matter, the study of languages. It goes as follows. There are essentially two types of linguist. The descriptivists, who do field work and write grammars. And the 'theoreticians' (i.e. the formalists, people working on non-basic theories), who do not gather data themselves but rather interpret it, from the point of view of their chosen formalism. The myth is that the work done by the 'theoreticians' is more difficult, more important, more intellectual, altogether on a higher plane than the basic work undertaken by the descriptivists.

从各个角度来看，这都是错误的。首先，每个描述语言的人也都是理论家；他们必须如此，才能做出任何分析决定。语法描述中的每一点都是一个理论陈述，必须通过适当的论证来证明。

This is wrong, from every angle. First of all, every person who describes a language is also a theoretician; they have to be, to make any analytic decisions. Every point in a grammatical description is a theoretical statement, and must be justified by appropriate argumentation.

我从事过多个领域的工作。我撰写过多种语言的综合语法（其中一些对语言理论产生了深远影响，例如 Dixon 1972），我还对每种语言的作格性语法参数进行了理论调查（Dixon 1994）。每一项工作都带来了巨大的智力挑战。但毫无疑问，对一种以前从未描述过的语言进行分析是语言学中最艰巨的任务。这也是最令人兴奋和最令人满意的工作。

I've worked on several fronts. I've written comprehensive grammars of several languages (some of which have had a deep effect on linguistic theory, e.g. Dixon 1972) and I've also produced a theoretical survey of the grammatical parameter of ergativity across every type of language (Dixon 1994). Each presented great intellectual challenges. But there is no doubt whatsoever that undertaking the analysis of a previously undescribed language is the toughest task in linguistics. It is also the most exciting and the most satisfying of work.

很难表达对一门新语言进行实地研究所带来的纯粹精神上的兴奋。首先，人们必须认识到重要的分析问题。然后，备选解决方案可能整夜在脑海中翻腾。黎明时分，人们将它们写下来，列出每种方案的优缺点。白天，人们可以通过检查已经收集的文本并向母语人士提出精心设计的问题来评估这些替代方案。一种解决方案显然是正确的，它比其他解决方案更简单，解释力更强。然后人们意识到，这个问题的解决方案揭示了另一个困扰人们数周的棘手难题。等等。

It is hard to convey the sheer mental exhilaration of field work on a new language. First, one has to recognise the significant analytic problems. Then alternative solutions may tumble around in one's head all night. At the crack of dawn one writes them down, the pros and cons of each. During the day it is possible to assess the alternatives, by checking back through texts that have already been gathered and by asking carefully crafted questions of native speakers. One solution is seen to be clearly correct it is simpler than the others, and has greater explanatory power. Then one realises that the solution to this problem sheds light on another knotty conundrum that has been causing worry for weeks. And so on.

有些语言学系开设了实地研究方法课程，但授课人却从未对语言进行过实地研究（他们别无选择，因为系里没有一个人曾经从事过实地研究）。这些“语言学家”大多属于内部团体；他们互相支持，帮助彼此获得终身教职和晋升。他们认为，要理解语言，不必研究语言；一切都可以通过内省认知来实现。这就像一群“外科医生”，他们中没有人真正做过手术，却在讲授手术原理的课程。

Some linguistics departments put on a Field Methods course but have it taught by someone who has never carried out original field work on a language (they have no choice, since not a single person in the department has ever undertaken field work). Most of these 'linguists' belong to in-groups; they support one another, help each other attain tenure and promotion. They argue that to understand language one doesn't have to work on languages; it can all be achieved by introspective cognition. This is rather like a group of 'surgeons', none of whom has ever actually performed an operation, giving courses of lectures on the principles of surgery.

总体而言，形式主义的弊病并没有蔓延到历史语言学。人们普遍认为，在能够有效地进行语言比较之前，必须对一种语言或最好是有关语系或地区的更多语言有透彻的了解。97困难在于，比较需要高质量的语言语法，需要进行比较。但很少有语言学家致力于这项重要任务。普通语言学的弊病导致缺乏良好的描述性语法，从而切断了比较语言学的原材料。

By and large, the malaise of formalisms has not spread into historical linguistics. It is generally recognised that before one can profitably work on comparing languages one must have a thorough knowledge of one language or, preferably, more of the family or area concerned.97 The difficulty is that comparison requires high-quality grammars of languages, something to compare. And too few linguists devote themselves to this vital task. The malaise of general linguistics, leading to a lack of good descriptive grammars, cuts off the raw materials for comparative linguistics.

 

 

9.3 每个语言学家应该做什么

9.3 What Every Linguist Should Do

语言是其使用者的象征。每种语言都决定着一种独特的世界观。它囊括了其族群的法律、传统和信仰。事实上，最近一份关于美国濒危语言的报告（由其中一种语言的使用者合著）指出：“每一种仍在使用的语言都是其使用者个人、社会和土著人民精神身份话语中的关键术语的基础。他们知道，如果没有这些语言，他们的存在将大不如前，他们正致力于保护自己的语言遗产，这是最紧迫的斗争”（Zepeda 和 Hill 1991：135）。

A language is the emblem of its speakers. Each language determines a unique way of viewing the world. It encapsulates the laws and traditions and beliefs of its ethnic group. Indeed, a recent report on endangered languages in the USA (co-authored by a speaker of one of these languages) states: 'Each language still spoken is fundamental to the personal, social and a key term in the discourse of indigenous peoples spiritual identity of its speakers. They know that without these languages they would be less than they are, and they are engaged in the most urgent struggles to protect their linguistic heritage' (Zepeda and Hill 1991: 135).

语言学家可以协助完成这项任务。记录语言是语言学家的责任。通过这样做，他们可以帮助母语人士记录他们的传统，并经常将一种语言的使用延续一代或两代。描述语言也是正确学习语言学的唯一方法；一个人必须经过适当的学徒期才能掌握一门艺术或职业。98

Linguists can assist in this task. Documenting languages is the responsibility of linguists. By so doing they can help native speakers to record their traditions, and often extend the use of a language by a generation or two. Describing languages is also the only way to learn linguistics properly; one must serve an appropriate apprenticeship to master an art or profession.98

我记得当我第一次参加语言学讲座并学习当时的各种理论时，我认为自己理解得相当透彻。但我确实觉得有必要进行实地考察。当我进入实地考察（在澳大利亚）时，我发现自己对语言的结构了解甚少。但我通过分析文本、尝试语法概括并与说话者核对，一点一点地学习。然后，当我开始理解它们与我所从事的任务的相关性时，我所读到的理论思想有了新的见解。

I recall that when I first attended lectures in linguistics, and studied the various theories of the day, I thought I understood it all pretty well. But I did feel the need to do field work. When I got out into the field (in Australia) I found that I actually understood very little about how language is structured. But I learnt, little by little, by undertaking analysis of texts, attempting grammatical generalisations, and checking these with speakers. And then the theoretical ideas that I had read about took on a new light, as I began to understand their relevance to the task I was engaged in.

许多现代语言学家都有不做实地考察的传统。许多教授劝阻学生不要做实地考察；如果学生坚持做实地考察，大多数老师就没有资格监督他们的工作。但如果语言学要回到正轨，就必须有代际隔阂。南希·多里安（1994：799）在讨论记录濒危语言的必要性时说：“可以说，最根本的障碍……是该行业缺乏动员意愿。在我看来，将实地考察作为职业要求至少在两个方面有很大好处。

There is a tradition of not doing field work among many modern-day linguists. Many professors dissuade their students from undertaking it; and if the students were to persist, most of the teachers would be unqualified to supervise their work. But if linguistics is to get back on track there must be an estrangement between generations. Nancy Dorian (1994: 799), discussing the need to document endangered languages, stated: 'Arguably the single most fundamental obstacle . . . is an absence of mobilizing will on the part of the profession. A case could be made, it seems to me, for great benefit in at least two different respects from making it a professional requirement that

语言学和语言人类学的博士候选人将对一种未记录或仅有少量记录的语言进行描述性研究，作为论文主题。'年轻的语言学家必须寻找有经验丰富的描述性语言学家的部门，他们可以指导他们的实地工作和语法分析。事实上，如果当今世界上的每一位语言学学生（和教职员工）都只研究一种需要研究的语言，那么对濒危语言进行全面记录（在它们消失之前）的前景将是光明的。我怀疑二十位语言学家中是否有一位在这样做。

Ph.D. candidates in linguistics and Linguistic Anthropology undertake a descriptive study of an undocumented or only minimally documented language as a dissertation topic.' Young linguists must seek out departments that have experienced descriptive linguists who can supervise their field work and grammatical analysis. Indeed, if every linguistics student (and faculty member) in the world today worked on just one language that is in need of study, the prospects for full documentation of endangered languages (before they fade away) would be rosy. I doubt if one linguist in twenty is doing this.

还有其他态度上的错误。一种是语言理论应该主要采用演绎法。有人提出“语言的普遍属性”（基于他们对英语、德语和意大利语的了解），然后将其作为理论进展发表。然后他们花费数年时间试图解释为什么其他语言不能轻易地符合这一想法。事实上，最有利可图的理论工作是归纳法。99人们研究多种语言（来自每个语系和每个语言领域）中的某个特征或特征相关性，看看会出现什么模式。这些可以形成假设的基础，该假设应该在进一步选择的语言（选择这些语言的理由是它们具有与假设相关的关键属性）中进行彻底验证，100然后才能提升到理论公设的地位。

There are other errors of attitude. One is that linguistic theorising should be largely deductive. Someone suggests a 'general property of language' (based on their knowledge of, say, English, German and Italian) and then publishes it as a theoretical advance. They then spend years trying to explain away why other languages do not fit easily into the idea. In fact, the most profitable theoretical work is inductive.99 One studies a certain feature or correlation of features across a wide selection of languages (from every family and every linguistic area) and sees what patterns emerge. These can form the basis for a hypothesis, which should be thoroughly verified across a further selection of languages (chosen on the grounds that they have critical properties with respect to the hypothesis),100 before being elevated to the status of a theoretical postulate.

有 2,000 或 3,000 种语言我们尚无合适的描述，它们将在未来几代内逐渐被废弃。我们急需训练有素的语言学家来记录这些语言。在某些情况下，母语人士可以接受语言学家的培训，但在许多情况下，需要外行。所有这些都需要花钱。如果可以聘请一位训练有素的语言学家，而他/她已经撰写了一篇语法博士论文，并且对基础理论有深入的了解，那么他们就需要支付自己和语言顾问的薪水、差旅费、设备、编写描述、编纂词典和文本集的设施等。做好这项工作至少需要 3 年时间；总成本（按 1997 年的价值计算）约为 200,000 美元。

There are 2,000 or 3,000 languages, for which we have no decent description, that will pass into disuse within the next few generations. Trained linguists are urgently needed to document them. In some cases native speakers can be trained as linguists but in many instances an outsider is required. All this costs money. If one can hire a properly trained linguist someone who has already written a grammar as a Ph.D. dissertation and has a thorough grounding in Basic Theory they will need salary for themselves and for their language consultants; travel funds; equipment; facilities for writing up the description, producing a dictionary and volume of texts; and so on. At least 3 years is needed to do a good job; the total cost will be (at 1997 values) around $US200,000.

如果不尽快完成这项工作，就永远无法完成。后代人将带着困惑和鄙视回顾 20 世纪末和 21 世纪初那些自称“语言学家”的人。

If this work is not done soon it can never be done. Future generations will then look back at the people who call themselves 'linguists' at the close of the twentieth and beginning of the twenty-first century, with bewilderment and disdain.

如前所述，良好的描述性工作是比较语言学的先决条件。迫切需要开展工作来区分表明遗传关系的语言相似性类型和可能由扩散引起的语言相似性类型。我们需要研究过去平衡时期演变的扩散区域，并寻找过去不同民族之间关系和起源的指标。

As already stated, good descriptive work is a prerequisite for comparative linguistics. Work is urgently needed to distinguish between types of linguistic similarity that are indicative of genetic relationships, and those likely to be due to diffusion. We need to study diffusion areas that evolved during past periods of equilibrium, and look for indicators of the past relationships between and origins of different peoples.

 

 

10 总结与展望

10 Summary and Prospects

10.1 间断平衡模型

10.1 The Punctuated Equilibrium Model

这里提出的假设是，在语言存在的 10 万年或更长的时间里，大部分时间里每个地理区域都处于一种均衡状态。许多小的政治团体，每个团体都有自己的语言或方言，生活在稳定的环境中，彼此相对和谐。没有大规模的等级组织，也没有一个团体、语言或方言在超过一个地方（或超过一段有限的时间）享有声望。

The hypothesis put forward here is that, during most of the 100,000 years or more that language has been in existence, there has been an equilibrium situation within each geographical area. A number of small political groups, each with its own language or dialect, lived in a stable situation, in relative harmony with each other. There was no large-scale hierarchical organisation and no one group or language or dialect was accorded prestige over more than a local area (or for more than a limited time).

事情从来都不是一成不变的。语言和政治团体总是处于变化之中。有稳定的起伏。有些语言会逐渐被淘汰，而另一些语言可能会一分为二；但这种情况只会在一定范围内发生。

Things were never static. Languages and political groupings are always in a state of shift. There is a steady ebb and flow. Some languages would fall out of use and others might split into two; but this would happen on a modest scale.

在每个地区，各种语言特征都会扩散。该地区以及该地区各地区的语言在音系、语法类别、词汇和语法形式（速度较慢）方面会变得更加相似。它们会趋向于该地区的语言原型。

In each area, linguistic features of all kinds would diffuse. The languages in the area, and in regions within the area, would become more like each other in phonological systems, grammatical categories, perhaps also in lexemes and, at a slower rate, in grammatical forms. They would converge towards a linguistic prototype for the area.

然后，平衡状态被打破。这可能是由于自然事件，或由于某种物质创新（最显著的是农业的引入），或由于出现了一个咄咄逼人的政治领袖或一种咄咄逼人的宗教。或者由于一个语言群体从其原有地区迁往一个新的无人居住的地区。

Then the state of equilibrium was punctuated. This could be due to a natural happening, or to some material innovation (most notably, the introduction of agriculture), or to the emergence of an aggressive political leader or an aggressive religion. Or to the movement of a language group away from its original area into a new and unpopulated region.

标点符号的出现通常伴随着扩展和分裂。语言关系的“家谱”模型恰当地模拟了标点符号出现期间所发生的情况，即许多语言从共同的原始语言（或具有收敛特征的原始语言群）中分离出来。最终，平衡将再次建立。

A period of punctuation is typically accompanied by expansion and split. The 'family tree' model of linguistic relationship appropriately models what happens during a punctuation period, when a number of languages diverge from a common proto-language (or proto-group of languages, with convergent profiles). Eventually, equilibrium will again be established.

科学家从未观察到过、也永远无法观察到平衡状态（尽管可以很容易地为澳大利亚重建平衡状态，也可能为世界其他地区重建平衡状态）。科学家（通过写作等）的介入起到了标点的作用。正因为如此，语言之间的平衡状态这一概念以前从未以这种方式提出过。

No equilibrium situation ever has been or ever could be observed by a scientist (although it can readily be reconstructed for Australia, and probably also for other parts of the world). The intrusion of a society that has scientists (with writing, and so on) serves as punctuation. It is because of this that the idea of an equilibrium situation between languages has not previously been posited, in this way.

近几个世纪以来，白人入侵和通讯的发展使世界各地的平衡地区突然中断。这导致了前所未有的语言流失，而且这种流失目前还在加剧，并将持续下去，直到每个国家都只有一种语言，如果情况保持目前的状态，最终将导致全世界只有一种语言。

Recent centuries featuring white invasions and developments in communication have brought equilibrium areas all over the world to an abrupt punctuation. This has led to unprecedented language losses which are currently increasing and will continue until there is just one language for each nation, eventually leading if things remain as they are at present to just one language for the whole world.

本文具有纲领性，表明间断平衡模型适合描述和解释全球背景下的语言发展。该假设是作为未来研究的基础提出的。本文提出的想法需要经过世界各地语言领域专家的研究后进行完善和进一步阐述。

This essay has been programmatic, suggesting that the punctuated equilibrium model is an appropriate one to describe and explain language development in a global context. The hypothesis has been presented as a basis for future research. The ideas suggested here will need to be refined and further articulated, after work by a range of specialists on linguistic areas across the world.

 

 

10.2 关于比较语言学

10.2 Concerning Comparative Linguistics

重点是，“家谱”只是解释过去 10 万年左右语言关系和发展所需的几个相互关联的模型之一。它适用于标点符号时期的情况。101在标点符号之间的长期平衡时期，语言之间原有的家谱关系逐渐被侵蚀，因为传播成为变化的主要因素。

The important point being made is that 'family tree' is only one of several interrelated models needed to explain linguistic relationships and development over the past 100,000 or so years. It is applicable to situations during periods of punctuation.101 In the long periods of equilibrium between punctuation the original family-tree relationships between languages are gradually eroded as diffusion becomes the major factor in change.

有必要设想一个语言家族的起源不是早期家族树的终点，而是平衡期结束时的语言状况。可能存在一个原始语言区，而不是原始语言区，其中包含少数结构和形式相当相似的语言（但根据可理解性标准，仍然是不同的语言）。如果一个家族确实源自一种原始语言，有时确实如此，那么必须记住，原始语言将具有人类语言的全部特征，并可能存在补充、不规则和底层。

There is need to conceive of a language family having its beginnings not in the end-point of an earlier family tree but in the linguistic situation that would hold at the end of a period of equilibrium. Rather than a proto-language there may have been a proto-linguistic-area, involving a small number of languages with considerable similarities of structures and forms (but still distinct languages, on the criterion of intelligibility). And if a family did emanate from a single proto-language, as might sometimes be the case, it must be borne in mind that the proto-language would have the full characteristics of a human language, with the likelihood of suppletions, irregularities and substrata.

在某些情况下，证明一组语言之间的亲缘关系比在其他情况下更容易。理想的情况是语言通常具有黏着结构，其词素和语法形式大多是多音节的。对于一组孤立语言，或具有许多非常短的词素（一个音节或可能只有一个音节）的语言，不太可能有信心证明亲缘关系并重建原始系统的很大一部分。

It is easier to prove genetic relationship between a group of languages in some circumstances than in others. The ideal situation is with languages of a generally agglutinative structure, with lexemes and grammatical forms that are mostly polysyllabic. With a group of isolating languages, or languages with many very short morphemes (one syllable or perhaps just one segment in extent), there is less prospect of confidently proving a genetic relationship and reconstructing a substantial part of the proto-system.

在一个语言家族内划分子群是一项艰巨的任务；只有部分分裂可能可以恢复。特别是，必须小心区分语言之间由于地理相邻和区域扩散而产生的相似性与由于共同遗传而产生的相似性。

Subgrouping within a language family is a difficult task; only some of the splits that took place are likely to be retrievable. In particular, care must be taken to distinguish similarities between languages due to geographical contiguity and areal diffusion from those due to shared genetic inheritance.

在许多情况下，无法判断语言之间的某种相似性是地域性的还是遗传性的。在目前的语言学状态下，对某些问题唯一诚实的回答是“我们不知道”（或“我们还不知道”）。试图对这类问题给出明确的答案，会使对其他问题提供的明确答案的价值丧失可信度。

In many situations it is impossible to tell whether a certain similarity between languages has an areal or a genetic origin. In the present state of linguistics the only honest answer to some questions is 'we don't know' (or 'we don't yet know'). To attempt to provide a definite answer to a question of this type takes credence away from the value of definite answers that can be provided for other questions.

比较语言学需要开展的工作包括：

Work that is needed in comparative linguistics is:

（a）对于每一组语言，考虑一下家谱模型、区域传播模型或两者的哪种组合在多大程度上是合适的。（撒哈拉以南非洲最迫切需要重新考虑这个问题。102）

(a) For each group of languages, consider to what extent the family tree model, or the areal diffusion model, or what sort of combination of the two, is appropriate. (Such a reconsideration is needed most urgently in Sub-Saharan Africa.102)

(b) 完成 (a) 中的重新考虑后，尽可能多地重建每个假定遗传群体的原始语言或原始语言区域的原始系统。目前全世界有 200 多个语系。这些可能的遗传关系必须通过重建原始系统和现代语言从中发展而来的系统变化来充分证明，或者被丢弃。

(b) Once the reconsideration under (a) has been completed, reconstruct as much as possible of the proto-system(s) for the proto-language or proto-linguistic-area for each putative genetic group. There are more than 200 language families currently posited across the world. These possible genetic relationships must be either fully proved by reconstructing proto-system(s) and the systematic changes by which modern languages have developed from them or discarded.

应始终牢记以下注意事项：

The following caveats should always be borne in mind:

(i) 完全重建原始语言或原始语言区域永远是不可能的。我们最多只能达到近似值。（它与实际原始语言的关系可能更像是警察根据观察者对他们的描述对犯罪者进行的身份识别与犯罪者本人之间的关系。）

(i) It will never be possible to fully reconstruct a proto-language or proto-linguistic-area. At best we can achieve an approximation. (Its relationship to the actual proto-language may be rather like that between an Identikit representation that the police produce of someone who has committed a crime, from what observers can describe of them, and that person themself.)

(ii) 试图比较各个语系的原始原始语言，并试图重建原始原始语言图景，这不是明智的做法。首先，我们对原始语言的了解还很有限。其次，它可能不是一种语言，而是一组语言。第三，原始语言或原始语言环境很可能是平衡期结束时扩散趋同的产物，而不是由家族树式扩张和分裂而产生的语言。
