(ii) It is not a sensible policy to try to compare the original proto-languages of language families, and attempt to reconstruct a proto-proto- tableau. Firstly, we have only an approximate idea of what a proto-language was like. Secondly, it may not have been one language, but instead a group of languages. And thirdly, proto-languages or proto-linguistic-situations are likely to be the product of diffusional convergence, at the end of a period of equilibrium, rather than languages which result from a family-tree-type expansion and split.

在语言发展的历史中，我们很可能经历了一系列的分化（在短时期内出现家族树式的分裂），然后是趋同（在长期的平衡时期内，语言领域内的扩散），然后是分化，然后是趋同，等等。分化时期的种子位于趋同时期的终点，反之亦然。

Over the history of language development it is likely that we have had a sequence of divergence (family-tree-type splits within a short period of punctuation), then convergence (diffusion within a linguistic area during a long period of equilibrium), then divergence, then convergence, and so on. The seeds for a period of divergence lie in the end-point of a period of convergence, and vice versa.

几乎无需多言，从语言学角度来看，我们不可能确定语言是只发展了一次（单源论）还是发展了多次（多源论）。尽管一些考古学家、遗传学家和媒体期望我们能够恢复“原始世界”（或“原始世界 1”、“原始世界 2”等）的结构，但语言学家肯定不可能恢复。

It should scarcely need to be said that it is unlikely that it will ever be possible to decide, on linguistic grounds, whether language developed just once (monogenesis) or more than once (polygenesis). And it will certainly never be possible for linguists to recover the structure of 'proto-World' (or of 'proto-World1', 'proto-World2', etc.) despite the expectations of some archaeologists and geneticists and the media that we should be able to.

 

 

10.3 关于描述语言学

10.3 Concerning Descriptive Linguistics

世界上的语言列表包括 5,000 至 6,000 种语言。他们通常给出澳大利亚大约 250 种语言。这是对白人入侵时所使用的语言数量的合理估计，但现在有 100 多种语言已经消亡，另有 100 种语言正在走向灭绝；儿童学习的语言不超过 20 种。同样的故事在世界各地重复上演。最近有人提议制作坦桑尼亚语言地图集，但“被联系的当局坚持认为，制作语言地图不应被视为研究重点，因为许多语言正在消亡，取而代之的是坦桑尼亚的国家和官方语言斯瓦希里语，因此语言边界变化如此之快，以至于这种语言地图很可能在几年内就不再适用”（Brenzinger、Heine 和 Sommer 1991：1920）。今天实际使用的语言可能约为 4,000 种，但数量正在稳步减少。在世界范围内，每年有几十种语言正在逐渐被淘汰。

Lists of the world's languages include 5,0006,000 names. They generally give about 250 languages for Australia. This is a reasonable estimate for the number of languages spoken at the time of the white invasion but over 100 languages are now dead while another 100 are moving towards extinction; no more than about 20 languages are being learnt by children. The same story is repeated world-wide. There was a recent proposal to produce a language atlas of Tanzania but 'the authorities who were approached insisted that producing a language map was not to be considered a research priority since so many languages were dying out in favour of Kiswahili, the national and official language of Tanzania, and for this reason language boundaries were changing so rapidly that such a language map might well be inapplicable within a few years' (Brenzinger, Heine and Sommer 1991: 1920). There may be around 4,000 languages actually spoken today, but the number is steadily decreasing. Languages are falling out of use, across the world, at the rate of several dozen each year.

每种语言都浓缩了其使用者的世界观，他们如何思考、他们看重什么、他们信仰什么、他们如何定义周围的世界、他们如何安排自己的生活。一旦一种语言消亡，人类文化的一部分就会永远消失。

Each language encapsulates the world-view of its speakers how they think, what they value, what they believe in, how they classify the world around them, how they order their lives. Once a language dies, a part of human culture is lost for ever.

当今语言学最重要的任务，事实上，唯一真正重要的任务是走出去，在还能做到的时候描述语言。在形式主义理论的镜子里自我欣赏可以等待；那永远是可能的。语言描述必须现在进行。103

The most important task in linguistics today indeed, the only really important task is to get out in the field and describe languages, while this can still be done. Self-admiration in the looking glass of formalist theory can wait; that will always be possible. Linguistic description must be undertaken now.103

语言描述很重要，原因有很多，包括：

Language description is important for many reasons, including:

（a）全面了解人类语言的类型学可能性，以及它们的成分之间的相关性（以及语法类别和生活方式的社会、经济等参数之间的相关性）。

(a) To gain a full picture of the typological possibilities across human languages, and the correlations between their components (and between grammatical categories and the parameters social, economic, etc. of life-style).

(b) 为比较研究提供基本输入。在非洲、新几内亚和南美洲，有些语言仅从简短的词汇表中为人所知。然而，它们却在此基础上被庄严地置于遗传分类中。遗传关系的证明主要取决于语法形式。在以有意义的方式对它们进行比较并系统地研究遗传关系的可能性之前，每种语言都需要完整的语法描述和词典。

(b) To provide the basic input to comparative work. In Africa and New Guinea and South America some languages are known only from a short word list. Yet they are solemnly placed within a genetic classification on this basis. The proof of genetic relationship depends most heavily on grammatical forms. A full grammatical description together with a dictionary for each language is necessary before they can be compared in a meaningful way and the possibility of a genetic relationship systematically investigated.

(c) 描述少数民族语言并编写供学校等使用的入门书有助于减缓（但不能阻止或扭转）一种语言走向灭绝的进程。它还有助于为使用少数民族语言的人提供更好的自我形象，帮助他们适应现代、大规模的国际化世界的生活。

(c) Describing a minority language and producing primers for use in schools, etc. can help slow down (but not halt or reverse) the path of a language towards extinction. And it can help provide a better self-image for the speakers as they adjust to life in a modern, large-scale cosmopolitan world.

语言描述应该由接受过全面专业培训的语言学家来做，而不是交给传教士（目前的情况大多如此）。而那些负责语言描述的传教士应该接受比现在更多的培训和监督。104

Language description should be undertaken by linguists who have had a thorough professional training, and not left to missionaries (as is largely the case at present). And those missionaries who do undertake language description should receive much more training and be provided with much more supervision than at present.104

 

 

10.4 关于语言

10.4 Concerning Languages

在世界各地，特定地区的权威语言或方言的使用越来越频繁，而非权威语言和方言的使用越来越少。在某些情况下，使用上的变化很小，几乎难以察觉；而在另一些情况下，变化很大，很明显。但这种变化始终存在。

In every part of the world, the prestige language or dialect of a given area is being used more and more, with non-prestige languages and dialects being used less and less. In some situations the change in use is slight and almost indiscernible; in others it is considerable and obvious. But this change is always there.

因此，在布列塔尼，布列塔尼语的使用越来越少，法语的使用越来越多。而在全球交流的背景下，英语作为目前国际上最有声望的语言，使用范围越来越广，而法语等其他语言的使用范围正在减少。

Thus, within Brittany, Breton is being used less and less and French more and more. And in the context of global communication, English the language with the greatest current international prestige is being used to an increasing extent, while the use of other languages, such as French, is declining.

如前所述，大部分非主流语言的使用者也会将当地的主流语言作为第二语言。反之则不然。设想一个由几百人或几千人组成的小型土著群体（在任何一个大陆）。他们在日常生活中使用自己的语言，但也知道通用语，这种语言用于与他们所居住的国家的日常生活的所有接触。他们自己的语言可能被使用 90% 的时间，而通用语只被使用 10%。随着他们与外界接触程度的增加，这些比例可能会逐渐发生变化。一旦通用语的使用时间超过 50%，它很快就会（在一代或更短的时间内）跃升至 100%。这是可以在生活的各个方面使用的语言。而土著语言不会继续作为第二语言（超过几代人）；它很快就会被废弃。

As already mentioned, a high proportion of the speakers of a non-prestige language will also know the prestige language of the area, as a second language. The reverse is not the case. Consider a small indigenous group (in any continent) of, say, a few hundred or a few thousand people. They use their own language in daily life but they also know the lingua franca, which is employed in all contact with the general life of the nation they live in. Their own language may be used 90% of the time and the lingua franca 10%. As their degree of contact with the outside world increases, these proportions may gradually shift. Once the lingua franca is used more than 50% of the time, it will soon (within one generation or less) jump to 100%. This is the language that can be used in every aspect of life. And the indigenous language will not continue as a second language (for more than a few generations); it will fairly soon fall into disuse.

这就是世界各地正在发生的事情。每一种非主流语言的使用率都在逐渐下降。（一个国家的少数民族语言可能是例外，它实际上是邻国的国语，例如芬兰的瑞典语。）这个过程缓慢但不可阻挡；所有这些语言都在走向废弃。

This is what is happening all over the world. Every non-prestige language is gradually being used less and less. (An exception may be a minority language of one nation which is in fact the national language of a neighbouring country, e.g. Swedish in Finland.) The process is slow but inexorable; all these languages are moving towards disuse.

语言消失的过程可以减缓，而且在少数地方，这种减缓正在通过语言学家、教育家或态度恰当的传教士的关注或通过人们自身的关注和努力而实现。但是，根据经验观察，这种进程永远无法停止，当然也无法逆转。还要注意的是，目前还没有真正消亡的语言复活的例子。

The process of language loss can be and, in a few places, is being slowed, through the attention of linguists, or educationalists, or missionaries with the appropriate attitude; or through the concern and efforts of the people themselves. But, as an empirical observation, it can never be halted and certainly not reversed. Note too that there is no example known of a truly dead language ever being revived.

世界各地地区和社会方言都在向“标准”语言形式靠拢。新语言从不同的方言中演化而来，但方言现在正在趋同。不仅语言正在以稳定的速度消失，而且没有新语言在演化，或者似乎不可能演化（除非通过克里奥尔化）。

It is also the case that all over the world regional and social dialects are converging on the 'standard' form of the language. New languages evolve from diverging dialects but dialects are now converging. Not only are languages being lost at a steady rate but no new languages are evolving or seem likely to evolve (save through creolisation).

能够幸存下来的语言是每个民族的权威语言。例如，拉脱维亚和哈萨克斯坦，将大国分化为小国，这将极大地帮助其语言的保存。当然，我们确实有一些语言拥有数百万或数千万使用者，但这些语言并不是其民族的唯一国语，例如伊博语和马拉地语。这些语言在短期或中期内显然不会受到威胁。但从长远来看，它们可能会受到威胁。105如果尼日利亚和印度等国家效仿苏联，分裂成若干个较小的国家，每个国家都使用一种主要语言，这将增加这些语言继续被使用最长时间的机会。（伊博语使用者当然尝试过这样做，比夫拉成立，他们从 1967 年到 1970 年为此而战。但最终，尼日利亚中央政府获胜了。）

The languages that will survive are the prestige languages of each nation. The making of small nations out of big ones for instance, Latvia and Kazakhstan will be of immense assistance for the maintenance of their languages. We do of course have languages with millions or tens of millions of speakers which are not the sole national language of their nation, e.g. Igbo and Marathi. These are plainly not threatened in the short or medium term. But they may well be in the longer term.105 If countries like Nigeria and India were to follow the lead of the Soviet Union and split into a number of smaller nations, each with one main language, this would enhance the chances of these languages continuing to be spoken for the longest possible time. (Speakers of Igbo did of course attempt this, with the formation of Biafra, and they fought a war over it from 1967 until 1970. But, in the end, the central government of Nigeria won.)

少数语言要生存下去，唯一的出路就是让其使用者与世隔绝地生活在新几内亚或南美洲的丛林中。现在还剩下几个这样的群体。但“文明”正在稳步侵入所有这些地区。很快，所有群体都将与他们所在国家的主流生活保持定期联系。

The only real way for a small language to survive is for its speakers to remain in isolation from the rest of the world in the jungles of New Guinea or South America. There are a few such groups left. But 'civilisation' is steadily encroaching into all of these areas. Soon there will be no groups not in regular contact with the mainstream of life in the country in which they are situated.

平衡局面在世界各地都已不复存在，而且没有迹象表明平衡将会或能够恢复。世界必须发生根本性变化，才能满足先决条件，形成小型平等群体，生活在稳定的环境中，彼此相对和谐，没有任何一个群体、语言或方言享有任何特殊的威望。

The equilibrium situation has been punctuated right across the world and there is no indication that equilibrium will or can ever be restored. The world would have to change in a radical way for the prerequisites to be met small egalitarian groups, living in a stable situation, in relative harmony with each other, without any particular prestige being attached to any one group or language or dialect.

如果世界继续按照目前的发展趋势发展，那么“每个国家使用一种语言”的局面也可能不会成为终点。全球化正在不断加强。例如，交流的范围正在扩大，但媒介却越来越受限。俄罗斯的俄罗斯人通过电子邮件用俄语与世界其他地方的同事交谈，但使用的是罗马字母（因为互联网不是为处理西里尔字母而设计的）。106在瑞典这样一个相对较小的国家，越来越多的人能说、读、写高质量的英语。事实上，瑞典大学的大多数博士论文都是用英语提交的。但懂瑞典语的英语母语人士并不多。

If the world continues on its present course even the situation of 'one language for each nation' may not be the ending point. Globalisation is increasing. For instance, communication is expanding in scope but becoming more restrictive in medium. Russians in Russia talk to colleagues in other parts of the world by electronic mail in Russian, but using the Roman alphabet (because the Internet is not designed to handle Cyrillic script).106 In a relatively small nation such as Sweden an increasing number of people speak, read and write English of good quality. Indeed, most Ph.D. theses at Swedish universities are submitted in English. But not too many native speakers of English know any Swedish.

如果情况不发生改变，我们现在所处的语言标点符号时代的最终结局将是，世界上只有一种语言享有最高声誉。虽然这需要几百年的时间，但这就是我们正在走向的最终局面。

If things don't change, the ultimate end to the period of linguistic punctuation that we are in now will be a single world language that which has the greatest prestige. It will take a few hundred years to get there, but this is the ultimate situation we are moving towards.

然而，情况可能会改变。

However, things may change.

 

 

附录

Appendix

比较方法发现程序失败的情况

Where the Comparative Method Discovery Procedure Fails

“比较方法”一词有两种不同的用法。其原始和最广泛的意义是指证明语言间遗传关系的一种方法。这涉及语法形式和词素的系统比较，建立音素之间的对应集，提出有关假定的原始系统的假设以及现代语言系统发展过程中的变化（例如，参见 Meil​​let 1925/1967）。

The term 'comparative method' has been used in two distinct ways. In its original and widest sense it refers to a method of proving genetic relationships between languages. This involves the systematic comparison of grammatical forms and lexemes, establishing correspondence sets between phonemes, putting forward hypotheses concerning a putative proto-system and the changes through which the systems of modern languages developed (see, for example, Meillet 1925/1967).

“比较法”也曾被狭义地用来描述一套自动重建原始语言音素的发现程序。这一程序最早由 Hoenigswald (1950) 提出，直接类比于当时流行的共时语言分析中用于确定音素的发现程序。Hoenigswald 认为，正如分布互补的音素相关音素可以归为一个音素的同位音（当时人们认为如此），分布互补的音素相似对应集也应该归为一个原始音素的反射。

'Comparative method' has also been used, in a narrower sense, to describe a set of discovery procedures which would automatically reconstruct the phonemes for a proto-language. This procedure was first put forth by Hoenigswald (1950), being directly analogised from the discovery procedures then in fashion for working out phonemes in synchronic linguistic analysis. Hoenigswald suggested that just as phonetically related phones that are in complementary distribution can be grouped together as allophones of one phoneme (as was believed at the time), so phonetically similar correspondence sets that are in complementary distribution should be grouped together as reflexes of a single proto-phoneme.

Hoenigswald 的比较重建发现程序迅速获得认可。他自己的教科书（Hoenigswald 1960）用其他对应集来陈述对应集的环境，并寻找将原始音素分组为原始音素的方法，从而为原始语言提供最简单的整体音位系统；这与音位程序类似，但 Hoenigswald 当时暗示这是一个不同于共时分析的问题。然而，Hockett 在他的教科书（1958：485505）中更进一步，用“比较方法”解释重建，就好像它与共时音位分析练习相同；每个不同的对应集都与原始语言中的一个音素相关，然后以熟悉的方式将它们分组为音素。Anttila 在他开创性的教科书（1972）中将比较方法描述为一种发现程序，但在某种程度上更类似于 Hoenigswald 而不是 Hockett。

Hoenigswald's discovery procedure for comparative reconstruction rapidly gained acceptance. His own textbook (Hoenigswald 1960) stated the environment for a correspondence set in terms of other correspondence sets and looked for the grouping into proto-phonemes that gives the simplest overall phonemic system for the proto-language; there is an analogy to phonemic procedures but Hoenigswald did now imply that it is a problem of a different type from synchronic analysis. However, Hockett, in his textbook (1958: 485505), went one step further and explained reconstruction by 'the comparative method' as if it were identical to an exercise in synchronic phonemic analysis; each distinct correspondence set relates to a phone in the proto-language and these are then grouped into phonemes in the familiar way. Anttila, in his seminal textbook (1972), describes the comparative method essentially as a discovery procedure but in a way more akin to Hoenigswald than to Hockett.

首先要注意的一点是，通过应用发现程序能够确定一种语言的音素的想法是一种幻想。首先，从来没有人以这种方式完全研究过一种语言的音素。其次，这是一个有缺陷的程序，它依赖于很少（或没有）语言遵循的假设。例如，它依赖于两个音素可能永远不会有重叠实现的假设。但它们往往确实如此。考虑一下：

The first point to note is that the idea of being able to establish the phonemes of a language through application of a discovery procedure is an illusion. First of all, no one ever has fully worked out the phonemes of a language in this way. Secondly, it is a flawed procedure, depending on assumptions that few (or no) languages comply with. For instance, it depends on the assumption that two phonemes may never have overlapping realisations. But they often do. Consider:

/i/ 在腭辅音后变形成 [i]

/i/ realised as [i] after a palatal consonant

以及其他地方

and as [e] elsewhere

/ ε / 在腭辅音后发成 [e]

/ ε / realised as [e] after a palatal consonant

和其他地方的[ε]一样

and as [ε] elsewhere

仅考虑手机及其分布，我们发现：

Considering just the phones, and their distribution, we find:

[i] 腭辅音后

[i] after a palatal consonant

[e] 在所有环境中

[e] in all environments

[ε] 腭辅音之后除外

[ε] except after a palatal consonant

这里 [i] 和 [e] 处于对立分布，因为它们都出现在腭音辅音之后，并且必须与不同的音素相关。 [e] 和 [ε] 也是如此。我们确实有 [i] 和 [ε] 处于互补分布，但这些声音在语音上并不相邻，不能被视为一个音素的同位异音。因此，应用发现程序对这些语音数据进行音位解决方案需要三个音素，这是错误的。

Here [i] and [e] are in contrastive distribution since they both occur after palatal consonants, and must relate to separate phonemes. The same applies for [e] and [ε]. We do have [i] and [ε] in complementary distribution but these sounds are not phonetically adjacent and could not be considered as allophones of one phoneme. Thus, the phonemic solution of this phonetic data, applying the discovery procedure, requires three phonemes, which is wrong.

当这种发现程序应用于重建时，也会出现类似的困难。我们可以用两个例子来说明。第一个例子涉及两种相关语言 A 和 B 中的条件变化：

Similar difficulties arise when this discovery procedure is applied in reconstruction. We can illustrate with two examples. The first involves conditioned changes in each of two related languages, A and B:

在 A 中：*d > t 最后在 B 中：*t > d 中间

in A: *d > t finally in B: *t > d medially

然后我们有：

We then have:

有三组对应关系，t:t、t:d 和 d:d。每组都与其他组呈对比分布：t:t 最后与 t:d 相对应，t:t 首先与 d:d 相对应，t:d 居中与 d:d 相对应。因此，我们必须重建三个原音素，每个对应关系一个。这是错误的解决方案。当然，我们需要将对应关系 t:d 分成两部分：居中位置的部分需要与 t:t 分组，而居末位置的部分需要与 d:d 分组。

There are three correspondence sets, t:t, t:d and d:d. Each is in contrastive distribution with the others t:t with t:d finally, t:t with d:d initially, and t:d with d:d medially. We must thus reconstruct three proto-phonemes, one for each correspondence set. This is the wrong solution. What was needed, of course, was to split the correspondence set t:d into two parts those in medial position need to be grouped with t:t and those in final position with d:d.

现在考虑一个例子，其中 A 有一个条件变化，但 B 有一个非条件变化（这里 j 代表腭塞音）：

Now consider an example where there is a conditioned change in A but an unconditioned change in B (here j represents a laminopalatal stop):

在 A 中：*d > j 在 i 之前 在 B 中：*j > d 处处

in A: *d > j before i in B: *j > d everywhere

然后我们得到：

We then get:

我们有两个对应集，d:d 和 j:d；j:d 无处不在，d:d 也无处不在（除了 i:i 之前），所以它们呈对比分布。每个对应集都必须与一个原始音素相关，大概是 d:d 对应的 *d 和 j:d 对应的 *j。这给出了正确的音素数量，但分配方式错误。(2) 的中间行来自 *d，但被错误地分配给 *j。请注意，这个错误的解决方案无法像 (1) 那样得到改进（通过区分 t:d 的中间和最后出现）。在 (2) 的第三行中，一些在 i:i 之前出现的对应集 j:d 来自 *d，但其中一些也来自 *j。没有办法解开这些集合。

We have two correspondence sets, d:d and j:d; j:d occurs everywhere and d:d everywhere except before i:i, so they are in contrastive distribution. Each must relate to a proto-phoneme, presumably *d for d:d and *j for j:d. This gives the correct number of phonemes but assigns them in the wrong way. The middle line of (2) comes from *d but is wrongly assigned to *j. And note that this wrong solution cannot be improved in the way that (1) could be (by distinguishing between the medial and final occurrences of t:d). Some of the correspondence sets j:d that occur before i:i come from *d, but some of them also come from *j, in the third line of (2). There is no way to disentangle these sets.

Hoenigswald 确实意识到了这些潜在困难，这些困难会影响他所建议的发现程序的有效运行（1960：124ff.），但他的警告在很大程度上没有引起后来的阐释者注意。当然，比较两种以上的语言会减少但绝不会消除通过应用此程序得到错误结果的可能性。

Hoenigswald did perceive some of these potential difficulties to the efficient operation of the discovery procedures he was suggesting (1960: 124ff.), but his caveats have largely gone unremarked by later expositors. Of course, comparing more than just two languages would lessen but by no means eliminate the potentiality for getting wrong results by applying this procedure.

可以看出，只有原始语言和现代语言之间发生的变化满足某些条件，比较方法发现程序才会产生正确的重建，而我们无法知道这些条件是否得到遵守。

It will be seen that the comparative method discovery procedure will only yield a correct reconstruction if certain conditions have applied to the changes that have taken place between the proto-language and modern languages and we have no way of knowing whether or not these conditions have been complied with.

这应该可以表明任何试图重建原始系统的尝试都是试探性的。通过比较重建的原始系统和原始形式来尝试将语言家族联系起来也是一种推测性行为。正如本文所建议的那样，语言家族通常在标点符号时期发展，但起源于平衡时期的末期。寻找家族谱系的谱系既不明智也不明智。

This should serve to indicate the tentative nature of any attempt to reconstruct a proto-system. And the speculative nature of trying to relate together language families by comparing reconstructed proto-systems and proto-forms. As suggested throughout this essay, language families generally evolve during a period of punctuation but have their origin in the end portion of a period of equilibrium. It is neither sensible nor provident to look for a family tree of family trees.

笔记

Notes

[ ←1 ]
[←1]

这里，间断平衡模型被应用于语言的演化和分裂。它也可以应用于其他层面，尽管这里不讨论这一点。例如，古迪纳夫（1992）描述了一种语言的静止期可能涉及微小的语音变化，这些变化将累积成突然而彻底的音系重构，并导致彻底的形态和词汇重构。

Here the punctuated equilibrium model is applied to the evolution and split of languages. It can also be applied at other levels, although this is not discussed here. For instance, Goodenough (1992) describes how a quiescent period within a language may involve small phonetic changes that will cumulate in a sudden and radical phonological restructuring, also leading to radical morphological and lexical restructuring.

[ ←2 ]
[←2]

建立语言平衡的地理区域将是交流相对容易的地区，通常是岛屿或河流盆地，或者是被交流障碍包围的区域，例如一边是海洋，另一边是山脉。这样的地区通常在地形、气候和食物资源方面相当同质，例如丛林地区可能包含一个语言区域，相邻的草原地区可能包含另一个语言区域，山区高原地区可能包含另一个语言区域。

A geographical area in which linguistic equilibrium is established will be a region within which there is relatively easy communication typically an island, or a river basin, or else an area enclosed by barriers to communication such as the sea on one side and a mountain range on another side. Such an area will generally be fairly homogeneous in terms of terrain, climate and food resources, e.g. a region of jungle may comprise one linguistic area, an adjacent region of grasslands another area, and a mountainous tableland region another area.

[ ←3 ]
[←3]

还要注意，语言的不同部分可能会以不同的速度变化。在一种语言中，动词的变化速度可能比名词快，而在另一种语言中，情况可能正好相反。

Note also that different parts of a language may change at different rates. In one language, verbs may change more rapidly than nouns, while this may be reversed in another language.

[ ←4 ]
[←4]

例如，英语长期以来一直是香港的主导语言，大多数人都试图学习英语，但英语对粤语的影响似乎很小（除了外来词）。相比之下，在台湾，普通话是主导语言，而台湾语被积极压制了四十多年，这两种语言都受到对方的严重影响，因此它们变得更加相似。（兰迪·拉波拉，个人通信。）

For instance, English has long been the prestige language in Hong Kong, and most people try to learn it, but there seems to have been very little English influence (other than loan words) on Cantonese. In contrast, in Taiwan, where Mandarin is the prestige language and Taiwanese was actively suppressed for more than forty years, each of the two languages has been heavily influenced by the other, so that they have become more alike. (Randy LaPolla, personal communication.)

[ ←5 ]
[←5]

我曾对多对澳大利亚语言的词汇进行过比较，结果发现短列表和长列表的同源词百分比相似（在 5% 以内）。Breen (1990: 54) 证实了这一点（参见下面第 3 章注释 4）。Comrie (1989) 讨论了巴布亚语言中不寻常的词汇百分比，这与这个问题有关。

I have compared vocabulary between many pairs of Australian languages and obtained similar cognate percentages (to within 5%) for shorter and longer lists. Breen (1990: 54) confirms this (and see note 4 to Chapter 3 below). Comrie (1989) discusses unusual vocabulary percentages in Papuan languages, which relate to this question.

[ ←6 ]
[←6]

考夫曼（例如 1990：26ff）是过去的声音，他仍然相信词汇统计学和语言年代学的有效性。确实，在某些情况下，这些方法确实能得到与其他来源获得的结果相符的结果；在其他情况下，它们之间存在很大分歧。因此，它们不值得信任。

 

Kaufman (e.g. 1990: 26ff.) is a voice from the past in still maintaining a belief in the validity of lexicostatistics and glottochronology. It is true that in some cases these methods do give results that are compatible with those obtained from other sources; in other cases there is wide divergence. As a consequence, they cannot be trusted.

 

[ ←7 ]
[←7]

还有其他一些特殊语言或说话风格被发明出来的例子，例如澳大利亚拉迪尔人的达明启蒙语言（Hale 1973；另见 Dixon 1980: 667）和瓦尔皮里人的 Tjiliwiri 风格（Hale 1971）。另见 Bakker 和 Mous 1994 的论文。

There are other examples of a special language or speech style simply being invented, e.g. the Damin initiation language of the Lardil people from Australia (Hale 1973; see also Dixon 1980: 667), and the Tjiliwiri style of the Warlpiri people (Hale 1971). See also the papers in Bakker and Mous 1994.

[ ←8 ]
[←8]

克里奥尔语通常是民族间精心混合的产物；它们可能是“语言进化的正常过程”的又一个例外。

Creole languages often result from engineered mixing of peoples; they may constitute a further exception to 'normal course of linguistic evolution'.

[ ←9 ]
[←9]

当然，也存在偶然的相似性，例如，在澳大利亚语言 Mbabaram 中，“狗”的单词是 dog（可以证明它是通过有规律的音位变化从原始形式 *gudaga 发展而来的 Dixon 1991c：362）。还有一些普遍的趋势，例如“吹”这个词通常模仿吹气的动作，并且通常具有类似 phu- 的形式。

There are also, of course, accidental similarities, e.g. in Mbabaram, an Australian language, the word for 'dog' is dog (it can be shown to have developed from an original form *gudaga by regular phonological changes Dixon 1991c: 362). There are also universal tendencies, such as the word for 'blow', which typically mimics the act of blowing, and often has a form something like phu-.

[ ←10 ]
[←10]

但请注意，通常无法判断相邻语言之间的相似点是由于共同的基因保留，还是由于借用（无论哪个方向）。

Note though that it is frequently impossible to tell whether a point of similarity between adjacent languages is due to shared genetic retention, or to borrowing (in either direction).

[ ←11 ]
[←11]

声调是最容易传播的特征之一（因此也是最不可靠的遗传关系指标之一）。兰迪·拉波拉（个人通信）报告说，羌语的南部方言中有声调，仅次于汉语（与汉语接触最多的方言声调数量最多，声调系统最稳定），但北部方言缺乏声调。

Tones are one of the features most open to diffusion (and thus one of the poorest indications of genetic relationship). Randy LaPolla (personal communication) reports that Qiang has tone in its southern dialects, spoken next to Chinese (and those with the most contact with Chinese have the largest number of tones and the most stable tone systems), but tones are lacking in the northern dialects.

[ ←12 ]
[←12]

造成这种情况的原因有很多。其一是，在许多语言中，名词是自由形式（词根可以不带词缀，用于引用和核心句法功能），而动词是束缚形式（词根从不单独使用，而必须从屈折系统中获取词缀）。

Breen (1990: 15463) 研究了澳大利亚多种语言中各种词语的可借性/遗传保留性。他的发现包括：动词的借用频率最低，动物名称的借用频率最高，物质文化项目的名称介于这两个极端之间。

There can be a number of reasons for this. One is that in many languages nouns are free forms (the root can occur with no affix, in citation and in one core syntactic function) whereas verbs are bound (the root is never used alone, but must take an affix from an inflectional system).

Breen (1990: 15463) has examined the borrowability/genetic retentiveness of various types of words across a selection of Australian languages. His findings include: verbs are borrowed least often and names for fauna most often, with names for items of material culture coming between these extremes.

[ ←13 ]
[←13]

例如，现代俄语借用动词和借用名词一样自由（Alexandra Aikhenvald，个人通信）。

For instance, Modern Russian borrows verbs as freely as it does nouns (Alexandra Aikhenvald, personal communication).

[ ←14 ]
[←14]

Campbell (1993) 讨论了语法借用的一些普遍趋势。这些趋势包括：一种语言倾向于借用与其整体语法组织模式相兼容的新结构；语言经常借用新结构来填补其自身语法系统的空白。

Campbell (1993) discusses some universal tendencies for grammatical borrowing. These include: a language tends to borrow new constructions that are compatible with its overall pattern of grammatical organisation; and languages often borrow to fill gaps in their own grammatical systems.

[ ←15 ]
[←15]

我们还得到了仿译，即短语或复合词的借译，保留了原始语言的语法，将形式逐个词素地翻译成借用语言。例如，现代英语单词 gospel 来自于古英语 god-spell *（“好消息”），而 god-spell * 是从希腊语 eu-angélion（“好消息”）仿译而来的。

We also get calques, the loan translation of a phrase or compound word, preserving the grammar of the original language with a morpheme-by-morpheme translation of forms into the borrowing language. For instance, the modern English word gospel comes from Old English god-spell * ('good-message') which was a calque from Greek eu-angélion ('good-message').

[ ←16 ]
[←16]

另一种特别容易借用的语法特征是连接词。当一种没有“或”、“和”、“直到”和“如果”等连接词的语言与一种有这些连接词的语言接触时，这些连接词可能成为最先被借用的语法项目之一。

Another type of grammatical feature particularly open to borrowing is connectives. When a language without connectives such as 'or', 'and', 'until' and 'if' comes in contact with a language that has them, these can be amongst the first grammatical items to be borrowed.

[ ←17 ]
[←17]

Heath (1978) 进行了类似的研究，调查在澳大利亚部分地区借用语法形式的条件。

Similar work has been done by Heath (1978) on investigating conditions under which grammatical forms may be borrowed in a part of Australia.

[ ←18 ]
[←18]

另一项开创性的研究是纳德卡尼 (Nadkarni) (1975) 的研究，该研究讨论了在接触情况下，卡纳达语（一种达罗毗荼语）中的关系从句结构如何取代孔卡尼语（一种印度-雅利安语）中的本土关系从句结构。

Another seminal study is that of Nadkarni (1975), discussing how the relative clause construction in Kannada, a Dravidian language, is replacing the native relative clause construction in Konkani, an Indo-Aryan language, in a contact situation.

[ ←19 ]
[←19]

例子见 Dixon (1980: 989, 151)。禁忌可以延伸到外来词。1980 年左右，一个叫 Jack 的人去世了，他的社区成员（讲西部沙漠语言的人）禁忌使用 cheque 这个词（如社会保障支票）。在禁忌持续期间，人们用 letter 这个词来代替它（Gloria Brennan，个人通信）。

Examples are in Dixon (1980: 989, 151). The tabooing can extend to loan words. Around 1980 a man called Jack died and members of his community (speakers of the Western Desert language) tabooed the word cheque (as in social security cheque). While the taboo lasted, the word letter was used in its place (Gloria Brennan, personal communication).

[ ←20 ]
[←20]

1963 年，当我开始在澳大利亚进行实地考察时，我的土著老师克洛伊·格兰特 (Chloe Grant) 解释说，她所在的地区有两个部落，并对他们的特征进行了如下描述：Jirrbal 用 bana 表示“水”，用 buni 表示“火”，而 Girramay 用 gamu 表示“水”，用 yugu 表示“火”。进一步的研究表明，这些是同一种语言（就该术语的语言意义而言）的相互可理解的方言，大约 80% 的词汇是相同的，语法也非常相似。但说话者会根据一些不同的词汇来识别部落归属，例如本例中的“水”和“火”。

 

When I began fieldwork in Australia in 1963, my Aboriginal teacher Chloe Grant explained that there were two tribes in her region and characterised them as follows: Jirrbal say bana for 'water' and buni for 'fire' but Girramay use gamu for 'water' and yugu for 'fire'. Closer study showed that these are mutually intelligible dialects of one language (in the linguistic sense of the term), sharing about 80% of their lexicon and with very similar grammar. But speakers identify tribal affiliation in terms of a few lexemes that differ, such as 'water' and 'fire' in this instance.

 

[ ←21 ]
[←21]

值得注意的是，50% 的词汇相同（70-80% 的语法）并不意味着 50% 的可理解性。在这种情况下，可理解性会很低（当然，学习和理解与自己的语言有这种程度相似性的语言相对容易）。

It is important to note that 50% vocabulary in common (and 7080% grammar) does not make for 50% intelligibility. There would be little intelligibility in such a situation (although, of course, it is relatively easy to learn to speak and understand a language which has this degree of similarity to one's own).

[ ←22 ]
[←22]

14 Alpher 和 Nash (ms. 1996) 认为实际均衡水平应低于 50%。然而，事实是大多数澳大利亚语言确实与至少一种邻近语言的词汇量得分达到 50%，这支持了这里提出的观点，以及澳大利亚大陆是一个长期存在的扩散区这一观点。

14 Alpher and Nash (ms. 1996) suggest that the actual equilibrium level should be less than 50%. However, the fact remains that most Australian languages do have a 50% vocabulary score with at least one neighbouring language, supporting the ideas put forward here, and the notion that the continent is a long-standing diffusion area.

[ ←23 ]
[←23]

但请注意布卢姆菲尔德的警告（1933：318）： “比较方法是我们重建史前语言的唯一方法，它对于绝对统一的语言群体和突然、尖锐的分裂都十分有效。由于这些前提从未完全实现，因此比较方法不能声称能够描绘历史进程。”

But note Bloomfield's caveat (1933: 318): 'The comparative method, then our only method for the reconstruction of prehistoric language would work accurately for absolutely uniform speech-communities and sudden, sharp cleavages. Since these presuppositions are never fully realised, the comparative method cannot claim to picture the historical process. '

[ ←24 ]
[←24]

格林伯格 (1989: 112) 表示，“尽管我已经非常小心，但如果在处理如此大量的材料时，没有事实或解释上的错误，那将是奇迹。”克丘亚语专家阿德拉尔 (1989: 253) 回应道：“如果看看格林伯格提供的数据的质量……错误形式的数量可能超过正确形式的数量”

Greenberg (1989: 112) stated 'although I have exercised great care, it would be miraculous if, handling such a vast amount of material, there were no errors of fact or interpretation'. Adelaar (1989: 253), a specialist on Quechua, responded: 'if one looks at the quality of the data Greenberg presents . . . the number of erroneous forms probably exceeds that of the correct forms'

[ ←25 ]
[←25]

还有格林伯格的“印度-太平洋假说”（1971），该假说旨在表明新几内亚的 60 多个巴布亚家族、塔斯马尼亚岛已灭绝的语言以及安达曼群岛上使用的各种语言在遗传上是相关的。他提出了 11 项语法标准，而塔斯马尼亚语仅满足其中一项。在列出的 84 个词汇项目中，假定的塔斯马尼亚同源词被提及的不到四分之一，没有一个令人信服。这个想法缺乏任何实质内容，甚至可能比格林伯格的美洲印第安人作品更加异想天开。

There is also Greenberg's 'Indo-Pacific hypothesis' (1971) purporting to show that the 60-odd Papuan families from New Guinea, the extinct languages of Tasmania, and the various languages spoken in the Andaman Islands are genetically related. He offers eleven grammatical criteria; only one of which is satisfied by Tasmanian. Of the eighty-four lexical items listed, putative Tasmanian cognates are mentioned for less than one quarter; none of them is convincing. This idea lacks any substance, and is perhaps even more fanciful than Greenberg's American Indian work.

[ ←26 ]
[←26]

马蒂索夫 (1990: 107) 评论说，格林伯格关于美国语言的研究“只是冰山一角。我们承诺不久后会再出版一本书……这将证明印欧语本身属于一个更大的语系，即“欧亚语系”，其中包括日语、乌拉尔-阿尔泰语和爱斯基摩-阿留申语。对于许多语言学家来说，这种观点更多地属于宗教信仰的范畴，而不是科学上可检验的假设，与“所有语言都具有相同的深层结构”和“我们出生时星星的位置决定了我们的性格”的说法差不多。

Matisoff (1990: 107) comments that Greenberg's work on American languages 'is only the tip of the iceberg. We are promised another book shortly . . . that will prove that Indo-European itself belongs to a much vaster language family called ''Eurasiatic", which includes Japanese, Ural-Altaic and Eskimo-Aleut. For many linguists, such views fall more into the category of religious beliefs than scientifically testable hypotheses, about on a par with claims that: "all languages have the same underlying deep structure" and "the position of the stars at the moment of our birth determines our character".

[ ←27 ]
[←27]

词汇统计学和语言年代学仍在世界少数几个角落使用（包括俄罗斯，这种方法于 20 世纪 80 年代引入该国，而西方的严肃语言学已经抛弃了这种方法 20 年）。我很遗憾地告诉大家，其中一个角落就在澳大利亚。我在《澳大利亚语言概况》一书的初稿（出版于 1980 年，名为 Dixon）中用了几页来阐述为什么不信任词汇统计分类法。约翰·里昂斯 (John Lyons) 是该书出版商的学术编辑，他建议缩短这一讨论，因为他认为所有语言学家当时都知道词汇统计学和语言年代学的缺点。我采纳了他的建议。但里昂斯不知道，有关词汇统计学的消息还没有（现在仍然没有）传到一些澳大利亚学者的耳朵里。

最新的此类研究成果来自麦康维尔，他之前曾发表过关于澳大利亚语言学描述和历史主题的优秀研究。麦康维尔 (1996) 引用了乌舍尔 (Ussher) 的话（乌舍尔通过汇总《圣经》中的日期得出世界是在公元前 4004 年创造的），并给出了假定家谱中中间节点的具体日期，并邀请考古学家根据该日期校准他们的结果。他指出：“奥格雷迪认为，根据标准的语言年代学，帕马-尼永甘语的年代应为 8000 年左右，但更现实的数字应该是这个数字的一​​半（4000 年前），因为词汇禁忌等因素加速了澳大利亚的词汇变化。”麦康维尔说，他“确信”这个年代“更像是 6000 年，而不是 40,000 年甚至 12,000 年。”迪克森（即将出版）解释了为什么不应将帕马-尼永根类型学群体赋予遗传地位，以及为什么有关澳大利亚语言区域内时间深度的所有问题都只有一个诚实的答案：“我们不知道”。

Lexicostatistics and glottochronology are still practised in a few odd corners of the world (including Russia, where these methods were introduced in the 1980s, twenty years after being discarded by serious linguistics in the West). I am sorry to have to report that one of these corners is in Australia. The first draft of my general survey of Australian languages (published as Dixon 1980) included a couple of pages on why the lexicostatistical classification should be regarded with distrust. John Lyons was the publisher's academic editor for the volume and he recommended this discussion be shortened, since he believed all linguists were by then familiar with the shortcomings of lexicostatistics and glottochronology. I took his advice. But Lyons wasn't aware that the news about lexicostatistics had not (and still has not) reached some Australianists.

The most recent piece of work along these lines is by McConvell, who had previously published excellent studies on descriptive and historical topics in Australian linguistics. Quoting Ussher (who by adding up the dates in the Bible decided that the world was created in 4004 BC), McConvell (1996) gives specific dates for intermediate nodes on a putative family tree against which he invites archaeologists to calibrate their results. He states: 'O'Grady argues that on the basis of standard glottochronology, Pama-Nyungan would be assigned an age of about 8000 years, but that a more realistic figure would be about half that (4000 BP) because of accelerated lexical change in Australia due to such factors as lexical taboo'. McConvell says he is 'convinced' it 'is much more like 6000 years old than 40,000 years or even 12,000 years'. Dixon (forthcoming) explains why the Pama-Nyungan typological group should not be assigned genetic status, and why all questions about time depth within the Australian linguistic area can have only one honest answer: 'we don't know'.

[ ←28 ]
[←28]

突厥语、蒙古语和通古斯语经常被认为属于一个更大的语系——阿尔泰语。然而，现在大多数研究这些语言的专家认为，它们的相似性主要是区域性的（例如，参见 Baldi 1990: 477-561）。

Turkic, Mongolian and Tungusic have often been taken to make up a larger family, Altaic. However, most experts on these languages now believe their similarities to be largely areal (see, for instance, Baldi 1990: 477561).

[ ←29 ]
[←29]

一些诺斯特拉蒂克主义者认为阿非罗亚细亚语是诺斯特拉蒂克内部的一个语系；另一些人则认为阿非罗亚细亚语是一个与诺斯特拉蒂克同级的语系，并且在诺斯特拉蒂克-阿非罗亚细亚语系内与其有遗传上的联系。

Some Nostraticists consider Afroasiatic to be a family within Nostratic; others have Afroasiatic as a family on a par with Nostratic, and genetically linked to it within Nostratic-Afroasiatic.

[ ←30 ]
[←30]

这些语系已经被认可了很长一段时间，但没有一位学者能够证明（令整个学术界满意）其中任何两个语系之间存在遗传关系。但莫斯科诺斯特拉主义者仅凭几年的工作就提出了所有这些语系之间的遗传关系。

一下子就得到了七八个显赫家族之间高层关系的证据，这种说法简直难以置信。这就像有人报道英国女王兼职上门推销百科全书（这就是她拒绝所有晚宴邀请的原因）。人们根本不会理会这样的建议；从我们对所处世界的了解来看，这显然是胡说八道。

一些受人尊敬的学者已经注意到该提案的细节，正如所料，最初的反应是该提案必定是无稽之谈，这一反应得到了证实。在许多情况下，所使用的基本词形是错误的；比较方法的方法论远远超出了其极限，在音系和语义“对应”方面允许了很大的自由度；而且“重构”是有选择性的和不完整的。（例如，请参阅 Campbell，即将出版-a，以及其中的许多进一步参考资料。）

These language families have been recognised for a considerable period of time and no scholar has been able to prove (to the satisfaction of the entire academic community) that any two of them are genetically related. But the Moscow Nostraticists put forward a genetic relationship between all of them on the basis of just a few years' work.

Such a scenario that a proof has been obtained, all at once, of the higher-level relationship of seven or eight well-established families is simply implausible. It is rather like someone reporting that the Queen of England moonlights as a door-to-door encyclopaedia salesperson (which is why she declines all invitations to dinner parties). One would simply pay no attention at all to such a suggestion; it is, from our knowledge of the world in which we live, palpable poppycock.

Some respected scholars have paid attention to the details of the proposal and, as expected, the initial reaction that it must be nonsensical is borne out. In many cases the basic word forms used are erroneous; the methodology of the comparative method is stretched way beyond its limits, allowing a wide latitude in phonological and semantic 'correspondences'; and the 'reconstructions' are selective and incomplete. (See, for instance, Campbell, forthcoming-a, and many further references therein.)

[ ←31 ]
[←31]

诺斯特拉主义者也犯了一个公理错误。他们提出了这样一种观点，即在构建两种语言之间的遗传联系时，主要要考虑的是词素。然而，从梅耶特开始，每一位比较方法的支持者都强调建立语法形式之间的对应关系，最好是语法范式之间的对应关系的重要性（例如，参见尼科尔斯 1996 年）。这是印欧语、乌拉尔语、南高加索语和达罗毗荼语的遗传证明所基于的原则。然而，诺斯特拉主义者在假设更高层次的关系时赋予了截然不同的优先级。

The Nostraticists are also guilty of an error of axiom. They have put forward the idea that the main thing to be considered when formulating a genetic connection between two languages is lexemes. Yet every proponent of the comparative method from Meillet on down emphasises the primary importance of establishing correspondences between grammatical forms, preferably between grammatical paradigms (see, for instance, Nichols 1996). This is the principle on which the genetic proofs of Indo-European, Uralic, South Caucasian and Dravidian are based. Yet the Nostraticists assign quite different priorities in positing higher-level relationships.

[ ←32 ]
[←32]

原始印欧语具有相当融合的结构（带有元音变换和重音转换）。这种结构可以重建，因为这些融合特征在许多后代中都保留了下来（在这方面我们很幸运有古老的记录）。

Proto-Indo-European had a fairly fusional structure (with ablaut and stress shift). This structure can be reconstructed because these fusional features have been retained in many of the descendants (and here we are fortunate in having old records).

[ ←33 ]
[←33]

其他有用的讨论包括 Matisoff (1976) 和 DeLancey (1985)。

Other useful discussions include Matisoff (1976) and DeLancey (1985).

[ ←34 ]
[←34]

壮侗语系的语言是孤立的，但语言之间和语言内部都存在语义相关的词组，这些词组似乎通过元音变换等方式相关联（Li 1977：3841，以及 Tony Diller，个人通信）。这表明原始语言可能具有融合性。

Languages of the Tai-Kadai family are isolating, but there are semantically related sets of words both between languages and within languages that have the appearance of being related through something like ablaut (Li 1977: 3841, and Tony Diller, personal communication). These suggest that the proto-language may have had a fusional character.

[ ←35 ]
[←35]

为了避免人们认为这是循环论证，请允许我提供一个标准，以识别一大批享有盛誉的历史语言学家：任何在美国或欧洲经济共同体国家一流大学教授该学科的人。

Lest this be thought circular, let me provide a criterion for recognising a large group of reputable historical linguists: anyone who teaches the subject at a leading university in the USA or in an EEC nation.

[ ←36 ]
[←36]

如果本文提出的间断平衡模型确实有效，那么考古学家和遗传学家在构建自己的假设时就应该注意平衡期的概念。事实上，最近有迹象表明他们可能开始这样做了。

If the punctuated equilibrium model, put forward in this essay, does have validity, it follows that archaeologists and geneticists should pay attention to the idea of equilibrium periods in framing their own hypotheses. Indeed, there are recent signs that they may be starting to do so.

[ ←37 ]
[←37]

体质人类学家 Krantz (1988) 为这一年代提供了合理的论证。考古学家 Renfrew (1987) 在一部广为人知的著作中也提出了类似的年代；作者思维敏捷，但缺乏适当的历史语言学方法论训练，因此他的著作无法为这场争论做出语言学上的重要贡献。

The physical anthropologist Krantz (1988) provides reasoned argumentation for such a date. A similar date is suggested by the archaeologist Renfrew (1987) in a work which has received wide publicity; the author has an agile mind but lacks an appropriate training in the methodology of historical linguistics for his work to constitute a linguistically significant contribution to the debate.

[ ←38 ]
[←38]

假定的原始语言可能在何处使用（原始家园）是一个重要问题，本文不作讨论。争论通常围绕着某些动植物（其名称可以重建）的分布，以及与特定地方物质文化阶段的假定相关性。所有这些类型的争论都与确定某种动物或植物的年代问题有关，例如，在 6000 年前和 10000 年前，它们可能具有不同的地理分布。另一个经常被援引的标准是，原始家园可能是该语系现代语言多样性最多的地方；这是需要仔细重新考虑的事情。

The question of the place where a putative proto-language is likely to have been spoken (the proto-homeland) is an important one, which is not discussed here. Arguments generally turn on where certain flora and fauna (whose names can be reconstructed) can be found, and on postulated correlations with stages of material culture in particular places. All these types of arguments relate to the question of dating a certain animal or plant may have had different geographical distributions at, say, 6000 BP and 10000 BP. A further criterion that is often invoked is that the proto-homeland is likely to be where the greatest diversity of modern languages from the family is found; this is something which demands careful reconsideration.

[ ←39 ]
[←39]

我所知道的关于确定遗传关系的标准和建立子群的标准的最佳表述是格林伯格的两篇论文 (1957: 3555)《语言之间的遗传关系》和《语言子群问题》。在格林伯格的非洲、印度太平洋和美洲著作中，他使用了“大规模比较”的方法，并指出这是一个初步步骤。作为后续步骤，应应用比较方法，通过为每个假定的遗传群重建原始语言来确认初始假设。对于建议的大多数分组，无论是格林伯格还是其他任何人都没有采取这个后续步骤。请参阅上文第 4.1 节 (a) 下的评论。

 

The best statements I know of the criteria for determining genetic relationship and the criteria for establishing subgrouping are Greenberg's two essays (1957: 3555) 'Genetic relationship among languages' and 'The problem of linguistic subgroupings'. In Greenberg's African, Indo-Pacific and American work he used his method of 'mass comparison' and stated that this was a preliminary step. As a later step the comparative method should be applied, with the initial hypotheses confirmed by reconstruction of a proto-language for every postulated genetic grouping. Neither Greenberg nor anyone else has taken this later step, for the majority of the groupings suggested. See comments under (a) of §4.1 above.

 

[ ←40 ]
[←40]

当语言传播到没有邻居的地方时，亚群化可能是一个更直接的问题。例如，波利尼西亚亚群以每个岛屿一种语言为基础传播，人群之间接触很少，也没有借用。在这种情况下，两种语言共同的发展几乎必然是语言发展共同时期的证据，即亚群化。（分裂发生后，每种语言都经历了同样的变化，这种可能性很小。）

Where languages spread into places where they have no neighbours then subgrouping can be a more straightforward matter. For instance, the Polynesian sub-group spread out on the basis of one language per island with very little contact between populations and no borrowing. In this circumstance any development common to two languages is almost bound to be evidence of a shared period of linguistic development, i.e. of subgrouping. (There is just a slight possibility that each language underwent the same change after splitting had taken place.)

[ ←41 ]
[←41]

关于是否应将恩加雅尔达语视为一个遗传亚群的研究仍在继续（艾伦·丹奇，个人通信）。

Work is continuing on whether the Ngayarda languages should be regarded as making up a genetic subgroup (Alan Dench, personal communication).

[ ←42 ]
[←42]

澳大利亚的情况也说明了这一点。Yanyula 语言位于一个地区的边缘，该地区的语言既有前缀，也有名词类，这两种特征最近才传入 Yanyula。名词类（或性别）由名词前缀表示。其中之一是“食物”类，以前缀 ma- 为标志，这显然是名词 mayi“可食用的植物食品”的语法化（这在澳大利亚非常普遍）。及物主语名词采用作格后缀。有趣的是，当“食物”前缀添加到作格形式的名词时，它的形式为 mungu- *（来自 ma- 加作格 -ngu*，第一个元音同化为第二个元音）。最初，及物主语名词短语由一般名词 mayi 加作格，以及特定名词加作格组成；在这个功能中，整个 mayi-plus-case 已经发展成为名词类前缀（Kirton 1971）。

This can also be illustrated from Australia. The Yanyula language is on the edge of a region whose languages show prefixing and also noun classes, and both traits have diffused into Yanyula rather recently. There is a system of noun classes (or genders) shown by a prefix to the noun. One of these is the 'food' class, marked by a prefix ma-, which is plainly a grammaticisation of the noun mayi 'edible vegetable food' (this occurs very widely in Australia). Nouns in transitive subject function take an ergative case suffix. The interesting point is that when the 'food' prefix is added to a noun in ergative form, it has the form mungu- * (from ma- plus ergative -ngu*, with the first vowel assimilating to the second). Originally a transitive subject noun phrase would have consisted of generic noun mayi plus ergative case, and specific noun plus ergative case; it is the whole mayi-plus-case which has developed into a noun class prefix in this function (Kirton 1971).

[ ←43 ]
[←43]

由于语言的变化速度不同，最明智的做法似乎是不要建议这个时间轴上的点对应多少个世纪。

Since languages change at different rates, it seems wisest not to suggest how many centuries might be appropriate for the points on this time axis.

[ ←44 ]
[←44]

另一种选择是，可以发展出一种通用方言；这是一种简化的方言，用于两种截然不同的方言使用者之间的交流。粗略地说，通用方言可能包括两种方言中都出现的特征，但不包括在一种方言中只出现的特征。（参见 Siegel 1993 中的论文。）

An alternative is that a koiné could develop; this is a simplified dialect used for communication between speakers of two rather different dialects. Roughly, a koiné is likely to include features that occur in both dialects, but not those that are found in just one of them. (See the papers in Siegel 1993.)

[ ←45 ]
[←45]

其中一种方言可能（或可能成为）在社会政治上占主导地位，然后可能会出现单方面的适应，即非知名方言的使用者会吸收知名方言的一些特征。

One of the dialects might be (or might become) socio-politically dominant, and there could then be unilateral accommodation, with speakers of the non-prestige dialect adopting some features from the prestige variety.

[ ←46 ]
[←46]

有关冲绳情况的信息由大西昌之 (Masayuki Onishi) 提供。

Information on the Okinawan situation was provided by Masayuki Onishi.

[ ←47 ]
[←47]

西班牙语和葡萄牙语就是一个例子。它们可以被视为一种语言的不同方言，也可以被视为两种非常密切相关的语言（见上文第 2 节）。每个国家都试图在语言上和其他方面尽可能地与其他国家不同，以加强他们各自的政治身份。例如，在正字法中，罗马字母未涵盖的声音使用不同的符号：西班牙语使用“ll”和“ñ”表示腭侧音和鼻音，而葡萄牙语使用“lh”和“nh”

One example of this involves Spanish and Portuguese. These could be regarded as divergent dialects of one language, or as two very closely related languages (see §2 above). Each nation tries to be as different as possible from the other in language, and in other matters to reinforce their separate political identities. For instance, in the orthography, different symbols are used for those sounds not covered by the letters of the Roman alphabet: Spanish uses 'll' and 'ñ' for the palatal lateral and nasal, while Portuguese employs 'lh' and 'nh'

[ ←48 ]
[←48]

许多现代语言都有拟声词，即在句子中具有语法功能的声音符号词。在一篇富有洞察力的论文中，Alpher (1994) 描述了北昆士兰州 Yir-Yoront 中的一类拟声词​​；其中包括 thut，其含义是“采取稳定的相对位置”（可能与放下某物的声音有关）。西澳大利亚州 Djaru 语中有一个覆盖词 yut“坐”，Alpher 认为，它可能起源于 Yir-Yoront 中类似于 thut 的拟声词。

意音在许多非洲语言中扮演着重要的角色，例如 pele-pele 表示“小”，Kpelle 中的 wclc-wclc * 表示“永远”（Welmers 1973: 469）。（请注意 dilly-dally 和 wishy-washy 等英语单词。）

Many modern languages have ideophones, sound-symbolic words that have grammatical function in a sentence. In a perceptive paper, Alpher (1994) describes a class of ideophones in Yir-Yoront, from North Queensland; it includes thut with the meaning 'assume a stable relative position' (presumably relating to the sound of putting something down). In Djaru, from Western Australia, there is a coverb yut 'sit' which, Alpher suggests, may have its origin in an ideophone similar to thut in Yir-Yoront.

Ideophones play an important role in many African languages, e.g. pele-pele 'small' and wclc-wclc * 'forever' in Kpelle (Welmers 1973: 469). (And note English words such as dilly-dally and wishy-washy.)

[ ←49 ]
[←49]

声音象征（或音感）是语言学教科书中很少提及的一个主题。问题在于人们对它的了解还不够，无法用科学的方法来论证它。但它太重要了，不容忽视，应该成为未来研究的重点。（同时，感兴趣的读者可以参考 Hinton、Nichols 和 Ohala 1994 年的著作，以及 Reichard 1940 年的开创性研究。）

Sound symbolism (or phonaesthesia) is a topic scarcely mentioned in textbooks on linguistics. The trouble is that not enough is understood to say anything scientific about it. But it is too important a topic to ignore, and should be a high priority for future research. (Meanwhile, the interested reader is referred to Hinton, Nichols and Ohala 1994, and to the pioneering study in Reichard 1940.)

[ ←50 ]
[←50]

语言是如何发展起来的是一个庞大而又困难的话题，超出了本文的讨论范围。这里我仅就可能涉及的众多因素中的两个提供一些提示。

How language developed is a large and difficult topic which falls outside the scope of this essay. Here I just offer hints concerning two of the many factors that may have been involved.

[ ←51 ]
[←51]

抽象术语自然是从具体术语发展而来的。在 Xerente（巴西 Jê 家族）中，“二”这个词 ponkwane 的本义是“鹿的足迹”，因为鹿的蹄子有两个相对的部分（Rinaldo de Matos 和 Diana Green，个人通信）；而在世界许多地方的语言中，“五”都来自“手”。

Abstract terms naturally develop from concrete ones. In Xerente (Jê family, Brazil) the word for 'two', ponkwane, has an original meaning 'deer track', since the cloven deer hoof has two apposed parts (Rinaldo de Matos and Diana Green, personal communication); and in languages from many parts of the world 'five' comes from 'hand'.

[ ←52 ]
[←52]

这在某种程度上是一种理想化。例如，请参阅 Barth (1969) 的论文，了解“族群”的定义（但所有定义都指标点符号模式中的社会）及其相关困难。这里给出的特征基于澳大利亚过去的情况以及亚马逊地区过去和现在的情况（来自对文献的研究和我自己的实地工作）。

This is, to some extent, an idealisation. See, for instance, the essays in Barth (1969) for definitions of 'ethnic group' (all, however, referring to societies in punctuation mode) and difficulties associated with these. The characterisation given here is based on the past situation in Australia and past and present situations in Amazonia (from study of the literature and from my own field work).

[ ←53 ]
[←53]

每个政治团体通常都有自己的名字，其邻人也会给他们起名字。这些名字可能有所不同；例如，我们有 German（英语）、allemand（法语）和 Deutsch（德语）。偶尔我们会发现一个团体没有自己的名字；但它的邻人总是有一个名字。我在亚马逊地区工作过的一个小部落没有自己的名字（当被问及这一点时，它的成员只是说他们是 ee jokana“我们，真正的人民”）。但邻近的 Jamamadi 部落称他们为 Amara；该地区的非印第安巴西人称他们为 Jarawara。Randy LaPolla 报告（个人通信）他目前正在一个横跨中国/缅甸边境的大型语言群体中进行实地工作，该群体整体上没有自己的名字。一方面，中国人称他们为独龙族（中国境内的该族群最近采用该族群作为自己的官方名称），而另一方面，缅甸人称他们为侬族或哈坎侬族（缅甸人民最近发明了“拉旺族”一词来描述自己）。

Each political group generally has a name for itself, and will also be named by its neighbours. These names may differ; for instance, we have German (in English), allemand (in French), and Deutsch (in German itself). Occasionally we find a group that has no name for itself; but its neighbours always have one. The small tribe I have been working amongst in Amazonia has no name for itself (when pressed on this point its members simply say that they are ee jokana 'we, the real people'). But the neighbouring Jamamadi tribe call them Amara; and the non-Indian Brazilians in the region call them Jarawara.Randy LaPolla reports (personal communication) that he is currently doing field work among a large language group straddling the China/Myanmar (Burma) border, which has no name for itself as a whole. The Chinese on one side refer to them as Dulong (which the group in China have recently adopted as their own official name) while the Burmese on the other side call them Nung or Hkanung (the people in Burma have recently invented the term Rawang to describe themselves).

[ ←54 ]
[←54]

请注意，有时人们可以断定语言借用了某种语言，但无法确定哪种语言借用了哪种语言。也就是说，我们可能有两种语言，X 和 Y（它们在遗传上没有密切的联系），它们共享一个语法特征，但可能很难或不可能判断 X 是从 Y 借用的，还是反之亦然。

Note that sometimes one can tell that there has been borrowing, without being certain which language has borrowed from which. That is, we may have two languages, X and Y (which are not closely genetically related) sharing a grammatical feature, and it may be difficult or impossible to tell whether X borrowed it from Y, or vice versa.

[ ←55 ]
[←55]

这个数字当然适用于澳大利亚（见§3.2），这是一个长期存在的平衡区，仅在过去 200 年内才出现过中断。需要做更多的工作来确定它在其他地区的适用程度。

This figure certainly applies in Australia (see §3.2), a long-standing equilibrium area which has only been punctuated within the last 200 years. More work is required to ascertain the extent to which it applies in other regions.

[ ←56 ]
[←56]

请注意，waru 和 warlu 似乎是同源的；它们一定是通过不同的遗传/传播途径进入该语言的。

Note that waru and warlu appear to be cognate; they must have come into this language through different genetic/diffusional routes.

[ ←57 ]
[←57]

一段过渡期必然会突然开始。但最终它会逐渐消退，进入一个新的平衡期。在平衡期内，可能会出现轻微的过渡，只影响一些社区及其语言（可能导致轻微分裂，形成一个小型家族树），但强度不足以传播和贯穿整个地区的平衡状态。显然，这一假设的全部影响仍有待研究。

A period of punctuation will necessarily begin abruptly. But at the end it will gradually fade into a new period of equilibrium. Within a period of equilibrium there could be minor punctuations, affecting just some communities and their languages (perhaps leading to a minor split, with a small family tree), but without enough strength to spread and punctuate the equilibrium state in the entire area. Obviously, the full ramifications of this hypothesis have still to be studied.

[ ←58 ]
[←58]

一些语言学家错误地认为“所有语言都是平等的”。虽然所有语言大致相同（即没有一种语言比其他语言复杂六倍，也没有原始语言），但它们绝不是完全相同的。（Slobin，1982 年，展示了不同语言的使用者如何以完全不同的速度掌握其语法的可比部分。）我曾在澳大利亚、大洋洲和亚马逊地区进行过实地研究，这些语言的描述难度当然不尽相同。毫无疑问，一种语言可能比另一种语言具有更大的整体语法复杂性和/或在某个领域具有交流优势。但这是另一本书的主题。

There is a mistaken belief among some linguists that 'all languages are equal'. While it is the case that all languages are roughly equal (that is, no language is six times as complex as any other, and there are no primitive languages), it is by no means the case that they are exactly equal. (Slobin, 1982, shows how speakers of different languages master comparable parts of their grammars at a quite different rate.) I have done field work on languages in Australia, Oceania and Amazonia and they were certainly not all equally difficult to describe. There is no doubt that one language may have greater overall grammatical complexity and/or a communicative advantage in a certain sphere, over another. But this is a topic for a separate book.

[ ←59 ]
[←59]

数学中有一个分支叫做突变理论，它研究自然进程中的突然不连续性，这是进程性质的一个特征（Arnol'd 1992 中有一个简单的介绍）。这可能与间断平衡的概念在语言学中的应用有关；这是一个有待进一步研究的课题。（另见上文第 1 章注释 1。）

There is a branch of mathematics called Catastrophe Theory, which deals with abrupt discontinuities within a natural progression, as a feature of the nature of the progression (there is an elementary introduction in Arnol'd 1992). This may well relate to the idea of punctuated equilibrium as applied to linguistics; it is a topic for further investigation. (See also note 1 to Chapter 1 above.)

[ ←60 ]
[←60]

直到大约 10,000 年前，塔斯马尼亚还是澳大利亚的一部分；后来海平面上升，将其与澳大利亚大陆隔绝。没有证据表明在此期间塔斯马尼亚与澳大利亚大陆有任何联系。因此，塔斯马尼亚没有传播到整个或大部分澳大利亚的各种文化特征，包括斧头、矛投掷器、回旋镖和土狗（或澳洲野狗）（Mulvaney 1975：161）。不幸的是，白人入侵者倾向于先开枪，然后再问问题。结果，塔斯马尼亚人的语言几乎没有保留下来（只有几个单词，几乎没有语法），因此我们无法说出语言是如何受到与大陆长期隔离的影响的。

Until about 10,000 years ago, Tasmania was part of Australia; the sea-level then rose, cutting it off. There is no evidence of any contract between Tasmania and mainland Australia during the intervening period. The various cultural traits that have diffused across all or most of Australia are thus absent from Tasmania these include axes, spear-throwers, boomerangs and the native dog (or dingo) (Mulvaney 1975: 161). Unfortunately, there was a propensity among the white invaders to shoot first and ask questions later. As a result, little was preserved of the Tasmanians' languages (just a few words, but almost no grammar), so that we can say nothing concerning how the languages were affected by this long period of isolation from the mainland.

[ ←61 ]
[←61]

我并不是想描绘“高贵野蛮人”的田园诗画。他们总是会害怕一些邻居（也可能害怕恶灵），发生一些冲突和杀戮。但这些冲突总是局限于地方层面，部分原因是政治团体规模较小，部分原因是双方心照不宣，不会走得太远。例如，澳大利亚土著人会通过有组织的部落间战斗来解决争端，但这些战斗通常在有人被杀之前就结束了（或者，一旦发生一人死亡就结束了）。

I am not trying to present an idyllic picture of the 'noble savage'. There would always be fear of some neighbours (and probably of evil spirits), some skirmishes and killings. But these would invariably be confined to a local level, partly because of the small size of political groups, and partly due to a tacit understanding not to go too far. Australian Aborigines, for instance, would settle disputes by organised inter-tribal fights, but these were generally terminated before anyone got killed (or else, as soon as one death took place).

[ ←62 ]
[←62]

一种新的激进宗教的出现可能会对语言产生深远的影响。任何语言中，最迅速的变化可能是公元 400 年至 600 年间古爱尔兰语的变化。这一时期末期使用的语言对于 200 年前的人来说是完全听不懂的。这些变化与基督教传入爱尔兰有关；我们认为，由于年轻人接受了新信仰，而老年人拒绝了新信仰，因此代际（或许是阶级）之间的沟通出现了障碍。

The arrival of a new and aggressive religion may have profound linguistic effect. Perhaps the most rapid series of changes that are known for any language are those that applied to Old Irish between about 400 and 600 AD. The language spoken at the end of this period would have been quite unintelligible to someone from 200 years earlier. These changes relate to the introduction of Christianity into Ireland; we assume that there was a breakdown of communication between generations (or perhaps between classes) as younger people adopted the new faith and older ones rejected it.

[ ←63 ]
[←63]

只有少数声望群体的成员会学习一些非声望语言，例如商人（尽管在这里也可能使用洋泾浜语）和口译员。

Just a few members of the prestige group will learn something of the non-prestige language, e.g. traders (although even here a pidgin may be in use) and interpreters.

[ ←64 ]
[←64]

通常，这种情况发生是因为用少数人使用的语言制作教科书或报纸太耗时且成本太高。但这可以通过法令实现。缅甸目前的军事政权不允许用英语或缅甸语以外的语言出版任何东西，除非将其完全翻译成英语或缅甸语，以便他们能够检查内容。这实际上扼杀了所有用许多少数民族语言出版的作品，因为这些少数民族语言的使用者没有资源或精力来满足这一要求（Randy LaPolla，个人通信）。

Generally this happens because it is too time-consuming and expensive to produce school textbooks or newspapers in languages with just a small number of speakers. But it can be by decree. The present military regime in Myanmar (Burma) does not allow anything to be published in a language other than English or Burmese unless it is fully translated into English or Burmese, for them to be able to check the content. This effectively stifles all publishing in the many minority languages, since their speakers don't have the resources or energy to meet this requirement (Randy LaPolla, personal communication).

[ ←65 ]
[←65]

关于书写的优缺点的有益讨论可以在 Coomaraswamy (1949)、Harrisson (1937)、Archer (1943)、Dixon (1980: 86ff.) 及其中的进一步参考文献中找到。

Useful discussion of the disadvantages and advantages of writing will be found in Coomaraswamy (1949), Harrisson (1937), Archer (1943), Dixon (1980: 86ff.) and further references therein.

[ ←66 ]
[←66]

亚马逊流域现存的大多数土著语言都是由远离主要河流的群体使用的。一个显著的例外是皮拉罕人，他们虽然居住在亚马逊南部主要支流马德拉河附近，但仍保留着自己的语言。皮拉罕人保持着内向的态度，对巴西的欧洲生活方式没有什么好奇心。特别是，他们表示不希望自己的语言被书写，他们说：“不，保留葡萄牙语的字母表，我们的语言不能被书写下来。”这种态度无疑有助于他们保留自己的语言。（有关皮拉罕的信息来自 Dan 和 Keren Everett 的个人通信。）

Most of the indigenous languages that survive in Amazonia are spoken by groups which live well away from the main rivers. A notable exception is the Pirahã who still retain their own languages although they live close to the Madeira, the major southern tributary of the Amazon. The Pirahã maintain an inward-looking attitude, with little curiosity concerning what the European life-style in Brazil has to offer. In particular, they have stated that they do not wish to have their language written, saying: 'No, keep the alphabet for Portuguese, our language is not to be written down.' This attitude has undoubtedly assisted them to retain their language. (Information on Pirahã from Dan and Keren Everett, personal communication.)

[ ←67 ]
[←67]

一些现代巴布亚群体确实拥有舷外支架独木舟；这些独木舟很可能是最近从南岛邻居（或商人）那里获得的。

A few modern-day Papuan groups do have outrigger canoes; it is likely that these were fairly recently acquired from Austronesian neighbours (or traders).

[ ←68 ]
[←68]

Foley (1986: 26975) 讨论了这个问题，并提出了澳大利亚语言中反复出现的词形与新几内亚东部高地语言中反复出现的词形之间 15 个高度推测性的相似性。其中一半是单音节词（不是同源词的最佳指标），其中五个是单音节动词词根。此后，对澳大利亚语言的研究发现了几十个反复出现的双音节动词词根；巴布亚语言中没有发现任何合理的同源词。任何严肃的遗传联系假设都需要系统的音系和形态对应关系，而 Foley 提供的比这多得多。

Foley (1986: 26975) discusses this matter and presents fifteen highly speculative similarities between recurrent Australian forms and forms in the Eastern Highlands languages of New Guinea. Half of these are monosyllables (not the best indicators of cognation), five of them monosyllabic verb roots. Work on Australian languages since then has found several dozen recurrent disyllabic verb roots; no plausible cognates have been found with Papuan languages. Any serious hypothesis of genetic linkage would require systematic phonological and morphological correspondences very much more than Foley has provided.

[ ←69 ]
[←69]

事实上，情况比这更复杂。我们经常发现，一个语言的传播区域的边界会穿过该语言的方言。仅举一个例子，粘着代词只出现在南昆士兰州比贾拉语的一些方言中，这些方言与粘着代词的传播区域相邻。

The situation is in fact more complex than this. We often find the boundary of a diffusion area passing between the dialects of a language. To quote just one example, bound pronouns are found in only some dialects of the Bidjara language from south Queensland, those dialects which adjoin a diffusion area for bound pronouns.

[ ←70 ]
[←70]

事实上，在澳大利亚原住民生活的大约 5 万年中，步骤 (ii) 和 (iii) 可能发生过多次。所有证据都让我们能够重建上一次人口收缩和扩张的过程。

In fact, steps (ii) and (iii) could have happened several times during the 50,000 or so years that Aborigines have been in Australia. All that the evidence allows us to do is reconstruct the last contraction-and-expansion of population.

[ ←71 ]
[←71]

我之所以采用间断平衡作为语言发展模型，主要是为了充分说明澳大利亚的语言状况。本文是 Dixon（即将出版）的序言。

It was largely in order to adequately account for the linguistic situation in Australia that I had recourse to the idea of punctuated equilibrium as a model for language development. This essay is among other things a prolegomena to Dixon (forthcoming).

[ ←72 ]
[←72]

Meltzer (1995) 提供了一项关于年代早于 12,000 年前的遗址的调查结果。他提到，在 1964 年确定的 50 个年代更早的遗址中，只有 4 个进入了 1976 年版的名单，而没有一个进入了 1988 年版的名单。

Meltzer (1995) provides an informed survey of claims for dates earlier than about 12,000 BP. He mentions that of the fifty sites identified in 1964 as having an older date, only four made a 1976 version of that list and none made a 1988 list.

[ ←73 ]
[←73]

Payne (1990) 对南美语言中反复出现的语法形式进行了有益的调查

Payne (1990) provides a useful survey of grammatical forms that appear to recur in South American languages

[ ←74 ]
[←74]

请注意 Meil​​let 在其印欧方言研究中的评论（1967：169；斜体部分为本人所加）：“另一个结论是……即使在分离之前，印欧语系也由已经高度分化的习语组成，我们无权将印欧语系视为一种单一语言。每个大语系（斯拉夫语、日耳曼语、波罗的海语等）的特征在很大程度上标志着不属于一般印欧语系但属于印欧语时期的现象的延续。”（另见 Trubetzkoy 1939。）

还要注意的是，对于阿尔冈昆语，Siebert (1967: 39) 说“没有证据表明原始阿尔冈昆语曾经是一种绝对统一的言语方式”。

Note Meillet's comments, in his study of Indo-European dialects (1967: 169; my italics): 'Another conclusion . . . is that even before the separation Indo-European was composed of idioms which were already highly differentiated, and that we have no right to view Indo-European as a single language. The characteristic features of each of the large groups (Slavic, Germanic, Baltic, etc.) mark, to a great extent, the continuation of phenomena that do not belong to Indo-European in general and yet do belong to the Indo-European period.' (See also Trubetzkoy 1939.)

Note also that for Algonquian, Siebert (1967: 39) says 'there is no proof that proto-Algonquian was ever an absolutely uniform mode of speech'.

[ ←75 ]
[←75]

布卢姆菲尔德 (Bloomfield, 1933: 318) 指出：“比较法只有在假设存在统一的母语的情况下才能发挥作用，但不可通约的形式（如原始印欧语中的工具复数格结尾 *[-mis] 和 *[-bhis]）表明，这种假设是没有道理的。”为了适应统一原始语言的概念，印欧语学家花费了大量时间试图“解释”这种形式的对，但没有达成任何共识。

Bloomfield (1933: 318) remarked: 'The comparative method can work only on the assumption of a uniform parent language, but the incommensurable forms (such as *[-mis] and *[-bhis] as instrumental plural case endings in Primitive Indo-European) show us that this assumption is not justified.' In order to accommodate the idea of a uniform proto-language, Indo-Europeanists spend a great deal of time trying to 'explain' pairs of forms of this nature, but without reaching any consensus.

[ ←76 ]
[←76]

Trubetzkoy (1939) 评论道：“可能几乎没有一个单词会同时出现在所有印欧语系中。事实上，最普遍的单词在个别印欧语系中呈现出如此多的音系不规则性，以至于只有通过破坏事实才能重建它们的原始形式。”这表明，由具有许多共同特征的多种语言组成的原始语言区可能值得考虑。

Trubetzkoy (1939) commented 'there is probably almost no single word that occurs in all Indo-European languages. It is in fact the most widespread words that present in the individual Indo-European languages such phonological irregularities that their original form can be reconstructed only by doing violence to the facts.' This suggests that a proto-linguistic-area, consisting of a number of languages with many features in common, might be worthy of consideration.

[ ←77 ]
[←77]

我们同样可以考虑不同的一对语系，例如印欧语系和非亚语系。

We could equally well have considered a different pair of families, e.g., Indo-European and Afroasiatic.

[ ←78 ]
[←78]

坎贝尔 (fortcoming-b) 讨论了印欧语系向乌拉尔语系的借用，发现没有与原乌拉尔语系相关的借用。最古老的借用语系是前印度-伊朗语系和印度-伊朗语系向芬兰-乌戈尔语系的借用语。

Campbell (forthcoming-b) discusses loans from Indo-European languages into Uralic and finds none that relate to proto-Uralic. The oldest loans are from pre-Indo-Iranian and Indo-Iranian into Finno-Ugric.

[ ←79 ]
[←79]

Hashimoto (1976a) 对此进行了有益的讨论，他认为“在解决同源词/借词区别问题之前，谈论汉藏语系的确立还为时过早”。另请参阅 Ballard (1985) 和 Haudricourt (1961)。

There is useful discussion in Hashimoto (1976a) where he suggests that 'it is still premature to talk about an established language family for Sino-Tibetan before solving the problem of cognate/loan distinction'. See also Ballard (1985) and Haudricourt (1961).

[ ←80 ]
[←80]

课程内容通常也是单一文化的，教授知名群体的历史、文化和价值观，很少或根本不关注本土文化和习俗。

The content of classes is also generally monocultural, teaching about the history, culture and values of the prestige group, and paying little or no attention to indigenous culture and customs.

[ ←81 ]
[←81]

事实上，一些民族确实有意识地试图让自己的方言与其他民族的方言有所不同。但这种努力大多是在发音方面，这也许是语言使用中最突出的方面。在人们没有意识到这一点的情况下，他们的方言的语法惯例和词汇资源正在逐渐趋同。

In fact, some ethnic groups do consciously try to make their dialect different from that of other groups. But such efforts are mostly in the area of pronunciation, perhaps the most salient aspect of language use. Without people realising it, the grammatical conventions and lexical resources of their dialects are steadily converging.

[ ←82 ]
[←82]

即使在拥有多种官方语言的国家，人们也会强烈倾向于用一种语言来处理某些话题，用另一种语言来处理其他话题，例如巴拉圭的西班牙语和瓜拉尼语。

Even in nations with more than one official language, there can be a strong preference for some topics to be dealt with in one language and other topics in the other, e.g. Spanish and Guaraní in Paraguay.

[ ←83 ]
[←83]

随着母语属于印欧语系（意第绪语、德语、法语、俄语等）的人们逐渐将希伯来语作为日常对话语言，希伯来语也呈现出一些印欧语系的特征。例如，疑问代词现在用作关系从句的引导词，这在希伯来语的早期阶段是没有的（Aya Katz 和 Alexandra Aikhenvald，个人通信）。

As Hebrew came to be adopted as the language of everyday conversation, by people whose native languages were of the Indo-European family (Yiddish, German, French, Russian, etc.), it took on some Indo-European features. For instance, interrogative pronouns are now used as introducers of relative clauses, something that was not found in earlier stages of Hebrew (Aya Katz and Alexandra Aikhenvald, personal communication).

[ ←84 ]
[←84]

举个例子就清楚了。20 世纪 90 年代初，我看到一对福音派夫妇（一位美国传教士和他的葡萄牙妻子）将一种竞技游戏 UNO 引入了亚马逊丛林中的一个印第安村庄。他们教孩子们相互竞争，并试图超越对方，这与他们的生活方式完全不同。然后，​​传教士们又带了一套 UNO 作为礼物送给当地人民。他们比赛看谁能赢得游戏。这些传教士没有受过人类学培训，也不知道他们正在将一个全新的概念引入印第安人的生活（他们可能确实注意到印第安人的语言中没有“竞争”或“赢”这样的词）。不知不觉中，传教士们将一个以标点符号模式为主的群体的价值观强加给了一个一直处于平衡模式的平等主义民族。

An example will make this clear. In the early 1990s I observed an evangelical couple (an American missionary and his Portuguese wife) introduce UNO, a competitive game, into an Indian village in the Amazonian jungle. They taught the children to compete against each other, and to try to be better than each other, something that is entirely alien to their way of life. Then the missionaries brought another set of UNO as a present for the people. They had a competition to see who would get the game. These missionaries had no anthropological training and had no idea that they were introducing a quite new concept into the Indians' life (they might indeed have noticed that there are no words 'compete' or 'win' in the Indians' language). Unwittingly, the missionaries have imposed the values of a dominant group in punctuation mode on an egalitarian people who had been in equilibrium mode.

[ ←85 ]
[←85]

Dixon (1991b: 2467) 引用了一个具体的例子。

A specific example is quoted in Dixon (1991b: 2467).

[ ←86 ]
[←86]

例如，20 世纪 90 年代初，马库部落的一个家庭生了一个病婴。根据部落文化，如果得到特定巫师的祝福，婴儿就能活下来，但这个家庭没有钱支付巫师的费用。一位在该部落工作的巴西福音传教士自掏腰包支付了巫师的费用。

For instance, in the early 1990s, a family of the Makú tribe had a sick baby. According to tribal culture, the baby would live if accorded ritual blessing by a specific shaman, but the family lacked the resources to pay the shaman. A Brazilian evangelical missionary, who was working with the tribe, paid for the shaman from his own pocket.

[ ←87 ]
[←87]

“头部标记”和“依赖性标记”这两个术语是由尼科尔斯（1986）在经典论文中提出的。

The terms 'head marking' and 'dependent marking' were introduced in a classic paper by Nichols (1986).

[ ←88 ]
[←88]

主要有两种依赖标记。在拉丁语中，及物主语 (A) 的标记与不及物主语 (S) 相同，即主格；及物宾语 (O) 的标记不同，即宾格。另一种系统是，S 和 O 以相同的方式标记，即绝对格，而 A 以不同的方式标记，即作格。（完整讨论见 Dixon 1994。）

There are two main kinds of dependent marking. In Latin the transitive subject (A) has the same marking as intransitive subject (S), nominative case; and transitive object (O) has a different marking, accusative case. The alternative system is where S and O are marked in the same way, by absolutive case, and A in a different way, by ergative case. (A full discussion is in Dixon 1994.)

[ ←89 ]
[←89]

许多语言结合了主语和从属标记。例如，在拉丁语中，由于动词包含有关人称和主语数量的信息，因此有完整的从属标记和部分主语标记；audit 实际上是“hear”的第三人称单数现在时（主动、直陈式）形式。

Many languages combine head and dependent marking. In Latin, for instance, there is full dependent marking and also partial head marking since the verb includes information about person and number of subject; audit is actually the third person singular present tense (active, indicative) form of 'hear'.

[ ←90 ]
[←90]

不及物动词有“分裂 S”系统。对于某些动词（主要指有意志行为），不及物主语 (S) 用与及物动词中 A 相同的前缀标记，而对于其他动词（主要指非意志行为和状态），S 用与及物动词中 O 相同的后缀标记。

Intransitive verbs have a 'split-S' system. For some verbs (mostly referring to volitional actions) the intransitive subject (S) is marked by the same prefix that shows A with a transitive verb, and with other verbs (mostly referring to non-volitional actions and states), S is marked by the same suffix that shows O with a transitive verb.

[ ←91 ]
[←91]

如果 A 和 O 都是第三人称，那么 O 会在 A 之前 (Merlan 1982)。

If both A and O are third person, then O will precede A (Merlan 1982).

[ ←92 ]
[←92]

事实上，对于某些语言，语言学家认为无法区分名词和形容词类，例如 Dench (1995: 5155)。

Indeed, for some languages linguists consider that a distinction between noun and adjective class cannot be made, e.g. Dench (1995: 5155).

[ ←93 ]
[←93]

在斐济语正字法中，c 代表浊齿根擦音（很像英语 this 的首音）。

In the Fijian orthography, c represents a voiced apico-dental fricative (rather like the initial sound in English this).

[ ←94 ]
[←94]

澳大利亚总体上是个例外。例如，在澳大利亚国立大学，20 世纪 70 年代和 80 年代完成的博士论文中约有 80% 是以前未描述过的语言的语法。美国只有少数语言学系鼓励学生撰写语言语法作为博士论文，尤其是加州大学圣巴巴拉分校和俄勒冈大学。

Australia is, by and large, an exception. At the Australian National University, for instance, about 80% of the Ph.D. dissertations completed in the 1970s and 1980s were grammars of previously undescribed languages. Just a few linguistics departments in the USA encourage their students to write grammars of languages for a Ph.D. dissertation, notably the University of California at Santa Barbara and the University of Oregon.

[ ←95 ]
[←95]

我不会尝试列出完整的清单，但过去四十年的一些理论包括：转换语法、标准理论、扩展标准理论、修订扩展标准理论、治理和约束理论、原则和参数理论（所有这些都与乔姆斯基有关）、标签学、量级和范畴语法、系统语法、功能语法、子依赖语法、分层语法、生成语义学、关系语法、弧对语法、词汇功能语法、广义短语结构语法、中心驱动短语结构语法、认知语法、角色和指称语法。非语言学家的读者肯定会同意我的愤世嫉俗的评论，即如果一门学科可以产生、拒绝和取代如此多的“理论”（在大多数情况下，无需费心根据“理论”来编写语言语法），那么可以说它是不平衡的。

I won't attempt a full list, but some of the theories of the past forty years are: Transformational Grammar, Standard Theory, Extended Standard Theory, Revised Extended Standard Theory, Government and Binding Theory, Principles and Parameters Theory (all of these associated with Chomsky), Tagmemics, Scale-and-category Grammar, Systemic Grammar, Functional Grammar, Daughter Dependency Grammar, Stratificational Grammar, Generative Semantics, Relational Grammar, Arc-Pair Grammar, Lexical Functional Grammar, Generalised Phrase Structure Grammar, Head-driven Phrase Structure Grammar, Cognitive Grammar, Role and Reference Grammar. The non-linguist reader will surely concur with my cynical comment that if a discipline can spawn, reject and replace so many 'theories' (in most cases without bothering to actually write a grammar of a language in terms of the 'theory') then it could be said to be off balance.

[ ←96 ]
[←96]

威廉·麦格雷戈 (William McGregor) 的博士论文（在悉尼大学）是关于澳大利亚语言 Gooniyandi 的语法，以系统语法（非基础理论）的形式进行阐述；这基本上就是在这种特定语言中识别形式主义指定的项目。在修改论文以供发表时，他确实为所设置的类别和结构提供了依据，并评论道（McGregor 1990：v）“特别强调了论证，而论证在系统理论中一直被忽视”。

William McGregor's Ph.D. thesis (at the University of Sydney) was a grammar of Gooniyandi, an Australian language, cast in terms of Systemic Grammar (a non-basic theory); this basically consisted in recognising in this particular language the items specified by the formalism. When revising the thesis for publication, he did include justification for the categories and structures set up, commenting (McGregor 1990: v) 'particular emphasis has been placed on argumentation, a consideration which has been consistently ignored in systemic theorising'.

[ ←97 ]
[←97]

据我所知，只有在莫斯科才出现了这样一种奇怪的信念：可能存在“训练有素的比较学家”，即可以自由研究某个语系（无需对该语系的任何语言进行过详细研究，也无需对其中任何一种语言有深入的了解）然后重建原始语言的人。这些“训练有素的比较学家”是由诺斯特拉学派的狂热爱好者“训练”出来的（见 §4.1）。无需多言。

Only in Moscow (to my knowledge) has the peculiar belief emerged that there may be such a thing as a 'trained comparativist', someone who can be let loose on a language family (without having done detailed work on any of the languages of the family, or having a close knowledge of any of them) and will then reconstruct the proto-language. These 'trained comparativists' have been 'trained' by aficionados of the Nostratic school (see §4.1). No more need be said.

[ ←98 ]
[←98]

除了形式主义者之外，最近还出现了另一群人，他们被称为“空谈类型学家”。他们回避形式主义，但从未深入研究过语言。由于缺乏必要的学徒，他们无法正确理解语言的工作原理，也无法区分可靠和不可靠的语法。他们参考语法，并撰写类型学概括的文章；但他们的结果往往是幼稚和无益的。

Besides the formalists, there is another group that has sprung up recently, who can be called 'armchair typologists'. They eschew formalisms but have never worked intensively on a language. Lacking the necessary apprenticeship, they don't have the appropriate understanding of how languages work or the ability to distinguish between reliable and unreliable grammars. They consult grammars, and make an essay at typological generalisations; but their results are frequently naive and unenlightening.

[ ←99 ]
[←99]

布卢姆菲尔德（1933：20）评论道：“关于语言，唯一有用的概括是归纳概括。我们认为应该具有普遍性的特征，在下一种可接触的语言中可能就不存在了……某些特征无论如何都是普遍存在的，这一事实值得注意，也需要解释；当我们掌握了关于多种语言的足够数据时，我们将不得不回到一般语法问题上，解释这些相似之处和不同之处，但这种研究不是推测性的，而是归纳性的。”

Bloomfield (1933: 20) remarked: 'The only useful generalizations about language are inductive generalizations. Features which we think ought to be universal may be absent from the very next language that becomes accessible . . . The fact that some features are, at any rate, widespread, is worthy of notice and calls for an explanation; when we have adequate data about many languages, we shall have to return to the problem of general grammar and to explain these similarities and divergences, but this study, when it comes, will not be speculative but inductive.'

[ ←100 ]
[←100]

例如，第 9.1 节中描述的中心词/从属标记与形容词类类型的相关性是基于对大约 300 种语言的语法的考察（我实际上查看了 500 多种语法，但并非全部都包含相关信息）。其中没有涉及“抽样技术”；我只是查阅了我可以访问的图书馆中所有可用的语法。

For example, the correlations described in §9.1 between head/dependent marking and types of adjective class are based on an examination of the grammars of about 300 languages (I actually looked at over 500 grammars, but they did not all include the relevant information). There was no 'sampling technique' involved; I simply consulted every available grammar in the libraries I had access to.

[ ←101 ]
[←101]

历史语言学家认为，比较法只能在有限的时间范围内起作用。尼科尔斯（1992：56）给出的时间段约为 8,000 年，但许多学者会选择更短的时间段（可能是 5,000 年）。

这与我的观点一致，即家谱（与比较方法相关）只适用于标点时期，而标点时期不太可能持续超过 5,0008,000 年，而且持续时间通常会短得多。

Historical linguists have suggested that the comparative method is only workable up to a limited time-depth. Nichols (1992: 56) gives a period of about 8,000 years, but many scholars would opt for a shorter period (perhaps 5,000 years).

This is compatible with my suggestion that family trees (for which the comparative method is relevant) are only applicable during periods of punctuation, which will not be likely to last longer than 5,0008,000 years, and will often last for a much shorter time.

[ ←102 ]
[←102]

非洲有如此多的语言，以至于很难看出那里的语言状况的秩序和组织。“尼日尔-刚果”和“尼罗-撒哈拉”的思想对于组织人们对这些语言的了解无疑是有益的。现在应该重新研究这些思想，看看其中哪些部分确实模拟了遗传联系，哪些部分本质上描述了地域关系。

There are so many languages in Africa that it is difficult to perceive order and organisation in the linguistic situation there. The 'Niger-Congo' and 'Nilo-Saharan' ideas have certainly been beneficial as a way of organising what is known about these languages. Now these ideas should be restudied, to see which parts of them do model genetic connection and which parts essentially describe areal relationships.

[ ←103 ]
[←103]

过去几年，人们对“濒危语言”问题的关注度不断提高，关于该主题的研讨会很多，甚至成立了“收集信息”的协会。真正需要做的只有一件事：走出去描述一种语言！我的总体印象是，相当一部分关心这个问题的人除了谈论之外什么也不做；他们甚至没有想过自己进行实地工作。

In the last few years there has been increased attention to the question of 'endangered languages' with a number of symposia on the topic and even societies formed to 'gather information'. There is only one thing that really needs to be done get out there and describe a language! My general impression is that a fair proportion of the people concerned about this issue do little besides talk; they are not even thinking about undertaking field work themselves.

[ ←104 ]
[←104]

允许语言传教士在当地人民中工作的国家应该密切关注从事这项工作的人的类型，并监督他们的行为。如第 8 节所述，一些传教士尊重当地文化，并认为自己为当地人民提供了基督教的额外选择。其他人则试图压制传统宗教、文化、歌曲等，并用他们自己的“基督教”品牌取而代之。

Countries which do allow linguistic missionaries to work among their indigenous peoples should pay close attention to the type of people undertaking this work, and monitor how they behave. As noted in §8, some missionaries respect the indigenous culture and see themselves as offering Christianity as an additional option for the people. Others attempt to suppress traditional religion, culture, songs, etc., and replace them with their own brand of 'Christianity'.

[ ←105 ]
[←105]

从语言消亡情况的研究中我们学到的一个令人悲伤的教训是，一个社区没有意识到其语言受到威胁，直到为时已晚，无法采取任何措施来补救这种情况。（见 Dixon 1991b：253。）

A sad lesson that has been learnt from the study of language-death situations is that a community does not realise its language is threatened until it is too late to do anything to remedy the situation. (See Dixon 1991b: 253.)

法国人最努力地保护（并扩大）他们语言的使用范围。然而，在被视为最领先的语言学系之一（位于里昂）中，所有年级的学生都会选修一门课程，帮助他们理解用英语撰写的语言作品。这是一个现实的策略，承认英语作为国际交流语言的稳步发展。

The French try most assiduously to preserve (and extend) the areas of use of their language. Yet in what is looked upon as one of the most go-ahead linguistics departments (in Lyon), students in all years take a course assisting them to understand linguistic works written in English. This is a realistic strategy, acknowledging the steady movement towards English as the language of international communication.
